

































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Omutanke Teofiro, abhanto abhaaru ꞉mbaikongʼiri kwandeka amangʼana ghano ghaakooru haare itu.
Amangʼana ghayo, ntwabhooriiru na abhanto bhano bhaagharooche na amaiso ghaabho, koru ekimbere momeremo ghe Yeesu. Bhayo nebhu bhaare kureghani amangʼana gha Yeesu.
Na eni ghwiki, ꞉nintamboneriire amangʼana ghayo ghansi. ꞉Nendooche bhwaheene nkwandekere,
korri iye umanye kemwe obhuheene bhwa amangʼana ghano weeghiribhu.
Hano omutemi Herode aare omukama wo omukowa gho Yuudeya, aareho omusengeri omwe, eriina reeche Sakariya, we eghekomo kyo omusengeri Abhiya. Saabheeti mughaache wunsi aare we ekehita kyo omusengeri Haruuni.
Bhansi bhabhere bhaare abhaheene mbere yo Omutemi Ghiteema. Bhaare kughoota amaragherri ghaache ghansi, no okughasooka bhataana risoro rinsirinsi.
Bhataare ꞉bhaibhwire omoona, gho okubha Saabheeti no omoghomba aare, na bhansi mbaakunguhire bhukongʼu.
Orosiko romwe, yaare enkaagha ye eghekomo kyo Sakariya ghukora emeremo ghyo obhusengeri mbere ya Ghiteema.
Sakariya aghachaghoru ghusoha mo Nyumba Ehoreeru ya Ghiteema, amuhemberre muyo ekoroso, ghote yaare esemoka yo obhusengeri.
Hano Sakariya aasohire kuhemba ekoroso, abhanto abhaaru bhaare bhaikomaine kibhara ye Enyumba Ehoreeru bharasaasaama Ghiteema.
Hari remwe, maraika wo Omutemi Ghiteema akamohyokera muyo. Maraika oyo, akaimerra orubhareka ro bhoryo rwa ahase ho okuhemberra ekoroso.
Hano Sakariya aamorooche, aghaitaki, akoobhoha bhukongʼu.
Ghasi bhoono maraika oyo akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Iye Sakariya, utakoobhoha! Ghano ꞉usabhire Ghiteema, ꞉naghoghuure. Mughaacho Saabheeti arakwibhorra omoona we eghesubhe, uramuroka Yohana.
Omoona oyo newe akugheri mubhe na amachomeru bhukongʼu. Abhanto abhaaru bharachomeru okwibhoru ghooche,
gho okubha arabha omokoro kubhanto mbere yo Omutemi Ghiteema. Atakaanyo amaro ghe emisabhiibhu hande kiyo ghinsighinsi kino ghekureebhi. Omutemi Ghiteema aramwichori Enkoro Ehoreeru, kuru aani monda ya nyakowaabho.
Aragheri Abhaisiraeri abhaaru bhahonchokere Omutemi Ghiteema waabho.
Aramukangata Omutemi, aseemi abhanto komoturungʼana, aani na amanagha, ne Enkoro ya Ghiteema ghote muno aare Eriya. Arabhaighwerani abhaibhori na abhaana bhaabho, na abhatamwe arabhakora bhabhe no obhungʼaini no obhuheene haare Ghiteema.”
Neho Sakariya ꞉abhoorri maraika akabhughaa, “Bhoono ghayo bhwe ghakubha na hano eni na mkaane ꞉ntokunguhire?”
Maraika oyo akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Neeni Ghabhurieri, ono nkwimerra mbere ya Ghiteema. Ghiteema ꞉antomire eno, niiche ghokubhoorra amangʼana amachomu ghayo.
Ghasi bhoono, gho okubha ꞉tumasire amangʼana ghaane, ghano obhuheene ghaghukoru, kuwansera bhoono urabha rimuumu. Tokunaghi kughamba kohikera enkaagha eno amangʼana ghano ghaghukoru.”
Enkaagha eyo, abhanto bhano bhaare kughanya Sakariya bhakaroghoora kurora ghote ꞉aghechiire mo Nyumba Ehoreeru ya Ghiteema.
Hano aruuremu, aghatamu kughambana nabhu. Hari remwe, bhakamanya arooche amaroro moore mo Nyumba Ehoreeru ya Ghiteema. Aare kubheerekerri na amabhoko, akaghenderri kubha rimuumu.
Hano enkaagha yaache yo oghusengera yaasirre, akaghi ka.
Hano ghayo ghaasirre, Saabheeti mughaa Sakariya akaritoha. Akamara emieri etaano ꞉aikaire mooche akabhughaa,
“Omutemi Ghiteema newe ꞉ankoriire ighoo no oghunsakeri. ꞉Anduusiri esooko kubhanto.”
Hano enda ya Saabheeti yaahikiri emyeri esansabha, Ghiteema aghatoma maraika Ghabhurieri ahike komonke wonde ono aare atamaraamanya omosubhe, eriina reeche Mariyamu. Omonke oyo aare momoghi gho Naasareeti, momukowa gho Ghariraaya. Mariyamu aare ꞉arwechiiru no omosubhe omwe, eriina reeche Yuusufu, we ekehita kyo omutemi Daudi.

Maraika oyo, akaghi haare Mariyamu, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Ndaghukeeri, iye ono ꞉unookiiru bhukongʼu! Omutemi Ghiteema hamwe aani na iye.”
Mariyamu akabhabhayera bhukongʼu kumangʼana ghayo oghuure, aghaitegherra akabhughaa, “N-gunkeeri ke kuno?”
Ghasi bhoono maraika oyo akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Iye Mariyamu, utakoobhoha, Ghiteema ꞉akunookiire enooko.
Tegherra, uraritoha, na uraibhora omoona we eghesubhe, uramuroka Yeesu.
Arabha omokoro, arabherekeru Omoona wa Ghiteema ono aani ighoro ya bhinsi. Omutemi Ghiteema, aramuha obhubhaahi bhwo omutemi Daudi, sookoro yaache.
Arabha omukama wa abhaibhoru bha Yaakobho amakora ghansi. Obhukama bhooche bhutaaghosira kemwe.”
Mariyamu akabhoori maraika oyo akabhughaa, “Ghano mbwe ghakubha, na hano eni ntamaraamanya omosubhe?”
Maraika akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Enkoro Ehoreeru araghwichera, na amanagha gha Ghiteema ono aani ighoro ya bhinsi gharakoghubha. No omoona ono okwibhora arabha omuhoreeru na arabherekeru Omoona wa Ghiteema.
Tegherra nkubhoorre! Kuru monke waanyu Saabheeti, ono bhaabherekire omoghomba, kobhokungu bhooche ꞉aritohire enda yo omoona we eghesubhe. Omweri ghuno ngo-gha sansabha koru ꞉aritohire.
Gho okubha Ghiteema itareho engʼana eno aghutamu ghukora.”
Mariyamu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Eni n-omubhaghasi wo Omutemi Ghiteema, ibhe haare eni ghote ꞉obhughire.” Hari remwe, maraika oyo akaghi.
Ghochensiko chiyochiyo, Mariyamu aghaseemi orughendo, akangoha koghi momoghi ghomwe mokyaro kye chinkereghe cha Yuuda.
Aghasoha monyumba ya Sakariya, akamukeeri Saabheeti.
Hano Saabheeti ꞉oghuure riraka ryo oghukeerani ko Mariyamu, omoona ono aare monda yaache akabharaana. Hayohayo, Saabheeti aghaichoribhu Enkoro Ehoreeru.
Neho aaghambire ko riiraka rikoro akabhughaa, “Kubhaghaikoro bhansi, iye niye ꞉unookiiru! No omoona ono okwibhora, wunsi ꞉nanookiru.
Eni ne-wuuye, kuru nyakowaabho Omutemi waito ꞉aichire ghunkeeri?
Hano ꞉nooghuure obhukeerani bhoocho, hayohayo omoona ono aani monda yaane, ꞉abharaanire ko ghuchomeru.
Wuuna echaghati, gho okubha ꞉wiitabheriiri amangʼana ghano Omutemi Ghiteema ꞉akubhooriire gharakorubhu!”
Mariyamu akabhughaa, “Omotema ghoone ghuramwitumi Omutemi Ghiteema,
ne enkoro yaane irachomera Ghiteema, Omutoori waane,
gho okubha ꞉arooche obhubhaabhayeri bho omubhaghasi waache. Koru bhoono, abhanto bha amakora ghansi bharabha bharamberekera omunooku.
Ghiteema wa amanagha ghansi ꞉ankoriire ekiroghooro, ne eriina reeche, ne-rihoreeru.
Araghenderri kubharorra amaabhera abhanto bha amakora na amakora, bhano bhakomusooka.
꞉Akorre amangʼana amakoro ku amanagha ghaache, ꞉asanchiri bhano bhaana eghesiraani mometema gheebho.
꞉Abhasekiiri abhakoro kobhetumbe bheebho bhyo obhubhaahi, ꞉abhatirri abhanyoohu.
꞉Abhaighotiri bhwaheene bhano ꞉bharambokire, ghasi bhoono, abhaame ꞉abhatyambiri mabhoko machwe.
꞉Asakiiri Abhaisiraeri abhabhaghasi bhaache, gho okohiita kubhaabhera.
Ghote aare ꞉arengire bhasookoro bhaitu, Ibhurahimu no orwibhoro rooche, amakora ghansi.”
Neho Mariyamu ꞉aikaire o Saabheeti emieri etato, akamara akagharoka waache.
Hano orosiko ro oghwitoorani ko Saabheeti rwahikire, akaibhora omoona we eghesubhe.
Hano abhamenyani bhaache na bha waabho bhooghuure ghaare Omutemi Ghiteema ꞉amwabhiire, bhaghachomeru hamwe.
Hano aahikiri orosiko ro kanaane, bhaghaacha ghusaara omoona oyo. Bhaghatuna komuroka eriina Sakariya, eriina re isawaabho.
Ghasi bhoono nyakowaabho akaanga akabhughaa, “Tekubha! Abherekeru Yohana.”
Bhakamugharokeri, “Aka! Endoko eyo itaremu mokehita keenyu!”
Neho bhaabhoorri isawaabho gho okomwereki na amabhoko, korri abhabhoorre eriina rino aghotuna kuroka omoona waache.
Akabhasabha ekibhaau, hano bhaamuhaire, akaandekaa, “Eriina reeche newe Yohana.” Bhansi bhakaroghoora.
Hayohayo, omonu gho Sakariya ghughaasama, ororeme rughatachoka, aghasimi kughamba ghwiki, araitumi Ghiteema.
Abhamenyani bhaache bhansi bhakoobhoha bhukongʼu. Engʼana eyo ighasancha bhukongʼu mokyaro ghinsi kye chinkereghe cha Yuudeya.
Abhanto bhansi bhano bhooghuure, bhakabha bharaibhoori mometwe gheebho, bharabhughaa, “Omoona oyo mbwe ariicha kubha?” Bhakabhugha ighoo, gho okubha n-obhuheene, Omutemi Ghiteema aare hamwe nawe.
Sakariya isawaabho omoona oyo, aghaichoribhu Enkoro Ehoreeru. Akaruusi obhurooti akabhughaa,
“Omutemi Ghiteema wa Abhaisiraeri akumibhu, gho okubha ꞉abhaichiire no oghutongora abhanto bhaache.
꞉Atuhaire omutoori ono aghoote amanagha, koru mokehita kyo omubhaghasi waache Daudi,
ghote aare ꞉aghambire hayo kare kuhetera abharooti bhaache abhahoreeru.
Naatubhooriire ighoo, aratutoorri koru kubhabhisa bhaitu, na koru mumabhoko gha bhano ꞉bhatureghire.
Akabhugha ighoo, arabharorra amaabhera bhasookoro bhaitu, no okohiita riraghano reeche rihoreeru rino aakorre nabhu.
Kurehera kuyo neku koore aaraheriire sookoro yiitu Ibhurahimu,
ighoo, aratusakeri itu, atutoorri koru mumabhoko gha abhabhisa bhaitu, tubhe turamubhaghasi tutaana ehaho.
Ghwiki, tubhe abhanyoohu na abhaheene mbere yaache, chensiko chiitu chinsi.
Iye moona waane, urabha urabherekeru omurooti wa Ghiteema ono aani ighoro ya bhinsi, uramutangorra Omutemi, komurabheri enchera.
Urareghaneri abhanto bhaache ighoo, bharatooribhu gho okwabheru ebhibhe bheebho.
Ghiteema waito aratwabhera ko ghotureetera obhutooribhu bhooche koru mwisaaro, ghote obhurabhu bhwe ereebha rekurasa,
na bhurabhamorekeri bhano bhaani mokeruutu, bhano bhaani gho chitaabhu na kohaho yo oghoku. Ghwiki bhuratutangorra, tughende monchera ye emirembe.”
Omoona oyo Yohana aghakiina, akabhona chenguru che Enkoro Ehoreeru. Akaghi ghwikara mwibhara, kohikera enkaagha eno ꞉aiyerekiri ku Abhaisiraeri.
Gho nkaagha eyo ꞉aibhwiru Yohana, Kaisari Aughusto akeerekerri ighoo, abhanto bhansi bhano bhaani wanse yo obhubhaahi bhooche, bhaghende kwandeku.
Kwandeku kuyo, neku kwaare ko ghwansa, ghughakoru enkaagha eno Kirenio aare omubhaahi wo omukowa gho Siriya.
Ko riyo, abhanto bhansi bhakaghi kira omonto momoghi gho waabho.
Yuusufu wunsi, akaru momoghi gho Naasareeti, momukowa gho Ghariraaya. Akariina koghi momoghi gho Bhetereheemu, momukowa gho Yuudeya. Bhetereheemu neghu ghware omoghi gho omutemi Daudi, na Yuusufu aare we ekehita ke Daudi.
Yuusufu akaghi kwandeku hamwe na Mariyamu, ono aare ꞉amorwechire. Enkaagha eyo Mariyamu aare ꞉aritohire.
Hano bhaahikire eyo, enkaagha yo oghwitoorani ghooche ikahekeerana.
Aghaitoorani omoona we eghesubhe omutangi, akamoswari chingebho che ekeena, akamuraari moghento kyo okoriiseri chetigho. Akaibhorru muyo, gho okubha bhataabhwine hokomisi monyumba ya abhagheni.
Bhaareho abhariisi bhe chetigho bhararaarerra chetigho chaabho kerisho obhotiko.
Hari remwe, bhakahyokeru na maraika omwe wo Omutemi Ghiteema, ne emirengaari ghyo Omutemi Ghiteema ghikabhamoreki hase hansi. Bhakoobhoha bhukongʼu.
Maraika oyo akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Mutakoobhoha, ꞉mbaretiire amangʼana amachomu ghano ghakubhachomera bhukongʼu abhanto bhansi.
Reero komoghi gho Daudi, ꞉aibhwiru Omutoori waanyu. Omutoori oyo newe Omutemi, ghwiki newe Kirisito omwenemwene.
Ekimanyerri kyo okwereki ghayo n-ighoo, murabhona ekengʼwerre kiraaribhu moghento kyo okoriiseri chetigho, ꞉bhagheswarri chingebho che ekeena.”
Hari remwe, ghaghaacha amakomo na amakomo gha abhamaraika koru ghwisaaro, ghakabha gharaitumi Ghiteema, gharabhughaa,
“Ghiteema aitumibhu ghwisaaro! Na monse, emirembe ghibhe kubhanto bhano ꞉akumiri.”
Hano abhamaraika bhayo bhaamarre, bhakagharoka ghwisaaro. Neho abhariisi bhaabhoorraine bharabhughaa, “Tughende Bhetereheemu, turore rino ꞉ribhaire eyo, ghote Omutemi Ghiteema ꞉atubhooriire.”
Bhakaghi ngurunguru. Hano bhaahikire, bhakabhona Mariyamu na Yuusufu, no omoona ekengʼwerre ꞉amisiri moghento kyo okoriiseri chetigho.
Hano bhaarooche omoona oyo, bhakareghani kubhanto amangʼana ghansi gho omoona oyo, ghano maraika aare aabhabhooriire.
Abhanto bhansi bhano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaabhooriiru na abhariisi bhayo, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu.
Ghasi Mariyamu aghakira naghu, akabha araghitegherra.
Neho bhoono abhariisi bhayo bhaahonchokire, eno bharamwitumi Ghiteema ku ghansi ghano bhooghuure no okurora. Amangʼana ghaare ghote bhaabhooriiru na maraika.
Hano omoona oyo aahikiri chensinko inyaanye, bhakamusaara, bhakamuroka eriina Yeesu. Riyo neru eriina rino ꞉ahaabhiru na maraika, enkaagha eno nyakowaabho atamaraaritoha.
Neho Yuusufu na Mariyamu bhaamarre chensiko cho okurabhibhu koobho, ghote amaragherri gha Musa ghaghotuna. Ko riyo bhakaghi Yerusareemu, kohira Yeesu, korri bhamutoore mbere yo Omutemi Ghiteema.
Mbaakorre kee hayo, ghote yaandekiru kumaragherri gho Omutemi Ghiteema, gharabhughaa, “Omoona omutangi we eghesubhe, ohoru kubha omuhoreeru mbere yo Omutemi Ghiteema.”
Hamwe na ghayo, mbaatunire bharuusi ekemwenso ghote yaandekiru kumaragherri gho Omutemi Ghiteema, gharabhughaa, “Bharuusi ebheghuuti bhibhere hande amaana abhere ghe ebheghuuti.”
Aareho omonto omwe Yerusareemu hayo, eriina reeche Simeoni. Aare omuheene, no omusaighi Ghiteema. Aare kughanya kurora ghutooribhu kwa Abhaisiraeri, na Enkoro Ehoreeru aare hamwe nawe.
Enkoro Ehoreeru aare ꞉amwighoriire ighoo, taghoku akeere kurora Kirisito koru ko Omutemi Ghiteema.
Hayo, Enkoro Ehoreeru aghakangata Simeoni ghusoha ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema. Hano aasohire muyo, akabhona abhaibhori bha Yeesu bharahira omoona ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, korri bhamukorre ghote amaragherri ghaare ghotuna.
Simeoni akaghegha omoona oyo mumabhoko ghaache, eno araitumi Ghiteema, arabhughaa,
“Omutemi, onyitabherri eni omubhaghasi waacho neku ne emirembe, ghote wandengire eni.
Gho okubha ꞉nendooche obhutoori bhuno ꞉ureetire,
bhuno ꞉useemiri korri bhohyoke kubhanto bhansi.
Obhutoori bhuyo nebhu obhurabhu bhuno bhokubhamorekeri bhano bhatare Abhayahudi, bhamanye. Na ghwiki abhanto bhaacho Abhaisiraeri, bhabhone emerengaari, ghino ghekugheri bhaitumibhu.”
Amangʼana ghano Simeoni aaghambire ghakaroghoori abhaibhori bha Yeesu.
Hayo Simeoni akabhanooka, akabhoorra Mariyamu, nyakowaabho omoona oyo akabhughaa, “Omoona ono, ꞉achaaghwiru na Ghiteema korri Abhaisiraeri abhaaru bhasire, na Abhaisiraeri abhande abhaaru, bhatooribhu. Arabha ekimanyerri ke Ghiteema, ono akwangu na abhanto.
Ko riyo amaitegherro gha abhanto abhaaru gharamanyikana bhurabhu. Iye ghwiki urooghu obhorro bhukongʼu momotema ghoocho, ghote ꞉utoochiru ne ekinyamaino ekyeghe.”
Ghwiki aareho omurooti omwe omokungu, ono ꞉akunguhire bhukongʼu, eriina reeche Ana. Isawaabho aare Fanueri, we ekehita ke Asheeri. Ana oyo, koru ꞉atetiru, akamenya emeeka mohungate eghyene na mosubhe waache, kumaruho mosubhe waache aghaku.
Aghasaagha omosino, akabha arasengera Ghiteema ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema omwise no obhotiko, ko ghusabha no okwiyima ebhyakori. Aare ꞉ahikiri emeeka mirongo enaane na ene (84).
Enkaagha eyoeyo Ana akahyoka, aghasimi ghwitumi Ghiteema. Akabhugha amangʼana gho omoona oyo kubhanto bhansi bhano bhaare komughanya Ghiteema aratongora Yerusareemu.
Hano Yuusufu na Mariyamu, bhaamarre ghukora ghansi ghano amaragherri gha Omutemi Ghiteema ghaare ghotuna, bhakagharoka waabho momoghi gho Naasareeti momukowa gho Ghariraaya.
Omoona aghakiina, akabha na amanagha, aghaichoribhu obhungʼaini, na akabha aranooku na Ghiteema.
Abhaibhori bha Yeesu, bhaare ne esemoka yo oghotiira momoghi gho Yerusareemu kira mooka, konyangi ye Ebhaasaka.
Hano Yeesu aahikiri emeeka ikomi ne ebhere, bhakaghi nawe konyangi, gho okubha n-esemoka yaabho yaare.
Hano chensiko che enyangi chaasirre, abhaibhori bhaache bhakagharoka ka, ghasi Yeesu naasaaghire Yerusareemu. Abhaibhori bhaache ꞉bhatamanyire ighoo,
gho okubha ꞉mbaitegheriire ighoo, hamwe aani na abhaghendi bhaache, bhano bhaare kugharoka ka. Hano orosiko romwe rwasirre, bhaghasimi komotuna kubhawaabho na kubhasaani bhaabho.
Hano aabhabhorre, bhakagharoka Yerusareemu, korri bhamotune eyo.
Orosiko ro ghatato, bhakamubhona ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema. Aare ꞉aikaire hamwe na abheeghi, arabhategherra no okubhabhoori chingʼana.
Abhanto bhansi bhano bhaamoghuure bhuno aare kughamba, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu ghote aare kumanya no okubhagharokeri.
Hano abhaibhori bhaache bhaamorooche, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu. Nyakowaabho akamubhoori akabhughaa, “Moona waane, ghooke ꞉otukoriire ke hayo? Eni na isawaanyu ntwahahire bhukongʼu hano twaare koghotuna!”
Akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Ghooke mwaare ghontuna? ꞉Mutamanyire ighoo, ndatunu nibhe mo Enyumba ya Taata?”
Ghasi bhoono righarokeri riyo, abhaibhori bhaache bhataamongwere.
Neho Yeesu aatanwere na abhaibhori bhaache, koghi waabho ka momoghi gho Naasareeti, aare kubhasooka. Ghansi ghano ghaabhaire, nyakowaabho akaghabhechi momotema ghooche.
Yeesu akaghenderri ghokiina, akabha no obhungʼaini, akabha arachomera Ghiteema na abhanto.
Ghware omooka gho ikomi na ghataano gho obhubhaahi bho Kaisari Tibherio. Bhontio Bhiraato aare omubhaahi wo mukowa gho Yuudeya. Herode Antibhasi aare omutemi wo mukowa gho Ghariraaya. Firipo, mura waabho Herode aare omutemi wo mukowa gho Iturea na gho Tarakoniti. Risania wunsi aare omutemi wo mukowa gho Abhirene.
Enkaagha eyo, Anasi na Kayabha nebhu bhaare abhasengeri abhakoro. Ghwiki, gho nkaagha eyo, Yohana omoona wa Sakariya, aare mwibhara. Hano aare eyo, akabhorru engʼana ya Ghiteema.
Akaghi ahase hansi hano haani rubhareka yo orooche ro Yorodani. Akabha arareghaneri abhanto engʼana eyo akabhughaa, “Momwishoorri Ghiteema no kubhaatiisu, korri abhaabhere ebhibhe bheenyu!”
Amangʼana ghayo ghaare ghote ghaandekiru moghitabho kyo omurooti Isaaya gharabhughaa, “Omonto aratiiri riiraka mwibhara arabhughaa, ‘Mukore bhwaheene enchera ya Omutemi Ghiteema, momuseemeri bhwaheene ahase hano akuheta!
Amaribha ghansi gharibhu, chinkereghe ne bhikereghe bhichanchibhu. Ahase hano haisisire harengoru, na hano haana amarooma, harengʼaanibhu.
Hayo neho, abhanto bhansi bhakurora Omutoori ono Ghiteema atomire.’”
Ko riyo, Yohana akabha arabhoorra eghekomo kya abhanto bhano bhaachire kubhaatiisu arabhughaa, “Inyu orwibhoro rwe nchoka! Ne-wuuye abhasimire ighoo muranaghi koryera ghukarra ko Ghiteema kuno koghuucha, gho okubhaatiisu okwene?
Mukore singata amangʼana ghano ghakwereki ighoo momwishoorri Ghiteema. Motighe ghwitegherra aghoo Ghiteema arabhaitabherri ghote mokwihacha murabhughaa, ‘Sookoro yiito ni-Bhurahamu!’ Ndabhabhoorra ighoo, Ghiteema ngutoraani ghoshoori amaghena ghano ghabhe abhaana bha Ibhurahimu!
Bhoono ghukenga ekiina ko Ghiteema kooni ighoro yaanyu, ghote bhoore eshooka eno eghotuna ghukenga emete. Omote ghuno ghutaghoote emehumo emichomu, ghuragheechu no ghukenyikenyibhu, ghutabhutu momorro.”
Abhanto bhayo, bhakabha bharamubhoori, bharabhughaa, “Mbwe turaakore?”
Akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Ono aghoote chingebho ibhere, amotweni ono ataghoote. Ono aghoote ebhyakori, akore kee hayo hayo.”
Abhaghooti bhe righooti nabhu bhaghaacha haare Yohana, korri abhabhaatiisi. Bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Omweghi, na itu mbwe toghukora?”
Wunsi akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Hano mokubha muraghoota righooti, mutakengeri ghote mokwerekeribhu.”
Abhasirikare bhansi bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Na itu mbwe toghukora?” Wunsi akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Mutakaaruusi omonto eghento gheeche, ghwiki motighe komuchongera omonto gho komwitamerri amangʼana gho bhurongo. Omoheera ghuno mokuhaabhu, mohiime naghu.”
Abhanto bhano bhaare kughanya Kirisito, bhakabha bharibhoori mometwe gheebho ighoo, ubhone Yohana newe Kirisito?
Ghasi bhoono Yohana akabhagharokeri bhansi akabhughaa, “Eni ndabhabhaatiisi ku amanche, ghasi araacha omonto wonde ono aghunkera amanagha. Tenkubha haare we korri ghusanchora chensiri che bhiraato bheeche! Ewe arabhabhaatisa ko Enkoro Ehoreeru na ko omorro.
Aghootire orohongo mokubhoko ghooche, korri ahonge chebhumba koru ko ngano. Engano eyo irakomanibhu moghitara gheeche, ghasi omwirro ghurachuukibhu momorro ghuno ghutaakorima kemwe.”
N-ighoo Yohana aghakumerri ku amangʼana amaaru ghayo, na aghande, aare arabhaseghani abhanto bhayo, na hayo arabhareghani Amangʼana Amachomu gha Ghiteema.
Yohana akabheeha omutemi Herode Antibhasi akabhughaa, “N-ngoke ugheghire Herootia, mukaa mura waanyu, omukorre kubha mughaacho?” Ghwiki, Yohana akamuseghani no obhosineenu bhooche obhonde bhuno aare ghukora.
Ko riyo, Herode akengeri obhosineenu bhonde ghwiki, gho ghutoora Yohana mokibhohe.
Enkaagha eno Yohana aare akeere kubhohu, nkubhaatiisi aare abhanto, Yeesu wunsi akabhatiisu. Na hano Yeesu aare ghusabha, mwisaaro hakaighoka,
Enkoro Ehoreeru aghasekera no ghwikara ighoro ya Yeesu, aitubhaine bhwe ekeghuuti. Riraka rikarwera mwisaaro, rirabhughaa, “Iye niye Omoona waane omusaighi, uno oghuntegheri.”
Enkaagha eno Yeesu asimiri emeremo gheeche ghyo kureghani Engʼana ya Ghiteema, aare ne emeeka ghote merongo etato. Abhanto mbaakabhughire aghoo, aare omoona wa Yuusufu. Yuusufu oyo, akaibhoru na Heri.
Heri akaibhoru na Mataati. Mataati akaibhoru na Raawi. Raawi akaibhoru na Meeriki. Meeriki akaibhoru na Yana. Yana akaibhoru na Yuusufu.
Yuusufu akaibhoru na Matatia. Matatia akaibhoru na Amoosi. Amoosi akaibhoru na Naahumu. Naahumu akaibhoru na Esiri. Esiri akaibhoru na Naghai.
Naghai akaibhoru na Maati Maati akaibhoru na Matatia. Matatia akaibhwiru na Semei. Semei akaibhoru na Yoseki. Yoseki akaibhoru na Yoota.
Yoota akaibhoru na Yoanani. Yoanani akaibhoru na Resa. Resa akaibhoru na Serubhabheeri. Serubhabheeri akaibhoru na Shearitieri. Shearitieri akaibhoru na Neeri.
Neeri akaibhoru na Meeriki. Meeriki akaibhoru na Ati. Ati akaibhoru na Kosamu. Kosamu akaibhoru na Erimatamu. Erimatamu akaibhoru na Eeri.
Eeri akaibhoru na Yoshuwa. Yoshuwa akaibhoru na Erieseri. Erieseri akaibhoru na Yorimu. Yorimu akaibhoru na Mataati. Mataati akaibhoru na Raawi.
Raawi akaibhoru na Simeoni. Simeoni akaibhoru na Yuuda. Yuuda akaibhoru na Yuusufu. Yuusufu akaibhoru na Yoonamu. Yoonamu akaibhoru na Eriakiimu
Eriakiimu akaibhoru na Merea. Merea akaibhoru na Mena. Mena akaibhoru na Matata. Matata akaibhoru na Natani. Natani akaibhoru na Daudi.
Daudi akaibhoru na Yeese. Yeese akaibhoru na Obheti. Obheti akaibhoru na Bhoasi. Bhoasi akaibhoru na Sarimoni. Sarimoni akaibhoru na Nasooni.
Nasooni akaibhoru na Aminatabhu. Aminatabhu akaibhoru na Atimini. Atimini akaibhoru na Hesiroomu. Hesiroomu akaibhoru na Bheresi. Bheresi akaibhoru na Yuuda.
Yuuda akaibhoru na Yaakobho. Yaakobho akaibhoru na Isaaka Isaaka akaibhoru na Ibhurahimu. Ibhurahimu akaibhoru na Tera. Tera akaibhoru na Nahoori.
Nahoori akaibhoru na Serughi. Serughi akaibhoru na Raghau. Raghau akaibhoru na Bhereghi. Bhereghi akaibhoru na Ebheri. Ebheri akaibhoru na Saara.
Saara akaibhoru na Kainani. Kainani akaibhoru na Aribhakisati. Aribhakisati akaibhoru na Shemu. Shemu akaibhoru na Nuhu. Nuhu akaibhoru na Rameki.
Rameki akaibhoru na Metusera. Metusera akaibhoru na Henoko. Henoko akaibhoru na Yareti. Yareti akaibhoru na Maharareri. Maharareri akaibhoru na Kenani.
Kenani akaibhoru na Enoshi. Enoshi akaibhoru na Seti. Seti akaibhoru na Atamu. Na Atamu aghateemu na Ghiteema.
Yeesu akaru ahase ho orooche ro Yorodani, aani aichwire Enkoro Ehoreeru. Enkoro oyo akabha aramukangata mwibhara, aghaikara eyo chensiko merongo ene,
Risambu ryare komusaghasa eyo. Ne enkaagha eyo yinsi, taarire ghento ghinsighinsi. Hano amarre chensinko chiyo akooghu arambokire.
Neho, Risambu ryaamubhoorri, rikabhughaa, “Ubhone maheene iye n-Omoona wa Ghiteema, honchora righena rino ribhe omughaate.”
Yeesu akarigharokeri akabhughaa, “Yandekiru mu Mandeko Amahoreeru, ‘Tere ebhyakori ebhyene bhekugheri omonto abhe omuhoru.’”
Neho Risambu ryaamotirri korukereghe orutambe bhukongʼu, rikamwereki ebhyaro bhinsi bhye ense gho nkaagha emwe.
Rikamubhoorra rikabhughaa, “Ndakuha amanagha gho obhubhaahi bho bhino bhinsi, hamwe no obhwame bhooche. Gho okubhamumabhoko ghaane bheeni, nkunaghi neeni komuha omonto oyo wunsi ono nkwenda.
Bhoono ubhone uransengera, ndakuha obhubhaahi bho ghayo ghansi.”
Yeesu akarigharokeri akabhughaa, “Yandekiru mu Mandeko Amahoreeru, ‘Omusengere Omutemi Ghiteema waacho, no komwighwera ewe omwene.’”
Neho, Risambu rikamohira momoghi gho Yerusareemu, rikamwimerri komusonge gho ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, rikamubhoorra, rikabhughaa, “Ubhone iye n-Omoona wa Ghiteema, itabhuta harense.
Tokunyahaareka, gho okubha yandekiru mu Mandeko Amahoreeru, gharabhughaa, ‘Ghiteema aratoma abhamaraika bhaache, bhakurende.
Nabhu bharakughegha kumabhoko ghaabho, korri amaghoro ghaacho ghataghaitema kwighena rinsirinsi.’”
Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akarigharokeri akabhughaa, “Ghwiki yandekiru mu Mandeko Amahoreeru, gharabhughaa, ‘Utakaacharibhu Omutemi, Ghiteema waacho.’”
Risambu hano ryaamarre kocharibhu Yeesu, rikamotigha, akaghi echaache okuhekera enkaagha yende.
Yeesu akagharoka momukowa gho Ghariraaya, eno aichwire amanagha ghe Enkoro Ehoreeru. Amangʼana gha Yeesu ghaghasancha bhukongʼu momukowa gho Ghariraaya ghunsi.
Akabha areeghi abhanto hase hansi mochenyumba cha Abhayahudi cho oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema. Abhanto bhansi bhakabha bharamwitumi.
Kumaruho, Yeesu akagharoka Naasareeti momoghi ghuno areriiru. Orosiko rwe Esabhaato, aghasoha monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema ghote aanarre, akaimerra korri ghusoma Engʼana ya Ghiteema.
Akahaabhu eghitabho kyo omurooti Isaaya, akahonyora ahase hano handekiru harabhughaa,
“Enkoro yo Omutemi Ghiteema hamwe yeeni na eni. Ghiteema anyoohwere ndeghaneri abhatobhu Amangʼana Amachomu. Antomire ndeghaneri abhabhohe kuhaatorubhu koobho. No kubhoorra abhahukuru ighoo, bhararamokibhu amaiso ghaabho, na ntongore bhano bhakunyankibhu.
Antomire ndeghaneri abhanto, omooka gho obhutooribhu, ghuno Omutemi Ghiteema akwereeki enooko yaache.”
Hano Yeesu aamarre ghusoma amangʼana ghayo, akahunya eghitabho, akagharokeri omubhaghasi, kumara aghaikara korri eeghi. Abhanto bhansi bhano bhaare monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, bhakamorigheeri bharaghanya kino aghotuna eeghi.
Aghasimi kubhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Amaandeko Amahoreeru ghano moghuure reero, ngahekeraine mbere yaanyu.”
Hano aamarre kweeghi, abhanto bhansi bhakamwitumi bhukongʼu, bhakaroghoorra amangʼana amachomu ghano aare kweeghi. Kumaruho, bhakabhoorani bhakabhughaa, “Ono tare omoona wa Yuusufu?”
Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Nimanyire ninga mumboorre righambo rino, murabhughaa, ‘Omureri, ihori iye omwene!’ Na ninga mumboorre murabhughaa, ‘Amakono ghano tooghuure ughakora momoghi gho Kabherenaumu, ughakore na momoghi ghoocho hano.’”
Yeesu akabhabhoorra, “Ndabhabhoorra obhuheene aghoo, omurooti taghusooku na abhanto bha waabho.
“Ghasi bhoono Mutegherre Obhuheene, gho nkaagha yo omurooti Eriya, bhaareho abhasino abhaaru mokyaro kya Abhaisiraeri. Enkaagha eyo embura tiyare ghuteeka ghonkaagha ye emeeka etato ne emieri esansabha. Ko riyo ekyaro ghinsi kya Abhaisiraeri ghikabha ne egheecha endoro.
Ghiteema taatomire Eriya ko omwe wa abhasino bhayo. Ghasi bhoono akamutoma ko omosino omwe wo moghi gho Sarebhuta, mokyaro ke Sitooni, kino ghitaare Isiraeri.
“Ne enkaagha yo murooti Erisha, bhaareho abhaghenge abhaaru mokyaro kya Abhaisiraeri. Ghasi bhoono taahoribhu omonto wunsiwunsi, ghasi Naamani omwene, omonto we ekyaro ke Siriya!”
Hano abhanto bhansi bhano bhaare bhaikomaine monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema eyo, bhooghuure amangʼana gha Yeesu, bhaghakarra bhukongʼu.
Bhakaimerra, bhakamoruusi momoghi ghoobho ghuno ghware ghwabhekiru morukereghe. Bhakamohira mokehiringito ekeroro kyo rukereghe ruyo, korri bhamosukumere harense.
Ghasi bhoono, aghishoori, akaheta ghati yaabho, akaghi echaache.
Neho Yeesu akaghi momoghi gho Kabherenaumu, momukowa gho Ghariraaya. Orosiko rwe Esabhaato, aghasoha monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, aghasimi kweeghi abhanto.
Ameeghi ghaache, ghakabharoghoori bhukongʼu, gho okubha naaghambire ku amanagha gho obhubhaahi.
Monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, aaremu omonto omwe ono aare no omusambu. Omusambu ghuyo, ghughakuura no ghucherra, ghorabhughaa
“Eee, Yeesu wa Naasareeti, nke ughotuna haare itu? Wuuchire ghotumaraho? Nimanyire, iye niye Omuhoreeru wa Ghiteema!”
Yeesu akahoronyokera omusambu ghuyo, “Kira! Oru ko omonto ono!” Hari remwe, omusambu ghuyo ghukamoghwisi harense mbere ya abhanto bhansi. Hano ghwaamarre ghukamuhatora ghutamunyaharre.
Abhanto bhansi bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu, bhakabhoorani bharabhughaa, “Ghano amangʼana ke? Gho kubha, ku amanagha gho obhubhaahi, na gho chenguru arahamera emisambu, ghiraru!”
Ko riyo amangʼana gha Yeesu, ghakabha gharasancha bhukongʼu, momukowa ghunsi gho Ghariraaya.
Yeesu akaru monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, akaghi momoghi gho omonto omwe ono aare kubherekeru Simooni. Nyakobhyera yaache Simooni, aare ne ehooma endoro. Abhanto bhano bhaare monyumba muyo, bhaghasaasaama Yeesu amuhori.
Yeesu aghaisuka akaimerra haghuhe nawe, akahamera ehooma, hari remwe ikamuhaatora. Neho aabhookire, aghasimi kubhabhaghasi.
Enkaagha eyo, ereebha ryare ghutebhera, orosiko rwe Esabhaato rware ghosira. Abhanto bhansi bhano bhaaghoote abharwire bha amarwire ghano ghaheteraine heteraine, bhakabhahira haare Yeesu. Akabhatorra amabhoko bhansi, akabhahori.
Hamwe na ghayo, Yeesu akahamera emisambu koru kubhanto abhaaru. Hano ghaare kubhahaatora, ghakabha gharacherra gharabhughaa, “Iye n-Omoona wa Ghiteema!” Ghasi bhoono Yeesu akaghahamera no kughaseghani ghatighe kughenderri kughamba ighoo, gho okubha ngaamanyire, newe Kirisito.
Hano bhwaakiire, Yeesu aghatanora, akaghi ahase hano hataana abhanto. Abhanto abhaaru bhakabha bharamotuna. Hano bhaamobhwine, bhaghatuna komwangera atakaabhatigha.
Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Ndatunu ngende komeghi ghende, korri nibhe ndareghani Amangʼana Amachomu gho Obhukama bho Ghiteema, gho okubha neghu ntoomiru nkore.”
Neho bhoono, Yeesu akaghenderri kuhetera mokyaro ghinsi kya Abhayahudi, arareghaneri abhanto Amangʼana Amachomu ghayo mochenyumba cha Abhayahudi cho oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema.
Orosiko romwe, Yeesu aare aimeriire mongoghoni ye enyancha ya Ghenesereeti, areeghi abhanto abhaaru engʼana ya Ghiteema. Abhanto bhayo, bhakabha bhamwinaarre bhakamwisokerra, korri bhamutegherre.
Yeesu akarora amooto abhere, mongoghoni ye enyancha eyo. Abhateghi bhaaghatighire gho okubha mbaaghiri kweeghi emitegho gheebho.
Akariina mo obhooto bhomwe, bhuno bhware bho Simooni, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Obhosuki hasuuhu koru mongoghoni.” Neho aikaire muyo, akeeghi abhanto.
Hano amarre kubheeghi, akabhoorra Simooni, “Suki obhooto bhughende mondibha ye enyancha, musekeri emitegho gheenyu, muteghe, korri mubhone chenswe.”
Simooni akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Ee Omutemi, tukorre emeremo ko ghwikongʼi obhotiko obhoghima, tutabhwine ghento! Ghasi bhoono gho okubha iye obhughire, ndasekeri emitegho mumanche.”
Simooni na bhaghendi bhaache bhaghasekeri emitegho gheebho mumanche, bhaghategha, bhakaghooti chenswe echaaru bhukongʼu. Emitegho gheebho ghighasimi ghutandoka.
Bhakangʼocha bhaghendi bhaabho bho obhooto bhonde, korri bhaache kubhatoorri. Hano bhaachire, bhaghaichori amooto ghansi abhere chenswe, hasuuhu bhaibhere.
Hano Simooni Peetero aarooche ghayo, akahighama harense mbere ya Yeesu, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Omutemi, nooru haare eni, gho okubha eni n-omwene bhibhe!”
Simooni aabhughire amangʼana ghayo, gho okubha ewe, na bhaghendi bhaache bhano aare hamwe nabhu, bhakaroghoora, ko bhooru bhwe chenswe chino bhaare bhabhwine.
Ko bhooto bhonde bhoore, bhaaremu Yaakobho na Yohana, abhaana bha Sebhetaayo, bhano bhaare bharatoorani na Simooni ghukora emeremo ghyo obhuteghi, bhansi bhakaroghoora ku ghano ghaabhaire. Yeesu akabhoorra Simooni, “Utakoobhoha! Kuwansera bhoono, urabha urategha abhanto ghote waare ghutegha chenswe.”
Simooni na bhaghendi bhaache bhakagharoki amooto mongoghoni, bhaghatigha ebhinto bheebho bhinsi, bhaghatambana Yeesu.
Hano Yeesu aare komoghi ghomwe, hari remwe akahika hayo omonto omwe, ono aare no obhorwirwe bho obhughenge omobhere ghunsi. Hano aarooche Yeesu, akairekera mbere yaache, akamusaasaama akabhughaa, “Omutemi, oghusaigha, uranaghi kunhori no okundabhi!”
Yeesu akarengora okubhoko ghooche, akamoturi, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Ndatuna uhorre no okurabhibhu!” Hayo hayo, akahora obhughenge bhooche.
Yeesu akamuseghani akabhughaa, “Utakaabhoorre omonto wunsiwunsi ighoro ya riyo! Ghasi bhoono, nooghi wiyereki ko omusengeri, oruusi ekemwenso ghote amaragherri gha Musa ghakwerekerri, korri obheereki abhanto ighoo urabhiribhu.”
Ghasi bhoono, amangʼana gha Yeesu, ghakaghenderri ghusancha bhukongʼu. Abhanto abhaaru bhakabha bhariikomana, korri bhategherre ameeghi ghaache na kuhoribhu amarwire ghaabho.
Ghasi bhoono enkaagha yende, Yeesu aare kubhatigha hayo, araghi omwene ghusabha Ghiteema.
Orosiko romwe, Yeesu aare kweeghi abhanto. Amabharisaayo hamwe na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa nehobhaare bhaikaire. Mbaarweriire mo bhechichi bhinsi bhyo mukowa gho Ghariraaya na Yuudeya, na momoghi gho Yerusareemu. Yeesu aare na amanagha koru ko Omutemi Ghiteema, korri ahori abhanto.
Neho abhanto bhaachire, bhagheghire omorwire omunyeeku gho ekiragho. Bhaghaseemi komusohi monyumba, bhamutoore mbere ya Yeesu.
Ghasi bhoono bhatanaghiri, gho okubha abhanto abhaaru bhaare bhaikomaine mogheseku. Hano bhaabhorri omweya gho komusohi, neho bhaariinire ne engachi koghisara kye enyumba, bhagheghire omorwire oyo ghokiragho gheeche. Bhakahaanyora ahase ko ghisara, bhakamusekeri ghatighati ya abhanto bhayo, obhoronge bho Yeesu, aani amisiri ghokiragho gheeche.
Hano Yeesu aarooche ghote abhanto bhayo bhaaghoote obhwitabherri, akabhoorra omorwire oyo akabhughaa, “Musaani, neekwabhiire ebhibhe bheecho!”
Abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa na Amabharisaayo bhayo, bhaghasimi kubhoorani bharabhughaa, “Ne-wuuye ono? Ake araghamba amangʼana gho ghutoka Ghiteema? Tareho ono aghutora kwabhera ebhibhe, ghasi Ghiteema omwene!”
Yeesu akangʼura ghote bhaare ghwitegherra, akabhabhoori arabhughaa, “Gho ke moghwitegherra ighoo mometwe gheenyu?
N-diihe reeni ritobhu bhukongʼu, komubhoorra, ‘Neekwabhiire ebhibhe bheecho,’ ghasi komubhoorra kobhughaa, ‘Imerra, utanore’? Kubhanto ghayo ghansi ghataakubha he.
Ghasi bhoono, ndatuna mumanye bhwaheene aghoo, eni Omoona wo Omonto nihabhiiru amanagha gho obhubhaahi gho kwabhera ebhibhe monse muno.” Neho Yeesu akabhoorra omonto oyo akabhughaa, “Ndakubhoorra, imerra! Ghegha ekiragho gheecho, oghi ka.”
Hayo hayo, omonto oyo akaimerra mbere ya abhanto, akaghegha ekiragho gheeche, akaghi ka eno aramwitumi Ghiteema.
Abhanto bhansi, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu no kughootu ne haho. Hamwe na ghayo, bhakamwitumi Ghiteema, bharabhughaa, “Bhamure! Reero, torooche amakono gho kuroghoori!”
Ghayo hano ghaasirre, Yeesu akaru monyumba, akarora omughooti we righooti omwe ono aare kubherekeru Raawi. Raawi oyo aare aikaire mokebhuru gheeche kyo kughootera righooti. Hayo, Yeesu akamubhoorra, “Untambane!”
Hayo hayo, Raawi akaimerra, aghatigha ebhinto bhinsi, akamutambana.
Enkaagha yende, Raawi akakorra Yeesu enyangi enkoro waache ka. O Raawi hayo, mbaaikomaine abhaghooti bhe righooti abhaaru, na abhanto bhande bhakabha bhararaaghera hamwe.
Amabharisaayo, na abheeghi bhaabho bha amaragherri gha Musa, bhakaghoota amasoro ku abheegha bha Yeesu, bharabhughaa, “Ake, muraraaghera no konyo hamwe na abhaghooti bhe righooti na abhakora ebhibhe abhande?”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Abhanto bhano bhaghoote obhuhoru bhatakwenda omureri, ghasi abharwire nebhu bhakwenda omureri.
Ghote eni wunsi ntaichire kubherekera abhanto bhano bhakwirora n-abhaheene, ghasi nichire kubherekera abhakora bhibhe, bhamwishoorri Ghiteema.”
Abhanto bhayo bhakabhoorra Yeesu bhakabhughaa, “Ake, abheegha bha Yohana bharaikubheri okori, bhasaasaame Ghiteema. Kuru abheegha bha Amabharisaayo, nabhu ngukora bhaani kee hayo hayo. Ngooke abheegha bhaacho bhataghwikubheri kori no konyo?”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Hano okubhona omuteti akeere hamwe na bhasaani bhaache monyangi yo obhuteti, muranaghi bhwe kubhabhoorra, bhaikubheri okori no konyo?
Ghasi bhoono, enkaagha irahika eno abhanto bhakoruusiho omuteti atighe abhasaani bhaache. Monkaagha eyo, neho bharabha bharaikubheri okori.”
Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani kende akabhughaa, “Atareho omonto ono aghutora ghukenga ekiraka koru kongebho ehe, korri aghitomerre kongebho enkungu. Gho kubha, hano aghukora kee hayo, arabha atandwire engebho ehe. Hamwe na ghayo, ekiraka kiyo kye engebho ehe, kitaakuhekaana ne engebho enkungu.
“Na atareho omonto ono aghutora ghutoora amaro amahyahya ghe emisabhiibhu mobhighancha bhe kare. Gho okubhaaraakore kee hayo, amaro amahyahya gharagheri ebhighancha bhisareke, na amaro gharahomoka.
Ghasi bhoono amaro amahyahya ghe emisabhiibhu, ghatooru mobhighancha ebhehe!
“Na omonto ono anarre amaro gha kare, urabhona taghotuna amaro amahyahya. Arabhughaa, ‘Amaro gha kare neghu amachomu!’”
Orosiko romwe rwe Esabhaato, Yeesu aare kuheta momeghondo ghye ngano, hamwe na abheegha bhaache. Abheegha bhaache bhakabhuna ebhisaawa bhye ngano, bhakabhebhunga mobhisaanyi, bhakari.
Neho Amabharisaayo bhande bhakabhabhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Ake murakora omoremo orosiko rwe Esabhaato, na eno no-moghiro?”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Ghasi bhoono, mutasomire mu Mandeko Amahoreeru ghote Daudi akorre hano aare arambokire hamwe na bhaghendi bhaache?
Daudi naasohire mokebhuru kye Ghiteema, akaghegha emighaate ghino ghyaatooru mbere ya Ghiteema, akari, ghwiki akabhaha bhaghendi bhaache, bhansi bhakari. Mbaariire emighaate ghino amaragherri gha Musa ghaseghaini bhataghaacha kori, ghasi abhasengeri abheene.”
Yeesu akengererri kughamba akabhughaa, “Eni Omoona wo Omonto, neeni Omutemi wo orosiko rwe Esabhaato.”
Orosiko ronde rwe Esabhaato, Yeesu aghasoha monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, aghasimi kweeghi abhanto. Muyo aaremu omonto omwe, ono okubhoko ghooche ko bhoryo kwaare kunyeekire.
Bhaaremu abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa, na Amabharisaayo, mbaatunire eghesegho ghyo kugheri bhachongere Yeesu. Ko riyo, bhakaghanya bharore ghote akuhori omonto orosiko rwe Esabhaato.
Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akangʼura ghano bhaare ghwitegherra. Ko riyo, Yeesu akabhoorra omonto wo kubhoko kuno kunyeekire, “Wuuche, wimerre ghatighati.” Omonto oyo akabhooka, akaghi akaimerra ghatighati yaabho.
Neho Yeesu akabhoori abhanto bhayo, “Ghasi bhoono, amaragherri gharitabherri ghukora riihe orosiko rwe Esabhaato? Ghukora amachomu, ghasi ghukora amasineenu? Ghutoori obhuhoru ghasi kumaraho?”
Akabhamoghorra chimbareka chinsi. Akabhoorra omonto oyo akabhughaa, “Rengora okubhoko ghoocho.” Nawe aghakurengora, na hayo hayo ghukahora.
Amabharisaayo na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa bhayo, bhaghakarra bhukongʼu. Bhakari eseemi ghote bhaghukorra Yeesu.
Orosiko ronde, Yeesu naaghire morukereghe ghusaasaama Ghiteema, aghasaasaama obhotiko obhoghima.
Hano bhwaakiire, akabherekera abheegha bhaache. Akoohora abhanto ikomi na bhabhere mubheegha bhaache, akabhabherekera Abhatomu. Amariina gha abhatomu bhayo, n-gano,
Simooni ono Yeesu arokire Peetero, Andereya mura waabho Simooni, Yaakobho, Yohana, Firipo, Bharitoromaayo,
Mataayo, Tomaaso, Yaakobho omoona wa Aribhaayo, Simooni Muserote,
Yuuda omoona wa Yaakobho, na Yuuda Isikariote ono aanyeriire Yeesu eseemi.
Yeesu akahiringita koru kurukereghe, hamwe nabhu. Hano aahikire ghokibhara, akaimerra. Hayo mbaare bhaikomaine abheegha bhaache abhaaru na abhanto bhande abhaaru koru ahase hansi ho mukowa gho Yuudeya, na koru Yerusareemu, na koru mongoghoni ye meghi ghe Tiiro na Sitooni. Abhanto bhayo mbaachire hayo, ghutegherra Yeesu no kuhoribhu amarwire ghaabho.
Kuru bhano bhaare kunyankibhu ne emisambu, akabha arabhahori.
Abhanto bhayo bhansi bhaare ghotuna bhamoturi, gho okubha naaghoote amanagha gho kubhahori bhansi.
Yeesu akarigherri abheegha bhaache bhayo, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Muuna echaghati bhano mooni abhatobhu, gho okubha Obhukama bho Ghiteema n-obhoonyu.
Muuna echaghati bhano mokooghu omuramboko enkaagha eno, gho okubha Ghiteema arabhaighoti. Muuna chaghati bhano moghokuura enkaagha eno, gho okubha muraseka.
Muuna echaghati bhano abhanto bhakubharegha, no kubhoohora, bharabhatoka no kubhabhoorra ighoo inyu na-abhasari, gho okugheri eni Omoona wo Omonto.
Hano ghayo ghaghukoru, muchomeru, ghote moghutema amatome no okobhina. Mumanye aghoo, murabha muratooru etuho enkoro mwisaaro. N-ke hayo na bhasookoro bhaabho, mbaanyankiri abharooti bha Ghiteema.
Ghasi bhoono inyu abhaame, haaho yaanyu, gho okubha mumarre kubhona obhughambisani bhoonyu.
Haaho yaanyu, inyu bhano mwighotire bhoono, gho okubha murabha no muramboko. Haaho yaanyu, inyu bhano moghuseka ko ghuchomeru bhoono, gho okubha murakuura no ghochiichiita.
Haaho yaanyu inyu hano abhanto bharabhaitumi, gho okubha, kuru bhasookoro bhaabho, n-kehayo bhaare ghukorra abharooti bho bhurongo.
“Ndabhabhoorra inyu bhano moghuntegherra, mubhasaighe abhabhisa bhaanyu. Abhanto bhano bhabhareghire, inyu mubhakorre amachomu.
Mubhanooke bhano bhakubhaihiima. Na bhano bhakubhanyanki, inyu mubhasabhere o Ghiteema.
“Omonto ono akoghusera aghuteme korubhoto romwe, omuhonchorre no ronde. No omonto ono aghokoruusi eghooti yaacho, omotighere agheghe ne saati.
Wunsiwunsi ono akoghusabha eghento, omuhe. No omonto ono aghokoruusi ebhinto bheecho, utakaamusabha akuhonchokeri.
Mubhe murakorra abhanto bhande ghote mokwenda ebhu bhabhakorre inyu.
“Hano murasaigha bhano bhabhasaighire inyu, omokumo ke mokubhona? Kuru bhe bhibhe bharasaigha bhano bhabhasaighire.
Ghwiki, ghote murabhakorre amachomu bhano bhakubhakorra amachomu abheene, omokumo ke mokubhona? Kuru bhe bhibhe mbarakora kee hayo!
Ghwiki, uraabhone murahaana esiire ku bhano moghwitengʼera bharabhagharokeri abheene, omokumo ke mokubhona? Kuru bhe bhibhe mbarahaana esiire ku bhaghendi bhaabho, bhe bhibhe, gho okubha bhamanyire bharagharokeribhu bhinsi!
“Ghasi bhoono inyu, musaighe abhabhisa bhaanyu, na mubhakorre amachomu. Muhaane esiire, motighe kughanya kugharokeribhu. Ghiteema arabhaha etuho enkoro, na murabha abhaana bho bhuheene haare Ghiteema ono aani ighoro ya bhinsi, gho okubha Ghiteema arakorra amachomu kubhanto abhasineenu na bhano bhataakomokumi.
“Mubhe abhanto bha amaabhera ku abhande, ghote Isawaanyu akwabhera abhanto.
“Mutaghaacha ghukengera abhanto ebhiina, neho na inyu mutaghukengeru ebhiina. Mutaghaacha ghutema abhanto amasoro, neho na inyu, mutaghutemu amasoro. Mwabhere bhano bhakubhasarri, neho na inyu bhansi mokwabheru.
Mubhahe abhanto ebhinto, neho mokuhaabhu na Ghiteema. Murahaabhu ekirengʼaini kino ghichwire no kwighateru, ghesingisiribhu, kiraharroka. Gho okubhaekirengʼaini kino mokurengʼaneri abhande, nekyu Ghiteema akubharengʼaaneri na inyu.”
Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani kino akabhughaa, “Omohukuru aranaghi ghukangata omohukuru mughendi waache? Hano iraabhe kee hayo, bhansi bhabhere ninga bhagho mwirooma!
“Omwegha takumanya amangʼana ghukera omweghi waache. Ghasi bhoono hano omwegha akumara kweeghibhu ghansi, neho akurengʼaana no omweghi waache.
“Ake urarora eghisaara kino keeni moriiso re mughendi waacho, na eno tookurora orumambo runo rooni moriiso reecho?
Ghasi bhoono mbwe okubhoorra mughendi waacho urabhughaa, ‘Mughendi waane, tigha nkoruusi eghisaara moriiso reechoʼ, eno iye omwene tookurora orumambo runo rooni moriiso reecho? Omwitaami iye, ruusi singata orumambo runo rooni moriiso reecho. Neho okunaghi kurora bhwaheene no koruusi eghisaara kino keeni moriiso re mughendi waacho.
“Ghutareho omote omuchomu ghuno ghoghutoora emehumo emesineenu. Na ghutareho omote omosineenu ghuno ghoghutoora emehumo emichomu.
Emehumo ghe emisabhiibhu ghiteghutwebhu ko ebhehore. Ebhisaka bhya amaho, bhiteekwama chetiini he. Omote ghoramanyikana ko emehumo gheeche.
“Kee hayo hayo, omonto nawe. Omonto omuheene, amangʼana ghaache gho bhuheene, nkorughaani mumaitegherro ghaache gho bhuheene, ghano aghoote momotema ghooche. Omonto omosineenu, amangʼana ghaache amasineenu, nkorughaani momaitegherro ghaache amasineenu ghano aghoote momotema ghooche. Mbe amangʼana ghano omonto akughamba, n-gaare ghaichwire momotema ghooche.
“N-gooke mokumberekera, ‘Omutemi, Omutemi,’ ghasi amangʼana ghano nkubhabhoorra, mutakughakora?
Tigha mbabhorre ekehekaani kyo omonto wunsiwunsi ono aghuucha haare eni no oghutegherra amangʼana ghaane no kughakora, ghote aani.
Arahekaana no mwabheki we enyumba, ono aatukire omosingi akahekeera ritare, akaabheka omosingi ghwitare. Ghasi bhoono, hano ehooro yaabhochire, amanche ghakaitema enyumba. Kuru, ghataihanywere, gho okubha yaare yabhekiru bhwaheene.
“Ghasi bhoono omonto oyo wunsi ono akooghu amangʼana ghaane ange kughakora, oyo arahekaana no omonto ono abhekire enyumba yaache komusense, ataatukire omosingi. Ghasi bhoono, hano ehooro yaabhochire, amanche ghakaitema enyumba eyo, ikihomorra yinsi harense.”
Hano Yeesu aamarre kweeghi eghekomo kya abhanto amangʼana ghayo ghansi, akaghi momoghi ghuno ghware kubherekeru Kabherenaumu.
Momoghi ghuyo, aareho omokoro omwe wa abhasirikare bhe Ekeruumi. Omokoro wa abhasirikare oyo, aare no omubhaghasi waache, na aare amusaighire bhukongʼu. Ghasi omubhaghasi oyo aare omorwire ono akerru.
Bhoono, omokoro oyo, hano oghuure amangʼana gha Yeesu, aghatoma abhakoro bha Abhayahudi haare Yeesu, korri bhamusaasaame, aache kuhori omubhaghasi waache.
Abhakoro bhayo hano bhaahikire haare Yeesu, bhakamokumerri bhukongʼu bharabhughaa, “Omokoro oyo, ngotunu yeeni omusakeri engʼana eno,
gho okubha naseeghire ekyaro ghiitu, na newe atwabhekiire enyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema.”
Ghasi Yeesu, aghatanora hamwe na abhakoro bhayo, akaghi komoghi gho omokoro oyo. Hano bhaahikire haghuhe ne nyumba yaache, omokoro oyo aghatoma bhasaani bhaache haare Yeesu, bhamubhoorre bhabhughee “Omutemi, tigha kwinyanki, tengotunu usohe monyumba yaane.
Nekyu ndooche ighoo, tengotunu niiche waacho. Ghasi, ghamba engʼana emwe eyeene, omubhaghasi waane arahora.
Gho okubhaeni wunsi, wanse ya amanagha gho obhubhaahi bho owonde neeni, na ningoote abhasirikare bhano bhaani wanse yo obhubhaahi bhoone. Hano nkubhoorra omwe, ‘Nooghi’, hari remwe araghi. Na hano nkubhoorra owonde, ‘Wuuche’, hari remwe araacha. Na nkubhoorra omubhaghasi omwe, ‘Kora omoremo ghuno’, wunsi ngukora ani.”
Hano Yeesu, oghuure amangʼana ghayo, akaroghoora bhukongʼu. Akaihonchorra eghekomo kya abhanto bhano bhaare komutambana, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Obhuheene ndabhabhoorra kubha, ntamarandora omonto ono aghoote obhwitabherri obhokoro kee bhuno, kuru ghati ya Abhaisiraeri bhansi!”
Hano abhanto bhano bhaare bhaatomiru bhaagharokire ka, bhakabhona, omubhaghasi woore ahorre.
Hasuuhu ighoo, Yeesu akaghi momoghi ghuno ghware kubherekeru Naini, aani hamwe na abheegha bhaache, na abhanto abhande abhaaru.
Hano ahikire haghuhe ne ekehita kyo omoghi ghuyo, aghasikana na abhanto bhano bhaare bhagheghire omoku bharaghi koryeka. Omoku oyo, n-omomura aare, rimwemwe haare nyakowaabho. Nyakowaabho n-omosino aare. Omughaikoro omosino oyo, nakangataine na abhanto abhaaru koru momoghi ghuyo, koghi koryeka.
Hano Omutemi Yeesu arooche omosino oyo, akamwabhera, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Notighe ghokuura.”
Kumaruho Yeesu aghaisokerra macheera eno bhaare bhagheghiire omoku, akayeturi. Abhanto bhano bhaare bhagheghire omoku bhakaimerra. Yeesu akabhoorra omoku oyo akabhughaa, “Iye omomura ono, ndakubhoorra bhooka!”
Omomura oyo akabhooka aghaikara, aghasimi kughamba ghwiki. Neho Yeesu, amukabhisiri haare nyakowaabho.
Abhanto bhayo bhansi, bhakabha ne ehaho bhukongʼu, bhaghasimi ghwitumi Ghiteema, bharabhughaa, “Omurooti omokoro, ahyokire ghati yiitu muno!” Ghwiki bhakabhughaa, “Ghiteema, aichire ghutoori abhanto bhaache!”
Amangʼana ghayo, ghakamanyikana bhukongʼu, momukowa gho Yuudeya ghunsi, na momikowa ghende ghe haghuhe hayo.
Abheegha bha Yohana Omubhaatiisi, bhakabhoorra Yohana amangʼana ghansi ghano Yeesu aare ghukora.
Neho Yohana abherekiire bhabhere bha abheegha bhaache bhayo, akabhatoma bhaghende bhabhoori Omutemi Yeesu, bhabhughee, “Kana iye ni-iye woore aghuucha, ghasi tughanye owonde?”
Hano abheegha bhabhere bhayo bhaahekerre Yeesu, bhakamubhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Yohana Omubhaatiisi atutomire haare iye, tokubhoori tobhughee, ‘Kana iye ni-iye woore aghuucha, ghasi tughanye owonde?’”
Enkaagha eyo eyo, Yeesu aare kuhori abhanto abhaaru bhano bhaare kunyanka na amarwire. Aare kuhori abhanto bhano bhatiirru ne emisambu na aare kugheri abhahukuru abhaaru bhararora.
Neho Yeesu aahonchokiiri abheegha bha Yohana bhayo akabhughaa, “Mughende mubhoorre Yohana, ghansi ghano morooche, na ghano moghuure. Abhahukuru bhararora, abhabheeru bharaghenda, abhaghenge bhararabha, abhakiro bharooghu, abhaku bhararyokoru, na abhatobhu bharareghaneribhu Amangʼana Amachomu.
Aghoote echaghati omonto ono akughenderri konyitabherri.”
Hano abheegha bhabhere bha Yohana bhayo bhatanwere, Yeesu aghasimi kubhoori ebhikomo bhya abhanto ighoro ya Yohana akabhughaa, “Hano mwaaghiire mwiteregho kurora Yohana, kana n-ke mwaaghiire kurora? Kanaa, mwaaghiire korigheeri rikore rino reghosingisibhu singisibhu no obhukama? Hasehe!
Ghasi, nke mwaaghiire korigheeri? Omonto ono aswarre chingebho chinchomu? Hasehe! Abhanto bhano bhaghoswara chingebho chinchomu, no ghwichomi ko obhooru bhwe ebhinto bheebho, mbaramenya mochenyumba che eghikama.
“Bhoono n-ke mwaaghiire korigheeri? Omurooti? Obhuheene n-omurooti, kuru ndabbhabhoorra aghoo, Yohana ngukera ani omurooti.
Yohana oyo, newe Amandeko Amahoreeru ghakughambera gharabhughaa, ‘Righeeri, ndatoma omubhaghasi waane, aghukangate korri aghuseemeri enchera.’”
Yeesu akaghamba akabhughaa, “Eni ndabhabhoorra ndabhughaa, ghati ya abhanto bhansi bhano bhaibhwiru monse, tareho kuru omwe omokoro ghukera Yohana. Ghasi bhoono, omosuuhu ghukera bhansi mo Obhukama bho Ghiteema newe omokoro ghukera Yohana.”
Abhanto bhayo bhansi, hamwe na abhaghooti bhe righooti, bhano bhategheriire amangʼana ghayo, bhaghaitabherri ghote Ghiteema abhaseemiiri. Abhanto bhayo nebhu bhaare Yohana abhaatiisire.
Ghasi bhoono Amabharisaayo na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa, ebhu mbaangire ghano Ghiteema aare abhaseemiiri, gho okubha mbaangire kubhaatiisu na Yohana.
Yeesu akaghenderri kughamba arabhughaa, “Abhanto bhe rikora rino, mbahekaani na ke? Kana mbwe bhaani?
Mbahekaine na abhaana bhano bhakobhina momoteera, bharabherekerana na bhaghendi bhaabho aghoo, ‘Tukabhatemera ekirereesi, ghasi bhoono mutabhinire! Tukabhareeteri amabhina gha amachiichiito, ghasi bhoono mutakuure!’
“N-ighoo yeeni na inyu! Hano Yohana Omubhaatiisi aachire atakuraaghera emighaate na ataakonyo amaro ghe emisabhiibhu. Ghasi bhoono inyu mukabhugha, aghoote omusambu!
Bhoono, eni Omoona wo Omonto niichire, nkuraaghera neeni ebhyakori no okonyo amaro ghe emisabhiibhu, inyu murabhughaa, ‘Murore embe omoyoku ono, kuru n-omurebhi na n-omusaani wa abhaghooti bhe righooti na bhe ebhibhe!’
Ghasi bhoono, abhanto bhano bhaghotuna obhungʼaini bho Ghiteema, bhareereeki kubha obhungʼaini bho Ghiteema, mbo-bhuheene.”
Aareho Omubharisaayo omwe, ono aare kubherekeru Simooni, akareghani Yeesu aghende kuraaghera waache. Neho, Yeesu aghiire aghasoha monyumba yo omonto oyo, aghaikara kuraaghera ebhyakori.
Momoghi ghuyo, aareho omughaikoro omwe, ono aare amanyikaine ighoo, n-we ebhibhe. Omughaikoro oyo, hano oghuure Yeesu araraaghera ebhyakori momoghi gho Omubharisaayo oyo, aghasoha muyo, agheghire enchubha ye righena rirabhu eno ighoote ekerumba eghichomu.
Akaimerra haghuhe na amaghoro gha Yeesu. Aghasimi ghokuura, chengisori chaache chaare ghutoonya kumaghoro gha Yeesu. Akabha arachisangori ne rituuki reeche, eno araghabhusu amaghoro gha Yeesu, araghahaka amaghuta ghano ghaghoote ekerumba eghichomu.
Omubharisaayo oyo, hano aarooche ghayo, aghaitegherra momotwe ghooche aghoo, “Omonto ono, akabhaire omurooti, aare kumanya kubha, omughaikoro ono akomoturituri, n-omonto wa teemo ke. Aare kumanya ighoo, n-we ebhibhe!”
Yeesu akamubhoorra, “Simooni, ningoote engʼana yo oghokubhoorra.” Nawe akamugharokeri, “Omweghi, tamboorra.” Yeesu akabhughaa,
“Bhaareho abhanto bhabhere, bhano bhaare bharasabhu chembiri che esiire na ono aare abhahaire esiire. Omwe waabho, aare ariire esiire ye chedinaari amaghana ataano. Mughendi waache naariire esiire ye chedinaari mirongo etaano.
Bhabhere bhayo, hano bhaabhorri chembiri cho okureha chesiire chaabho, ono aare aabhahaire esiire, akabhaabhera, bhatighe komureeha. Bhoono ku bhabhere bhayo, ne-wuuye ono aramusaighe bhukongʼu ghukera mughendi waache?”
Simooni akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Ndamanya, woore aabhiiru esiire enkorro.” Yeesu akamubhoorra, “Ugharokiiri bhwaheene.”
Yeesu akaihonchorra omughaikoro oyo, akabhoorra Simooni akabhughaa, “Urarora omughaikoro ono? Hano nsohire monyumba yaacho, iye tungaghaaniri gho kunha amanche gho kweeghi amaghoro ghaane. Ghasi ewe, eeghiri amaghoro ghaane ne chengisori chaache, no okughasangori ne rituuki reeche.
Iye tunkerri gho kombuusu, ghasi koru nsohire muno tamararosa kombuusu amaghoro ghaane.
Tunsookire gho okuhaka omotwe ghoone amaghuta. Ghasi ewe, nahakire amaghoro ghaane amaghuta ghe ekerumba eghichomu.
Bhoono, ndakubhoorra ighoo, ebhibhe bhyo omughaikoro oyo ne-ebheeru, ghasi bhoono aabhiiru bhinsi. Kiyo nekyu ghekugheri arabha no obhusaighi obhokoro. Ghasi bhoono omonto ono akwabheru ebhibhe ebhesuuhu, oyo arabha na obhusaighi obhosuuhu.”
Neho Yeesu akabhoorra omughaikoro oyo akabhughaa, “Wabhiiru ebhibhe bheecho.”
Abhagheni bhano bhaare hamwe nawe, bhaghasimi kubhoorani, agho, “Ne-wuuye ono, kuru akwabhera ebhibhe?”
Yeesu akabhoorra omughaikoro oyo akabhughaa, “Kino kigherri utoribhu n-obhwitabherri bhoocho! Oghi no omurembe.”
Hano ghayo ghaasirre, Yeesu aghatanora, akabha araheta momeghi na mobhechichi. Ahase hansi hano aare kuheta, aare kureghaneri abhanto Amangʼana Amachomu gho Obhukama bho Ghiteema. Aare na abhatomu bhaache ikomi na bhabhere.
Ghwiki, aare koghi na abhaghaikoro bhande hamwe, bhano Yeesu aare aruusiri emisambu, abhande aare abhahorri amarwire. Ku bhaghaikoro bhayo, aareho Mariyamu wa Maghidara, ono Yeesu aare amoruusiri emisambu mohungate.
Ghwiki, aareho Yowana, mughaa Ghusa. Ghusa oyo, newe aare omwimererri omokoro we enyumba yo omutemi Herode. Ghwiki aareho Susana, na abhaghaikoro bhande abhaaru, bhano bhaare ghusakeri Yeesu na abheegha bhaache, gho koruusi ebhinto bheebho abheene korri bhasekeri Yeesu na abhatomu bhaache.
Orosiko romwe, abhanto abhaaru koru ko emeghi emeeru bhakaichera Yeesu, bhaghaikomana hamwe. Kumaruho, Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani akabhughaa,
“Aareho omobhusuri we embusuro omwe, akaghi kobhusura ko moghondo ghooche. Hano aare kobhusura, chiheke chende, chikagho mwikongeera. Abhaheti bhano bhaare kuheta, bhaghachitacha tacha, ne ebhinyonyi bhighaacha bhighacheri.
Chiheke chende, chikagho ghwitare. Hano chaamerre, chikabhori amanche, chikanyaara.
Chiheke chende, chikagho mumaho. Amaho ghayo ghakamera hamwe ne chiheke chiyo, ghaghachibhanda chighaku.
Chiheke chende chikagho ko bhutoto obhuchomu, chikamera chighakiina, chikaama bhukongʼu.” Hano Yeesu amarre kughamba ghayo, akaghamba ko riraka rikoro akabhughaa, “Ono aghoote amatwe gho okooghu, na ooghu!”
Abheegha bha Yeesu bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “N-ke oghotuna ghotubhoorra gho ekihekaani kino?”
Akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Inyu, Ghiteema abhasakiiri kumanya amangʼana ghano ghatahonywiru kurenga Obhukama bhooche. Ghasi abhande ndabhabhoorra ko ebhihekaani, korri, ibhe ghote omurooti Isaaya abhughire ighoo, ‘Bharigherri, ghasi bhatighe kurora, bhooghu, ghasi bhatighe kumanya n-gentoke kighambiru.’
“Ekihekaani kiyo n-ighoo, embusuro ne Engʼana ya Ghiteema.
Ne chiheke chino chaatoonyire mwikongeera, chireereki abhanto bhano bhakooghu Engʼana ya Ghiteema, kumaruho, Risambu righaacha no koruusi engʼana eyo mometema gheebho, bhataghaacha koyitabherri no ghutooribhu.
“Ne chiheke chino chaatoonyire ghwitare, chireereki abhanto bhano bhakooghu Engʼana ya Ghiteema, bharayitabherri ko ghuchomeru, gho enkaagha ensuuhu. Ghasi bhoono hano bhakubhona amacharibhu, bharayetigha, gho okubha obhwitabherri bhoobho bhutahirre emeri.
“Ne chiheke chino chaatoonyire ku amaho, chireereki abhanto bhano bhakooghu Engʼana ya Ghiteema. Ghasi bhoono hano enkaagha ensuuhu ekuheta bharanyankera obhotuni, okwighombu obhwame, no oghutegheribhu na amangʼana ghe ense. Ghayo neghu ghakugheri obhwitabherri bhoobho, bhutaakoruusi emehumo emichomu.
“Na chiheke chino chaatoonyire ko bhutoto obhuchomu, chireereki abhanto bhano bhakooghu Engʼana ya Ghiteema. Hano bhakumara koyooghu, bharayighoota mometema gheebho emichomu. Bhayo nebhu bhakoruusi emehumo emichomu gho koghumerri koobho.
“Tareho omonto ono akughooti etara, kumaruho ayekundekeri ne ekibhakori, hande aitoore monkorre yo obhorre. Ghasi arayitoora koghento kyo ghutoorra etara, korri hano abhanto bhaghusoha monyumba eyo, bharore obhurabhu.
“Ko riyo, ghinsi ghinsi kino ghekundekiiribhu, na kino kebhisiru, kirabha harabhu. Na bhinsi bhino bhekundekiiribhu, bhiratooru harabhu bhimanyikane.
Bhoono, ghayo mokooghu, mughategherre bhwaheene! Oyo wunsiwunsi ono akughamanya amangʼana ghayo, Ghiteema aramwengerri kughamanya bhwaheene. Ghasi bhoono, oyo wunsiwunsi ono atakughamanya amangʼana ghayo, Ghiteema aramoruusi kuru aghasuuhu kaare akurora amanyire.”
Enkaagha yende, bhamura bhaabho Yeesu na nyakowaabho, mbaaichire haare Yeesu. Ghasi bhoono bhataamuhekeere, gho okubha abhanto abhaaru mbaaighataine.
Abhanto abhande bhakabhoorra Yeesu bhakabhughaa, “Nyakowaanyu na bhamura bhaanyu, mbaimeeriire kibhara, bharatuna ghokurora.”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Yaaya na bhamura bhaitu m-mbano bhakooghu Engʼana ya Ghiteema no okoighoota.”
Orosiko romwe, Yeesu na abheegha bhaache bhakariina mo obhooto. Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Twomboke enyancha, tughende humbu.” Bhaghatanora, bhakaghi.
Enkaagha eno bhaare komboka, Yeesu akamisi chitoro mobhooto muyo. Rikama righaacha, obhooto bhoobho bhughasimi ghwichora amanche, bhakabha gho enkaagha ensineenu yo okwibhera.
Abheegha bhayo, bhakaghi kubhooki Yeesu, bhakamubhooki, bhakamubhorra bhakabhughaa, “Omutemi! Omutemi! Turaibhera!” Yeesu akabhooka, akahamera rikama riyo na amayengo, hari remwe, enyancha ighatenda.
Neho, Yeesu abhoorri abheegha bhaache akabhughaa, “Hai bhooni obhwitabherri bhoonyu?” Abheegha bhayo bhaghatiina na bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu, bhakabhoorani, “Ne-wuuye ono, akuhamera kuru rikama na amayengo, hari remwe, bhiramutegherra?”
Hano Yeesu na abheegha bhaache, bhoombokire enyancha ya Ghariraaya, bhakahika ekyaro kya Abhagheraasi, kino keeni rohumbu ro Ghariraaya.
Hano Yeesu aasekiire koru mo obhooto, aghasikana no omonto omwe wo omoghi ghuyo, ono atiiru ne emisambu. Omonto oyo, chensiko echaaru taare ghuswaara chingebho, ghwiki taare ghwikara monyumba, aare ghwikara mochimbeehera chino chaare ghochehunguru.
Omusambu ghuyo, ghukabha ghuramusakora hari kaaru. Abhanto mbasakiiri komurenda, gho okomubhoha ne eminyorro ne chensiri. Nankabha bhaakorre kee hayo, aare ghutenatena eminyorro ne chensiri chiyo bhaare komubhoha nachu kumara omusambu ghware komohira mwibhara. Neho, Yeesu akabhoorra omusambu ghuyo ghuhaatore omonto oyo. Omonto woore hano arigheraini na Yeesu, aghatema egheturi ko riiraka rikoro. Akairekera kebhumari mbere ya Yeesu, aramubhoorra ko riiraka rikoro, “Iye Yeesu, Omoona wa Ghiteema ono aani ighoro ya bhinsi, kana nke oghontuna? Ndaghusaasaama, utakaanyanki!”

Yeesu akamubhoori, “Eriina reecho ne-wuuye?” Wunsi akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Eriina reene, neeni, richeshi.” Naabhughire kee hayo, gho okubha aare aghoote emisambu emeeru.
Emisambu ghiyo, ghighasimi ghusaasaama Yeesu ghirabhughaa, “Otighe ghotutyambi tusohe mwirooma re nyaari.”
Ahase hayo, rubhareka ro orukereghe, ryaareho rihicho rikoro rye chimbeeche, rino ryare koriisi. Neho, emisambu ghiyo ghyasaasaamire Yeesu, ghikabhughaa, “Otumasere tusohe mo chimbeeche cheere.” Yeesu akaghimasera.
Emisambu ghikaru ko omonto oyo, ghikaghi ghighasoha mo chimbeeche chiyo. Hayo hayo, rihicho rinsi rye chimbeeche, rikaryerra engirimanta, ko omohiringito omororo, chighasoha monyancha, chighakweramu.
Hano abhariisi bhe chimbeeche chiyo, bhaarooche ghayo ghansi Yeesu aakorre, bhakaryera, bhakaghi momoghi omokoro na mobhechichi bhe chimbareka, bhakareghani amangʼana kubhanto ghano ghaabhaire.
Kumaruho abhanto bhaghatanora koghi kwirorra amangʼana ghayo ghote ghaabhaire, bhakahekeera Yeesu. Hano bhaahikire haare Yeesu aare, bhakarora omonto oyo emisambu ghyaaruure. Aare naikaire haghuhe na amaghoro gha Yeesu, aibhohire engebho, aani omuhoru. Abhanto bhayo bhakoobhoha.
Abhanto bhano bhaarooche amangʼana ghayo, bhakabha bharabhoorra bhaghendi bhaabho ghote Yeesu aahorri omonto oyo.
Abhanto bhansi bhe ekyaro kya Abhagheraasi, bhakaghootu no obhoobha bhukongʼu. Bhaghasaasaama Yeesu, aru mo ekyaro keebho. Ko riyo, Yeesu akariina mo obhooto korri atanore.
Omonto ono aaruusiribhu emisambu, aghasaasaama Yeesu kubha, amwitabherri kuru bhaghi hamwe. Ghasi bhoono Yeesu akaanga, akamubhoorra akabhughaa,
“Honchoka ka, ubhoorre abhanto amakoro gha Ghiteema ghano aghukoriire.” Neho, omonto oyo atanwere hayo, akaghi kureghaneri abhanto, ahase hansi momoghi ghuyo, ghaare Yeesu aamukoriire.
Hano Yeesu aagharokire koru orubhareka ruyo aaghire, aghaturungʼanu ne eghekomo kya abhanto bhano bhaare komughanya.
Aghaachaho omonto omwe, ono aare kubherekeru Yairo. Oyo, newe aare omokoro we enyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema. Hano Yairo oyo aahikire haare Yeesu, akahighama mbere yaache. Akamusaasaama aghende waache ka,
gho okubha, monke waache newe omwene aghoote, na aghote emeeka ikomi ne ebhere, aani ko obhorre arenda ghoku. Hano Yeesu aare koghi ko moghi gho Yairo, eghekomo kya abhanto, bhakabha bharamutambana bhamwinaarre bhukongʼu.
Kubhanto bhayo, aaremu omughaikoro, ono aare no obhorwire, bho okoru amaanyinga ko emeeka ikomi ne ebhere. [Nankabha amarre ebhinto bheeche bhinsi koghi kureru ku abhareri,] taareho kuru omwe ono anaghiri komuhori.
Neho omughaikoro oyo aachire nyuma ya Yeesu, aghaturi ekeghuchi kino kyare kongebho yaache. Hayo hayo, akahora obhorwire bhooche bhwa amaanyinga.
Yeesu akabhoori akabhughaa, “Ne-wuuye ono anturri?” Abhanto bhansi, bhakanga. Peetero akamugharokeri Yeesu akabhughaa, “Omutemi waito, abhanto n-abhaaru bhakwinaarre, bhaghusangeriire.”
Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akabhughaa, “Niimanyire neho aani omonto ono antuuri, gho okubha ndaiyoghu amanagha ghaane ngaruure.”
Hano omughaikoro oyo aarooche ataana ghote akwibhisa, akaghi haare Yeesu, araghankana. Akahighama mbere ya Yeesu, akamubhoorra kino kigherri amoturri, na ghote ahoriibhu, na abhanto bhansi, ngutegherra bhaare, ghayo aare kughamba.
Yeesu akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Monke waane, kino kigherri uhorre n-obhwitabherri bhoocho. Oghi no omurembe!”
Hano Yeesu aare akeere araghamba, aghaacha omonto omwe koru o Yairo omokoro we nyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, akabhoorra Yairo akabhughaa, “Monke waacho, namarre ghoku. Tigha kughenderri kunyanki omweghi.”
Hano Yeesu, oghuure amangʼana ghayo, akabhoorra Yairo, “Utaghatiina! Ubhe no obhwitabherri, na monke waacho arahora.”
Hano Yeesu aahikire o Yairo, aghaseghani abhanto abhande ghusoha hamwe nawe, ghasi bhoono, aghaitabherri Peetero, Yohana, Yaakobho, isawaabho na nyakowaabho omonke oyo.
Abhanto bhansi bhano bhaare ka hayo, bhaare ghokuura no kubhaabhayera ko oroku ro omonke oyo. Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Motighe ghokuura! Omonke ono taamara aku, ghasi bhoono namisiri!”
Abhanto bhayo bhaghasimi komuseka, gho okubha mbaamanyire, obhuheene omonke oyo namarre ghoku.
Yeesu, akaghoota okubhoko ko omonke oyo, aghatiiri riraka, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Omonke ono, bhooka!”
Hari remwe, omonke oyo, enkoro yaache ikamuhonchokera akaimerra hayo hayo. Yeesu akabhabhoorra, bhamuhe ebhyakori.
Hano abhaibhori bhaache bhaarooche ghayo, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu. Ghasi bhoono Yeesu akabhaseghani, bhatakabhoorra omonto wunsiwunsi ghano akorre ho.
Orosiko nyabhurebhe Yeesu akabherekera abhatomu bhaache ikomi na bhabhere. Akabhaha amanagha gho obhubhaahi, na amanagha gho koruusi emisambu ghinsi kubhanto, na gho okuhori abharwire.
Kumaruho akabhatoma, bhaghende kureghaneri abhanto amangʼana gho Obhukama bho Ghiteema, no okuhori abharwire.
Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Morughendo ronyu, mutakaaghegha ghento kiyo ghinsi ghinsi, ehimbo, omokumbe, ebhyakori, chembiri, hande chingebho cho kuhonchora.
Enyumba yinsiyinsi eno bhakubhaghaghaani musohe, mwikare muyo, kohikera orosiko runo moghutanora koru momoghi ghuyo.
Na omoghi, ghuno abhanto bhatakubhaghaghaani, moru muyo, mukongʼonte orotu rwa amaghoro ghaanyu, korri rubhe ekimanyerri kyo okwanga koobho.”
Neho bhoono abhatomu bhayo, bhatanwere, bhakabha bharaheta mobhechichi bharareghaneri abhanto amangʼana amachomu, no okuhori abharwire ahase hansi.
Hano Omutemi Herode Antibhasi oghuure amangʼana ghano Yeesu aare ghukora, akahaha, gho okubha abhanto bhande bhaare kughamba bharabhughaa, “Yeesu newe Yohana aaryokire koru kubhaku.”
Abhande, bhaare kobhugha kubha, n-omurooti Eriya newe ahyokire. Ghwiki abhande bhaare kobhugha, n-omwe wa abharooti bha kare newe aaryokire.
Ghasi bhoono, Herode Antibhasi akaibhoori akabhughaa, “Yohana naamutenire omotwe! Kana ghwiki ono! Ne-wuuye nkooghu amangʼana ghaache?” Ko riyo Herode akaighombu bhukongʼu arorane na Yeesu.
Hano abhatomu bha Yeesu bhaahonchokire haare Yeesu, bhakamubhoorra amangʼana ghansi ghano bhaakorre. Neho, Yeesu abhakangatire abheene ighoo haghare koghi momoghi ghuno ghware kubherekeru Bhetisaita.
Hano eghekomo kya abhanto kyaamanyire hano aghiire, bhakamutambana. Hano bhaahikire, Yeesu akabhaghaghana bhwaheene. Aghasimi kubheeghi Amangʼana gho Obhukama bho Ghiteema. Na akabha akahori abharwire bhano bhaare kwighombu kuhoribhu.
Hano omughoroobha ghwaahikire ereebha riraghi ghutebhera, abhatomu bhayo ikomi na bhabhere bhaghaacha haare Yeesu, bhakamubhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Hano mwiteregho tooni, bhoono otighe abhanto bhano, bhaghende mobhechichi na momeghondo ghino gheeni haghuhe hano, korri bhaitunere obhuraari ne ebhyakori.”
Ghasi bhoono Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Inyu, mubhahe ebhyakori!” Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, “Itu, tutaghoote ebhyakori bhino bhekubhaisa. Tuuna emighaate etaano ne chenswe ibhere ebhyene. Ghasi ngotuna wooni tughende kughorra abhanto bhansi bhano ebhyakori?”
Abhanto bhano bhaare hayo, abhasubhe abheene bhaare kye ebhikwe bhitaano. Yeesu akabhoorra abheegha bhaache akabhughaa, “Mubhoorre abhanto bhayo, bhaikare ebhikomo bhya abhanto mirongo etaano etaano.”
Neho, bhaakorre ghote abhabhooriire, abhanto bhansi bhaghaikara.
Yeesu akaghegha emighaate etaano ghiyo ne chenswe ibhere. Akagharamera mwisaaro, aghakumi Ghiteema. Neho, akasonora emighaate ghiyo, hano amarre akabhaha abheegha bhaache emighaate ghiyo ne chenswe chiyo, korri, bhatweni abhanto bhayo bhansi.
Abhanto bhansi bhakari, bhakaighota. Abheegha bha Yeesu bhaghakomani amasaaghi ghe ebhyakori, bhaghaichori ebhighabho ikomi na bhibhere.
Orosiko romwe, Yeesu na abheegha bhaache bhaare hamwe, abheene bhaiyohwere. Yeesu aare ghusaasaama Ghiteema. Kumaruho, akabhoori abheegha bhaache akabhughaa, “Abhanto bharabhugha kubha eni ne-wuuye?”
Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, “abhande, bharabhugha agho, iye niye Yohana Omubhaatiisi. Abhande, bharabhugha iye n-omorooti Eriya, ghwiki abhande bharabhugha, iye n-omwe wa abharooti bha kare aaryokire.”
Yeesu akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Ghasi bhoono, inyu murabhugha eni ne-wuuye?” Peetero akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Iye niye Kirisito. Ni-iye waatomiru na Ghiteema!”
Yeesu akabhaseghani bhatakabhoorra omonto engʼana eyo.
Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Eni Omoona wo Omonto, ndatunu nyankibu no kwangu na abhakoro bha Abhayahudi, na abhakoro bha abhasengeri na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa. Bhayo bharagheri niitu. Ghasi bhoono, orosiko ro ghatato, ndaryoka.”
Kumaruho Yeesu akabhoorra abhanto bhansi akabhughaa, “Omonto wunsiwunsi ono aghotuna ghuntambana eni, iratunu aiyange omwene, aitabherri enyanko yo ghuntambana chensiko chaache chinsi.
Gho okubha omonto wunsi wunsi ono aghotuna kwiyitanera, oyo newe araitabhute. Na omonto wunsiwunsi ono araitabhute gho kugheri eni, oyo naraitoori.
Omonto arabhona ghento ke, hano araabhone obhwame bhwe ense engima eno, ghasi bhoono atabhotire obhuhoru bhooche?
“Omonto ono akundorra chinsoni eni na ameeghi ghaane, oyo newe eni Omoona wo Omonto ndamurorra chinsoni ko mirengaari ghe Taata Ghiteema, hano nguucha koru ghwisaaro hamwe na abhamaraika abhahoreeru.
“Ndabhabhoorra obhuheene kubha, haare inyu bhano mwimeriire hano, nehobhaani bhano bhataghoku, bhakeere kurorra Obhukama bho Ghiteema!”
Hano Yeesu aamarre kughamba amangʼana ghayo, chikaheta chensiko ghote inyaanye, akaghegha Peetero, Yohana, na Yaakobho, akariina nabhu korukereghe korri asaasaame Ghiteema.
Enkaagha eno aahikire korukereghe, aghasimi ghusaasaama Ghiteema. Na hano Yeesu aare ghusaasaama Ghiteema, etuubho yaache ighaishoori. Chingebho chaache, chikabha chindabhu chai, chikabharibhari bhukongʼu.
Hayo hayo bhakahyokeru na abhasubhe bhabhere, bhakabha bharaghambana na Yeesu. Abhasubhe bhayo bhaare Musa na Eriya. Bhaare kubharibhari gho okubha mbaaghoote emirengaari. Bhakabha bharaghambera ghote Yeesu akumareeri ghano Ghiteema amutunire akore, gho ghukwera Yerusareemu.

Gho enkaagha eyo, Peetero na bhaghendi bhaache bhaare bhamisiri chitoro chendito. Hano bhaabhookire, bhakarora Yeesu arabharibhari ko emirengaari gheeche. Mbaarooche na abhanto bhande bhabhere, bhaimeeriire haghuhe na Yeesu.
Hano Musa na Eriya bhaare kwenda ghutaanana na Yeesu, Peetero akabhoorra Yeesu, “Omutemi waito, bhwaheene tumenye hano. Twabheke hano, ebhebhuru bhitato, egheecho, ke Musa, ne ekende ke Eriya.” Ghasi bhoono Peetero, taamanyire kino akughambera.
Enkaagha eno Peetero aare akeere araghabha ghayo, risaaro rikabhaghubha. Abheegha bhayo, bhaghatiina bhukongʼu hano bhaaghubhiru ne risaaro riyo.
Bhakooghu riraka koru ghwisaaro riyo, rirabhughaa, “Ono newe Omoona waane, ono noohwere. Mubhe muramutegherra!”
Amangʼana ghayo hano ghasire, abheegha bhayo bhakarora Yeesu aani omwene. Ghayo ghansi bhaarooche hayo, bhataabhooriire omonto wunsiwunsi gho chensiko chiyo.
Hano bhwaakiire, Yeesu na abheegha bhatato bhayo, bhaghasekera koru morukereghe, bhaghasikana ne eghekomo kya abhanto.
Omonto omwe koru moghikomo kya abhanto bhayo, aghatiirri riiraka akabhughaa, “Iye Omweghi, ndaghusaasaama, uhori omoona waane, gho okubha n-omumwemwe.
Omusambu nguramughoota, hari remwe arabha aratema ekereghe. Ghwiki, aragho ririmo, rihuro riraru momonu. Ndiramunyanki bhukongʼu, na ritaraamuhaatora bhongo.
Naasaasaamire abheegha bhaacho bhareruusi, ghasi bhoono bhaghatamu.”
Yeesu akabhughaa, “Inyu abhanto bhe rikora rino, n-abhasineenu mooni, mutaana obhwitabherri! Ndaghenderri ghwikara na inyu, kohikera ruuhe? Ndetera omoona waacho oyo hano.”
Hano omoona oyo, aare koghi haare Yeesu, hari remwe, omusambu ghuyo ghukamurekera harense, akabha ne ririmo. Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akarihamera, akahori omoona oyo, akamugharokeri isawaabho.
Hano abhanto bhansi bhaarooche amanagha amakoro gha Ghiteema, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu. Enkaagha eno bhaare kuroghoorra amakono ghayo Yeesu aakorre, ewe akabhoorra abheegha bhaache akabhughaa,
“Amangʼana ghano nkubhabhoorra bhoono, mughategherre bhwaheene. Eni Omoona wo Omonto nakaghi ghutooru mu mabhoko gha abhanto.”
Ghasi bhoono, amangʼana ghano Yeesu aabhabhooriire, bhataaghongwere, gho okubha ghaabhisiru bhatamu kughongora. Nabhu mbaatiinire kubhoori Yeesu, kino aarengire.
Abheegha bha Yeesu bhaghatonani, ne-wuuye omokoro ghukera bhaghendi bhaache.
Yeesu akamanya amaitegherro ghaabho, akaghegha omoona omosuuhu, akamwimerri haghuhe nawe,
akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Omonto ono akughaghaanera omoona ke ono ko eriina reene, neeni akughaghaani. Ghwiki omonto ono akungaghaani, hayo tare eni akughaghaani, araghaghaani ono aantomire. Gho kubha, omonto ono aani omosuuhu haare inyu bhansi, oyo newe omokoro ghukera bhansi.”
Yohana akabhoorra Yeesu akabhughaa, “Iye Omutemi waito, ntwaarooche omonto ono aare koruusi emisambu ko eriina reecho, tukamuseghani, gho okubha ewe, tare mughendi waito.”
Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Mutakamuseghani ghwiki, gho okubha omonto ono atakuhangana na inyu, newe aani orubhareka ronyu.”
Hano enkaagha ya Yeesu yo kugharoka mwisaaro yaare ehikire haghuhe, neho aarooche aghende Yerusareemu.
Aghatoma abhahiri bha amangʼana bhaache bhamukangate. Abhahiri bha amangʼana bhayo, bhakaghi bhaghasoha mo eghechichi kemwe kya Abhasamaariya, korri bhamuseemeri ahase ho okuhekera.
Ghasi bhoono, abhanto bha hayo bhataitabheeriiri komughaghaanera, gho okubha Yeesu nkuheta aare araghi Yerusareemu.
Hano abheegha bha Yeesu, Yaakobho na Yohana, bhaarooche ghayo, bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Omutemi waito, ngotuna wooni tusabhe omorro ghusekere koru mwisaaro ghubhasiki [ghote bhoore Eriya aakorre]?”
Ghasi bhoono Yeesu, akabhaishooreri, akabhaseghani. [Akabhughaa, “Inyu mutamanyire m-mbanto bha teemo ke mooni],
gho okubha Omoona wo Omonto tiniichire ghosiki abhanto ghasi kubhatoori.” Kumaruho, Yeesu na abheegha bhaache bhaghatanora bhakaghi eghechichi ekende.
Enkaagha eno Yeesu na abheegha bhaache bhaare ghonchera bharaghi, omonto omwe akabhoorra Yeesu akabhughaa, “Eni ndabha ndaghutambana ahase hansihansi hano okoghi!”
Ghasi bhoono Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Nyamobhwe, mbaghoote chehunguru, ne ebhinyonyi mbighoote chintara, ghasi bhoono, eni Omoona wo Omonto, tingoote kuru hokuraari omotwe ghoone.”
Yeesu akabhoorra omonto owonde akabhughaa, “Untambane!” Omonto oyo akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Omutemi onyitabherri singata, ngende ndyeke taata.”
Ghasi bhoono Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Tigha abhaku bharyeke abhaku bhaabho. Ghasi bhoono iye, nooghi ureghaneri abhanto amangʼana gho Obhukama bho Ghiteema.”
Ghwiki omonto owonde, akabhoorra Yeesu akabhughaa, “Ee Omutemi, ndabha ndaghutambana. Ghasi bhoono, singata, onyitabherri, ngende mboorre abhanto bha ka, ngiire.”
Yeesu akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Omonto wunsiwunsi ono asimiri kurema kumaruho aghaishyori akarigheeri hano arwerire, oyo taghotunu ko Obhukama bho Ghiteema.”
Kumaruho, Omutemi Yeesu akoohora abheegha abhande, mirongo mohungate na bhabhere. Akabhatoma bhabhere bhabhere, bhakangate koghi momeghi na ahase hansi, hano omwene atunire kohika.
Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Ebhyakori ne-ebheeru moghondo, ghasi bhoono abhaghesi m-basuuhu. Bhoono musabhe omwene moghondo, ahire abhaghesi komoghondo bhaghese.
Bhoono inyu mughende. Ghasi mumanye kubha, kubhatoma kuno nkubhatoma ghati ya abhanto, n-ke haare ebhimaano bhya amangʼondi, bhekohirru mochesunche ghati.
Mutakaaghegha omukobha, esako ye chembiri, hande ebhiraato bhende. Mutakagheechera ghonchera ko ghukeerikeeri abhanto.
“Na enyumba yinsiyinsi eno moghusoha, mukeeri abhanto bha muyo mobhughee, ‘Bha muno, mubhe no omurembe!’
Na araabhemu, omonto wo omurembe oghukeerani konyu ko omurembe kuramunooka. Ghasi bhoono, uraabhone omonto wo omurembe ataremu, omurembe ghoonyu ghurabhagharokera.
Mokughaghaanibhu mutaghasaama saama, ghasi bhoono mwikare monyumba eyo musohire. Mori ebhyakori bhino bhaakubhaha gho okubha omubhaghasi naisire kuhaabhu omoheera ghooche.
“Hano musohire omoghi ghunsighunsi bhabhaghaghaane, mori ebhyakori bhino bhakubhaha.
Muhori abharwire bhano bhaani momoghi ghuyo. Mureghaneri abhanto bha momoghi muyo mobhughee, ‘Obhukama bho Ghiteema mbwisukire haghuhe.’
“Ghasi bhoono, hano moghusoha momoghi, na abheene omoghi bhabhatyambi, inyu muhete gho chihogho chaabho murabhughaa,
‘Kuru orotu ro momoghi ghoonyu runo rooni kumaghoro ghiitu, turarukongʼonta, rubhe ekimanyerri kyo okwanga koonyu. Ghasi bhoono, mumanye engʼana eno ighoo, Obhukama bho Ghiteema mbwisukire haghuhe!’
