Ndabhabhoorra ndabhugha, orosiko rwa abhanto ghukengeru ebhiina, Ghiteema araghoota enchagho okubhanto bha momoghi ghuyo bhukongʼu, ghukera ghote akughootera enchagho abhanto abhateeyu bha Sotoma.”
“Haaho yaanyu inyu abhanto bha Koorasiini! Haaho yaanyu inyu abhanto bha Bhetisaita! Sungu amakono ghano naakorre mbere yaanyu, neghu naakorre momeghi ghe Tiiro na Sitooni, obhuheene abhanto bha Tiiro na sitooni, nguswara bhaare chingebho cha maghonera no kwihaka riibhu kwereki mbatiitire ebhibhe bheebho mbere ya Ghiteema.
Ghasi bhoono, orosiko ro ghukengerru ebhiina, Ghiteema araghootera enchagho bhukongʼu inyu abhanto bha Koorasiini na Bhetisaita, ghukera ghote akughootera enchagho abhanto abhateeyu bha Tiiro na Sitooni!
“Na inyu, abhanto bha Kabherenaumu, muraitegherra kubha Ghiteema arabhariini mwisaaro? Tare ighoo! Ghasi bhoono arabhatabhuta nyaari!”
Neho, Yeesu aamarerirri akabhoorra abheegha bhaache akabhughaa, “Omonto ono akubhategherra inyu, arantegherra eni. No omonto ono akwanga kubhategherra inyu, kuru eni naangire ghuntegherra. Ono aangire ghuntegherra eni, naangire kuru Ghiteema ono aantomire.”
Neho abheegha bhayo mirongo mohungate na bhabhere bhaagharokire, bhachomiiru. Bhakabhoorra Yeesu bhakabhughaa, “Omutemi waito, kuru hano tokutyambi emisambu ku amanagha ghe eriina reecho ngotooghu gheeni.”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Aarooche Risambu riragho koru mwisaaro kyo okubhari ghwe enkobha.
Righeeri, mbahaire amanagha gho obhubhaahi, ghoghukera chenguru cho omobhisa waanyu oyo. Ku amanagha ghayo, muratacha chinchoka ne ebhitoomaani, na ghitareho kino ghekunaghi kubhanyahaara.
“Mutaghaachomeru gho okubha emisambu ghirabhategherra hano mokoghetyambi. Ghasi bhoono muchomeru, gho okubha, amariina ghaanyu, ngandekiru mwisaaro.”
Enkaagha eyo eyo, Enkoro Ehoreeru akagheri Yeesu achomeru bhukongʼu, kuru akabhughaa, “Taata ono wooni Omutemi wa mwisaaro na monse muno. Uchomiri gho okubha, amangʼana ghaacho ghano obhisire bho obhungʼaini na abhasomi, ghasi bhoono uhonyoriire abhanto bhano bhaana obhwitabherri na iye, ghote abhaana abhasuuhu. N-ighoo waakorre Taata, gho okubha nighoo yaaghuchomiire.”
Neho ghwiki Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Taata Ghiteema, ahaire bhinsi. Atareho omonto ono amanyire Omoona wa Ghiteema, kuru Taata Ghiteema omwene. Na atareho omonto ono amanyire Taata Ghiteema, ghasi Omoona waache omwene newe amumanyire, na bhaare Omoona asaighire kubhahonyorra.”
Yeesu akaihonchorra abheegha bhaache bhaani abheene haghare, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Inyu muuna echaghati, gho okubha kwiroorra mooni amangʼana ghano na amaiso ghaanyu!
Ndabhabhoorra aghoo, bhaareho abharooti abhaaru, na abhakama, bhano bhaighombiru kurora ghano mokurora, ghasi bhoono bhataagharooche. Ghwiki, mbaighombiru kooghu ghano inyu mokooghu, ghasi bhoono bhataaghoghuure.”
Orosiko nyabhurebhe, omweghi wa amaragherri gha Musa naimeriire, akabhoori Yeesu engʼana yo komucharibhu. Akamubhoori akabhughaa, “Omweghi, nkore ke, korri mbone eghabho yo obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi?”
Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Mumaragherri gha Musa mbwe yandekiru? N-ke iye oghusoma no kumanya mumaragherri ghayo?”
Omweghi wa amaragherri, akagharokeri Yeesu akabhughaa, “Yaandekiru aghoo, ‘Omusaighe Omutemi Ghiteema waacho, ko omotema ghoocho ghunsi, gho enkoro yaacho yinsi, gho chenguru chaacho chinsi, na ko obhungʼaini bhoocho bhunsi.’ Ghwiki ‘Omusaighe mughendi waacho, ghote wisaighire iye omwene.’”
Yeesu akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Ugharokiiri bhwaheene! Kora kee hayo, urabhona obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi.”
Ghasi bhoono, omweghi oyo wa amaragherri, naatunire kwereki kubha ewe n-omuheene mbere ya Ghiteema, nekyu kyagherri ghwiki akabhoori Yeesu akabhughaa, “Na mughendi waane, ne-wuuye?”
Yeesu akamuhekaaneri ekihekaani akabhughaa, “Aareho omonto nyabhurebhe, ono aaruure Yerusareemu, araghi momoghi gho Yeriko. Monchera hayo, aghasoheeru na abhaibhi. Bhakamoruusi chingebho, bhakamutema bhukongʼu, bhakamotigha arenda ghuteni.
“Enchera tekubhoorra omughendi, omusengeri nyabhurebhe akaheta monchera hayo. Ghasi bhoono omusengeri oyo, na-amaiso amurekerire akaheta rubareka.
Omuraawi wunsi akaheta ghonchera kuyo, akamurekera amaiso akaheta rubhareka.
“Ghasi bhoono Omusamaariya nyabhurebhe akaheta, ono aare morughendo rooche. Hano aamorooche omonto oyo, akamwabhera.
Akamwisokerra, akamuhaka amaro ghe emisabhiibhu na amaghuta ku maghaati ghaache. Hano amarre, akamubhoherra bhwaheene kumacheraha ghayo, akamoriini gho entikere yaache, akamohira monyumba ya abhagheni, akabha aramubhabhari.
“Icho yaache, Omusamaariya oyo akaruusi chedinaari ibhere akamuha omwene nyumba. Akamubhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Omubhabhari omonto ono. Ubhone omubhabhairi chembiri chino nkuhaire chesirre, hano nkugharoka ndakureha.’ ”
Neho, Yeesu abhoorri omweghi oyo wa amaragherri akabhughaa, “Bhoono mbe mboorra ghote iye okurora. Ku bhayo bhansi ne-wuuye aare mughendi waache wo komughaghaani?”
Omweghi wa amaragherri akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Wo-oore aamwabhiire.” Yeesu akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Iye wunsi nooghi, ubhe ne eteemo ke eyo!”
Enkaagha Yeesu na abheegha bhaache bhaare korughendo ro koghi Yerusareemu, bhaghasoha moghechichi nyabhurebhe. Moghechichi kiyo, aareho omughaikoro omwe, eriina reeche Maarita, akabhakarabhisi ka mooche.
Maarita oyo, aare na monke waabho, eriina reeche Mariyamu. Mariyamu aghaikara haghuhe na amaghoro gho Omutemi, aramutegherra.
Maarita, aare kunyanka ne emeremo emeeru, akaiyoghu bhobhe, akaghi akabhoorra Yeesu akabhughaa, “Omutemi waito, tokurora, omoona waito nanteghiire emeremo ghinsi? Mubhoorra antooreri emeremo!”
Ghasi bhoono, Omutemi akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Maarita, Maarita! N-ke okunyankerra?
Engʼana ne-emwe eyeene eno yeeho, kuru nkuheta yeeni bhinsi. Eyo neyu Mariyamu achaghwere, engʼana enchomu, na atareho omonto ono akomureki ghuntegherra.”
Orosiko romwe, Yeesu aare ahase nyabhurebhe arasaasaama Ghiteema. Hano aamarre, omwe wa abheegha bhaache akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Omutemi waito, otweghi ghusaasaama Ghiteema, ghote Yohana Omubhaatiisi eeghiri abheegha bhaache.”
Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Hano moghusaasaama Ghiteema, mobhughe aghoo, ‘Taata [waito ono wooni mwisaaro] eriina reecho, richongibhu. Obhukama bhoocho, bhuuche. [Amaigha ghaacho, ghahekeerane monse hano, ghote ghaani eyo mwisaaro.]
Ubhe uratuha ebhyakori bhiitu kira rosiko.
Otwabhere ebhibhe bhiitu, ghote na itu tokwabhera bhansi bhano bhaghotusareri. Utaghatuhatora mumacharibhu, [ghasi otutoori kumacharibhu gho omosineenu woore.]’”
Neho Yeesu abhabhooriire akabhughaa, “Tobhughe aghoo iraabhe omwe haare inyu araaghi haare musaani waache, obhotiko ke ghati, na amubhoorre abhughee, ‘Musaani waane, ndasabha unsakeri emighaate etato.
Gho kubha, musaani waane aare morughendo, bhoono ahekiire waane, na eni tingoote ebhyakori bhyo okomuha.’
“Ghasi bhoono, musaani waache oyo amugharokeri abhughee, ‘Tigha kunnyanki! Niimarre kwighara orwighe, eni na abhaana bhaane ntomisiri. Tengutora kubhooka nkuhe eghento ghinsighinsi.’
“Ndabhabhoorra aghoo, uraabhone omonto oyo atakubhooka no okomuha emighaate ghiyo, gho okubha ewe m-musaani waache, ghasi bhoono, arabhooka komuha kino aghotuna, gho okubha naghenderiri komusabha.
“Bhoono, eni ndabhabhoorra, mubhe murasabha Ghiteema, murahaabhu. Mubhe muratuna koru haare Ghiteema, nawe arabhaha, mubhe muratema hooti mogheseku, na Ghiteema arabhaighorra.
Gho kubha, omonto wunsiwunsi ono aghusabha Ghiteema, arahaabhu. Ono aghotuna koru haare Ghiteema, arabhona. Na ono aghutema hooti mogheseku, Ghiteema aramwighorra.
“No-omwibhori ke, ono omoona waache akomusabha omughaate, amuhe righena? Hande amusabhe enswe, amuha enchoka?
Hande omoona amusabhe ribhurunge, amuhe eghitoomaani?
Ke hayo, inyu n-abhasineenu mooni, ghasi bhoono mumanyire kubhaha abhaana bhaanyu ebhinto ebhichomu. Ghwiki Taata wa mwisaaro n-omuheene, na arabhaha Enkoro Ehoreeru bhano bhakomusabha.”
Orosiko romwe, Yeesu aghatyambi omusambu ghuno ghwakorre omonto abhe rimuumu. Hano omusambu ghuyo ghyaamotighire, aghasimi kughamba. Abhanto bhano bhaareho, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu.
Ghasi bhoono, abhande bhakabhughaa, “Aratyambi emisambu ku amanagha gha Bherisebhuri omokoro we emisambu!”
Abhande mbaatunire kosaghasa Yeesu, bhakamusabha abheereki ekimanyerri kwereki kubha naarure o Ghiteema.
Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akamanya amaitegherro ghaabho, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Hano abhanto bho obhukama bhomwe bhaghwitana, obhukama bhuyo mbotyambire. Ke hayo hayo, abhanto bhe enyumba emwe hano bhaghwitana, enyumba eyo nesikire.
Uraabhone obhukama bhwe Risambu, bhutakwighwerrana, obhukama bhuyo mbwe bhokwimerra? Ndabhabhoorra kee hayo, gho okubha inyu mobhughire aghoo, ndatyambi emisambu ku amanagha gha Bherisebhuri.
Uraabhone eni ndatyambi emisambu ku amanagha gha Bherisebhuri, abheegha bhaanyu nabhu, bharatyambi emisambu ku amanagha gha Bherisebhuri? Bhoono, abheegha bhaanyu abheene kwereki bhaani aghoo, ghayo mokughamba tare gho obhuheene.
Ghasi bhoono, amanagha gha Ghiteema neghu ghakugheri ndatyambi emisambu. Hayo ireereki Obhukama bho Ghiteema bhubhahekeere.
Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani arabhughaa, “Hano omonto we chenguru ne ebhiitanero, akurenda ebhinto bhe monyumba yaache, abhaibhi bhataaghutora kwibha ebhinto bheeche.
Ghasi bhoono, hano aghuucha omonto wonde ono akomukeri chenguru, aramutema, amoruusi ebhiitanero bheeche bhino aghwisegha ne ebhinto bheeche bhinsi, na kubhatweni abhande.
“Bhoono, omonto ono atare hamwe na eni, oyo no-omobhisa waane. No omonto ono ataghukomani abhanto bha Ghiteema hamwe na eni, oyo no-omusanchi wa abhanto bha Ghiteema.”
Yeesu akaghenderri kughamba akabhughaa, “Hano omusambu ghokoru ko omonto, ghurainangoora nangoora ahase ahahoomu, ghuratuna ahase ho okomuunya. Hano hakubhora, ghurabhughaa,
‘Mbe, ndagharoka ko omonto woore ndaikara.’
Hano ghokugharoka ko omonto oyo, ghubhone n-ke haare enyumba itarekiribhu no oghuchochu bhwaheene, hayo bhoono neho omusambu ghokoghi ghotuna emisambu ghende mohungate, emesineenu bhukongʼu ghukera eghu. Ne emisambu ghiyo ghinsi ghiraacha kumenya ko omonto oyo. Bhoono, omonto oyo arabha ne ehari ensineenu bhukongʼu ghukera ekimbere.”
Hano Yeesu aare kughamba ghayo, omughaikoro nyabhurebhe mubhanto bhayo, akaghamba ko riiraka rikoro akabhughaa, “Aghoote echaghati omughaikoro ono akwibhwire no oghokughonki!”
Ghasi bhoono Yeesu akagharokeri akabhughaa, “Hasehe! Ghasi mbaghoote echaghati bhano bhakooghu Engʼana ya Ghiteema, no okoighoota.”
Enkaagha eno abhanto abhaaru bhaare ghwikomani, Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Abhanto bhe erikora rino, n-abhasineenu bhukongʼu. Bharatuna nkore amakono, ghabhe ekimanyerri kubha Ghiteema naantomire. Ghasi bhoono tengukora ekimanyerri ghinsighinsi haare inyu. Ekimanyerri kino muraarore, n-ge keere kyo omurooti Yoona.
Gho kubha, ke haare Yoona aare ekimanyerri ku abhanto bho omoghi ghuno ghokubherekeru Ninaawi, n-kee hayo hayo, na eni Omoona wo Omonto, ndabha ekimanyerri ku abhanto bhe erikora rino.
“Orosiko ro Ghiteema ro ghukengera abhanto ebhiina, omutemi we ekighaikoro, we ekyaro kino keeni orubhareka ro bhachuuta araimerra no ghukengera ebhiina abhanto bhe erikora rino kubha na-abhakori bhe ebhibhe. Gho okubha ewe naaruure mokyaro ghe kure bhukongʼu, korri ategherre amangʼana gho obhungʼaini gho omukama Suremani. Na bhoono nehwani hano omonto omokoro ghukera Suremani.
“Orosiko roore rwa abhanto ghukengeru ebhiina, abhanto bha Ninaawi bharaimerra na abhanto bhe erikora rino. Abhanto bha Ninaawi ninga bhakengere ebhiina abhanto bhe erikora rino kubha na-abhakori bhe ebhibhe. Irabha kee hayo gho okubha hano Yoona abhareghaniiri Engʼana ya Ghiteema, remwe ighoo, mbaatiitire ebhibhe bheebho. Bhoono omonto omokoro ghukera Yoona hano aani, ghasi bhoono inyu mutaaghotigha ebhibhe bheenyu hano mokureghaneribhu Engʼana ya Ghiteema!”
“Tareho omonto ono akughooti etara, kumaruho ayebhise, hande ayekundekeri. Omonto oyo arayitoora o koghento kyo ghutoorra etara, korri, enkaagha eno abhanto bhaghusoha monyumba, bharore obhurabhu.
“Amaiso ghaacho n-kye etara yo omobhere ghoocho. Gharaabhe na-amahoru, omobhere ghoocho ghunsi ghurabha no obhurabhu. Ghasi bhoono, amaiso ghaacho gharaabhe amasareku, omobhere ghoocho ghunsi mokeruutu ghooni.
Ko riyo, wirende korri obhurabhu bhuno ughoote bhutakaabha ekeruutu.
Gho kubha, uraabhone omobhere ghoocho ghunsi ghughoote obhurabhu, ekeruutu ghitaremu, urarora bhwaheene, ke haare okumorekeribhu ne etara eno eghooka.”
Hano Yeesu amarre kughamba ghayo, Omubharisaayo omwe akamughaghaani koghi waache kuraaghera. Hano Yeesu ahikire o Omubharisaayo oyo, aghasoha monyumba, aghaikara kuraaghera.
Omubharisaayo oyo, akaroghoora hano arooche Yeesu araraaghera ataisaabhire amabhoko ghote yaare esemoka yaabho.
Ghasi bhoono, Omutemi Yeesu akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Inyu Amabharisaayo, mooni kya abhanto bhano bhakweeghi kibhara ye eghikombe ne esahaani. Ghasi bhoono obhobhe no oghusara nebhu bhwichwire mometema gheenyu.
Inyu m-bakangi mooni! Ghiteema ono ateemire kibhara, newe ateemire na gha morense.
Mubhasakeri abhatobhu ko emetema gheenyu ghinsi, neho na inyu mokubha abhaheene.
“Haaho yaanyu inyu Amabharisaayo, gho okubha, muraruuseri Ghiteema, ahase ha ikomi he ebhinto bhinsi, kuru ebhirongero kye echumbe, ebhetunguri ne ebhende, ghasi bhoono mutaghukorra abhanto amangʼana gho bhuheene no oghusaigha Ghiteema. Ghayo neghu moghotunu mukore hamwe no komoruuseri chisataaka chiyo.
“Haaho yaanyu, inyu Amabharisaayo, gho okubha, murasaigha ghwikara ko ebhetumbe bhya abhakoro mochenyumba cha Abhayahudi cho oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema. Murasaigha ghukeeribhu gho chinsoni mometeera.
Haaho yaanyu inyu bhano mokubha ghye chimbeehera, chino chitakuroru, kuru abhanto bharaheta bharachitacha bhatamanyire.”
Omweghi omwe wa amaragherri gha Musa akabhoorra Yeesu akabhughaa, “Omweghi, hano okughamba amangʼana gho bhobhe ghayo na itu bhansi ngotukoherani wooni.”
Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Na inyu abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa, haaho yaanyu. Gho okubhamuratweka abhanto emerigho emerito ghya amaragherri, ghino bhataghutora kughegha. Na inyu mutakogheturi kuru ne ekeera!
Haaho yaanyu, inyu abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa, gho okubha muraabheka chimbeehera cha abharooti, ghasi bhoono abhanto bhano bhaaitire abharooti bhayo, m-basookoro yaanyu!
Ko riyo, mureereki murimererra ghayo bhasookoro yaanyu bhaakorre. Gho okubhaebhu mbaaitire abharooti bhayo, na inyu muraabheka chimbeehera chaabho.
“Kiyo nekyu kyagherri Ghiteema, ko obhungʼaini bhooche akabhughaa, ‘Ndabhatomera abharooti na abhatomu. Ghasi bhoono, abhamwe bharaitu, na abhande bharanyankibhu.’
Ko riyo abhanto bhe rikora rino, bharaabhooribhu amaanyinga gha abharooti bhansi bhano bhaaitiru, koru esemoka ye ense.
Kuwansera ku amaanyinga gha Abheeri, kohikera ku amaanyinga gha Sakariya, ono aitiiru mu ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, ghati ya ahase ho koruseri ebhemwenso, ne Enyumba Ehoreeru ya Ghiteema. Obhuheene, ndabhabhoorra aghoo, abhanto bhe rikora rino nebhu bhakubhooribhu ghayo ghansi.
“Haaho yaanyu, inyu abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa. Gho kubha, murighara orwighe, muraseghani abhanto bhataghaasoha kumanya Ghiteema, inyu abheene mutaghusoha.”
Hano Yeesu aruure hayo, Amabharisaayo na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa, bhaghasimi komunyeera chinkaani bhukongʼu bhakaraire. Ghokoru hayo, bhakabha bharamubhoori amangʼana amaaru maaru,
korri bhabhone engʼana yo okomuchongera.
Enkaagha eyo, abhanto ebhirara ne ebhirara, bhaare bhaikomaini, kuru bhakabha bharatachana. Yeesu aghasimi kughambana na abheegha bhaache akabhughaa, ‘‘Mwiyangarre ne ehamiira ya Amabharisaayo, kuyo neku okughamba ighoo, obhwitaami bhoobho.
“Eghento ghinsighinsi kino omonto akundekiiri, Ghiteema araghekundokori, na ghinsighinsi kino kebhisiru, kiramanyikana.
Amangʼana ghano mughambire mokeruutu, abhanto bhansi ninga bhaghooghu. Na ghansi ghano mware ghusemerrani riiko, gharareghanibhu bhurabhu.
“Ndabhabhoorra inyu abhasaani bhaane, mutakoobhoha abhanto bhano bhaghwita omobhere oghwene. Gho okubha hano bhakumara ghwita omobhere, bhataana engʼana yende eno bhakunaghi kubhakora.
Ghasi bhoono, tigha mbabhorre wo okoobhoha. Mwobhohe Ghiteema, gho okubha naghoote amanagha gho obhubhaahi bho ghwita omonto no okomutabhuta momorro gho chehanaamu. Oyo newe wo okoobhoha omwene.
“Ebhisanchi bhitaano, bhitekughoribhu ko obhughori obhosuuhu? Ghiteema takwebha kuru kemwe keebho.
Ghasi bhoono inyu, Ghiteema namanyire kuru obhooru bhwe rituuki re kometwe gheenyu. Ko riyo mutakoobhoha, gho okubha inyu mughoote obhwera ghukera ebhisanchi haare Ghiteema.
“Ndabhabhoorra aghoo, omonto wunsiwunsi ono akonyitabherri mbere ya abhanto kubha ewe n-owaane, eni Omoona wo Omonto, ndamwitabherri mbere ya abhamaraika bha Ghiteema kubha, omonto oyo n-owaane.
Ghasi bhoono, omonto wunsiwunsi ono akonyanga mbere ya abhanto, na eni wunsi ndamwanga mbere ya abhamaraika bha Ghiteema.
Omonto wunsiwunsi ono akungamba bhobhe eni Omoona wo Omonto, Ghiteema aramwabhera. Ghasi bhoono omonto wunsiwunsi ono aghutoka Enkoro Ehoreeru, oyo takwabheru.
“Hano mokohiru mochenyumba cha Abhayahudi cho oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, na mbere ya abhakoro, na mbere ya bha amanagha gho obhubhaahi, mutakaitegherra bhwe moghwikorerra na ghote mokughamba.
Gho okubhaEnkoro Ehoreeru arabheeghi hayo hayo ghano moghutakeru kughamba.”
Omonto omwe mubhanto bhayo, akabhoorra Yeesu akabhughaa, “Omweghi, tabhoorra mura waito, antweni eghabho eno taata atuteghiire.”
Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Iye! Ne-wuuye antoorre nibhe omorwechi hande omotweni we eghabho yaanyu?”
Neho Yeesu aabhooriire abhanto bhayo akabhughaa, “Mwirende no omwingʼangʼo ghwe ebhinto, gho okubha obhuhoru bho omonto bhutaakoru ko ebhinto bheeche ebheeru.”
Kumaruho, Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani akabhughaa, “Aareho omwame omwe, ono omoghondo ghooche ghware ghwamire bhukongʼu omooka nyabhurebhe.
Omwame oyo, akaibhoori momotwe ghooche akabhughaa, ‘Bhoono, nkorebhwe? Gho okubhatingoote ahase ho ghutoora ebhyakori bheene bhingʼana hano!’
Neho abhughire aghoo, ‘Ndahanyora ebhitara bheene, korri ndoke ebhende ebhekoro ghukera bhino. Ntoore muyo ebhyakori bheene bhinsi ne ebhinto bheene ebhende.
Neho kwibhoorra momotema ghoone mbughee, “Bhoono nitooriire ebhinto ebheeru ebhichomu, bhino bhekonyisa ko emeeka emeeru! Bhoono, niikare muunye, neri no okonyo, nchomeru!”’
“Ghasi bhoono, Ghiteema akamubhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Omukangi ono! Obhotiko bhuno bho reero ngoku wooni! Bhoono ebhinto bhino wibhechiiri mbe-wuuye bhekubha?’”
Yeesu, akamarerri gho kubhughaa, “N-ke hayo eghuucha kubha ko omonto ono akwibhecheri ebhinto, ghasi bhoono aranga kwibhecheri haare Ghiteema.”
Neho Yeesu akabhoorra abheegha bhaache akabhughaa, “Ko kiyo, ndabhabhoorra aghoo, motighe kwihahera no okwibhoori aghoo ‘Hai tokubhona ebhyakori na n-ke toghoswara.’
Gho okubha obhuhoru mbukerre ebhyakori, no omobhere ngukerre chingebho!
“Morigheeri ku amakoorukooru. Ghataakwemi, ghataakughesa, ghataana ebhitara, hande ahase ho kubhecheri ebhyakori, ghasi bhoono Ghiteema araghaha ebhyakori. Ghasi bhoono inyu mughoote obhwera ghukera ebhinyonyi bhiyo!
Ne-wuuye haare inyu ono ehaho yaache ekomutoori kwiyengerri kuru ensa emwe mobhuhoru bhooche?
Gho okubha ghote mutakunaghi ghukora engʼana ensuuhu ke eyo, n-ngoke mokubha ne ehaho ku ghande?
“Morigheeri ebhibharyo, ghote bhekumera, bhitaghukora emeremo hande bhitaaghwisonera chingebho. Ghasi bhoono ndabhabhoorra ndabhughaa, kuru omukama Suremani mobhokoro no obhwame bhooche, taghasware bhwaheene kye ekemwe kye ebhibharyo bhiyo!
Iraabha Ghiteema araswari amanyanki gha mwiteregho, ghano reero ghaaho na icho gharatabhutu momorro, bhwe aghutamu kubhaswari inyu bho obhwitabherri obhosuuhu?
“Ghasi bhoono, inyu motighe kwinyanki ghwitegherra kubha nke mokori. Hande nke mokonyo. Motighe kooreka na ghayo!
Abhanto bhano bhatamanyire Ghiteema nebhu bhakunyankera ebhinto bhiyo. Ghasi bhoono inyu, Taata waanyu wa mwisaaro namanyire bhwaheene kubha, nkobhetuna mooni.
Ko riyo, motune singata Obhukama bho Ghiteema, na aghande ghayo murengereribhu.
“Mutakoobhoha inyu eghekomo eghesuuhu, gho okubha Taata waanyu wa mwisaaro nasaighire abhahe obhukama bhooche.
Mughori ebhinto bheenyu, mubhahe abhatobhu chembiri che ebhinto bhiyo. Muraakore kee hayo murabha mwitoorire ekeghuku mwisaaro kino ghitaghosira ahase hano ghitakuhobhoka. Mwisaaro eyo abhaibhi bhatareho, hande omoso ghutaghusari.
Gho okubha ahase hano ebheghuku bheenyu bheeni, neho ne emetema gheenyu ghekubha.
“Mwiseemi chinkaagha chinsi, ne chitara chaanyu chibhe chirooka.
Mubhe kya abhabhaghasi, bhano bhakughanya omutemi waabho agharoke koru monyangi yo obhuteti, korri hano aghuucha abherekere, bhangohe komwighorra.
Bhaghoote echaghati abhabhaghasi bhano omutemi waabho akohika abhone bharamughanya. Ndabhabhoorra obhuheene aghoo, ninga aiseemi kubhabhaghasi, abhaghaghaani ebhyakori.
Bhaghoote echaghati abhabhaghasi bhano omutemi waabho akugharoka kuru obhotiko bho ghati, hande etabhoori chiri, abhone bharamughanya.
“Ghasi bhoono mumanye bhwaheene rino. Ghote omwene enyumba akamanyire enkaagha eno omwibhi aghuucha, ngutengecha aare kurenda korri omwibhi ataghaacha komuhanyorra enyumba yaache.
Ko riyo, na inyu mwibhange, gho okubha eni Omoona wo Omonto ndaacha gho enkaagha eno mutaghwitegherra kubha neyu nguucha.”
Neho Peetero akabhoori Yeesu akabhughaa, “Omutemi, ekihekaani kiyo ni-itu abheene uhekaaniiri ghasi na-abhanto bhansi?”
Omutemi Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Ne-wuuye omwimererri omuheene na ono aghoote obhungʼaini? Newe ono omutemi waache amutoorre aimererre bhaghendi bhaache, korri abhe arabhaha ebhyakori gho enkaagha yaache.
Aghoote echaghati omubhaghasi ono omutemi waache akugharoka koru morughendo, amubhone arakora kee bhoore amwerekeriri.
Obhuheene ndabhabhoorra aghoo, aramutoora abhe omwimererri we ebhinto bheeche bhinsi!
“Ghasi bhoono omubhaghasi oyo akughamba momotema ghooche abhughee, ‘Omutemi waane aghechiire kugharoka.’ Neho aghasimi ghutema abhabhaghasi bhaghendi bhaache, abhasubhe ku abhaghaikoro, aikarre kuraaghera, konyo amaro, no kureewa.
Bhoono, omutemi waache oyo aragharoka orosiko ne enkaagha eno omubhaghasi oyo atareghwitegherra. Ko riyo omutemi waache aramutema enchagho enkoro, kumaruho amutoore hamwe na abhanto bhano bhataghwitabherri Ghiteema.
“Omubhaghasi ono amanyire ghote omutemi waache aghotuna, ghasi bhoono taghukora, hande taghuseemi komoturungʼana, omubhaghasi oyo aratemu bhukongʼu.
Ghasi bhoono, omubhaghasi ono atamanyire ghano omutemi waache aghotuna, hano aghukora engʼana eno eghotunu atemu enchagho, oyo hasuuhu aghutemu. Omonto ono ahaabhiru ebhinto ebheeru, ne-ebheeru aghusabhu. Na ono ahaabhiru ebhinto ebheeru bhukongʼu ne-ebheeru bhukongʼu aghusabhu.
“Eni niichire korri ngooti omorro monse hano. Nkwighombu neeni ndore omorro ghurooka.
Kuru eni omwene, ningoote obhubhaatiiso bhwe enyanko eno nkuheteramu. Na ndaghenderri kunyanka momotema ghoone, kohikera hano ghaghukoru.
Muraitegherra ighoo, niichire kureeta omurembe monse? Ndabhabhoorra ighoo hasehe! Ndabhabhoorra niichire koohokani abhanto.
Koru bhoono, monyumba ya abhanto bhataano, bhatato bharoohokana na bhabhere. Bhabhere nabhu, bharoohokana na bhatato bhayo.
Omomura aroohokana na isawaabho, na isawaabho aroohokana na omomura waache. Omonke aroohokana na nyakowaabho, na nyakowaabho aroohokana na omonke waache. Omukwe aroohokana nyakobhyera yaache, na nyakobhyera aroohokana no omukwe waache.”
Yeesu akabhoorra abhanto abhaaru bhano bhaare hayo akabhughaa, “Hano mokurora amasaaro ghararwera orubhareka ro nyancha, murabhugha aghoo, ‘Embura haghuhe yeeni iteeke,’ obhuheene irateeka.
Na hano mokurora obhukama bhurahuuta koru orubhareka ro bhachuuta, murabhugha aghoo, ‘Reero oroowa rurabhamu,’ na niigho ekubha.
Inyu m-baitaami mooni! Mbwe mokumanya koongora ense ne risaaro, ghasi bhoono mutaghutora kumanya amangʼana ghano ghaghwikora reero eno?
“Ake inyu abheene mutakwamora ko bhuheene?
Enkaagha eno omuchongi waacho aghokohira komorwechi, wikongʼi kwighwerana nawe mukere mooni ghonchera. Urabhone toghukora kee hayo, arakohiki ko omorwechi, no omorwechi wunsi arakohira kubhasirikare, korri bhakubhohe mo kibhohe.
Ndakubhoora obhuheene ndabhughaa, tokorichoka koru gho kibhohe kohikera hano okureha esiire yinsi.”
Enkaagha eyo eyo, abhanto bhaghaacha bhakabhoorra Yeesu bhakabhughaa, “Omubhaahi Bhiraato naaitire Abhaghariraaya abhande, amaanyinga ghaabho akaghaichoghani na amaanyinga ghe ebhemwenso bheebho bhino bhaare koruseri Ghiteema.”
Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Kana, muraitegherra kubha, Abhaghariraaya bhayo bhaakuure oroku ruyo, gho okubha mbaghoote ebhibhe ebheeru ghukera Abhaghariraaya abhande bhansi?
Ndabhabhoorra, obhuheene, tare ighoo! Ghasi bhoono, hano mutatiitire ebhibhe bheenyu, na inyu bhansi kee hayo hayo moghosika!
Ghasi bhoono, nkohiita mooni abhanto ikomi na bhanaane bhaare, bhano bhaghweriiru no omunara eyo Sirowamu, na ghukabhaita. Kana, muraitegherra kubha ebhu mbaghoote ebhibhe ebheeru ghukera abhamenyi abhande bhansi bha Yerusareemu?
Ndabhabhoorra tare ighoo! Ghasi bhoono hano mutatiitire ebhibhe bheenyu, inyu bhansi, murasika kee hayo hayo!”
Kumaruho, Yeesu akabhabhoorra abhanto bhayo ekihekaani kende akabhughaa, “Aareho omonto omwe ono eemiri omote gho omotiini komoghondo ghooche. Hano aghiire ghotuna emehumo komote ghuyo, taaghebhwine.
Akabhoorra omukori waache we emeremo ghyo omoghondo ghuyo akabhughaa, ‘Righeeri! Gho nkaagha ye emeeka etato, ndaacha ghotuna emehumo ko omote gho omotiini ghuno, ghasi bhoono tenkubhona ghento! Oghukenge, ghotighe ghunsaari ahase hano bhuchu!’
Ghasi bhoono, omukori we emeremo ghyo omoghondo oyo, akamugharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Omutemi, oghotighe, omoka ghuno nguremerre no okoghutoorra oruse.
Hano ghokwaama emehumo omooka ghuno mbwaheene! Na hano ghutaamire, oghugheeche.’”
Orosiko romwe rwe Esabhaato, Yeesu aare monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, areeghi abhanto.
Monyumba muyo, aaremu omughaikoro omwe, ono aare aghootiru no omusambu gho obhorwire emeeka ikomi na enaane. Omusambu neghu ghyamokumbire omughongo, na taare kunaghi kwimerra bhoronge.
Hano Yeesu aamorooche, akamubherekera. Akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Yaaya, uhorre obhorwire bhoocho bhoono oruure mokibhohe!”
Yeesu akamutoorra amabhoko, na hari remwe, akaimerra bhoronge, aghasimi ghwitumi Ghiteema.
Omokoro we nyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, aghakarra gho okubha, Yeesu aahorri omonto oyo orosiko rwe Esabhaato. Akabhoorra abhanto akabhughaa, “Mowiiki engima, chensiko cho ghukora emeremo cheeni isansabha. Bhoono mbe, mubhe muraacha muhoribhu gho chensiko chiyo, ghasi bhoono tare morosiko rwe Esabhaato!”
Ghasi Omutemi Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Inyu, na abhaitaami mooni! Ne-wuuye ghati yaanyu ono ataghushokorra chingʼombe chaache hande chentikere koru bhoori, korri achehire konyiisi orosiko rwe Esabhaato?
Bhoono mbe omughaikoro ono, wo orwibhoro ro Ibhurahimu, amarre emeeka ikomi ne enaane abhohiru ne Risambu. Bhoono, wunsi taghotunu ghutachoru koru mokibhohe kiyo, orosiko rwe Esabhaato?”
Hano Yeesu aghambire ghayo, bhano bhansi bhaghoote chinkaani nawe, bhaghasooka. Ghasi bhoono abhande bhansi, bhaghachomeru bhukongʼu kumangʼana amachomu gha amakono ghano Yeesu aare ghukora.
Neho Yeesu aabhoorri akabhughaa, “Obhukama bho Ghiteema, n-ke bhuheekaine nakyu? Mbuhekaani na ke?
Mbuhekaine na aghatetere ko omuharataari, kano omonto agheghire akeemi komoghondo ghooche. Aghatetere ghakamera, ghakabha omote omokoro, ebhinyonyi bhighaacha bhikaabheka chintara chaabho kobhisaghare bhyo omote ghuyo.”
Yeesu akabhabhoori ghwiki rekabhere akabhughaa, “Obhukama bho Ghiteema mbuhekaani na ke?
Mbuhekaine ne ehamiira eno omughaikoro agheghire, akayichooghani na ebhirengero bhitato bhyo obhosi bhwe engano, obhosi bhuyo bhunsi, bhukabhuusa.”
Hano Yeesu aare morughendo koghi Yerusareemu, aare kweeghi abhanto bhe emeghi ne ebhechichi bhino aare kuhetera.
Orosiko romwe, omonto omwe akabhoori Yeesu akabhughaa, “Omutemi, abhanto bhano bhaghutooribhu, m-bhasuuhu bhakubha?” Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa,
“Mwikongʼi kuheta mogheseku ekenyintu, gho okubha ndabhabhoorra aghoo, n-abhaaru bharatuna ghusoha, ghasi bhoono bharatamu.
Enkaagha eno omwene nyumba akwighara egheseku, inyu muraimerra kibhara, murabherekera no ghusaasaama, murabhughaa, ‘Omutemi, utatwighoorra!’ Ghasi bhoono arabhagharokeri abhughee, ‘Timbamanyire he! Kuru timanyire hayi mokorwera!’
“Na inyu muramubhoorra, murabhughaa, ‘Itu m-baare twaraaghiire no okonyo hamwe na iye! Na iye waare kweeghi abhanto kobhechichi bhiitu!’
Ghasi bhoono ewe arabhagharokeri, arabhughaa, ‘Timbamanyire he! Kuru timanyire hayi mokorwera. Muntandwera hano, inyu abhakori bhe ebhibhe!’
“Hayo murakuura no okuromani amaino, gho okubha, murarora Ibhurahimu, Isaaka, na Yaakobho, na abharooti bhansi, bhaani mo Obhukama bho Ghiteema, ghasi inyu, murabha mutabhotiru kibhara!
Abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahudi bharaacha koru chimbareka cha roghoro na nyancha, ghoosi na bhachuuta, bhaikare kuraaghera ebhyakori ko Obhukama bho Ghiteema.
“Mbe muntegheerre mbabhoorre! Abhanto bhano bhataana obhwera, bharabha no obhwera, na bho obhwera, bharabhori obhwera.”
Enkaagha eyo eyo, Amabharisaayo abhande bhakaghi haare Yeesu bhakamubhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Nooru hano, ughende ahase ahande, gho okubha omubhaahi Herode aratuna koghwiita.”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Mughende, mubhoorre omucharachambani oyo mobhughee, ‘Reero na icho, ndatyambi emisambu koru kubhanto no okuhori abharwire. Orosiko ro ghatato, ndamarerri emeremo gheene.’
Ghwiki, ninga ngenderri no orughendo roone ro okoghi Yerusareemu, reero icho na bhaseere, gho okubha, iratunu omurooti akweere Yerusareemu.”
Mbe Yeesu akaghamba akabhughaa, “Inyu abhanto bha Yerusareemu, bhano moghwita abharooti no okubhatema na amaghena, abhanto bhano Ghiteema atomire haare inyu. Hari kaaru nikongʼirri kubhakomani kee haare engoko eghukomani ebhechuuchu bheeche mumabhabha ghaache, ghasi mwangire.
Righeeri, Ghiteema aatigha haare inyu mubhe ritongo! Eni ndabhabhoorra ndabhughaa, ronde mutakundora ghwiki, kuru kohikera enkaagha eno mokughamba mobhughee, ‘Anooku ono aghuucha ko eriina ryo Omutemi Ghiteema.’”
Orosiko romwe rwe Esabhaato, Yeesu akaghi kuraaghera ebhyakori monyumba yo omwe wa abhabhaahi bha Amabharisaayo. Hano aare muyo, Amabharisaayo na abhanto abhande bhakabha bharamuroherra bhukongʼu.
Yeesu aare korigherrani no omonto omwe, ono aghoote obhorwire bho kobhimba omobhere.
Yeesu akabhabhoori Amabharisaayo na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa akabhughaa, “Amaragherri gha Musa ghwitabherri ghaani kuhori abhanto orosiko rwe Esabhaato, ghasi nkwanga ghaani?”
Ghasi bhoono, bhansi bhaghakira kiri, bhataamomurri. Yeesu aghaturi omorwire oyo, akamuhori. Akamubhoorra aghende echaache.
Yeesu akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Ne-wuuye haare inyu, ono engʼombe yaache hande entikere yaache ekogho moghesima orosiko rwe Esabhaato, atighe koyeruusi mu?”
Abhanto bhayo, bhataabhwine engʼana yo komugharokeri.
Hano Yeesu arooche abhagheni bhano bhareghainibhu konyangi eyo, ghote bhaare ghwichangorra ebhetumbe bhe mbere, akabharengeri ekihekaani kino akabhughaa,
“Hano ureghainibhu monyangi yo obhuteti, otighe ghwikangati ghwikara ahase ha abhagheni abhakoro, gho okubha itaghachakubha nareghainibhu omugheni omokoro ono aghoghukera iye.
Hano aghuucha ono abhareghaini inyu bhansi bhabhere, akubhoore abhughee, ‘Iheeneri ono koghetumbe aikare,’ hayo, neho okoruho usookire bhukongʼu, gho okubha urahonchoka ghwikara nyuma.
Ghasi bhoono, hano bhakureghaini monyangi, ughende wikare kobhetumbe bhe nyuma. Hayo neho aghuucha ono akureghaini, akubhoorre ighoo, ‘Musaani waane, wuuche mbere hano! Neho ahachomu bhukongʼu.’ Hayo neho okubha uhaabhiru chinsoni mbere ya abhagheni bhansi,
gho okubha, omonto wunsiwunsi ono aghwitiiri, Ghiteema aramusekeri harense. Ghasi bhoono omonto wunsiwunsi ono aghwisekeri harense, Ghiteema aramotiiri ighoro.”
Neho, Yeesu akabhoorra omonto oyo aare amureghaini konyangi hayo akabhughaa, “Hano oghuseemi enyangi ye ebhyakori bhyo omwise hande bhyo obhotiko, utakareghani bhasaani bhaacho, bhamura bhaanyu, hande abhamenyani bhaacho abhaame. Hano uraakore kee hayo, kuru nabhu hano bhaghukora enyangi bharakureghani waabho ka. N-kee hayo uraabhone bharehaini.
Ghasi bhoono, hano oghuseemi enyangi, ureghani abhatobhu, abhabheeru, na abhahukuru.
Neho ughoote echaghati, gho okubha bhayo bhataghoote amanagha gho kureha. Ghasi bhoono, Ghiteema arakureha enkaagha eno akoryokora abhanto abhaheene.”
Hano omugheni omwe ono aare aikaire hamwe na Yeesu komeeza, oghuure amangʼana ghayo akabhughaa, “Aghoote echaghati omonto ono akori enyangi haare Obhukama bho Ghiteema!”
Yeesu akamurengeri ekihekaani akabhughaa, “Aareho omonto omwe, ono aaseemiri enyangi enkoro, akareghani abhanto abhaaru.
Hano enyangi yaahikire, aghatoma omubhaghasi waache, kubhanto bhansi bhano areghaini, abhabhoorre abhughee, ‘Enyangi ibhaire muuche!’
“Ghasi bhoono, bhansi bhano aare areghaini, omwe omwe bhakabha bharamusabha abhaabhere. Wa ghwansa akabhughaa, ‘Ningorre omoghondo, ndatuna ngende ngurabhe. Ndaghusabha onyaabhere.’
Owonde akabhughaa, ‘Ningoore chingʼombe ikomi cho kuremera, ndatuna ngende ghochisaki. Ndaghusabha onyaabhere.’
No owonde akabhughaa, ‘Mbongo hano ntetire, ko riyo tengucha.’
“Hano omubhaghasi oyo agharokire ko omwene enyangi, akamubhoorra ghansi ghano abhooriiru na bhano aghiire kureghani. Neho omokoro oyo wo omoghi ghuyo ghwaghote enyangi aghakarra, aghatoma omubhaghasi waache akabhughaa, ‘Nooghi bhongo bhongo gho chinchera chinkoro na ko ehichera ehesuuhusuuhu bhyo momoghi ghuno, ureete hano abhatobhu, abhabheeru, na abhahukuru.’
“Hano omubhaghasi oyo aagharokire, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Omutemi, ghano waare untomire ghamarekubha. Kuru ighoo, omweya ghukeere ghooho.’
“Omutemi akamubhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Nooghi gho chinchera chino chekoghi mobhechichi na momeghondo ubhahamerri bhaache, bhasohe monyumba yaane, korri yiichore.
Ghasi bhaare natangoriire kureghani atareho kuru omwe ono araasame enyangi yaane!’ ”
Enkaagha eno Yeesu aare kughenda ne eghekomo eghekoro kya abhanto, akaihonchora akabhughaa,
“Omonto wunsi wunsi ono aghotuna ghuntambana no kubha omwegha waane, iratunu anseeghe eni ghukera isawaabho, nyakowaabho, mughaache na abhaana bhaache, bhamura bhaabho na abhanke bhaabho, na kuru ghukera ewe omwene bhuno aiseghire.
Omonto wunsiwunsi ono ataghotuna kubhona enyanko yo ghuntambana, taghutora kubha omwegha waane.
“Muntegheerre mbaragherri bhwaheene. Tobhughe aghoo, omonto aghotuna kwabheka ekebhuru eghekoro kino ghekwabhekerru amaghena. Taghwikara singata aitegherre, korri arore ubhone naghoote ebhinto bhino bheghwisa kwabhekera?
Hano atakorre kee hayo, aratora ghotuka obhurosa, kumara atamu kughenderri koghwabheka. Abhaheti bha mochinchera nangabhabhe bharamuserra,
bharaghamba bharabhughaa, ‘Righeeri omonto ono! Aghasimi kwabheeka, ghasi bhoono kumarerri komutamire!’
“Ghwiki ghote omukama aghotuna ghwitana riihe no omukama owonde, bhwe aghukora? Obhuheene singata araitegherra, kubha aranaghi ghwitana no omukama ono aghoote abhasirikare ebhikwe mirongo ebhere (20,000), na hano ewe aghoote abhasirikare ebhikwe ikomi (10,000) abheene.
Hano araarore ataghutora ghwitana riihe riyo, aratoma abhabhaghasi bhaache, bhaghende bhamubhoorre akeere aani kure, bhaitabherrani, bhakore amangʼana ghayo ko omurembe.
“Kee hayo hayo na inyu, ono ataghotigha bhinsi bhino aghoote, taghutora kubha omwegha waane.
“Echumbe n-eghento eghichomu kino keghusambaaroki. Ghasi bhoono hano echumbe ekubhori obhusambaaroku, nke eghutoru korri isambaaroke?
Echumbe ke eyo tighoote obhwera kobhutoto, hande oruse. Abhanto bharaitabhuta. Ono aghoote amatwe gho okooghu, na ooghu!”
Orosiko romwe abhaghooti bhe righooti na abhanto abhande bhano bhaghoote ebhibhe, bhaare komwisokerra Yeesu, korri bhamutegherre.
Neho Amabharisaayo na abheeghi bha amaragherri, bhaibhereriri haare Yeesu, bhakabhughaa, “Omonto ono, aka ndora araghaghaani bhano bhaghoote ebhibhe! Ghwiki arasanga nabhu ebhyakori!”
Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani akabhughaa,
“Ne-wuuye haare inyu ono aghoote amangʼondi righana, hano remwe reghosira, mbwe aghukora? Ataaghotigha mirongo kenda na kenda keriisho, no koghi ghotuna rino resiire, kohikera hano akoribhona?
Na hano akoribhona, ararighegha kumabhegha ku amachomeru.
Na hano akohika ka, arabhabherekera abhasaani bhaache, na abhamenyani bhaache, no kubhabhoorra abhughee, ‘Tuchomeru hamwe, gho okubha nebhwine engʼondi yaane, eno yasirre!’
“Ndabhabhoorra ighoo, kee hayo hayo, harabha na amachomeru amaaru mwisaaro, enkaagha eno we bhibhe omwe atiitire ebhibhe bheeche. Amachomeru ghayo gharabha amakoro ghukera abhanto abhaheene mirongo kenda na kenda bhano bhatatoniribhu ghotiita ebhibhe bheebho.”
Ghwiki Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani ekende! Akabhughaa, “omughaikoro omwe ono aghoote chembiri ikomi, na emwe esire, mbwe aghukora? Tere arooki etara, no oghutareki monyumba yinsi, arayetuna ko ghwikongʼi kohika hano akoibhona?
Na hano akoibhona, arabhabherekera abhasaani bhaache na abhamenyani bhaache, no kubhabhoorra, ‘Tuchomeru hamwe, gho okubha neyebhwine embiri eno yasirre!’
“Ndabhabhoorra ighoo, n-ke hayo hayoabhamaraika bha Ghiteema bhaghuchomeru mbere ya Ghiteema, hano we ebhibhe omwe atiitire ebhibhe bheeche.”
Yeesu akaghenderri kobhabhoorra ekihekaini kende akabhughaa, “Aareho omonto omwe, ono aare na abhamura bhabhere.
Omomura omosuuhu, akabhoorra isawaabho akabhughaa, ‘Taata, ntweeni eghabho yaane!’ Neho, isawaabho oyo akabhatweni ebhinto bheeche.
“Hano chaahetire chensiko chensuuhu, omomura omosuuhu aghakomani ebhinto bheeche bhinsi, akaghi ekyaro ghe kure. Hano aahikire gho ekyaro kiyo, aghasimi ghusarisari ebhinto bheeche ghokobheri no kobhisarisari.
Hano aamarre ebhinto bheeche bhinsi, egheecha endoro ikabha gho ekyaro keere aare ghwikara, akabha ne etaabhu.
Neho hayo, aghiire ko omonto omwe we ekyaro kiyo, akamusabha abhe omubhaghasi waache. Omonto oyo, akamwitabherri no okomohira moghondo koriisi chimbeeche chaache.
Omomura oyo akabha araighombu okori amakanda ghe chimbeeche ghano chaare kori! Ghasi bhoono taareho omonto wo komuha ebhyakori.
“Kumaruho, obhungʼaini bhukamwichera, aghaitegherra momotwe akabhughaa, ‘Abhabhaghasi bha taata, bhaghoote ebhyakori ebheeru, bhararaaghera kuru bhirasaagha! Ghasi bhoono eni hano, ndaku no omuramboko.
Bhoono ndagharoka o taata, no okomubhoorra, “Taata, ninkoriire Ghiteema ebhibhe, na ghwiki nengusariiri na iye.
Tiniisire kubherekeru omoona waacho. Bhoono, unkore kyo omwe wa abhabhaghasi bhaacho.” ’
“Neho asimiri orughendo ro kuhonchoka o isawaabho. Na hano aare akeere kure ye enyumba ya waabho, isawaabho aakamurora, akamwabhera. Akaryera koghi haare momura waache, akamughoterra no okomobhusu.
Omomura oyo, akabhoorra isawaabho akabhughaa, ‘Taata, ninkoriire Ghiteema ebhibhe, na nengusariiri na iye. Tiniisire ghwiki kubherekeru omoona waacho.’
“Ghasi bhoono, isawaabho akabhoorra abhabhaghasi bhaache, ‘Momureetere Bongobhongo chingebho chinchomu momuswari. Momuswari ne ebhete gho ekeera gheeche, na momuswari ebhiraato.
Mureete rikoohe rinoru, morighooghe! Turaaghere na tuchomeru hamwe,
gho okubha, omoona waane aare ghote akuure ghasi bhoono ahyokire. Aare asirre, ghasi bhoono atookire!’ Neho bhayo bhansi bhaasimiri ghuchomeru hamwe.
“Enkaagha eyo, mura waache omokoro aare moghondo. Hano aare kugharora ka, na hano ahikire haghuhe na waabho, akooghu abhanto bharaririyeta no okobhina waabho hayo.
Akabherekera omubhaghasi omwe, akamubhoori ighoo, ‘N-ke keeho?’
Omubhaghasi oyo akamugharokeri akabhugha, ‘Omosuuhu waacho naichire, na isawaanyu namughoghiire rikoohe rinoru reere, gho okubha namobhwiine omoona waache ghwiki, aani bhwaheene na omuhoru.’
Neho omomurra wa ghwansa oyo akaraire bhukongʼu, akaanga ghusoha monyumba. Neho isawaabho arichokire kibhara, akabha aramusaasaama asohe.
“Ghasi bhoono, mura waache oyo akamugharokeri, ‘N-emeeka emeeru ngukoriire emeremo! Ntakangire kughoota amaragherri ghaacho kuru hasuuhu! Ghasi bhoono, utakahaire kuru akaghorohe, korri nkore enyangi hamwe na bhasaani bhaane.
Ghasi bhoono omoona waacho ono, asanchiri ebhinto bheecho na abhasimbe, ewe aichire omughoghiire rikoohe rinoru!’
“Isawaabho akamubhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Omoona waane, iye wooni hamwe na eni chensiko chinsi, ne ebhinto bhinsi bhino ngoote n-ebheecho.
Ghasi bhoono omosuuhu waacho, nkubhayeni tomukore enyangi no ghuchomeru hamwe. Gho okubhaaare ghote akuure, ghasi bhoono ahyokire. Aare asirre, ghasi bhoono atokirre!’ ”
Yeesu akarengeri abheegha bhaache ekihekaani akabhughaa, “Aareho omwame omwe, ono aare aghote omwimererri we ebhinto bheeche. Omwimererri oyo, aghachongeru ko omwame waache, kubha arasarisari ebhinto bhyo omwame waache.
Ko riyo, omwame oyo, akabherekera omwimererri oyo, akamubhoori akabhughaa, ‘M-mangʼana ke, ghano nkooghu bharakughamba? Ndetera hano amangʼana gho obhwimererri bhoocho, gho okubha tokughenderri kubha omwimererri we ebhinto bheene!’
“Omwimererri oyo akaibhoori, ‘Omwame waane araantyambi emeremo. Bhoono nkore bhwe? Chenguru cho okurema tingoote, no oghusabhasabha ngusooka neeni.
Bhoono manyire mbwe ngukora, korri hano nkuheebhu emeremo, abhanto bhankarabhisi momeghi gheebho.’
“Omwimererri oyo akabherekera abhasiire bhansi bho omwame waache, omwe omwe. Akamubhoori wa ghwansa, ‘Esiire yaacho ko omokoro waane n-irenge?’
Akamugharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Esiire yaane, n-amabhiibha righana gha amaghuta ghe emiseituuni.’ Omwimererri akamubhoorra akabhugha, ‘Ghegha ekarataasi eno ye esiire yaacho, Ikara hano, uhonchore nguru, wandeke mirongo etaano.’
Kumaruho akabhoori omosiire wonde akabhughaa, ‘Na iye, esiire yaacho n-irenge?’ Akamugharokeri, ‘Amaghonera righana ghe engano.’ Omwimererri akamubhoorra akabhugha, ‘Ghegha ekarataasi eno ye esiire yaacho, wandeke mirongo enaane.’
“Hano omwame waache oghuure amangʼana ghayo, akamokumi omwimererri oyo atare omuheene ko obhungʼaini bhooche bhuno akorre. Gho kubha, abhanto bha mo ense eno, mbaghoote obhungʼaini, enkaagha eno bhaghusakerani abheene ku bheene, ku amangʼana gha monse muno, ghukera abhanto bha Ghiteema.
Naane ndabhabhoorra mwikorre obhusaani ko ebhinto bhino mughoote monse muno, korri enkaagha eno moghuserru, mughaghanibhu mo obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi.
“Omonto omuheene ku amangʼana amasuuhu, no-omuheene kuru ku amangʼana amakoro. Kee hayo hayo, omonto ono atare omuheene ku amangʼana amasuuhu, taakubha omuheene kuru ku amangʼana amakoro.
Uraabhone mutaabhaire abhanto abhaheene ko ebhinto bhe monse muno, ne-wuuye akubhaha ebhinto bhyo obhuheene bhe mwisaaro!
Uraabhone mutaabhaire abhaheene gho okwimererra ebhinto bhya abhande, ne-wuuye akubhaha ebhinto bheenyu abheene!
“Tareho omubhaghasi ono aghutora ghukorra emeremo abhatemi bhabhere. Hano aghukora kee hayo, araregha omwe, arasaigha owonde. Hande araghootane no omwe, kumaruho arasere owonde. Kee hayo hayo na inyu mutoghutora ghukorra emeremo obhotuni bhwe ebhinto hamwe no ghukorra Ghiteema emeremo!”
Enkaagha eno Amabharisaayo, bhooghuure amangʼana gha Yeesu ghayo, bhakamusera, gho okubha mbasaighire bhukongʼu chembiri.
Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Inyu, muraikori kubha mughoote obhoronge mbere ya abhanto. Ghasi bhoono, Ghiteema namanyire amangʼana ghano ghaani mometema gheenyu. Gho kubha, amangʼana ghano abhanto bhakurora na-amachomu bhukongʼu haare ebhu, ghayo neghu amanyenyeeri haare Ghiteema!”
“Amaragherri gha Musa, na amaandeko gha abharooti, bhyakangatire abhanto kohika enkaagha ya Yohana Omubhaatiisi. Ghokoru enkaagha eyo, Amangʼana Amachomu gho Obhukama bho Ghiteema gharareghanibhu, na abhanto bhansi bharasighinyeribhu kubha bhasohe muyo.
Ghasi bhoono, n-oghutobhu risaaro ne ense koruho, ghukera akangʼoore akasuuhu ka Amaragherri gha Musa ghusangoribhu.
“Omosubhe, ono aaghotyambi mughaache kumaruho ateta owonde, oyo n-obhotwari aghukora. No omosubhe ono aghuteta omughaikoro ono aheebhiru na mosubhe waache, oyo wunsi n-obhotwari aghukora.”
Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani akabhughaa, “Aareho omwame omwe, ono aare kuraaghera bhwaheene chensiko chinsi. Aare ghuswaara chingebho chinchomu che erangi ya sambarau, chino chaare che gharama.
Mokehita kyo omwame oyo, aareho omutobhu omwe, ono aare kubherekeru Rasaaro. Rasaaro oyo, aare aghoote ebhetonda omobhere omoghima,
kuru chiseese, chaare ghuucha kumensa ebhetonda bheeche. Rasaaro nkwighombu aare kuru kori amasaaghi ghe ebhyakori ghano ghaare ghutoonya koru ko emeesa yo omwame oyo, gho okubha naarambokire.
“Kumaruho, omutobhu oyo Rasaaro aghaku. Maraika bhakamohira mwisaaro, haghuhe na Ibhurahimu. Omwame oyo wunsi aghaku, akaryeku.
Omwame oyo, akabha aranyanka bhukongʼu Nyaari. Hano akugharamera ighoro, akarora Ibhurahimu kure, na Rasaaro aani haghuhe nawe.
Akabherekera ko riiraka rikoro, ‘Taata Ibhurahimu, tanyaabhera! Ndanyanka bhukongʼu momorro muno! Utatoma Rasaaro aache, achabhi kuru ensonge ye ekeera gheeche mumanche, aghatoonyi ko ororeme roone korri romitite.’
“Ghasi bhoono, Ibhurahimu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Omoona waane, ohiite kubha waabhwine amangʼana amachomu ko obhuhoru bhoocho, na Rasaaro, naabhwine amasineenu. Ghasi bhoono, ewe hano aani araghambisanibhu, na iye uranyanka.
Hamwe na ghayo, haare itu eno na inyu eyo, Ghiteema atoorre rirooma rikoro, korri omonto ataghaatamboka ghuucha haare inyu, hande koru haare inyu ghuucha haare itu.’
“Omwame oyo akabhoorra Ibhurahimu akabhugha, ‘Mbe taata, ndaghusabha utome Rasaaro aghende ka o taata, korri aseghani bhamura bhaito bhataano, bhataghaacha ghuucha ahase hano he enyanko endoro.’

Ghasi bhoono, Ibhurahimu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Abhaana bhaanyu, mbaghoote amaandeko ghano ghaandekiru na Musa na abharooti. Bhategherre ghayo!’
“Omwame oyo akamugharokeri, ‘Hasehe, taata Ibhurahimu! Ghasi bhoono, omonto arabhe aruure eno ku abhaku abhahekeere, hayo mbaraatiite ebhibhe bheebho.’
“Ibhurahimu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Uraabhone abhaana bhaanyu bhayo, bhatakooghu ghano ghaandekiru na Musa na abharooti, kuru omonto araryoke koru kubhaku bhatakooghu he.’”
Yeesu akabhoorra abheegha bhaache akabhughaa, “Amacharibhu ghano ghakugheri abhanto bhakore ebhibhe, gharabhaho enkaagha yinsi. Ghasi bhoono, haaho yaache omosemori wa amacharibhu ghayo!
Yaare kubha bhwaheene omonto oyo abhoheru oroghena mwighoti reeche, kumaruho arekeru monyancha, ghasi bhoono atakaagheri omwe waabho wo obhwitabherri obhosuuhu akore ebhibhe!
Ko riyo, mwiyangarre mutaghaacha ghukora kee hayo! “Hano mughendi waacho akoghusarri, omuseghani, uraabhone amasire obhusari bhooche, omwabhere.
Kuru uraabhone araghusarri hari mohungate ko orosiko romwe, ne enkaagha yinsi aragharoka waacho araghusabha, ‘omwabhere,’ mwabhera!”
Neho abhatomu bha Yeesu bhaamubhooriire bhakabhughaa, “Omutemi, otwengererri obhwitabherri bhwitu!”
Akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Uraabhone mwakabhaire no obhwitabherri obhosuuhu ghote aghatetere ke eharataari, mwarekubhoorra omote ghuno gho omoko aghoo, ‘Iheka hano ughende wemibhu monyancha!’ Naghu ghwarekubhooghu.”
“Tobhughe omwe waanyu aghoote omubhaghasi ono akurema hande arariisi amangʼondi. Hano omubhaghasi oyo akugharoka ka, omutemi waache aramubhoorra abhughee, ‘Wuuche wikare hano uraaghere’?
Hasehe! Takomubhoorra kee hayo. Ghasi bhoono, aramubhoorra abhughee, ‘Nkoorra ebhyakori ndaaghere, ghwiki useemi kumbaghasi enkaagha eno kwenda kuraaghera no okonyo. Neho na iye uraaghere no okonyo.’
Bhoono, arakumi omubhaghasi oyo, gho okubha naakorre ghano atomiru ghukora? Hasehe!
“Kee hayo hayo na inyu, hano mokumara ghukora ghansi ghano mubhooriru na Ghiteema, mobhughe aghoo, ‘Itu n-abhabhaghasi n-ighoo tooni. Tukorre ghano toghotunu ghukora.’”
Enkaagha eyo Yeesu aare araghi Yerusareemu, akahetera mochimbagho cho omukowa gho Samaariya, na gho Ghariraaya.
Hano aasohire moghechichi kemwe, aghasikana na abhaghenge ikomi. Abhaghenge bhayo, bhaare bhaimeeriire kure na Yeesu.
Bhakaghamba ko riiraka rikoro bhakabhughaa, “Yeesu, Omutemi waito, otwabhere!”
Hano Yeesu abharooche, akabhabhoorra, “Mughende mwiyereki ku abhasengeri kubha muhorre.” Hano bhaare monchera bharaghi, bhakarabhibhu.
Omughenge omwe, hano aarooche kubha nahorre, hari remwe akahonchoka haare Yeesu, eno araitumi Ghiteema ko riiraka rikoro.
Hano aahikire haare Yeesu, akairekera kebhumari, kumaghoro gha Yeesu, akamokumi. No omonto oyo, aare Omusamaariya.
Yeesu akabhoori akabhughaa, “Bhatarabhibhu bhansi ikomi? Bhoono abhande kenda mooke bhaani?
Ebhu bhatagharokire ghwitumi Ghiteema! N-omugheni ono omwene newe agharokire?”
Yeesu akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Imerra, ughende echaacho, kino kigherri uhorre n-obhwitabherri bhoocho.”
Orosiko romwe, Amabharisaayo bhakabhoorri Yeesu bhakabhughaa, “Obhukama bho Ghiteema, bhuraacha ruuhe?” Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Oghuucha ko Obhukama bho Ghiteema, tare eghento ghyo kuroherra na amaiso.
Abhanto bhataghutora kobhugha aghoo, ‘Mutarigheeri! Mbobhuno hano!’ Hande, ‘Mutarigheeri! Mbobhoore haare bhamure!’ Mutegheerre mooghu, Obhukama bho Ghiteema morense yaanyu bhooni.”
Kumaruho, Yeesu akabhoorra abheegha bhaache akabhughaa, “Ghochensiko chino cheghuucha, murabha muraighombu kurora kuru orosiko romwe rwo Omoona wo Omonto ghasi bhoono mutaakorurora.
Abhanto barabha bharabhabhoorra bharabhughaa, ‘Mutarigheeri! Ngore haare!’ Hande ‘Mutarigheeri! Ngono hano!’ Ghasi bhoono abhanto bhayo, mutakaabharyererra.
Mbaabhooriire ghayo gho okubha, enkaagha eno nguucha eni Omoona wo Omonto, ndaacha kyo okubhari kwe enkobha, remwe ighoo irarabhi chimbareka chinsi cha mwisaaro.
Ghasi bhoono singata, ninga Omoona wo Omonto mbone enyanko eyaaru, ghwiki naangu na abhanto bho orwibhoro runo.
“Ke haare yaare gho chensiko cha Nuhu, nighoo ekubha gho enkaagha yo kugharoka ko Omoona wo Omonto.
Enkaagha ya Nuhu, abhanto na-amangʼana ghaabho ghabhatoniri. Bhaare kuraaghera no okonyo, bharateta no oghutetu, kohika orosiko roore hano Nuhu aasohire mosafina. Ehooro ighaacha ikabhasiki bhansi.
“Kuru gho enkaagha ya Ruutu amangʼana ghaare kee hayo hayo. Abhanto bhaare kuraaghera no okonyo, bharaghora no kughori, bhararema no kwemi, kuru bharaabheka.
Ghasi bhoono, orosiko runo Ruutu aaruure momoghi gho Sotoma, omorro omororo ghughasekera kye embura koru mwisaaro, ghukabhasiki bhansi.
“N-ke hayo ekubha ko orosiko ro kuhonyoru ko eni Omoona wo Omonto.
Orosiko ruyo, omonto ono aani ighoro ye rirongo rye enyumba yaache, ne ebhinto bheeche bheemu monyumba, ataghaseekera kobhighegha, ghasi bhoono kino arakore no-okoryera. No omonto ono aani moghondo, atakaagharoka ka kughegha ghinsighinsi, ghasi aryere.
Mohiite ghaare ghabhwine mukaa Ruutu!
Omonto wunsiwunsi ono aghotuna kurenda obhuhoru bhooche, newe akobhutabhuta. Na wunsiwunsi ono akobhutabhuta, newe akobhurenda.
“Ndabhabhoorra aghoo, obhotiko bho orosiko ruyo, abhanto bhabhere bharabha bhamisiri obhorre bhomwe. Omwe aragheghu na Ghiteema no owonde aratighu hayo.
Orosiko ruyo, abhaghaikoro bhabhere bharabha bharasi hamwe. Omwe aragheghu na Ghiteema no owonde aratighu” [
Abhanto bhabhere bharabha bharakora emeremo komoghondo, omwe aragheghu na Ghiteema no owonde aratighu hayo.]”
Abheegha bhaache bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Omutemi waio, ghayo mooke ghaghukorru?” Akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Ahase hano haghoote ebheghuusi, neho amatoonyi ghaghwikomani.”
Yeesu akarengeri abheegha bhaache ekihekaani kino, kubheereki kubha iratunu bhaghenderri ghusaasaama Ghiteema chensiko chinsi, bhataghaaku emetema.
Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Aareho omorwechi we ebhiina omwe, momoghi nyabhurebhe. Omorwechi oyo, ataare ghusooka Ghiteema, ghwiki tatoniribhu na omonto.
Momoghi ghuyo, aareho omosino omwe. Omosino oyo aare kugheera omorwechi oyo singerere komusaasaama aramubhoorra, ‘Ndasabha untoorri mbone obhoronge bhoone ko omobhisa waane.’
“Gho enkaagha entambe, omorwechi oyo naangire komutoorri omosino oyo. Ghasi bhoono enkaagha ikahika, akaighambera mometema ghooche akabhughaa, ‘Gho okubhakuru Ghiteema tenkomusooka, hande tintoniribhu na omonto,
ghasi bhoono, gho okubha omosino ono aranyanki nyanki bhukongʼu, bhoono ndamuha obhoronge bhooche, korri atakaannyora!’ ”
Kumaruho, Omutemi Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Mutegheerre ghote omorwechi omosineenu oyo aaghambire!
Ko riyo mumanye aghoo, Ghiteema arakorra bhwaheene abhoohoru bhaache, bhano bhakomusengera obhotiko no omwise! Takugheechera kubhatoorri.
Ndabhabhoorra aghoo, arabhaha obhoronge bhoobho bhongo. Ghasi bhoono, enkaagha eno eni Omoona wo Omonto nkugharoka monse, ndabhona abhanto bhakeere bhaghoote obhwitabherri?”
Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani kino, Abhanto bhano bhakwirora kubha, nebhu bhaani obhoronge mbere ya Ghiteema, na hano bharasera abhande. Akabhughaa,
“Bhaareho abhanto bhabhere, bhano bhaatirre koghi ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, ghusaasaama Ghiteema. Omwe aare Omubharisaayo, no owonde aare omughooti we righooti.
“Hano bhaahikire, Omubharisaayo oyo akaimerra, aghasaasaama momotema ghooche arabhughaa, ‘Ndaghokumi Ghiteema, gho okubha eni ntare omosineenu kya abhanto abhande, abhaibhi, abharongo, na abhatwari, hande kyo omughooti we righooti ono!
Eni ndaikubheri ebhyakori hari kabhere ko ewiiki, na ndaruusi ekirengero kemwe kye ebhirengero ikomi kye ebhinto bheene.’
“Ghasi bhoono omughooti we righooti oyo, ewe akaimerra kure, kuru tatunire korigheeri mwisaaro. Ghasi akabha araitematema koghekubha gheeche gho okubhaabhayera akabhughaa, ‘Ghiteema, onyaabhere, eni we ebhibhe!’ ”
Neho Yeesu engereriri akabhughaa, “Ndabhabhoorra aghoo, omughooti we righooti oyo, naagharokire ka, amarre kwaabheru na Ghiteema ebhibhe bheeche. Ghasi bhoono Omubharisaayo woore taabhiiru he! Omonto wunsiwunsi ono akwighegha, Ghiteema aramosuuhi. No omonto wunsiwunsi ono aghwisuuhi, Ghiteema aramughegheri.”
Mbe abhanto bhakareetera Yeesu ebhengʼwerre, korri abhitoorre amabhoko ghaache abhinooke. Enkaagha abheegha bhaache bhaarooche kee hayo, bhakahamera abhaibhori bhayo.
Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akabherekera abhaana bhayo, gho kubhoorra abheegha bhaache arabhughaa, “Motighe abhaana abhasuuhu bhaache haare eni. Kuru mutakabhahocherra, gho okubha, Obhukama bho Ghiteema, mbwa-abhanto kee bhano.
Ndabhabhoorra ghano ghaani maheene, omonto wunsiwunsi ono ataghwitabherri Obhukama bho Ghiteema kyo omoona omosuuhu, oyo taaghutora ghusoha.”
Aareho omubhaahi omwe, uno aabhoorri Yeesu akabhughaa, “Omweghi omuchomu, nke ndaakore, korri mbone obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi?”
Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Ake uramberekera omuchomu? Tareho omonto omuchomu, ghasi Ghiteema omwene!
Ndora numanyire bhwaheene amaragherri gha Ghiteema, ‘Utaghatwara, Utaghaita omonto, Utakaibha, Utakaimererra obhurongo, Usooke isawaanyu na nyakuwaanyu’”
Omubhaahi oyo, akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Amaragherri ghansi ghayo, niingaghotire koru obhoona bhoone.”
Hano Yeesu oghuure ghayo, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Usohiiru ne engʼana emwe. Nooghi ughori ebhinto bhinsi bhino ughoote, chembiri chino okubhona, ochetweni abhatobhu, neho okubha witoorire ekeghuku mwisaaro. Kumaruho wuuche, untambane.”
Hano omubhaahi oyo, oghuure ghayo, akabhaabhayera bhukongʼu, gho okubha aare omwame bhukongʼu.
Hano Yeesu, aamorooche ghote abhaabhayire, akaghamba akabhughaa, “Ne-engʼana enkongʼu abhaame, ghusoha mo Obhukama bho Ghiteema!
Ne-engʼana entobhu, engamia kuheta mwibhanga re esindani, ghukera omwame ghusoha mo Obhukama bho Ghiteema!”
Hano abheegha bhoghuure ghayo, bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Ne-wuuye bhoono, ono akunaghi ghutooribhu?”
Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Amangʼana ghano abhanto bhatamiru, Ghiteema nkunaghi aani.”
Hayo, Peetero akabhoorra Yeesu akabhughaa, “Righeeri itu, totighire ebhinto bhiitu bhinsi, toghutambaine!”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Ndabhabhoorra obhuheene, omonto wunsiwunsi ono atighire enyumba yaache, mughaache, bhamura bhaache, abhaibhori bhaache, hande abhaana bhaache, gho okugheri ko Obhukama bho Ghiteema,
obhuheene arabhona amaaru bhukongʼu ghukera bhino atighire, akeere aani mo ense eno. Ghwiki, arabhona obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi monse eno eghuucha.”
Yeesu akaghegha abheegha bhaache ikomi na bhabhere rubhareka, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Mutegheerre! Turatiira koghi Yerusareemu. Na hayo, ghansi ghano abharooti bhaandekire ighoro ya eni Omoona wo Omonto, gharahekerana.
Ndahiru ku bhano bhatare Abhayahudi, bhansere, bhantoke no ghutwera amate.
Ghwiki, bharantema emicharichi no okonyita, ghasi bhoono orosiko ro ghatato, ndaryoka.”
Amangʼana ghano Yeesu aghambire, abheegha bhaache bhataaghamanyire, gho okubha mbaare bhabhisiru amangʼana ghayo. Kuru bhataamanyire ghano aare kughambera.
Hano Yeesu ahikire haghuhe no omoghi gho Yeriko, akabhona omohukuru omwe, aikaire rubhareka rwe enchera, arasabhasabha.
Enkaagha eno omohukuru oyo oghuure eghekomo kya abhanto bharaheta hayo, akabhoori, “N-ke keeni eyo?”
Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, “Yeesu wa Naasareeti newe akuheta.”
Omohukuru oyo akaghamba ko riiraka rikoro akabhughaa, “Yeesu, Omoona wa Daudi, utaanyaabhera!”
Abhanto bhano bhaare bhatangoriire morughendo ruyo, bhakamuhamera korri akire. Ghasi bhoono ewe, aghaikongʼi kubherekera gho chenguru, “Omoona wa Daudi, utaanyaabhera!”
Yeesu akaimerra, akabhugha omohukuru oyo ahiru haare ewe. Hano omohukuru oyo amwisokerire, Yeesu akamubhoori akabhughaa,
“N-ke oghotuna ngukorre?” Akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Omutemi, ndasabha nnaghi kurora.”
Yeesu akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Urore! Kino kigherri uhorre n-obhwitabherri bhoocho.”
Enkaagha eyo eyo omohukuru akarora, aghatambana Yeesu, eno araitumi Ghiteema. Abhanto bhansi, hano bhaarooche ghayo, nabhu bhaghaitumi Ghiteema.
Hano Yeesu aasohire momoghi gho Yeriko, akaheta ghatighati yo omoghi ghuyo araghi Yerusareemu.
Momoghi ghuyo, aareho omonto omwe ono aare kubherekeru Sakaayo. Oyo newe aare omokoro wa abhaghooti bhe righooti, ghwiki n-omwame aare.
Aare kwighombu kurora Yeesu bhwe aani. Ghasi bhoono tanaghiri komurora, ghokugheri kwe eghekomo eghekoro kya abhanto kino kyaareho, na ghote aare omoghuhe.
Ke hayo akaryera engirimanta, aghatangorra mbere ye eghekomo kiyo kya abhanto, akariina ko omoko, korri hano Yeesu akuheta gho enchera eyo amurore.
Hano Yeesu aahikire ko omoko hayo, akarigheeri ighoro yo omote ghuyo, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Sakaayo, sekera bhongobhongo! Reero ndatunu nibhe omugheni waacho ka.”
Bhongo bhongo Sakaayo aghasekera, akaghaghaani Yeesu waache ko ghuchomeru.
Hano abhanto bhansi bhaarooche ghayo, bhaghasimi kongʼunya, bharabhughaa, “Ake aghiire kuraaghera komoghi gho we ebhibhe!”
Ghasi bhoono, Sakaayo akaimerra, akabhoorra Omutemi Yeesu akabhughaa, “Tegherra, Omutemi! Bhoono, ritingita rye ebhinto bheene ndabhaha abhatobhu. Na uraabhone nenduusiri omonto wunsiwunsi gho komungʼaachera, ndamuhonchokeri hari kane ya keere namoruusiri.”
Yeesu akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Obhutoori bhubhahekeere reero eno, iye na abhanto bhe nyumba yaacho, gho okubha omonto ono, wunsi we ekehita ke Ibhurahimu.
Gho okubhaeni Omoona wo Omonto niichire ghotuna no oghutoori abhanto bhano bhasirre.”
Hano Yeesu aare haghuhe kohika Yerusareemu, abhanto bhano bhaare komutegherra, bhaare kumanya aghoo, Obhukama bho Ghiteema bhuraacha hari remwe. Ko riyo Yeesu akabharengeri ekihekaani akabhughaa, “Aareho omonto omwe we ekehita ke eghikama. Omonto oyo, naatanwerre koghi ekyaro ghe kure, korri ahaabhu obhutemi, agharoke kubhaaha ekyaro gheeche.

“Hano aare akeere ghutanora koghi orughendo ruyo, akabhabherekera abhabhaghasi bhaache ikomi, akabhaha chembiri echaaru ke omwe omwe, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Mukore orutani ne chembiri chino mbahaire kohika enkaagha eno nkugharoka.’
Ghasi bhoono omonto oyo, naareghiru bhukongʼu na abhanto bhe ekyaro gheeche. Neho bhatomire abhanto bhahire amangʼana aghoo, ‘Tutaakwenda omonto ono abhe omutemi waito!’
Gho okubhabhaakorre ke hayo, ghasi omonto oyo naahaabhiru obhukama. Hano aagharokire, akabherekera abhabhaghasi bhaache bhaare ateghiire chembiri, kuru bhamubhoorre chiwaara chino bhaabwiine.
“Omubhaghasi wa mbere aghaacha, akamubhoorra, ‘Omutemi, gho chembiri ikomi cheere wanteghiire, nche-chino, ghwiki mbwine ewaara hari ikomi gho chiyo.’
Omutemi oyo akamugharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Omubhaghasi waane omuheene, ukorre bhwaheene! Gho okubhaubhaire omuheene ko engʼana ensuuhu bhukongʼu, ndakuha amanagha gho obhubhaahi ighoro ye emeghi ikomi.’
“Omubhaghasi wa kabhere wunsi aghaacha, akamubhoorra, ‘Omutemi, korwera gho chembiri chino wanteghiire, mbwine ewaara hari ghataano yaache.’
Omutemi oyo akamugharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Na iye, ndakuha amanagha gho okubhaaha emeghi etaano.’
“Omubhaghasi wa ghatato aghaacha akabhughaa, ‘Omutemi, chembiri chaacho chino wanteghiire nche-chino hano. Naare nchebhisire mo eghitambaara, korri chitaghasira.
Naakorre kee hayo gho okubha ndaghotiina. Iye n-omonto omobhe wooni, Uraghegha eghento kino utatoorre, na uraghesa kino utemiiri.’
“Omutemi oyo akamubhoorra ighoo, ‘Iye omubhaghasi omobhe wooni! Bhoono ndaghukengera ekiina ku amangʼana ghaacho omwene ghayo ughambire. Ukaamanya umanyire kubha eni neeni omonto omobhe bhukongʼu, ndaghegha eghento haare ntatoorre, na ndaghesa kino ntemiri.
Uraabhone nighoo neeni, bhoono ghoke utambechiiri chembiri chaane mo bhenki, korri hano nguucha nchigheghe hamwe ne chiwaara?’
“Neho omutemi oyo, abhabhooriire abhanto bhano bhaare bhaimeeriire haghuhe hayo akabhughaa, ‘Momoruusi chembiri chiyo aghoote, momuhe ono aabhwine chiwaara ikomi.’
Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, ‘Omutemi, aka, Ndorra ono amarekubhona chiwaara ikomi!’
“Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Ndabhabhoorra kubha, omonto wunsiwunsi ono aghukora emeremo bhwaheene ghino aghoote, arengeribhu eghende. Ghasi bhoono, omonto ono ataghukora bhwaheene emeremo ghino aghoote, kuru ebhesuuhu bheere aghoote ararusibhu.
Ghasi bhoono abhabhisa bhaane, bhano bhatarekwenda eni nibhe omutemi waabho, mubhareete hano mbere yaane, korri mubhaite!’”
Hano Yeesu amarre kughamba ghayo, akaghenderri no orughendo rooche ro koghi Yerusareemu. Aghakangata abhanto bhayo aare nabhu.
Hano aare haghuhe ne ebhechichi bhe Bhetibhaghe na Bhetania, korukereghe runo rwabherekiiru rwe Emiseituuni, aghatoma abheegha bhaache bhabhere.
Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Mughende mo eghechichi kino keeni mbere yaanyu. Na hano moghusoha mo eghechichi kiyo, murabhona ekeheeri kye entikere kibhohirru kino ghitamaraghesimi kughegha omonto. Moghitanchore, mokindeetere hano.
Hano omonto akubhabhoorri abhughee, ‘Ngooke moghoghitanchora?’ Momugharokeri mobhughee, ‘Omutemi araghetuna.’ ”
Neho, abheegha bhayo bhaaghiire, bhakabhona ghansi ghaare, ghote Yeesu aare abhabhooriire.
Hano bhaare ghutanchora ekeheeri kiyo kye entikere, neho abheene ekeheeri abhabhoori, “Ngooke moghutanchora ekeheeri kiyo?”
Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, “Omutemi araghetuna.”
Neho bhakigheghire no ghokihererra Yeesu ekeheeri kiyo kye entikere, bhakaari chingebho chaabho gho ekeheeri kiyo, kumara bhakarini Yeesu gho ekimori kiyo.
Enkaagha eno Yeesu aare araghi, abhanto mbaare kwaari chingebho chaabho monchera ino aare kuheta.
Ne enkaagha eno ahikire haghuhe na ahase hano haghoote ekingʼaraaro kyo orukereghe rwe emiseituuni, eghekomo kya abheegha bhaache bhansi, bhaghasimi ghokumi Ghiteema ko amachomeru, ighoro ya amakono ghansi ghano bhaarooche.
Bharaghamba bharabhughaa, “Anooku Omukama ono aghuucha ko eriina ryo Omutemi Ghiteema! Habhe no omurembe haare Ghiteema na abhanto bhaache. Na aitumibhu Ghiteema ono aani ighoro ya bhinsi.”
Mo eghekomo kiyo kya abhanto, nemubhaare Amabharisaayo. Bhakabhoorra Yeesu, bhakabhughaa, “Omweghi, taseghani abheegha bhaacho bhatighe kughamba kee hayo!”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Ndabhabhoorra ighoo, uraabhone bhano bharakira, amaghena gharatiirri riraka!”
Hano Yeesu ahekerre omoghi gho Yerusareemu no okoghurorra, aghasimi koghukoorra.
Akaghughambera akabhughaa, “Sungu wakamanyire enchera yo kureeta omurembe! Ghasi bhoono nebhisiru waacho.
Gho chinkaagha chino cheghuucha, abhabhisa bhaanyu bharatubhaghera orubhagho orukongʼu, korri bhabhaitani koru chibhareka chinsi.
Hayo neho inyu moghosikibhu, hamwe na abhaana bhaanyu bhansi. Ritareho righena rino reghutama reeni ighoro ye erende, omoghi ghuno ghurahanyooru, gho okubha mutamanyire enkaagha eno Ghiteema aichire kubhatoori.”
Neho Yeesu asohire ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, aghasimi kotyambi abhanto bhano bhaare bharaghori ebhinto muyo.
Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Yandekiru mu Amaandeko Amahoreeru gha Ghiteema, ‘Enyumba yaane, irabha enyumba ya amasabhi.’ Ghasi inyu, muraikora kubha ehunguru ya abhasara!’”
Yeesu akabha areeghi abhanto mu ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema. Abhakoro bha abhasengeri, hamwe na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa na abhagharuka bha Abhayahudi, bhakabha bharatuna enchera yo komwita.
Ghasi bhoono bhatabhwine omweya, gho okubha abhanto mbaamwichoriire, bharamutegherra.
Orosiko romwe, Yeesu aare ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, areeghi abhanto, no kubhareghaneri Amangʼana Amachomu gha Ghiteema. Abhakoro bha abhasengeri, abheeghi bha amaragherri, na abhagharuka bha Abhayahudi bhakamwichera.
Bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Otubhoorre, amangʼana ghano oghukora, uraghakora ku amanagha gho obhubhaahi ke? Ne-wuuye akuhaire amanagha ghayo?”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Naane mbabhoori, mumboorre,
Kanaa, amanagha gha Yohana gho okubhaatiisi abhanto, hayi gharweriire? Ngarweriire o Ghiteema ghasi ngarweriire kubhanto?”
Neho, bhaasimiri kubhoorani abheene ku bheene bharabhughaa, “Turaamugharokeri kubha, ngaaruure haare Ghiteema, aratubhoorra abhughee, ‘Ngooke! Mutamwitabheriiri?’
Na hano turaamubhoorre kubha amanagha ghano aghoote ghakarweera kubhanto, nangatutemu amaghena na abhanto bhano bhaani hano, gho okubha mbaakumiri aghoo, Yohana n-omurooti aare.”
Neho, bhaamugharokiiri, bharabhughaa, “Tutamanyire hai ghaarweriire.”
Yeesu wunsi akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Kuru eni, tenkubhabhoorra he ndakora amangʼana ghano ku amanagha gho obhubhaahi bho wuuye.”
Yeesu akarengeri abhanto ekihekaani akabhughaa, “Aareho omonto omwe. Omonto oyo aakeemi emisabhiibhu komoghondo ghooche, akaghukodisha ku abharemi. Kumaruho, akaghi orughendo mo ekyaro ghe kure, aghaikara eyo chensiko echaaru.
Hano enkaagha yo kughesa yaahikire, aghatoma omubhaghasi waache ku abharemi bhayo, korri bhamotweni omotweeno. Ghasi bhoono, enkaagha eno omubhaghasi oyo aahikire ku abharemi bhayo, bhakamutema bhukongʼu, bhakamotyambi amabhoko machwe.
“Omwene moghondo, aghatoma omubhaghasi waache owonde. Ghasi bhoono wunsi bhakamutema no okomusookeeri, kumara bhakamotyambi amabhoko machwe.
Ghwiki aghatoma omubhaghasi wa ghatato, oyo wunsi bhakamunyahaara bhukongʼu, bhakamutabhuta kibhara.
“Neho omwene moghondo oyo, aghaitegherra ighoo, ‘Bhoono, nkore bhwe? Bhoono, mutome omoona waane omusaighi! Ewe bharamusooka.’
Ghasi bhoono, hano abharemi bhayo bhaarooche omoona oyo, bhakabhoorani abheene ko abheene, ighoo, ‘Ono newe akughabha ebhinto bhe isawaabho. Tomwite, korri eghabho yaache eno ibhe eyiitu.’
Neho, bhamorichokiri kibhara yo omoghondo, bhakamwita.” Neho Yeesu aabhoorri abhanto bhayo bhaare komutegherra akabhughaa, “Bhoono, omwene omoghondo oyo mbwe arabhakore abharemi bhayo?
Omwene omoghondo araacha no kubhaita bhansi, no omoghondo ghuyo, akodishere abhande!” Abhanto bhano bhoghuure amangʼana ghayo bhakabhughaa, “Ghayo ghahombere kure!”
Yeesu akabhamoghorra, akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Bhoono mumboorre obhumanyi bhwa Amaandeko ghano. ‘Righena rino abhaabheki bhangire, neryu ribhaire righena rikoro re ghokoona yo omosingi’
“Omonto wunsiwunsi araaghwere righena riyo, araghechoka ghechoka ebhetenetene, na hano righena riyo riraaghwere omonto, riramughochaghocha.”
Abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa, na abhakoro bha abhasengeri, bhakamanya kubha ekihekaani kiyo, nebhu ahekaaniiri. Bhoono bhaghatuna komughoota hayo hayo, ghasi bhoono mbaatiinire abhanto.
Ko riyo, abhakoro bha Abhayahudi bhayo, bhakabha bharaghonyera Yeesu korri bhamughoote. Neho, bhatomire abhanto, bhaghende haare Yeesu bhaitami ghote n-ambanto abhaheene. Ghasi bhoono bhatune enchera yo kughoota Yeesu ku amangʼana ghaache, bhamohire ko omubhaahi we Ekerumi.
Neho, abhanto bhayo bhabhoori Yeesu bhakabhughaa, “Omweghi, ntumanyire kubha uraghamba no okweeghi amangʼana gho obhuheene. Iye tokoobhoha echeo kyo omonto, ghasi n-obhuheene bhwa amangʼana gha Ghiteema neghu okweeghi abhanto.
Tubhoorra ambe, amaragherri ghiitu gharaitabherri kureha righooti o Kaisari, ghasi kwanga ghaani?”
Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akangʼura obhwitaami bhoobho, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa,
“Monyereki etinaari. Hano bhamwerekiri edinaari eyo, akabhabhoori akabhughaa, obhosho ne eriina rino reeni kotinaari iyo mbe-wuuye?” Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, “M-bhe Kaisari.”
Neho Yeesu aabhagharokiiri akabhughaa, “bhe Kaisari, mubhe muramuha Kaisari, na bhe Ghiteema mubhe muramuha Ghiteema.”
Righarokeri riyo re Yeesu, rikabharoghoori bhukongʼu, bhaghakira kiri. Bhaghakeru komughooti kumangʼana ghano abhughire mbere ya abhanto.
Ghwiki bhaareho abhanto bhande bhano bhaare kubherekeru Amasatukaayo. Ebhu bhaare kobhugha ighoo, abhaku bhataakoryoka. Bhakagharoki Yeesu, bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa,
“Omweghi, Musa aaghatwandekera kubha, uraabhone omonto akuure, na atighire mughaache ataana omoona, ninga mura waabho amughabhe omosino oyo, korri aibhorre abhaana, murra waabho oyo okubhona akuure.
Bhaareho abhamura mohungate. Omutangi aghateta omughaikoro, kumara aghaku ataibhwire nawe omoona.
Murra waabho ono aare komoosera, [akaghabha omosino oyo, nawe ghwiki aghaku ataibhwire nawe omoona.]
Kuru wa ghatato wunsi akamughabha, aghaku ataibhwire nawe. Ikabha kee hayo hayo ku bhansi mohungate. Bhaghaku bhataibhwire nawe omoona.
Kumaruho, omughaikoro oyo wunsi aghaku.
Ghasi bhoono! Urabhone abhaku bhararyoka, omughaikoro oyo, arabha mukaa wuuye? Gho okubhabhansi mohungate, mukaabho aare.”
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Abhanto bha mo ense muno bharateta no oghutetu.
Ghasi bhoono, bhano Ghiteema araarore, ngotunu yeeni koryokoru koru mubhaku, no kumenya mo ense ehe, bhayo bhataaghutetana he.
Na bhataghoku ghwiki, bharabha ghote maraika. Bharabha abhaana bha Ghiteema, gho okubha mbaaryokwiru koru mubhaku.
“Kuru Musa naandekire ighoo, bhano bhakuure bhararyoka. Hano aare kughambana na Ghiteema, ko engʼana ye eghisaka kino kyare ghooka omorro, naabhughire agho Omutemi Ghiteema newe Ghiteema wa Ibhurahimu, Ghiteema wa Isaaka, Ghiteema wa Yaakobho.
Haare Ghiteema, bhansi bhatato bhayo bhakeere ghoku nankabha bhakuure. Ghiteema tare Ghiteema wa bhano bhakuure abheene, ghasi n-Giteemi wa abhaku na abhahoru bhansi.”
Hayo neho abheeghi abhande bha amaragherri gha Musa, bhaabhughiree, “Omweghi, uhonchokiiri bhwaheene!”
Korwera enkaagha eyo, bhatatunire ghwiki kubhooribhoori Yeesu amangʼana aghande.
Neho, Yeesu abhabhoori abhanto bhayo bhaare hayo akabhughaa, “Ake abhanto bharabhugha agho, Kirisito arabha Omoona wo omutemi Daudi?
Ghasi bhoono Daudi omwene, naandekire mo eghitabho ke Sabhuri arabhughaa, ‘Omutemi Ghiteema naamubhoriire Omutemi waane, “Wikare orubhareka roone ro bhoryo, ahase hano haghusooku bhukongʼu
okuhekera hano oghutachera harense abhabhisa bhaacho.” ’
“Ghote, Daudi akubherekera Kirisito, Omutemi waache, bhoono bhwe ekubha Kirisito newe Omoona waache?”’
Enkaagha eno abhanto bhaare komutegherra, Yeesu akabhoorra abheegha bhaache akabhughaa,
“Mwiyangarre na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa! Ebhu Mbasaighire kughenda bhaswaare chingancho chintambe, no ghukeeribhu gho chinsoni mometeera. Mbaseghire ghwikara kobhetumbe bhya abhakoro mochenyumba cha Abhayahudi cho oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, na mochinyangi mbaseghire ghwikara ahase ha abhakangati.
Bhararuusi abhasino ebhinto bheebho bhinsi, bharaikori na-abhanto abhanyooku koghusabha amasabhi amatambe mbere ya abhanto. Abhanto bhayo, Ghiteema arabhakengera ebhiina bhosineenu Bhukongʼu!”
Hano Yeesu aare akeere mo Nyumba ya ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, akarora abhaame bharatoora chisataaka chaabho moghento ghyo koruuseri chisataaka.
Akarora omosino omwe omutobhu aratoora muyo chitongoro ibhere chensuuhu bhukongʼu.
Neho Yeesu aaghambire akabhughaa, “Ndabhabhoorra obhuheene kubha, omosino omutobhu ono, newe aruusiri bhukongʼu ghukera bhansi.
Ndabhugha kee hayo, gho okubha abhande bhano bhansi, mbaruusiri hasuuhu, he ebhinto bheebho. Ghasi bhoono omosino omutobhu ono, aruusiri bhinsi bhino aare nabhyu.”
Abheegha abhande bha Yeesu, bhaare bharasumacherra ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, ghote haare habhekiru na amaghena amachomu, haghakonu ne ebhinto bhyo obhughori obhokoro, bhino abhanto bhaaruusiiri Ghiteema. Ghasi Yeesu akabhughaa,
“Ghano ghansi mokurora hano, enkaagha iraacha eno righena riteghusaagha ighoro ye erende. Ghasi ghansi gharahaanyoru!”
Neho abheegha bhayo bhamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Omweghi, amangʼana ghayo n-duuhe ghakubha? N-kimanyerri ke kino kiratwerekerri kubha haghuhe ghaani ghabhe?”
Akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Mwiyangarre, mutaghaacha kungʼainu! Abhanto abhaaru bharaacha ko eriina reene, na bharabhughaa, ‘Neeni kirisito!’ Ghwiki, bharabhughaa, ‘Enkaagha yeere mwabhooriiru, haghuhe yeeni kohika!’ Ghasi mutakabhatambana!
Ghwiki hano mokooghu amangʼana ghe riihe, na ghoghwitana, motighe koobhoha. Ghayo ghansi iratakeru ghakoru ghwansa, ghasi omohiko ghurabha ghukeere.”
Yeesu akaghenderri kubhabhoorra arabhughaa, “Ekyaro kemwe, kiraitana ne ekyaro kende. Obhukama bhomwe bhuraitana no obhukama obhonde.
Bhirabhaho ebherighiti ebhekoro hase hansi, egheecha endoro na amarwire amasineenu gho ghosiki. Ebhimanyerri bhya amakono gho kuroghoori bhirarwera mwisaaro, bhino bhekoobhohi abhanto bhukongʼu.
“Ghasi bhoono, ghayo ghansi hano okubhona ghataamara ghabha, abhanto muraghootu munyankibhu. Bharabhahira ku abhakoro bhe chenyumba cha Abhayahudi cho oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, kuru bhabhabhohe mokibhohe. Bharabhahira mbere ya abhabhaahi na abhakama gho okubha murantambana.
Hano muraahaabhu omweya gho kughamba, eyo neyu ekubha enkaagha enchomu, yo konyimererra.
“Ke hayo, mutaghaitegherra mometema gheenyu kubha bhwe moghukora korri mwitoori ne ekiina kiyo.
Eni omwene, ndabhaha obhungʼaini na amangʼana gho kughamba, kuru abhabhisa bhaanyu bharatamu kwanga hande kubhanyeera chinkaani.
“Bharabhainaara kuru abhaibhori bhaanyu, bhamura bhaanyu, abhanto bhaanyu, na abhasaani bhaanyu. Bharagheri abhamwe bhaanyu mwitu.
Abhanto bhansi, bharabharegha gho okubha murantambana.
Ghasi bhoono, amangʼana ghayo ghatakubhanyahaara, kuru orotuuki romwe kometwe gheenyu rutaaghosira!
Hano muraaghomerri, muratoori obhuhoru bhoonyu.”
“Hano mokurora omoghi gho Yerusareemu ghunaariibhu na abhasirikare abhaaru, neho mokumanya agho, enkaagha yo kuhaanyoru haghuhe yeeni.
Neho, bhano okubhona bhaani momukowa gho Yuudeya, bharyererre ghochinkereghe. Na bhano okubhona bhaani momoghi gho Yerusareemu, bharumu bhongo. Na bhano bhaani moghondo, bhatakaagharoka momoghi muyo.
Chiyo nechu chensiko chino Ghiteema akurehani esiire, korri amangʼana ghansi ghano ghaandekiru ghahekerane.
Haaho yaabho abhaghaikoro bhano okubhona bharitohire, na bhano bhakughonki gho enkaagha eyo, gho okubha irabhaho enyanko endoro bhukongʼu gho ekyaro ke Isiraeri. Ghwiki Ghiteema arakengera ebhiina abhanto bhe ense yinsi.
Abhanto abhande, bharaitu gho kugheechu ne ekinyamaino. Na abhande, bharaghootu hari remwe, no okohiru mo ebhyaro bhinsi. Na Abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahudi, bharaacha bhabhaahe gho chenguru omoghi gho Yerusareemu, kohika okuhekeerana kwa abhanto bhayo.”
“Ebhimanyerri bhirabhaho ko ereebha, ko omweri, na gho chinchota. Okuherra no oghusareka kwe enyancha, bhiragheri abhanto bhansi monse, bhabhe ne enyanko endito ne ehaho.
Enkaagha ghayo ghansi, ghaghuucha mo ense, abhanto bharacheecheka ko obhoobha. Bharitengʼera kubhonu na amangʼana amasineenu monse, gho okubha, ereebha, omweri na chinchota bhirasingisibhu.
“Hayo neho abhanto bhakundora eni Omoona wo Omonto, ndaacha neeni ghwisaaro, niina amanagha ne emirengaari emekoro.
Hano ghayo ghaghosimi kohyoka, inyu mughomerri no ghuchomeru. Gho okubhaenkaagha yo ghutongorubhu koonyu, irabha ehikire haghuhe.”
Kumaruho, Yeesu akarengeri abheegha bhaache ekihekaani akabhughaa, “Morighereeri komote gho omotiini, ne emete ghende ghinsi.
Hano mokurora kubha, omote ghosimiri ghusebhoka, hayo neho mokumanya kubha enkaagha ye emaaho ehikire.
“Kee hayo hayo, na hano mokurora ghayo ghasimiri kohyoka, mumanye kubha, Obhukama bho Ghiteema bhohikire haghuhe.
Obhuheene ndabhabhoorra ighoo, orwibhoro runo rutaakuheta ghano ghansi ngambire ghataamara ghahekeerana.
Risaaro ne ense bhiraheta, ghasi Amangʼana ghaane ghataakuheta he.
“Mwiyangarre mutakaaritoheru no omwingʼaho no obhureebhi, ne ehaho yo obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi. Hano mutayiyangarre orosiko ro omohiko rurabhabhacha mutamanyire.
Orosiko ruyo, ruraacha hari remwe kubhanto bhansi, monse engima.
Mbe, mwiyangarre enkaagha yinsi! Mughenderri ghusaasaama Ghiteema, korri abhahe amanagha gho kwiheeneri ghayo ghansi ghakohyoka, no kwimerra obhoronge bhoone, eni Omoona wo Omonto.”
Gho chensiko chiyo chinsi, Yeesu aare kweeghi abhanto omwise, mu ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema. No obhotiko, aare koghi komisi mo orukereghe rwe Emiseituuni.
Abhanto abhaaru bhaare komuta etabhoori chiri no koghi ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, korri bhamutegherre.
Orosiko rwe enyangi ye emighaate ghino ghitatorru ehamiira rware rohikire haghuhe. Enyangi eyo, yaare kubherekeru Ebhaasaka.
Abhakoro bha abhasengeri na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa, bhaare ghotuna enchera yo ghwita Yeesu. Ghasi bhoono, mbaatiinire abhanto bhataghakora riihe.
Mbe, mubheegha bha Yeesu ikomi na bhabhere bhaare, aaremu omwegha ono aare kubherekeru Yuuda Isikariote. Yuuda oyo, newe Risambu ryamusoheriire.
Bhoono, Yuuda oyo, akaghi kughambana na abhakoro bha abhasengeri, na abhakoro bha abharendi bha ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, ghote araarweche Yeesu.
Amangʼana ghayo, ngaabhachomiire bhukongʼu, bhaghaitabherri komureha chembiri.
Yuuda aghaitabherri, ko riyo aghasimi ghotuna enchera yo kubhaghooti Yeesu, enkaagha eno abhanto bhatareho.
Orosiko rwe enyangi ye emighaate ghino ghitatorru ehamiira rukahika. Orosiko ruyo, neru rware ro okughoogha ekeghuruki kye ringʼondi rye Ebhaasaka.
Neho Yeesu aatomire Peetero na Yohana, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Mughende motuseemeri ebhyakori bhye Ebhaasaka, korri, tuuche kori hamwe.”
Bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Hayi oghotuna tuseemeri?”
Akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Hano mokohika momoghi gho Yerusareemu, murasikana no omosubhe omwe, agheghire ensengo. Omosubhe oyo, mutambane nawe kohika monyumba eno aghusoha na inyu musohemu.
Hano mokohika, mubhoori omwene enyumba eyo mobhughee, “Omweghi arabhoori, ‘Eghechumba kya abhagheni mooke keeni? Ndatuna kunyeeramu ebhyakori bhye Ebhaasaka, hamwe na abheegha bhaane.”
Hayo neho akubheereki eghechumba eghekoro ke moghorofa, kino kimarre ghuseemibhu. Muyo nemu, motuseemeri Ebhaasaka.”
Hano, abheegha bhayo bhaaghiire, bhakabhona amangʼana ghaani ghote Yeesu abhabhooriire. Bhaghaseemi ebhyakori bhye Ebhaasaka.
Hano enkaagha yo kuraaghera yaahikire, Yeesu aghaikara kuraaghera, hamwe na abhatomu bhaache.
Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Nighoombiru bhukongʼu, kori ebhyakori bhye Ebhaasaka eno, hamwe na inyu nkeere kunyankibhu!
Ndabhabhoorra aghoo, tengusanga na inyu ghwiki ebhyakori bhye enyangi ye Ebhaasaka, kohikera hano rokuhekeerana ko Obhukama bho Ghiteema.”
Kumaruho, Yeesu akaimoki eghikombe ke etibhai, aghakumi Ghiteema akabhughaa, “Mugheghe etibhai eno, monyo!
Ndabhabhoorra kee hayo, gho okubha koru bhoono tenkonyo etibhai ghwiki, kohikera hano Obhukama bho Ghiteema, bhoghuucha.”
Yeesu akaimoki omughaate, aghakumi Ghiteema, akaghusoonora, akabhaha abhatomu bhaache, arabhabhoorra arabhughaa, [“Ghuno, neghu omobhere ghoone, ghuno mokumwenseru, mubhe murakora kee hano gho okohiita!”
Hano bhaamarre kori ebhyakori, Yeesu akaimoki ghwiki eghikombe kiyo ke etibhai akabhughaa, “Etibhai eno, irimererra riraghano riihe rya amaanyinga ghaane, ghano ghaghwiteka gho kugheri yaanyu.]
“Ghasi bhoono, mumanye ngukori neeni bhoono bhoono na ono aghunkorra omorwecho!
Eni Omoona wo Omonto, ninga neghi ghwitu, ghote Ghiteema aare aseemiri. Ghasi bhoono, haaho yaache omonto ono aghunkorra omorwecho!”
Hayo neho, abhatomu bha Yeesu bhaasimiri kubhoorani abheene ku bheene, ne-wuuye haare ebhu, ono aghukora engʼana eyo.
Abheegha bha Yeesu, bhakanyeerana chinkaani, ne-wuuye aani omokoro haare ebhu.
