Chinkaani chiyo, chikagheri Yeesu abhabhoorre abhughee, “Abhakama bhe ebhyaro nkubhanderri bhaani abhanto bhaabho, na bha amanagha gho obhubhaahi ighoro yaabho, bharabhaitumi kubha n-abhasakeri bha abhanto.
“Ghasi bhoono inyu, motighe kubha kee bhayo. Ghasi haare inyu, omokoro abhe kyo omosuuhu. No omukaangati, abhe kyo omubhaghasi.
Bhoono! Ne-wuuye omokoro bhukongʼu hano? Ono aghwikara ko mesa araaghere, ghasi woore akureeta ebhyakori? Ndamanya woore aghwikara kuraaghera. Kuru eni neeni hano, neeni nkubhabhaghasi.
“Inyu ni-inyu musaaghire hamwe na eni monyanko yaane.
Bhoono, ghote bhoore Taata aahaire obhukama, eni wunsi, ndabhaha obhukama.
Murabha muraraaghera no okonyo ko mesa yaane. Na muraikara ko ebhetumbe bhye eghikama, murakengera ebhiina amakabhira ikomi na abhere gha Abhaisiraeri.”
Yeesu akabhughaa, “Simooni, Simooni! Risambu ndisabhire orongʼusa haare Ghiteema, ribhacharibhu inyu. Irabha kyo oghusensa obhore.
Ghasi bhoono, nengusabhiire haare Ghiteema, korri obhwitabherri bhoocho, bhutaghaasuuha. Hano okungarokera, utooreri bhaghendi bhaacho.”
Simooni akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Omutemi nkunaghi neeni kubhohu monyumba ya abhabhohe, hamwe na iye. Kuru ndaaku tare engʼana he.”
Yeesu akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Iye Peetero, reero uranyaanga hari ghatato esarighooko itamarairaghora.”
Kumaruho, Yeesu akabhoori abheegha bhaache akabhughaa, “Hano naabhatomire mutaana esako ye chembiri, omokumbe, na ebhiraato, n-ke mwasohiiru?” Bhakamugharokeri, “Tutaasohiiru.”
Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Ghasi bhoono, uraabhone omonto aghoote esako ye chembiri, hande omokumbe, abhigheghe. Uraabhone ataghoote ekinyamaino, aghori eghooti yaache, korri aghore ekinyamaino.
Gho okubhagharatunu ghahekerane amangʼana ghano ghaandekiru, kubha ‘Arabharru hamwe na bhe ebhibhe.’ Amangʼana ghayo neeni ghaare kughambera. Naghu, gharahekerana haare eni.”
Nabhu bhakamubhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Omutemi, righeeri! Ebhinyamaino bhibhere mbebhino hano.” Akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Motighane na ghayo.”
Neho Yeesu aruure hayo, akaghi ko orukereghe rwe Emiseituuni, ghote aare anarre. Abheegha bhaache bhansi bhaghatambana nawe.
Hano aahikire ko orukereghe kuyo, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Momusaasaame Ghiteema, korri mutaghasoha mumacharibhu.”
Yeesu akabhatigha hayo, aghaisuka mbere hasuuhu. Akahighama, aghasaasaama Ghiteema, arabhughaa,
“Taata! Uraasaighe onduuseriho enyanko eno eghuucha. Ghasi bhoono, kino ghinsi oghotuna ghukora, ghikoru ghote usaighire na tare ghote eni nsaighire!” [
Hayo neho maraika koru mwisaaro, akamwichera, akamuha chenguru.
Yeesu, aare kee hano aghoote obhorro bhukongʼu, bhuno bhwagherri aikongʼi ghusaasaama Ghiteema. Ebhigheri bheeche bhikabha bhiratoonya harense kya amatonyo gha amaanyinga.]
Hano amarre ghusaasaama Ghiteema, akaimerra, akagharoka koghi kubheegha bhaache. Hano aahikire, akabhona mbamisiri, gho okubha, mbaabhaabhayire.
Akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Ake momisiri chitoro? Mutabhooka! Musaasaame Ghiteema, korri mutaghasoha mumacharibhu.”
Hano Yeesu aare akeere araghamba amangʼana ghayo, eghekomo kya abhanto abhaaru ghikamwichera, kino kyaakangatiru na Yuuda omwe wa abheegha bhaache, ikomi na bhabhere bhaare. Yuuda aghaisokerra Yeesu korri amukeeri gho komobhusu.
Yeesu akamubhoori akabhughaa, “Iye Yuuda! Uranyinaara eni Omoona wo Omonto gho ghonkumbatia?”
Hano abheegha bha Yeesu bhaarooche ghayo ghaare koghi ghukoru, bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Omutemi waito! Utatigha tugheeche abhanto bhano ne ekinyamaino?”
Takeere, omwegha omwe, akagheecha omubhaghasi wo omokoro wa abhasengeri ne ekinyamaino, akamutena oghotwe ko bhoryo.
Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Murengere hayo haisire!” Akaghoota oghotwe ko mubhaghasi oyo akamuhori.
Abhanto bhano bhaachire kughoota Yeesu, bhaaremu abhakoro bha abhasengeri, abhakoro bha abharendi bha ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema na abhagharuka bhe Ekiyahudi. Yeesu akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Ngooke muchire haare eni ne ebhinyamaino ne cherungu, ke hano mokoghi kughoota omwibhi?
Chensiko chinsi, hamwe tware kuhooya ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, ake mutangootire! Ghasi bhoono, eno neyu enkaagha yaanyu, na yo obhusari.”
Hari remwe, abhanto bhayo bhakamughoota, bhakamohira monyumba yo omokoro wa abhasengeri. Peetero akabharu nyuma, aani kure.
Hano abhanto bhayo bhaahikire, bhakaheemba eghyoto gho ekehorro, bhaghaikara hamwe. Peetero wunsi, aghaacha aghaikara nabhu.
Hano omorro ghookire, omubhaghasi omwe we eghenke akarora Peetero, akaghamba akabhughaa, “Omonto ono, hamwe aare na Yeesu.”
Ghasi bhoono, Peetero akaanga akabhughaa, “Omughaikoro ono! Eni temumanyire!”
Kumaruho, omonto wonde akarora Peetero, akamubhoori akabhughaa, “Na iye wunsi, n-omughende waabho.” Ghasi bhoono, Peetero akagharokeri akabhughaa, “Mura ono! Abhaabhe, tare eni!”
Hano ensa yemwe yaahetire, omonto wonde aghakumerri, kughamba “Obhuheene, omonto ono, hamwe aare na Yeesu! Gho okubhawunsi n-omughariraaya!”
Ghasi bhoono, Peetero akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Mura! Amangʼana ghayo okughamba, tingamanyire!” Kuru akeere araghamba amangʼana ghayo, esarighooko ikaraghora, kokorikoooo, koo!
Omutemi Yeesu akaihonchora, akarigheeri Peetero kumaiso. Peetero akahiita, amangʼana ghano Omutemi amubhooriire akabhughaa, “Reero, esarighooko itamarairaghora, uranyangisi hari ghatato.”
Neho, Peetero angʼosire koghi kibhara, aghakuura chengisori.
Abhanto bhano bhaare kurenda Yeesu, bhakamusera no okomutema.
Bhakamoribha amaiso, bharamubhoori bharabhughaa, “Rengerri, ne-wuuye aghutemire?”
Bhakaghenderri komutoka, amatoki amaaru.
Ritongo rya abhagharuka bha Abhayahudi righikara etabhoori chiri, hamwe na abhakoro bha abhasengeri, na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa. Yeesu akareetu mwitongo riyo, bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa,
“Uraabhone iye niye Kirisito, otubhoorre.” Yeesu akagharokeri akabhughaa, “Kuru Nankabhabhoorra, mutaaghwitabherri.
Ghwiki nankabhabhoorri engʼana, mutaakungarokeri.
Ghasi bhoono, koru bhoono hayo, eni Omoona wo Omonto, ndabha niikaire orubhareka ro bhoryo bho Ghiteema wa amanagha ghansi.”
Bhansi, bhakabhoori Yeesu ghwiki, bhakabhughaa, “Bhoono kana iye n-Omoona wa Ghiteema wooni?” Yeesu akagharokeri akabhughaa, “Ake abheene mumarre kobhugha kubha, neeni!”
Abhakoro bhayo bhakaghamba bhakabhughaa, “Kana, m-bwimererri ke obhonde bhuno toghotuna? Ake itu abheene ntooghuure amangʼana ghano aaghambire omwene.”
Neho, abhakoro bhayo bhansi bhakaimerra, bhakahira Yeesu o Bhiraato. Omubhaahi we ekeruumi.
Bhaghasimi komuchongera bharabhugha, “Omonto ono, ntomobhwine arasari ekyaro ghiitu no ghuseghani abhanto bhaitu, bhatighe kureha righooti o Kaisari. Ghwiki arabhugha aghoo, ewe newe Kirisito omukama.”
Hayo neho Bhiraato aabhoorri Yeesu akabhughaa, “Kana, ni-iye omukama wa Abhayahudi?” Yeesu akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Ni-iye ughambire!”
Bhiraato akabhoorra abhakoro bha abhasengeri bhayo, hamwe ne eghekomo kya abhanto bhansi bhano bhaareho akabhughaa, “Omonto ono, tenkurora aghoote risari rinsirinsi.”
Ghasi bhoono abhanto bhayo, bhaghakumeerri bharabhughaa, “Ameeghi ghaache gharasegherri abhanto, aghasimeri Ghariraaya, na bhoono ghasanchire momukowa ghunsi gho Yuudeya.”
Hano Bhiraato oghuure ghayo, akabhoori akabhughaa, “Kana, omonto ono n-Omughariraaya.?”
Hano Bhiraato aamanyire Yeesu n-Omughariraaya, koru ku amanagha gho obhubhaahi bho Herode Antibhasi, akamohira haare Herode. Gho okubhagho chensiko chiyo, Herode Yerusareemu hayo aare.
Hano Herode aarooche Yeesu, naachomiiru bhukongʼu, gho okubha, nkooghu aare amangʼana ghaache. Ghwiki, gho chensiko echaaru, nkwighombu aare kurora Yeesu, korri, airorre omwene ebhimanyerri bhya amakono ghano ghakoru nawe.
Herode akabhoori Yeesu amangʼana amaaru. Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu taamugharokiiri engʼana.
Abhakoro bha abhasengeri na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa, bhakaimerra, bhakachongera Yeesu gho chenguru bhukongʼu.
Herode na abhasirikare bhaache, bhaghasimi ghusera Yeesu, na bhakamoswari chingebho che eghikama. Kumaruho, bhakamugharoki haare Bhiraato.
Orosiko ruyo, neru Herode na Bhiraato bhaighweraine, bhakaghotana obhusaani, gho okubha m-bhabhisa bhaare ghokoru kare.
Neho, Bhiraato abherekiire abhakoro bha abhasengeri, abhabhaahi bha Abhayahudi, na abhanto bha momoghi.
Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Omonto ono mundetiire hano, muramuchongera kubha arasegherri abhanto, bhoono Muntegheerre! Omonto ono nemubhoorri murategherra inyu abheene. Na kumachongero ghaanyu ghansi, tenkurora aghoote risari rinsirinsi.
Kuru Herode wunsi, tarooche risari reeche, nekyu kigherri amuhonchokiri haare itu. Mbe Muntegheerre, omonto ono, takorre engʼana ensineenu yo okugherri aitu!
Ko riyo ndamutema emicharichi, kumaruho ndamuhaatora.” [
Bhiraato aare kubhahaatorra omubhobhe omwe, gho enkaagha ye enyangi ye Ebhaasaka.]
Abhanto bhayo bhansi, bhaghacherra kwighamba remwe bhakabhughaa, “Mwita aruho, otutachorre Bharaabha.”
Bharaabha oyo, naabhohiru mokibhohe, gho kugheri ko bhwiti bhwa abhanto ne ebhetina momoghi.
Bhiraato ghwiki aare ghotuna kuhaatora Yeesu, ko riyo akaghambana na abhanto bhayo.
Ghasi bhoono, bhakaghenderri ghucherra bharabhughaa, “Utamubhamba komusarabha, mubhamba komusarabha!”
Bhiraato akaghambana nabhu ghwiki re ghatato, akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “M-mabhe ke akorre? Aka tendooche engʼana eno ekugheri aitu! Bhoono ndamutema emicharichi, kumaruho, ndamuhaatora.”
Ghasi bhoono, abhanto bhayo bhakaghenderri ghucherra bhukongʼu bharabhughaa, “Abhambu komusarabha.” Enkaagha ikahika egheturi keebho ghikabhaaha.
Neho Bhiraato aakengire ekiina kya Abhayahudi bhayo, bhakore ghote bhaghotuna.
Akabhahaatorra Bharaabha ono bhaare ghotuna. Bharaabha oyo naabhohiru ko kugheri yo ghukora riihe momoghi, no ghwita abhanto. Akabhaha Yeesu, korri bhakore ghote bhaare ghotuna.
Hano Abhasirikare bhaare koghi ghwita Yeesu, bhaghasikana no omonto omwe, eriina reeche Simooni, wo omoghi gho Kirene. Simooni oyo, aare koru mobhechichi, bhakamughoota, korri agheghe omusarabha eno araru nyuma Yeesu.
Abhanto n-abhaaru bhaare kuru nyuma Yeesu. Mubhayo, bhaaremu abhaghaikoro bhano bhaare komukorra bhabhaabhaayiire.
Yeesu akabhaishooreri, akabhabhoorra, “Inyu abhaghaikoro bha Yerusareemu! Motighe ghunkorra! Ghasi bhoono, mwikorre abheene, na abhaana bhaanyu!
Gho kubha, chensiko chino cheghuucha, abhanto bharabhughaa, ‘Mbaghoote echaghati abhaghomba, na bhano bhataaghonkiri!’
Neho, abhanto bhaghosimi, kubhoorra chinkereghe, ‘Mutatoghwera!’ Ne ebhikereghe, ‘Mutatokundekeri!’
Uraabhone bharakorra kee hano omonto ono atasarri, mbwe ekubha ku abhasari?”
Gho enkaagha eyo, abhasirikare bhakahira abhasari bhabhere koghi ghwitu hamwe na Yeesu.
Bhakahika ahase hano hakubherekeru ekehoore kyo omonto, bhakabhamba Yeesu komusarabha. Na abhasari bhabhere bhaare bhansi bhakabhambu, omwe, bhoryo no owonde bhumosi bho Yeesu.
Yeesu akaghamba akabhughaa, “Taata! Ubhaabhere, gho okubha bhatamanyire kino bhaghukora.” Abhasirikare bhayo, bhaghatwena chingebho cha Yeesu ko ghutema ekuura.
Abhanto mbaare bhaimerire bhararigheerri. Abhabhaahi bha Abhayahudi bhaghasekerra Yeesu, bharamubhoorra bharabhughaa, “Aka aghatoori abhande, uraabhone obhuheene newe Kirisito omoohoru wa Ghiteema, aitoori omwene turore!”
Abhasirikare bhansi, bhaghasera Yeesu. Bhakamureetera etibhai endoro anyo.
Bhakamubhoorra bharabhughaa, “Urabhone iye n-omukama wa Abhayahudi wooni, itoori mbe turore!”
Ighoro yo omotwe ghooche, bhaghatoora ekibhaao, kyandekiru, “ONO NEWE OMUKAMA WA ABHAYAHUDI.”
Kubhasari bhabhere bhaare, omwe aghatoka Yeesu akabhughaa, “Kana, tenkooghu iye niye Kirisito? Taitoori omwene! Na itu, otutoori!”
Ghasi bhoono, Omusari wonde wa kabhere, akamuseghani akabhughaa, “Kana kuru tokoobhoha Ghiteema? Gho kubha, enchagho eno tuteniiru, neyu eyoeyo, omonto ono ateniiru.
Itu, ntukengiru ekiina kyo obhuheene kumangʼana ghano tware ghukora, ghasi omonto ono, takorre risari rinsirinsi.”
Kumaruho, akaghamba akabhughaa, “Yeesu! Hano oghusoha ko obhukama bhoocho, ohiite na eni!”
Yeesu akamugharokeri, “N-obhuheene ngokubhoorra, reero ninga tubhe hamwe mwisaaro.”
Hano yaahikire saa isansabha cho omwise, bhukabha obhwiri bho kabhere, kuhekera saa kenda.
Ribhasia rye Enyumba Ehoreeru ya Ghiteema rikabhaaroka ghatighati.
Yeesu aghakuura koriraka rikoro akabhughaa, “Ee Taata! Enkoro yaane ndaitoora mumabhoko ghaacho.” Hano aamarre kughamba ghayo, aghateni.
Hano omokoro wa abhasirikare aarooche ghayo, aghaitumi Ghiteema akabhughaa, “N-obhuheene kemwe, omonto ono no-omuheene aare haare Ghiteema!”
Hano abhanto bhansi bhano bhaare bhaikomaine hayo bhaarooche amangʼana ghayo ghaabhaire, bhakahonchoka waabho ka, bharaitematema ebhekubha bheebho, bhabhaabhaayiire.
Abhanto bhansi bhano bhaamanyire Yeesu, mbaimerire kure, bhararigheeri ghano ghansi ghaare ghukoru. Mubhayo, nemu bhaare abhaghaikoro bhano bhatambaine Yeesu koru ko mukowa gho Ghariraaya.
Aareho omonto omwe ono aare kobherekeru Yuusufu, wo momukowa gho Yuudeya, momoghi ghuno ghware kubherekeru Arimateya. Yuusufu oyo wunsi n-omukangati wa Abhayahudi aare. Ghasi bhoono, ewe taitabherraini na abhaghendi bhaache gho kiina kyo ghwita Yeesu, gho okubha n-omuheene aare haare Ghiteema. Kuru nkughanya aare Obhukama bho Ghiteema.

Neho Yuusufu oyo, aghiire haare Bhiraato ghusabha omobhere gho Yeesu.
Hano Bhiraato aitabherri, Yuusufu akaghi aghasekeri omobhere gho Yeesu koru komusarabha. Akaghobhisi engebho endabhu chai! Kumaruho, akaghuraari mombeehera eno yaabhaachiru ghwitare. Mombeehera muyo, takaryekirumu omonto wonde.
Orosiko ruyo, ndo-ghuseemi Esabhaato rware, no orosiko rwe Esabhaato ruyo, waabhwine rohikire haghuhe.
Abhaghaikoro bhano bharetaini na Yeesu koru Ghariraaya, bhaghatambana Yuusufu koghi kurora ghote rihundughu re Yeesu ryaarairibhu mombeehera.
Kumara, bhakagharoka ka, bhaghaseemi amaghuta ghe ekerumba eghichomu bhyo kuhaka omobhere gho Yeesu. Ghasi bhoono, orosiko rwe Esabhaato, mbaamunyire ghote amaragherri ghaare kwerekerri.
Etabhoori chiri orosiko ro Chumaabhiiri, abhaghaikoro bhayo, bhakaghegha amaghuta ghe ekerumba eghichomu, ghano bhaare bhaseemeri, bhakaghi kombeehera.
Hano bhaahikire, bhakabhona righena rino ryaahunyire embeehera, rimarre kohingiru, ritooru rubhareka.
Bhaghasoha morense, ghasi bhoono, rihundughu ryo Omutemi Yeesu, ghutaaremu.
Hano bhaare kuroghoorra engʼana eyo, takeere abhasubhe bhabhere bhakaimerra haghuhe nabhu, bhaare bhaswarre chingebho chindabhu chai, chino chekubharibhari.
Neho abhaghaikoro bhayo bhoobhohire bhukongʼu. Bhakahiinya, obhosho bhoobho harense. Ghasi bhoono, abhasubhe bhaare bhakabhabhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Kana, n-ngoke moghotuna omuhoru, mubhaku?
Tareho hano, naryokire! Kana mutakohiita amangʼana ghaare abhabhooriire hano mware nawe momukowa gho Ghariraaya.
Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, Omoona wo Omonto, ninga ahiru ku bhe ebhibhe, nabhu, bharamubhamba komusarabha, kumaruho, orosiko ro ghatato araryoka!”
Neho abhaghaikoro bhayo, bhakahiita amangʼana ghano Yeesu aaghambire.
Hano bhaagharokire koru kombeehera, bhakabhoorra amangʼana ghayo abhatomu bhaare bha Yeesu ikomi na omwe, na abhanto bhansi bhano bhaareho.
Abhaghaikoro bhayo, bhaare Mariyamu wa Maghidara, Yowana, Mariyamu nyakowaabho Yaakobho, na abhande, bhano bhaare hamwe nabhu.
Ghasi bhoono, hano bhaare kubhoorra abhatomu bha Yeesu amangʼana ghayo, abhatomu bhayo, bhataghaitabheriiri. Bhakagharora m-bukangi.
Ghasi, Peetero akaimerra, akaryera engirimanta koghi kombeehera. Hano aahikire, akaihiinya, aghashoomerri morense, akarora chingebho echeene, chino bhaaryekiire Yeesu. Akaroghoora bhukongʼu, kumangʼana ghayo arooche, akagharoka ka.
Ko orosiko ruyo ruyo ro Chumaabhiiri, abheegha bhabhere bha Yeesu, bhaare kughenda koghi moghechichi kino kyare kubherekeru Emawu. Eghechichi kiyo, kyare chekirometa ikomi na yemwe koru Yerusareemu.
Hano abheegha bhayo bhaare kughenda, na-amangʼana ghano ghaatokiire neghu bhaare kughambera.
Enkaagha bhakeere bharaghaghamba, Yeesu omwene aghaacha, akaghendani hamwe nabhu.
Bhakamurora, ghasi bhoono, Ghiteema akabhakora bhatighe komwongora.
Yeesu akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Kana, n-ke mokughambera hano muraghenda?” Bhakaimerra, bhabhaabhaayiire.
Omwegha omwe, ono aare kubherekeru Kireobha, akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Kana, hayi orweriire, kuru utamanyire amangʼana ghano ghatokiire Yerusareemu gho chensiko cha bhongo chino?”
Wunsi akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Amangʼana ke ghayo?” Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, “Amangʼana gha Yeesu wa Naasareeti. Yeesu oyo aare omurooti wa amanagha gho kughamba no ghukora haare Ghiteema na kubhanto bhansi.
Ghasi bhoono abhakoro bha abhasengeri, na abhabhaahi bhaito, bhakamohira, korri akengeru ekiina kyo ghwitu, abhambu komusarabha.
Ewe newe tware ghwitengʼera, kubha, aratutongora Abhaisiraeri. Ghasi bhoono, reero n-orosiko ro ghatato koru amangʼana ghayo ghatookire.
“Ghwiki, reero abhaghaikoro bhande bha waio mbaturoghoorri, hano bhaaghiire mombeehera, etabhoori chiri,
Hano bhaahikire, bhakabhona omobhere ghutaremu. Bhakagharoka bhaghatubhoorra kubha mbahyokiiru na Abhamaraika bhabhere. Abhamaraika bhayo, bhakabhabhoorra bhakabhughaa, Yeesu n-omuhoru.
“Kumaruho, bhaghendi bhaito abhande, bhakaghi mombeehera, bhakabhona amangʼana ghansi ghano twabhooriiru na abhaghaikoro bhayo n-obhuheene. Ghasi bhoono Yeesu omwene bhataamorooche.”
Yeesu akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Kana inyu, mbakangi mooni! Ngooke mooni abhakongʼu mometema gheenyu, ghwitabherri ghaare ghaaghambiru na abharooti?”
Ghasi tiyaareghotunu Kirisito ahetere enyanko eyo no ghusoha mo mirengaari gheeche?”
Neho Yeesu abhabhooriire amangʼana ghansi ghano ghaandekiru haare ewe, koru mumaandeko gha Musa, mu Amandeko Amahoreeru ghansi, na mumaandeko gha abharooti.
Hano bhaare haghuhe kohika koghechichi kino bhaare koghi, Yeesu aghaikori kee hano aghotuna kughenderri no orughendo.
Ghasi bhoono, bhakamusaasaama bhukongʼu, bhakamubhoorra bharabhugha, “Taikara hamwe na itu hano! Aka, ritebhiire ghyakaruuta.” Yeesu aghaitabherri, aghasoha komoghi ghuyo, aghaikara nabhu.
Hano bhaikaire kuraaghera, Yeesu akaimoki omughaate. Akaghunooku akaghusoonora, akabhaha.
Hayo neho, Ghiteema aabharamokiri amaiso bhakarora, bhakamwongora kubha n-Yeesu. Takeere, akabhasira.
Bhakabhoorani bhakabhughaa, “N-ke kyagherri tughachomeru kuru tukanga komongora, enkaagha eno aare kughambana na itu, aratuhonyorra Amaandeko Amahoreeru ghonchera haare?”
Gho enkaagha eyo eyo, bhaghatanora, bhakagharoka Yerusareemu. Hano bhaahikire, bhakabhona abhatomu ikomi na omwe bha Yeesu, mbaikomaine hamwe na abhanto abhande.
Abhatomu bhayo, bhakabhoorra abheegha bhabhere bhaare bhakabhughaa, “N-obhuheene, Omutemi waito naryokire! Nahyokiire Simooni!”
Neho bhansi, bhaabhooriire abhatomu na abhanto bhayo, amangʼana ghansi ghote ghaare monchera. Bhakabhabhoorra ghote bhongwere Yeesu, hano aare ghusoonora omughaate.
Hano abheegha bha Yeesu bhayo bhaare bhakeere bharaghamba amangʼana ghayo, takeere, Yeesu omwene, akaimerra ghatighati yaabho. Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Mubhe no omurembe!”
Bhaghaitaki, bhakoobhoha bhukongʼu, mbaitegheriire, hande n-ekehwe bharooche.
Ghasi bhoono, Yeesu akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Haake mutaaghwitabherri mometema gheenyu na ghwiki murabhaabhayera? Na ngooke mokuhaha bhukongʼu mometema gheenyu!
Morigheeri amabhoko ghaane na amaghoro ghaane, neho mokumanya neeni mwene! Muntabhetabhe, murore, ekehwe ghitaghoote omobhere na amaghuha, ghote mokundora neeni.”
Hano Yeesu aamarre kubhabhoorra ghayo, akabheereki amabhoko na amaghoro ghaache.
Nankabha bhaarooche ghayo ghasi bhataitabheriiri. Gho okubhambaachomiiru kuru bhakaroghoora. Mbe, akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Mughoote ebhyakori bhinsibhinsi hano?”
Bhakamuha eghetene ghe enswe engeekere.
Aghakiimoki, aghakeri bharamorigheeri.
Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Ghano neghu amangʼana ghano naabhabhooriire enkaagha eno tware hamwe. Nkaabhabhoorra nkabhughaa, ghansi ghano ghaandekiru gharahekeerana ghabhe n-gaare gha amaragherri gha Musa, amaandeko gha abharooti hamwe na gha mo Sabhuri.”
Neho Yeesu abharebhwere amatwe, bhakamanya Amaandeko Amahoreeru.
Ghwiki, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Yandekiru aghoo, Kirisito aranyankibhu no oghwitu, orosiko ro ghatato, araryoka koru mubhaku.
Ku amaragherri ghaane, na ku amanagha gho obhubhaahi bhwe eriina reene, amangʼana ghano, gharareghanibhu kubhanto bhe ebhyaro bhinsi, ghosimeri Yerusareemu. Amangʼana ghayo n-ga abhanto ghotiita ebhibhe bheebho korri bhaabheru.
Inyu ninyu abhaimererri bha amangʼana ghano, kubhanto.
“Mutegheerre! Taata, namarre kubharenga, na bhoono, ndabhareetera ekirengeri gheeche. Ghasi bhoono, mwikare Yerusareemu hano, kohikera enkaagha eno mokuhaabhu amanagha ghe Enkoro Ehoreeru koru mwisaaro ono Taata abharengire.”
Kumaruho, Yeesu aghakangata abheegha bhaache, bhakaghi moghechichi ke Bhetania. Hano bhaahikire eyo, akaghegheri amabhoko ghaache, akabhanooka.
Enkaagha eno aare arabhanooka, akabhatigha. Akaimokibhu koghi mwisaaro.
Bhakamusengera, bhakagharoka Yerusareemu, bhachomiiru bhukongʼu.
Bhaghaikara ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, chensiko chinsi bharakumi Ghiteema.















































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































































Omusoke Teobhiro, mo eghitabho keene ke ghwansa, naakwandekiire ighoro ya amangʼana ghansi ghano Yeesu asimiri ghukora no okweeghi, koru ekimbere ke emeremo gheeche,
kuhekera orosiko runo aagheghiru koghi mwisaaro. Hano aare akeere kugheghu, aakabhaha amaragherri abhatomu bhaache bhano aare ohwere, Akabharagheeri gho enchera ye Enkoro Ehoreeru ighoro ye emeremo ghino bhaghukora.
Gho enkaagha ye chensiko mirongo ene koru runo Yeesu aakuure no koryoka ghooche, Aare kobhahyokera abhatomu bhaache ko ebhimanyeri ebheeru, kubha obhuheene n-omuhoru, na aare kweeghi engʼana ighoro yo obhubhaahi bho Ghiteema
Orosiko ronde Yeesu aghasikana na abhatomu bhaache, akabharagheri akabhughaa, “Mutakaaru momoghi gho Yerusareemu. Mughanyemu, kuhekera hano mokuhaabhu Enkoro Ehoreeru eno Taata aabharengire, ghote muno naare mbaabhooriire.
Yohana Omubhaatiisi, aare arabhaatiisi abhanto ko amanche, ghasi kuru hano chesiko chensuuhu chekuheta, inyu murabhaatiisibhu gho Enkoro Ehoreeru.”
Hano ghwiki abhatomu bha Yeesu bhaikomaine hamwe na Yeesu, bhakamubhoori bhakabhughaa, “Omutemi, enkaagha eno neyu akugharokeri Abhaisiraeri obhubhaahi bhoobho?”
Akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Taata Ghiteema naatunire omwene ko amanagha ghaache aghoo, n-duuhe gharaabhe. Inyu mutaghutakeru kumanya enkaagha ya ghayo.
Ghasi, murabhona chenguru enkaagha ino Enkoro Ehoreeru ekubhaichera, murabha abhaimererri bhaane Yerusareemu, ahase hansi ha Yuuteya, na Samaariya, kuhekera ahase hansi monse.”
Hano Yeesu aamarre kubhabhoorra abhatomu bhaache ghayo, bhansi bhaare komorigheeri. Hayo hayo akagheghu koghi mwisaaro. Risaaro rikamoghubha, bhatamorooche ghwiki.
Hano bhaare kugharamera ighoro, bhakarora Yeesu araghi mwisaaro, hari remwe abhanto bhabhere bhakaimerra haghuhe nabhu bhaare bhaswarre chingebho chindabhu.
Abhanto bhayo bhakabhughaa, “Inyu Abhaghariraaya bhano, ake mwimeeriire hano, eno muragharamera mwisaaro? Yeesu oyo aimokiribhu koru haare inyu koghi mwisaaro, kehayo hayo aghuucha ghwiki, ghote bhuno momorooche araghi.”
Kumaruho, abhatomu bhayo bhakagharoka Yerusareemu, koru korukereghe runo rware kubherekeru orukereghe rwe Emiseituuni, runo rware haghuhe ghote ekiromiita emwe koru momoghi gho Yerusareemu.
Hano bhaahikire Yerusareemu hayo, bhaghasoha mo eghechumba kye eghorofa kino bhaare ghwikara. Abhatomu bhayo bhaare, Petiro, Yohana, Yaakobho, Antireya, Firipo, Tomaaso, Bharitoromaayo, Mataayo, Yaakobho mura wa Aribhaayo, Simeoni Muserote, na Yuuta mura wa Yaakobho.
Bhayo bhansi ghwikomana bhaare hayo, ghusaasaama Ghiteema ko omotema ghomwe, hamwe na Mariyamu nyakuwaabho Yeesu, na abhaghaikoro abhande, na bhamura bhaabho Yeesu.
Gho chensiko chiyo, Petiro akaimerra ghati yaabho abhaitabherri bha Yeesu bhano mbaikomaine muyo, bhaare ghote righana remwe na mirongo ebhere. Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa,
“Bhaghendi bhaane, amangʼana ghano ghaandekiru mo Amandeko gha Ghiteema ighoro ya Yuuta, ono aahiire abhanto bhaghoote Yeesu, yaare ghotunu ghahekerane. Amangʼana ghano ghaaghambiru no omutemi Tauti gho Enkoro Ehoreeru.
Yuuta no omutomu mughendi waito aare, hamwe twahaabhiru emeremo ghino.”
Yuuta ono Petiro akughambera hano, naaghoore omoghondo ko chembiri chino aabhwine koru ko engʼana yaache ensineenu. Kumaruho, akagho komoghondo ghuyo kebhumari, akabhasooka enda, ebhyanda bheeche bhinsi bhighiteka kibhara.
Engʼana eyo, ikamanyikana ko abhamenyi bhansi bha Yerusareemu. Ke hayo, omoghondo ghuyo, bhaghaghubherekera eriina ko ekighambo keebho, Hakeri Tama, okwerekerri ghooche n-omoghondo ghwa Amaanyinga.
Ghwiki, Petiro akaghenderri kughamba arabhughaa, “Moghitabho kye Esabhuri yandekiru ighoro ya Yuuta, kirabhughaa, ‘Omoghi ghooche ghutame ghutaana ghento, omonto wunsiwunsi, ataghaacha kumenyamu.’ “Ghwiki yandekiru irabhughaa, ‘Omonto owonde agheghe omweya ghooche ghwe emeremo ghyo obhotomu.’
“Ko riyo, turatunu tuchaghore omonto owonde ono tware kohinani nawe, enkaagha yinsi eno Omutemi Yeesu aare hamwe na itu,
kuwansera enkaagha eno Yeesu abhaatiisiru na Yohana, kuhekera koimokibhu ghooche koghi mwisaaro. Tubhe turasakerani nawe, kureghani okuryoka ko Yeesu.”
Ghwiki, bhakaghamba amariina gha abhanto bhabhere. Wa ghwansa, n-yusubhu, eriina erende aare kubherekeru Bharisabha ghwiki erende Yusito. Na wa kabhere, aare kubherekeru Matiya.
Kumaruho, bhaghasaasaama Yeesu bharabhughaa, “Omutemi, iye newe umanyire emetema ghya abhanto bhansi. Ko riyo, turaghusabha utwereki, ne-uye uchaghwiire ghati ya bhabhere bhano,
kuru agheghe omweya ghwe emeremo ghyo obhutomu ghino Yuuta aatighire. Ewe hano aakuure, aaghire ahase hano omorro ghotokorima.”
Neho bhaatamire chekuura na chikaghwera Matiya. Neho, Matiya oyo, engiribhu ko abhatomu abhande bhaare ikomi na omwe.
Hano orosiko rwe enyangi ya Bhentekosite rwahikire, abhaitabherri bhansi bha Yeesu, hamwe bhaare bhaikomaine monyumba.
Hari remwe, bhakooghu koru mwisaaro riraka rirahuuta ghote ekiirumbe, kighaacha kighiichora enyumba yinsi muyo bhaare bhaikaire.
Neho bhyabhahyokire ebhinto ghote ebhemore bhyo omorro . Ebhinto bhiyo, bhighasancha, bhighasekera ighoro ya kira omwe waabho.
Abhanto bhayo bhansi bhaghaichuribhu Enkoro Ehoreeru, bhaghasimi kughamba kira omonto ko ebhighambo ebhende bhino bhitaare ebheebho, ghote muno Enkoro Ehoreeru aare arabharagheeri kughamba.
Ghwiki, neho bhaare Yerusareemu hayo, Abhayahuti bhano bhaasookire Ghiteema. Abhayahuti bhayo, bhaare koru ko ebhyaro bhinsi.
Hano bhooghuure riraka rya amangʼana ghayo, eghikomo eghekoro kya abhanto ghikaikomana hamwe. Bhansi bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu, gho okubha kira omwe waabho, noghwiire ekighambo gheeche kiraghambu na abhaitabherri bha Yeesu bhaare.
Bhansi bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu, bhakabhoorani bharabhughaa, “Muntegheerre! Abhanto bhano bhansi bhakughamba bhatare Abhaghariraaya?
Bhoono mbwe ibhaire, itu bhansi turabhooghu bharaghamba ebhighambo bhe esemoka yiitu?
Na ghati yiito, nehobhaani abhanto koru ko ebhyaro bhe Pariti, Medi, Erami. Na abhande koru ko ebhyaro bhe Mesobhotamiya, Yuuteya, Kabhatokiya, Ponto, na Asiya,
Furighiya, Pamufiiriya, na Miisiri. Na abhande koru orubhareka ro ghati ye ekyaro ke Ribhiya, bhino bheeni haghuhe no omoghi gho Kirene. Abhande n-Abhayahuti bhano bhakoru momoghi gho Ruumi. Ghati yaabho neho bhaare abhande esemoka yaabho n-Abhayahuti, na abhande mbaasohire mo Bhuyahuti ko ghusengera Ghiteema.
Abhande n-Abhakerete na abhande na-Abhaarabhu. Ghasi itu bhansi, nkobhooghu tooni bharaitumi Ghiteema ko amakora ghaache amakoro, ko ebhighambo bhiitu!”
Abhanto bhansi bhano bhaare hayo, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu na bhatamanyire kino kyare ghukoru. Bhakabha bharabhorana bharabhughaa, “Kanaa bhamure ekyereki kya amangʼana ghayo n-kiihe?”
Ghasi abhamwe bhaabho, bhakabhanoghori abhaitabherri bhayo, bharabhughaa, “Mbarewire amaro ghe emisabhiibhu!”
Neho Petiro aimeriire hamwe na abhatomu bhaghendi bhaache ikomi na omwe bhaare. Akabhoorra eghikomo kya abhanto bhayo, ko riraka rikoro akabhughaa, “Inyu Abhayahuti bha Yerusareemu bhano, na inyu Abhayahuti bho koru ko ebhyaro ebhende, Muntegheerre bhwaheene, mbabhoorre!
Abhanto bhano bhatareewire, ghote muno moghwitegherra. Ikeere etabhoori bhukongʼu, n-saa taatu yeeni!
Ghasi amangʼana ghayo, neghu ghaare, Ghiteema abhughire kuhetera omurooti waache Yoweri, akabhughaa,
‘Gho chensiko cho omohiko, Ghiteema arabhugha, ndasekeri Enkoro Ehoreeru waane ighoro ya abhanto bhansi. Abhamura na abhanke bhaanyu bhararuusi obhurooti, abhaana bhaanyu bhararora amaroro, na abhagharuka bhararoota chindooto.
Gho chensiko chiyo, ndasekeri Enkoro Ehoreeru waane kuru ko abhabhaghasi bhaane, bhe ghesubhe na bhe ekighaikoro, bhansi bhararuusi obhurooti.
Ndakora amakono ighoro mwisaaro ne ebhimanyerri monse muno. Abhanto bhararora ebhimanyerri bhya amaanyinga, omorro, ne endumbe ke eryooki.
Ereebha riraishoori kubha ekeruutu, no omweri ghurabha omubheretu kya amaanyinga. Ghansi ghayo , gharakangata kubha ghwansa, hano orosiko ro Omutemi Ghiteema rutamara ruucha, runo rooni n-orokoro na oruchomu bhukongʼu.
Enkaagha eyo, kira omonto uno akubha arasaasaama ko ghwitengʼera eriina ryo Omutemi, aratooribhu.’”
Petiro akaghenderri kughamba arabhughaa, “Inyu abhanto bha Abhaisiraeri, Muntegheerre amangʼana ghano nkubhabhoorra! Ghiteema omwene aamutomire haare inyu. Akabheereki bhurabhu aghoo arakora emeremo kuhetera Yeesu wa Naasareeti, gho enchera ye ebhiroghooro, amakono na ebhimanyerri. Inyu abheene mumanyire ghayo ghansi.
Yeesu ono atooruubhu mumabhoko ghaanyu, ghote bhuno Ghiteema omwene aatunire koru ekimbere. Na inyu mukamwitera komusarabha, gho enchera ya abhanto abhasari.
Ghasi Ghiteema akamoryokora koru mubhaku, akamutoori ko obhooro bho oroku, gho okubha itaare ghutakeru aku!
Kuru omutemi Tauti, naarootire amangʼana gha Yeesu ghano ghaare kobhughaa, ‘Nkomurora naare Omutemi Ghiteema mbere yaane, enkaagha yinsi. Na gho okubha no orubhareka roone ro bhoryo aare, ntengosingisibhu.
Ko riyo, omotema ghoone ghughoote amachomeru bhukongʼu, ghwiki ororeme roone ruraririyeta. Kuru omobhere ghoone, ghurikara mo obhuhoru,
gho okubha iye Omutemi Ghiteema, toghontigha nyaari. Eni n-omubhaghasi waacho omuhoreeru, na utaghwitabherri omobhere ghoone ghoghundere nyaari eyo.
Iye onyerekeriri enchera yo obhuhoru. Uraaha amachomeru amaaru, gho okubha haghuhe ooni na eni.’”
Ghwiki Petiro akaghenderri kughamba arabhughaa, “Bhaghendi bhaane, nkunaghi neeni kobhabhoorra obhuheene aghoo, sookoro waito omutemi Tauti taighambire omwene gho okubha, naakuure, akaryeku ne embeehera yaache ikeere yeeho kuru reero.
Tauti oyo no omurooti aare , namanyire kubha, Ghiteema aamurengiire gho ekemiira aghoo, arakora omonto omwe koru mo rikora reeche, kubha omukangati ighoro yo obhukangati bhooche.
Tauti naarooche amangʼana ghano ghakubha, akaghamba ighoro yo koryokoru ko Kirisitoaghoo, Kirisito tatighiru nyaari he, no omobhere ghooche ghutaaghundire.
Ghiteema naamoryokwiire, Yeesu oyo koru mobhaku, na itu bhansi n-abhaimererri bhe engʼana eyo.
Ghiteema amoriiniri, no komukorra omunene, korri amutoore kubhoko koryo ghooche. Na Taata Ghiteema newe akorre ghote bhuno aarengire aghoo, akaha Yeesu Enkoro Ehoreeru ghokugheri yiitu. .
Tauti omwene tariinire no oghusoha mwisaaro, Ghasi akabhughaa, ‘Omutemi Ghiteema aakamubhora Omutemi waane akabhughaa, “Ikara orubhareka roone ro bhoryo,
kuhekera hano ngutoora abhabhisa bhaacho harense bhabhe ghote ebhetumbe bhyo oghutoora amaghoro ghaacho.”’”
Petiro akamarerri kughamba akabhughaa, “Ko riyo, Abhaisiraeri bhansi, mumanye obhuheene aghoo, Ghiteema akorre Yeesu kubha Omutemi na Kirisito. Ghasi inyu mukamwita oyo oyo, ghokomubhamba komusarabha!”
Ghwiki, abhanto bhayo hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu. Kumaruho, bhakabhoori Petiro na abhatomu abhande bhakabhughaa, “Bhamura bhiitu, bhoono n-ke turaakore?”
Petiro akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Kira omwe waanyu amwishooreri Ghiteema, na abhaatiisibhu ko eriina re Yeesu Kirisito, kuru abheeru ebhibhe, na arahaabhu Enkoro Ehoreeru.
Mumanye aghoo, okurengi kuno Ghiteema aarengire, kwaare gh-okugheri yaanyu, orwibhoro roonyu, na abhande bhano bhaare kure. Ekyereki gheeche n-ke bhansi bhano Omutemi Ghiteema waito arabhabherekera.”
Petiro akaghenderri kubhabhoorra amangʼana aghande amaaru no kubhaseghani arabhughaa, “Momusabhe Ghiteema abhatoori koru ko orwibhoro orosineenu runo, kuru ataghaacha kubhakengera ekiina!”
Orosiko ruyo, abhanto ghote ebhikwe bhitato [3,000] bhaghaitabherri amangʼana ghano Petiro abhabhooriire, bhakabhaatiisibhu. Kumaruho, bhakengeribhu ko eghikomo kya abheegha bha Yeesu.
Abheegha bhansi, bhakaghenderri kweegha koru ko abhatomu bha Yeesu. Hamwe bhaare ghusakerani , ghusoonora omughaate,na hamwe bhaare ghusaasaama Ghiteema .
Abhatomu bhayo, bhaare bharakorra amakono na ebhimanyerri ebheeru. Kuru kira omonto akabha ne ehaho.
Ghwiki, abhaitabherri bhansi bhaare no obhomwe, bhaare ghusanga hamwe no ghotweena ebhinto bheebho bhino bhaare nabhyu.
Bhaare bharaghori ebhinto bheebho, ne chembiri chino bhaare kubhona, mbaatwenire, ghokurengʼaana ke bhuno kira omwe aare ghotuna.
Chensiko chinsi bhaare ghosikana mo ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema. Ghasi, enkaagha yo oghusoonora omughaate, bhaare ghosikana monyumba yaabho, bhaare kuraaghera hamwe ko amachomeru na ko omotema gho obhuheene,
bhaare ghwitumi Ghiteema, mbhaasaighiru na abhanto bhansi. Na kira orosiko, Omutemi Yeesu aare kwengeri abhanto bhano bhaamwitabheriiri ko kubhatoori.
Orosiko romwe, saa kenda yo omwise, Petiro na Yohana mbaghiire ko ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema. Ensa eyo neyu yaare ya abhanto ghusaasaama Ghiteema.
Ko ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema hayo, ghwaareho omurango ghuno ghware kubherekeru aghoo, Omuchomu. Komurango hayo aareho omonto omwe uno aare omubheeru koru kwibhoru ghooche. Kira orosiko naatooriibhu mo egheseku kiyo asabhe chembiri ko abhanto bhano bhaaghusoha mo ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema muyo.
Omubheeru oyo, hano aarooche Petiro na Yohana bharasoha mo ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema muyo, akabhasabha chembiri.
Petiro na Yohana bhakamorigheeri bhukongʼu, kumaruho Petiro akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Otorigheeri itu!”
Akabharigheeri, ino araghanya kubhona eghento koru haarebhu.
Ghwiki, Petiro akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Eni tingoote chembiri chinsi chinsi cho oghokuha, ghasi kino ngoote nekyu ngokuha.” Neho amubhooriire akabhughaa, “Ko eriina re Yeesu Kirisito wa Naasareeti, imerra na ghenda!”
Kumaruho Petiro akamughoota okubhoko ko bhoryo, akamwimerri. Hayo hayo amaghoro ne ebhiimo bheeche bhya amaghoro bhikabha ne chenguru.
Akabhoka ghuru akaimerra, aghasimi kughenda omwene. Aghasoha ko ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema hamwe na Petiro na Yohana, ino aratuumatuuma na araitumi Ghiteema.
Abhanto bhansi bhakamurora araghenda na ino aramwitumi Ghiteema.
Na hano mbaamanyire kubha, omonto oyo wo-oore aare ghusabhasabha mo egheseku kya ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema kino kyare kubherekeru aghoo, Omuchomu, abhanto bhansi bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu ko ghano ghaamobhwine.
Enkaagha eyo, omonto oyo, aare aghooteriire Petiro na Yohana. Abhanto bhansi bhaare kuroghoora bhukongʼu, bhakaryera hamwe, bhakaghi ghwikomana ghokihooro kya ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema, ko ahase hano hakubherekeru aghoo, rihooru re Suremani. Bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu.
Hano Petiro aarooche abhanto bhayo, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Bhano Abhaisiraeri bhaghendi bhaane, ngooke amangʼana ghano ghakobharoghoori? Ake, muratumoghoorra? Muraitegherra aghoo, omonto ono nahoriibhu ko amanagha ghiitu? Ghasi gho okubha itu ntuminyire ghote Ghiteema aghotuna? Hasehe!
Tare niigho yeeni! Ghiteema wa bhasookoro bhiitu, Bhurahamu, Isaaka, na Yaakobho, newe amwitumiri Yeesu omubhaghasi waache, (newe omuhori wa ono.) Na Yeesu newe inyu mwaamohire ghwitongo akengeru ekiina kyo oghwitu! Kuru omubhaahi Bhiraato, enkaagha eno aare ghotuna amuhatore, inyu mwangire.
Mughasabha Bhiraato aghoo, abhatanchoore omwiti, wunsi akabhatanchorra Yeesu. ono aare omuhoreeru no omuheene, ghasi inyu mwaamwangire.
Ke hayo, mukamwita ono aare esemoka yo obhuhoru. Ghasi, Ghiteema naamoryokwire koru mobhaku, na itu nebhu abhaimererri bho okoryoka ghooche.
Ghwiki, omonto ono mokurora hano, momumanyire bhwaheene. Abhwine chenguru ko amanagha ghe eriina re Yeesu, gho enchera yo ghwiitabherri eriina riyo. Gho komwitabherri Yeesu, ahorre kemwe, ghote muno inyu abheene mokurora.
“Bhoono abhanto bha waito, nimanyire aghoo, mwaamwitire Yeesu ghokwanga kumanya kino mware ghukora, na kuru abhabhaahi bhaanyu bhatamanyire kino bhaakorre.
Ghasi ko enchera eno, Ghiteema akahekerani amangʼana ghano aabhughire ko abharooti bhansi aghoo, Kirisito waache aranyankibhu.
Ko riyo, motiite ebhibhe bheenyu, mwishooreri Ghiteema, kuru abhaabhere ebhibhe bhyeenyu. Ko ghukora kehayo, Omutemi Ghiteema arabhamuunyi gho okubhaho ghooche,
na aratoma Kirisito. Kirisito oyo newe Yeesu uno ohwiiru koru ekimbere gho okugheri yaanyu.
Ghasi Yeesu, ewe iratunu abhe mwisaaro, kuhekera enkaagha ino Ghiteema aghukora ebhinto bhinsi bhohe, ghote aaghambire koru kare, ko enchera ya abharooti bhaache abhahoreeru.
“Omurooti Musa akabhughaa, ‘Ghati yaanyu, Omutemi Ghiteema waito arabhohoora omurooti ghote eni. Muntegheerre bhwaheene kira engʼana eno akobhabhoorra.
Omonto wunsiwunsi ono atakomutegherra omurooti oyo, araghiru no oghosikibhu makora ghansi koru ko abhanto bhano bhaghitabherri Ghiteema.’
Kuru abharooti bhansi, kuwansera Saamweri na bhano bhaachire nyuma, mbaareghani amangʼana ghano ngukoru ghaani mo chensiko chino.
Obhurengi bhuno Ghiteema naarusiri ko enchera ya abharooti, gh-okugheri koonyu. Na mrasanga riraghano rino Ghiteema aakorre na bhasookoro bhaanyu, ghote bhuno aabhooriire Bhurahamu akabhughaa, ‘Ko kuhetera orwibhoro rooche, abhanto bhansi bharanooku.’
Ghwiki, Ghiteema naamohwire Yeesu, omubhaghasi waache, akamutoma ghati yaanyu ghwansa, kuru abhanooke ghokubhahonchora kira omwe koru mo ebhibhe bheeche.”
Hano Petiro na Yohana bhaare bhakeere bharaghambana na abhanto bhayo, abhasengeri, Amasatukaayo no omokoro wa abharendi bha ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema, bhakahika.
Abhakoro bhayo, bhaghakarra bhukongʼu, gho okubha Petiro na Yohana bhaare kweeghi abhanto no kobhabhoorra aghoo, Yeesu aaryokire koru mobhaku, na okuryoka ghooche kureereki aghoo, Ghiteema araryokora abhaku.
Ko riyo, bhakaghoota Petiro na Yohana. Na gho okubha obhotiko bhware bhusohire, bhakabhatoora mwighereza kuhekera etabhoori yaache.
Ghasi, amangʼana ghano Petiro na Yohana bhaare bhamaare kubhoorra abhanto bhe eghikomo kiyo, abhaaru ghati yaabho mbaghaitabherri. Ekirengero kya abhasubhe abheene, bhano bhaare bhaitabheriiri Yeesu, ikahika ghote ebhikwe bhitaano [5,000].
Etabhoori yaache, abhasengeri abhakoro bha Abhayahuti na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa, bhaghaikomana Yerusareemu hayo.
Ghokiina kiyo, bhaareho Anasi, uno aare omusengeri omokoro, hamwe na Kayabha, Yohana, Arekisanda, na abhanto abhande koru gho ekehita kyo omusengeri omokoro.
Mbe, bhakabhugha aghoo, Petiro na Yohana bhaaretu mwitongo. Bhakabhaimeeri ghatighati yaabho, bhaghasimi kobhabhoori bharabhughaa, “Amangʼana ghayo ghano mware ghukora, mwakorre ko amanagha ke? Ghasi ko amanagha gha uye?”
Hayo, Petiro aani aichwire Enkoro Ehoreeru, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Inyu abhakangati bha abhanto na abhakoro bha Abhayahuti!
Reero muratubhoori amaswari gho okubha ntutoori omonto ono aare omubheeru na muratubhoori bhuno ahoriibhu.
Mbe, inyu bhansi, hamwe na Abhaisiraeri abhande bhansi, ndatuna mumanye obhuheene aghoo, omonto ono aimeriire mbere yaanyu, nahorre ko amanagha ghe eriina re Yeesu Kirisito wa Naasareeti. Yeesu newe woore mwaamwitire komusarabha, ghasi Ghiteema akamoryokora koru mobhaku.
Ewe newe Amandeko Amahoreeru gharabhugha ighoro yaache gharabhughaa , ‘Righena rino inyu abhaabheki mwangire, bhoono neru ribhaire righena rikoro ryo omosingi.’
“Obhutoori bhunsi haare eriina re Yeesu bhoghutoka! Ritareho eriina erende monse, ghukera Yeesu, rino Ghiteema ahaire abhanto, korri bhabhone ghutooribhu!”
Hano abhakoro bhe ritongo bhayo, bhaarooche ghote Petiro na Yohana bhakughamba kobhukare, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu, gho okubha mbamanyire aghoo abhatomu bhayo bhatare abhasomi hande bhataghote obhungʼaini. Ghasi bhakamanya aghoo, Yeesu hamwe aani nabhu.
Na ko bhoore mbaarooche omonto ono aare ahoriibhu aimeriire hamwe na Petiro na Yohana, engʼana yo kugharokeri ikabhabhora.
Kumaruho, abhakoro bhayo, bhakahamera Peturo na Yohana bharu mwitongo muyo. Ebhu abheene bhaghatama bhararagherani bhuno bharakorre.
Bhakabhoorani bharabhughaa, “Mbwe Tokobhakora abhanto bhano? Abhamenyi bhansi bha Yerusareemu hano, bhamanyire aghoo, mbakorre ekimanyerri kino eghekoro, na itu tutaghutora kubhanyeera chinkaani.
Ghasi engʼana ino itaghasancha bhukongʼu ko abhanto, tubhaseghani kughambana no omonto wunsiwunsi ghwiki ko eriina re Yeesu.”
Hano abhakoro bhe ritongo bhayo bhaamarre, bhakabherekera Petiro na Yohana. Bhakabhaseghani ko obhorro bharabhughaa, “Mutaghaacha kughamba kuru mutakeeghi ghwiki ko eriina re Yeesu oyo!”
Ghasi, Petiro na Yohana bhakabhagharokeri bhakabhughaa, “Inyu abheene mukenge ekiina, ghote n-bhwaheene mbere ya Ghiteema, kubhategherra inyu ghukera Ghiteema omwene.
Itu, tutaghotigha kughamba ighoro ya amangʼana ghano twaaroche no okooghu!”
Hano Petiro na Yohana bhaamarre kughamba ghayo, abhakoro bhe ritongo riyo, bhakabhahahi ko obhorro bhukongʼu, kumaruho bhakabhahatora bhaghende echaabho. Bhataabhwine enchera yo kubhaghoota enchagho, gho okubha abhanto bhansi bhaare bharamwitumi Ghiteema bhukongʼu ighoro yo obhuhorri bho omubheeru.
Mbaamanyire aghoo, omonto oyo ahoriibhu, naabheere koru kwibhoru ghooche na aare ahikiri emeeka mirongo ene.
Hano Petiro na Yohana bhaahatiru, bhakagharoka ko abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaabho. Bhakabhabhoorra amangʼana ghansi ghano bhaabhooriiru na abhakoro bha abhasengeri na abhakoro bha Abhayahuti.
Hano bhaghendi bhaabho bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhansi hamwe bhaghasimi ghusaasaama Ghiteema ko omotema ghomwe bharabhughaa, “Eee Omutemi, omokoro wa bhinsi. Iye newe waateemire risaaro, ense, ne chinyancha na bhinsi bhino bheemu.
Iye ukaghamba gho Enkoro Ehoreeru kuhetera omonu gho sookoro yiitu Tauti omubhaghasi waacho, ukabhughaa, ‘Ngooke abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti bhaghukarra? Na ngooke amakabhira gha Abhaisiraeri bhaghwitegherra ghukora emeremo ghino ghitaana chiwaara?
Abhakama bhe ense na abhabhaahi mbaikomaine hamwe, korri bhamwange Omutemi Ghiteema, na Kirisito waache.’
“N-obhuheene aghoo, omukama Herote Antibhasi na Bhontio Bhiraato, mbaikomaine hamwe Abhaisiraeri na abhanto bhano bhatare Abhaisiraeri momoghi ghuno, korri bhamwange Yeesu omubhaghasi waacho omuhoreeru, ono wachaghwiire abhe Kirisito.
Amangʼana ghayo mbakorre, niigho waatunire ghakoru koru ekimbere? Ghwiki waghakangatire ko amanagha ghaacho?.
Bhoono Omutemi Ghiteema waitu, umarre kumanya bhuno bhaghotobhohi! Otusakeri itu abhabhaghasi bhaacho, kureghani amangʼana ghaacho kobhukare obhokoro
Urengore okubhoko ghoocho kuhori abhanto, ebhimanyerri na amakono bhikoru ko eriina re Yeesu, omubhaghasi waacho omuhoreeru!”
Hano bhaamarre ghusaasaama Ghiteema, ahase hano bhaare mbaikomaine, haghasingisibhu. Bhansi bhaghaichuribhu Enkoro Ehoreeru, bhakaghenderri kweeghi abhanto amangʼana gha Ghiteema kobhukare.
Abhaitabherri bhansi, bhaare no obhomwe, ko amaitegherro ghaabho, ne chinkoro chaabho. Taareho kuru omonto omwe ono abhughire aghoo, ebhinto bhino aghoote n-ebheeche omwene omwene. Hamwe bhaare ghusanga ebhinto bhinsi.
Abhatomu bha Yeesu bhaare kureghaneri abhanto koghwikongʼi oghokoro aghoo, Omutemi Yeesu naaryokire. Na Ghiteema akabhanooka bhukongʼu.
Atareho omonto ghati yaabho ono asohiiru eghento, gho okubha bhaare bhaghoote ebhewancha ne chenyumba mbaabhighoori, bhakareetera abhatomu chembiri chino bhaabhwine
Chembiri chiyo, abhatomu bhaare bharachetweni ko abhanto, kurengʼaana na bhuno omonto akwenda.
Mbe aareho Omuraawi omwe omwibhoru wa Kipuro eriina reeche aare kubherekeru Yusubhu, ghasi abheegha bha Yeesu bhakamuha eriina Bharinabha (ekyereki gheeche kirabhughaa, “Omonto ono akubhaghaghana omotema”).
Bharinabha oyo naghoori omoghondo ghooche. Ne chembiri chino aabhwine, akabhaha abhatomu bhayo.
Aareho omonto nyabhurebhe, aare kubherekeru Anania. Na mughaache aare kubherekeru Sabhira. Bhayo bhansi bhakaghori omoghondo ghoobho.
Hano bhamaare kughori omoghondo ghuyo, Anania akabhisa chembiri echende koru gho chembiri chino bhaabhwine. Mbaitabherani na mughaache ghukora kehayo. Kumaruho, Anania akaimoki chembiri chino chaatamire, akaghi akabhaha abhatomu bha Yeesu, arabhugha aghoo nechu chinsi chino abhwine.
Ghasi, Petiro akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Iye Anania! Ake Risambu reghusoheriire momotema ghoocho, na righeeri ughambire obhurongo ko Enkoro Ehoreeru? Obhughire aghoo, ureetire chembiri chinsi, na eno notighire chembiri echende chino obhwine ko obhughori bho omoghondo!
Hano waare ukeere kughori omoghondo, n-oghoocho ghware , na hano wamarre koghughori, chembiri chiyo ne chaacho chaare, ngochetumia waare ghote okwenda. Bhoono, ghoke ukorre kehayo momotema ghoocho, witegherirre ghukora engʼana ke eyo? Utaghambire obhurongo ko abhanto, ghasi, ughambire obhurongo haare Ghiteema!”
Anania hano ooghuure amangʼana ghayo, hari remwe akagho harense aghaku. Abhanto bhansi bhano bhooghuure engʼana eyo, bhakoobhoha bhukongʼu.
Kumaruho abhamura bhakaimerra bhaghaghokundekeri omobhere ghooche ne chingebho, bhakamohira kibhara yo omoghi, bhakamoryeka.
Hano chinsaa isato chaahetire, mughaache wunsi akahika aghasoha moghechumba muyo, eno atamanyire kino kebhwiine mosubhe waache.
Petiro akamubhoori akabhughaa, “Mborra, chino nechu chembiri chinsi chino mobhwine hano mwaaghori omoghondo ghoonyu?” wunsi akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Nechu changʼana twaaghori!”
Petiro akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “N-gooke, iye na omosubhe waacho mwaaitabherani ghusaki kungʼaina Enkoro Ehoreeru wo Omutemi Ghiteema? Righeeri, abhamura bhano mbaryekire omusubhe waacho mbagharokire, hayo bhaani mogheseku, bharakohira kibhara na iye ghwiki!”
Hari remwe, Sabhira wunsi akagho harense mbere ya amaghoro gha Petiro, aghaku hayo hayo. Kumaruho abhamura bhayo bhaghasoha, bhakabhona Sabhira wunsi akuure. Bhakamorichoki kibhara, bhakamoryeka haghuhe ne embeehera ya omusubhe waache.
Amangʼana ghayo ghakagheri abhanto bhansi bha mokanisa, hamwe na abhande bhansi bhano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaghatiina bhukongʼu.
Abhatomu bha Yeesu, bhaakorre ebhimanyerri na amakono amaaru ko abhanto. Ghwiki abhaitabherri bhaare bhansi bhaikomaine ko omotema ghomwe, ko ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, ko ahase hano hakubherekeru Ritongo re Suremani.
Abhanto bhano bhataitabheriiri Yeesu, bhaare bharabhakumi bhukongʼu abhaitabherri bhayo, ghasi bhakoobhoha kughootana nabhu, kuru omwe.
Abhanto abhande abhaaru, abhasubhe na abhaghaikoro bhaitabheriiri Omutemi Yeesu, ekirengero keebho kyare kwengeri bhukongʼu.
Kurengʼaana na amakono gha abhatomu, abhanto bhaare kureeta abharwire kibhara haghuhe ne enchera. Eno bhabharairi kochimborre na kobhiragho, korri Petiro hano akuheta, ekiriiri gheeche kebhaturi abhande mubhayo, bhahore.
Gho chensiko echaaru, abhanto abhaaru bhaare bharaacha koru ko emeghi ghe mbareka ya Yerusareemu. Mbaaretire abharwire bhaabho na bhano bhaare bhaghootiru ne emisambu, na bhansi mbaahoribhu.
Kumaruho omusengeri omokoro, na abhaghendi bhaache bhansi bhe eghikomo kya Amasatukaayo, bhakabhakorra orunyeera abhatomu bha Yeesu.
Ko riyo, bhakaghoota abhatomu bhayo, bhakabhabhoha mokibhohe eghekoro.
Ghasi obhotiko bhuyo, maraika wo Omutemi Ghiteema aghaacha, aghasengora ebheseku bhwe ebhibhohe bhiyo, akabharichoki kibhara. Kumaruho akabhabhoorra akabhughaa,
“Mughende mwimerre ko ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, mubhoorre abhanto amangʼana ghansi ighoro ya obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi!”
Hano abhatomu bhayo, bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhakamuta koghi ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, bhakaghenderri kweeghi abhanto muyo. Enkaagha eyo eyo, omusengeri omokoro, hamwe na bhaare bhaghendi bhaache, bhakabherekera abhakoro bhansi bha Abhaisiraeri bhasikane ghwitongo rikoro. Bhaghatoma abharendi mokibhohe, bhagheere abhatomu bhaare.
Ghasi, abharendi bhayo hano bhaasohire muyo, bhataabhwine abhatomu bhaare. Kumaruho bhakagharoka ko abhakoro bhe ritongo, bhakabhabhoorra bhakabhughaa,
“Hano twahikire mokibhohe, tukabhona emirango ghinsi ghighaire bhwaheene, na abharendi bhaimeeriire mbere ye emirango. Ghasi hano twaighwiire emirango na ghusoha morense, tutabhwine omonto wunsiwunsi!”
Mbe, omokoro wa abharendi bha ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema na abhakoro bha abhasengeri, hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaghatamu kumanya, bhakabhoorani bhakabhughaa, “Engʼana eyo bhwe ibhaire?”
Neho omonto omwe aichire, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Muntegheerre! Abhanto bhano mwaabhohire mokibhohe, ko ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema bhaani bhareeghi abhanto!”
Neho omokoro wa abharendi bha ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema akaghiire hamwe na abhasirikare bhakareeta abhatomu bhaare. Ghasi bhaakorre kehayo tare gho chenguru, gho okubha mbobhohire ghutemu amaghena na abhanto.
Mbe, bhakabhareeta ko ritongo rikoro, Bhakabhaimeeri mbere ya bhansi. Kumaruho omusengeri omokoro akabhabhoori akabhughaa,
“Tutabhaseghani ko obhorro aghoo, motighe kweeghi abhanto ko eriina re Yeesu? Ghasi inyu murasanchi ameeghi ghaanyu ighoro yaache, momoghi ghunsi gho Yerusareemu! Ghwiki murabhugha aghoo, amaanyinga gho Oghoku ghooche yeeni ighoro yiitu!”
Petiro na abhatomu bhaghendi bhaache, bhakabhoorra abhagharuka bhayo bhakabhughaa, “Iratunu komwighwera Ghiteema, ghukera abhanto!
Inyu mughaita Yeesu gho komubhamba komusarabha, ghasi Ghiteema wa bhasookoro bhiitu naamoryokwiire.
Kumaruho akamoriini no okomuha obhubhaahi bho komutoora orubhareka rooche ro bhoryo, korri abhe Omubhaahi na Omutoori wa abhanto. Ghiteema aamukorre kehayo, korri abhasakeri Abhaisiraeri bhatighe ebhibhe bheebho, na bhaabheru.
Itu hamwe ne Enkoro Ehoreeru ono Ghiteema abhahaire bhansi bhano bhakomusooka, n-abhaimererri bha amangʼana ghayo ghansi.”
Abhakoro bhayo hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaghakarra bhukongʼu, na bhaare ghuseemi kubhaita abhatomu bhayo.
Ghasi mwitongo muyo, aaremu Omubharisaayo owonde, aare kubherekeru Ghamarieri. Ghamarieri oyo, aare omweghi wa amaragherri gha Musa, na aare ghusooku bhukongʼu na abhanto bhansi. Akaimerra mbere ya abhanto bhe ritongo, aghakenga ekiina aghoo, abhatomu bharichokibhu kibhara gho enkaagha ensuuhu.
Kumaruho akabhabhoorra abhakoro bhaghendi bhaache bhayo akabhughaa, “Inyu abhanto bha Abhaisiraeri, ghwansa Muntegheerre bhwaheene, mutamara mukorra engʼana ino moghotuna ghukorra abhanto bhano!
Inyu, mohiite chensiko chino chaahetire, naahyokire omonto omwe ono aare kubherekeru Tauti. Tauti oyo, naitamiri aghoo, n-omonto omokoro, na abhanto ghote maghana ane [400] bhaghasakerani nawe. Ghasi komohiko, aghaitu, bhansi bhano bhaamwitabheriiri, bhaghatyamba. Na emeremo gheebho ghinsi ghighasira.
Ghwiki, enkaagha yo kubhara abhanto, naahyokire omonto owonde. Omonto oyo, aare Omughariraaya, eriina reeche aare kubherekeru Yuuta. Ewe wunsi naabhwine abhanto bho komutambana, ghasi wunsi aghaitu, na bhansi bhano bhaamwitabheriiri bhaghatyamba.
Mbe bhoono, ndabharagheri aghoo, motighe abhanto bhano! Mutakaabhakorra engʼana yinsiyinsi ensineenu. Ghote emeremo gheebho ghino, ghyaaseemiribhu na abhanto, ghirasira eghyene.
Ghasi, ghote emeremo ghiyo, n-ghe Ghiteema, mutaghutora kubhaseghani, murabha muramureki Ghiteema omwene.”
Kumaruho bhaghendi bhaache bhayo, bhaghaitabherri amangʼana ghaache. Bhakabherekera abhatomu morense, bhaghakenga ekiina aghoo bhatemu ebhimboko. Hano bhaamarre, bhakabhaseghani ghwiki bhatighe kweeghi abhanto ko eriina re Yeesu. Kumaruho, bhakabhahatora bhaghende echaabho.
Abhatomu bhayo, bhakaru ghwitongo riyo bhachomiiru bhukongʼu, gho okubha Ghiteema naatunire bhasooku gho kuhetera ghuseru ko eriina re Yeesu.
Ghasi bhatahatwire kweeghi abhanto mochenyumba chaabho, no kureghaneri abhanto Amangʼana Amachomu mo ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema. Chesiko chinsi nkureghani bhaare aghoo, Yeesu newe kirisito.
Gho chensiko chiyo, abhatambani bha Yeesu bhakaghenderri kwengeri abhanto bhukongʼu. Ghati yaabho bhaareho Abhayahuti bhano bhaare kughamba Ekeyunaani, Na Abhayahuti bhaghendi bhaabho bhano bhaare kughamba Ekiyaramu. Neho, Abhayahuti bhe Ekeyunaani bhangunyire aghoo, Abhayahuti bhe Ekiyaramu bhatare kubhatweeni Abhayahuti abhasino Ekiyaramu ebhyakori bhe kira orosiko.
Ko riyo, abhatomu ikomi na bhabhere bhaare, bhaghakomani abhatambani bhansi, bhakabhabhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Itakubha bhwaheene itu totighe kweeghi Engʼana ya Ghiteema, twikarere ghotweeni abhanto ebhyakori.
Bhoono abhanto bha waito, muchaghore ghati yaanyu abhasubhe mohungate bhano bhaana eteemo enchomu, bhano bhaana obhungʼaini, na bhano bhaichwire Enkoro Ehoreeru. Bhayo tubhahe emeremo ghiyo,
korri itu tughenderri ghusaasaama Ghiteema, no okweeghi abhanto engʼana yaache.”
Obhughambi bhuyo bhwachomiire abhatambani bhansi bhano bhaare hayo. Ko riyo, bhaghachaghora Sitebhano, omonto wo obhwitabherri bhukongʼu na ono aare aichwire Enkoro Ehoreeru. Ghwiki bhaghachaghora Firipo, Bhurokoro, Nikanori, Timooni, Bharimena na Nikorao we Antiyokiya, ono aare aishoriri kare ghutambana etiini ye Ekiyahuti.
Abhasubhe mohungate bhayo, bhakahiru ko abhatomu. Abhatomu bhakabhasabhera, bhaani bhabhatorire amabhoko kubhanooka ko emeremo gheebho ghiyo.
Engʼana ya Ghiteema, ikaghenderi ghusancha ko abhanto. Ghwiki ekirengero kya abheegha bha Yeesu ghikaruha bhukongʼu Yerusareemu hayo. Kuru abhasengeri abhaaru bhaghasimi ghusooka Ghiteema no kwighwera Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro yo Omutemi Yeesu.
Sitebhano n-omonto ono ahaabhiru na Ghiteema enooko eyaaru na amanagha amaaru. Kiyo nekyu kyaagheri aare ghukora amakono ne ebhimanyerri ebhekoro ko abhanto.
Ghasi, Abhayahuti abhande, bhaaghasaki Sitebhano ko amangʼana . Abhamwe bhaabho bhaare bhe enyumba ye ebhiina emwe, ino yaare kubherekeru Enyumba ye bhiina ya abhanto bho Obhutonoonu. Abhande, bhaare bharweriire ko emeghi ghe Kirene na Arekisantiriya. Abhande bhaare bharweriire ko mikowa ghe Kirikiya na Asiya.
Ghasi, bhatanaghiri komukera gho okubha naaghambire amangʼana gho obhungʼaini na Enkoro Ehoreeru naamukangatire kughamba.
Mbe, Abhayahuti bhayo, bhakangʼaina abhanto nyabhurebhe, bharongohe aghoo, “Tooghuure Sitebhano araghamba amangʼana gho oghutoka Musa na Ghiteema!”
Bhaghasegheeri bhukongʼu abhanto, hamwe na abhakoro bha Abhayahuti na abheeghi bha amaragherri gha Musa. Bhakaghi haare Sitebhano, bhakamughoota, bhakamohira ghwitongo rikoro rya Abhayahuti.
Bhakareeta abhaimererri bho obhurongo. Abhaimererri bhayo, bhakaghamba obhurongo ighoro ya Sitebhano, bhakabhughaa, “Omonto ono ataghotigha kughamba amangʼana amasineenu ighoro ya ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema ahahoreeru, na ighoro ya amaragherri gha Musa.
Kuru ntoomoghuure arabhugha aghoo, Yeesu wa Naasareeti, arahahanyora ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, na arahonchora chisemoka chino twaahaabhiru na Musa.”
Abhanto bhansi mwitongo muyo, bhakaroghoorra Sitebhano, bhakarora obhosho bhooche bhubhaire ghote bho maraika.
Kumaruho, omusengeri omokoro akabhoori Sitebhano akabhughaa, “Amangʼana ghayo ghansi bhaaghambire hano n-go obhuheene?”
Sitebhano akagharokeri akabhughaa, “Abhanto bha waito na bhataata bhaane, Muntegheerre bhwaheene mbabhoorre! Ghiteema omwene obhokoro naamuhyokiire sookoro yiito Bhurahamu, mokyaro ke Mesobhotamiya. Enkaagha eyo, aare akeere koghi momoghi gho Harani.
Ghiteema akamubhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Oru mokyaro gheecho, na ko abhanto bhawanyu, oghi mokyaro kino ngokwereki.’
Neho, Bhurahamu asamire koru gho ekyaro gheeche kya Abhakaritaayo, akaghi kumenya momoghi gho Harani. Enkaagha eno isawaabho aare amarre ghoku, Ghiteema akamusameri mokyaro kino mumenyire bhoono.
“Ghiteema tahaire Bhurahamu eghabho yinsiyinsi, kuru obhwame obhosuuhu, gho ekyaro kino. Ghasi, naarengire okomuha ekyaro kino, kibhe egheeche na kyo orwibhoro rooche, nankabha enkaagha eyo, ataare na omoona.
Ghiteema akabhoorra Bhurahamu akabhughaa, ‘Abhanto bhaacho, bharabha abhagheni gho ekyaro kyende. Abhanto bhe ekyaro kiyo, bharabhakora kubha abhabhaghasi bhaabho na bharabhanyanki bhukongʼu, ko enkaagha ye emeeka maghana inye.’
Kumaruho Ghiteema akabhughaa, ‘Abhanto bhe ekyaro kino, eni ndabhakengera ekiina. Hano ghayo ghaghosira, ndaruusi abhanto waacho ko ekyaro kiyo, korri bhaache hano ghusengera.’
Neho, Ghiteema akore riraghano na Bhurahamu, gho nchera yo ghusaara abhaana bhe eghesubhe. Hano Bhurahamu aibhwire Isaaka, akamusaara orosiko ro kanaane koru okwibhoru ghooche. Isaaka nawe, akaibhora Yaakobho, akamusaara. Na Yaakobho nawe akaibhora abhamura ikomi na bhabhere, akabhasaara. Na bhayo nebhu bhasookoro bhiitu.
“Bhasookoro bhaitu bhayo, mbaamorochire orunyeera Yusubhu mura waabho, bhakamughori abhe omubhaghasi we ekyaro ke Miisiri. Ghasi, Ghiteema hamwe aare nawe,
Ghiteema akamutoori koru mo chitaabhu chinsi chino aabhwine. Ghwiki akamuha amachomu no obhungʼaini, mbaka Bharaao, omutemi wa Miisiri akamusaigha. Bharaao akamutora kubha omwimererri omokoro gho ekyaro gheeche ke Miisiri, na monyumba yaache yo obhutemi.
“Mbe, egheecha endoro ikabha gho ekyaro ghinsi ke Miisiri na ke Kanaani, abhanto bhakanyanka bhukongʼu. Bhasookoro bhiitu bhaakabhori ebhyakori.
Hano Yaakobho oghuure kubha, mokyaro ke Miisiri engano ghutukaho yeeni, aghatoma abhamura bhaache eyo. Na ruyo neru rware orughendo roobho ro ghwansa ko bhasookoro bhiitu koghi Miisiri.
Ko orughendo roobho ro kabhere koghi Miisiri, Yusufu akaitobhora ko bhamura bhaabho, na bhansi bhakamanyikana o Bharaao.
Kumaruho, Yusufu aghatoma amangʼana o Yakobo isawaabho aghoo, aache Miisiri, hamwe na bhamura bhaabho bhansi. Bhamura bhaabho bhayo, bhaare mirongo mohungate na bhataano.
Yaakobho akaghi Miisiri, aghakweera eyo. Bhasookoro bhiitu bhansi mbakweriire Miisiri eyo.
Amaghuha ghaabho, ghakahonchokibhu momoghi gho Shekemu, bhakagheryeka mo embeehera ya mohunguru eno Bhurahamu aare aghoore ko chembiri nyabhurebhe, koru ko abhaana bha Hamori.
“Enkaagha ya Ghiteema yo oghukora reere arengire Bhurahamu rware ruhekeraine. Abhanto bhaitu bhakaghenderri kwiyengerri bhukongʼu Miisiri eyo.
Komohiko, omukama owonde aghasimi kubhaaha mokyaro ke Miisiri, ono ataare amanyire eghento ighoro yo Yusufu.
Omukama oyo, aare omunyenterera haare bhasookoro bhiitu, na aare kubhakorra amasineenu, ko kubhahamerri bhatabhute abhaana bhaabho ebhengʼwerre, korri bhaku.
“Enkaagha eyo neyu Musa aibhwiru. Aare omoona uno aare ghuchomera bhukongʼu Ghiteema. Abhaibhori bhaache bhaakamurera ko enkaagha ye emieri etato eghyene.
Enkaagha ikahika ino abhaibhori bhaache bhaatamiru kughenderri komobhisa, bhakamohira moghitaaro komobhisa. Neho omonke o omukama Bharaao akamuroghota, akamotugha kyo omoona waache.
Musa akeeghibhu amangʼana ghansi gho obhungʼaini bho Miisiri, akabha na amanagha gho kumanya amangʼana na amakora.
“Hano Musa aahikiri enkaagha ye emeeka mirongo ene [40], akaighombu momotema ghooche, koghi kurorana na Abhaisiraeri bhaghendi bhaache.
Eyo, akarora Omwisiraeri omwe aratemu no Omomiisiri. Hayo hayo Musa akaghi komutoori, akamwiita Omomiisiri oyo nokurehani esiire .
Musa aare ghwitegherra aghoo, Abhaisiraeri bhaghendi bhaache bhayo, mbamanyire aghoo, Ghiteema arabhatoori koru kobhubhaghasi bhaabho kuhetera ewe. Ghasi bhatare bhamanyire kehayo.
Hano bhwaakiire, aghasikana na Abhaisiraeri bhabhere bhano bhaare ghwitana. Aghasimi kubhatanani no kubhaingwerani , akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Bhamure, inyu mbamwe mooni Ake! ngooke mokuyaharana?’
Ghasi Omwisiraeri ono aare konyahaara mughendi waache, akamosukuma Musa mbareka, ino arabhughaa, ‘Ne-uye aghutoore iye kubha omubhaahi waito na omwamori waito?
Ghasi ngotuna ooni konyita ghote bhuno waitire Omomiisiri woore icho?’
Hano Musa ooghuure amangʼana ghayo, akangʼosera akamenya mokyaro ke Midiani. Akamenya eyo na akaibhoraho abhaana bhabhere.
“Hano amarre emeeka mirongo ene [40] Midiani, Musa aghaicheru na maraika mwiteregho, haghuhe no orukereghe Sinai. Maraika oyo, aare ko eghisaka kino kyare ghooka omorro.
Hano Musa aarooche ekiroghooro kiyo, akaroghoora bhukongʼu. Aghaghiisokera korri akirorre bhwaheene, akooghu riraka ryo Omutemi Ghiteema riramubhoorra rirabhughaa,
‘Eni neni Ghiteema wa bhasookoro bhaacho, Bhurahamu, Isaaka, na Yaakobho!’ Hano Musa ooghuure amangʼana ghayo, akaghankana ko obhoobha, tanaghiri ghwiki korigheeri eghisaka kiyo.
Omutemi Ghiteema akamubhoorra akabhughaa, ‘Ruusi ebhiraato bheecho, gho okubha hayo wimeriire n-ahase ahahoreeru.
Obhuheene nendooche bhuno abhanto bhaane bhakunyankibhu gho ekyaro kye Miisiri. Noghwiire orokweeri roobho. Kiyo kigherri nsekirre koru mwisaaro kubhatoori koru kobhubhaghasi. Bhoono mbe, ndaghutoma Misiri eyo.’
“Musa oyo newe abhanto bha Isiraeri bhaamwangire, bhakamubhoorra bhakabhughaa, ‘Uye aghutoore iye kubha omubhaahi waito na omwamori waito?’ Ghasi Musa newe ono aatomiru na Ghiteema abhe omubhaahi waabho na omutoori waabho. Ghiteema akamutoma ko kuhetera maraika ono aamohyokiire ko eghisaka keere .
Musa newe aaruusiri Abhaisiraeri ko ekyaro ke Misiri, gho enchera yo ghukora amakono ne ebhimanyerri ebheeru gho ekyaro kiyo, na ko enyancha Emberetu. Akaghenderri na ghayo mwiteregho, ko enkaagha ye emeeka mirongo ene [40].
Musa oyo, newe aabhooriire Abhaisiraeri akabhughaa, ‘Ghati yaanyu, Ghiteema arabhaha omurooti ke eni.’
Musa oyo, aare ghwikara hamwe na bhasookoro bhaitu mwibhara. Newe oyo aaghambaine na ko orukereghe ro Sinai. Akahaabhu amangʼana gho obhuhoru, aghaturetera itu
“Ghasi Abhaisiraeri bhayo, bhasookoro bhaitu, bhakanga komusooka Musa, bhakamutoora mbareka. Bhakaighombu kometema gheebho kugharoka Misiri.
Bhakamubhoorra Haruuni bhakabhughaa, ‘Otukorre chisanamu chino chekubha chiratukangata ko enchera. Gho okubhaMusa ono aatorusiri Miisiri, tutamanyire kino keemobhwine.’
Mbe, gho chensiko chiyo, bhaghakora esanamu ino yaatubaine ne ekimoori. Bhakabha bharayeruseri ekemwenso, ne emeremo ghya amabhoko ghaabho abheene.
Ko riyo, Ghiteema akabhatigha bhasengere ereebha, omweri, ne chinchota, ghote yandekiru ko eghitabho kyo abharooti kirabhughaa, ‘Inyu Abhaisiraeri, hano mwaamenyire mwiteregho ko emeeka mirongo ene, mutare kungoghera eni chetigho korri monduseri ekemwenso!
Ahase hansi hansi hano mware koghi, mwagheghire ne ekebhuru kyo ghusaasaameramu ghiteema waanyu Moreki, ne etuubho ye enchota ya Refani, chisanamu chino mwaikooriire korri murachisengera. ko riyo ndabhasameri kure eyo, kuheta ekyaro kino ghekubherekeru Baberi.’”
Sitebhano akaghenderri kughamba arabhughaa, “Mwiteregho eyo, bhasookoro bhaitu bhayo, bhaaghiire ne ekebhuru kyo obhwimererri, bho kubhaho ko Ghiteema. Ikabha Ghiteema akeerekerri Musa, arikore ribhe ghote bhuno Ghiteema aamutomire.
Kumaruho bhasookoro bhaitu bhayo, ino bhaghakangatu na Yoshuwa, mbaghiire ne ekebhuru kiyo. Nabhu bhakakireeta gho ekyaro kino bhaaruusiiri abhanto bha amakabhira aghande, bhano Ghiteema abhatyambiri mbere ya bhasookoro bhiitu. Mbe, ekebhuru kiyo, kighatama ko ekyaro kiyo, kuhekera ko enkaagha ya omutemi Tauti.
Tauti ono asaighiru na Ghiteema, Tauti aghasabha Ghiteema wa Yaakobho amwitabherri korri amwabhekere ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema.
Ghasi ono amwabhekiire Ghiteema enyumba eyo, no omukama Suremani.
“Ghasi, Ghiteema ono aani ighoro ya bhinsi, taghwikara monyumba iyo yinsiyinsi he. N-gote bhuno omurooti aghambire akabhughaa,
‘Omutemi Ghiteema naaghambire aghoo, Risaaro, neku eghetumbe keene kyo obhukama, na ense, neho ahase haani ho ghutoora amaghoro ghaane. Bhoono, muranyabhekerra enyumba ya bhwe? Hande ahase haane ho kumonyera harabha hayi?
Ebhinto bhinsi bhino, tare neni omwene naabhiteemire?’”
Sitebhano akaghenderri kughamba arabhughaa, “Inyu na-abhanto bhe emetwe emikongʼu mooni! Emetema gheenyu na amatwe ghaanyu, ghanga gha abhanto bhano bhataghusooka Ghiteema. Chensiko chinsi murareki Enkoro Ehoreeru, ghote bhuno bhasookoro bhaanyu bhakore.
Obhuheene neho aani omurooti kuru omwe ono bhasookoro bhaitu bhatamunyankiri. Bhaghaita kuru abharooti bha kare bhano bhaare bhararigheeri oghuucha ko woore Omwene bhoronge! Na oyo newe woore mwakorirre omorwecho, mukamwita!
Inyu mwaahaabhiru amaragherri gha Ghiteema, ghokwerekeribhu na maraika bhaache, ghasi mutaghaghotire he.”
Hano abhakoro bhayo bha Abhayahuti, bhooghuure amangʼana gha Sitebhano ghayo aghambire, bhaghakara bhukongʼu, bhakaroma amaino ghaabho ko obhooro.
Ghasi Sitebhano, akagharamera mwisaaro na ino aichwire Enkoro Ehoreeru, akarora obhurabhu bho Ghiteema, na Yeesu aimeriire orubhareka ro bhoryo ro Ghiteema.
Kumaruho akabhughaa, “Righeeri! Ndarora mwisaaro haighokire, no Omoona wo Omonto aimeriire orubhareka ro bhoryo ro Ghiteema!”
Hayo, abhakoro bhayo bha Abhayahuti, bhakariibha amatwe ghaabho ne amabhoko ghaabho, eno bharatema ekereghe bhukongʼu. Bhansi bhakamwichora Sitebhano hari remwe, bhakamughoota.
Kumaruho, Bhakamorichoki kibhara yo omoghi gho Yerusareemu, bhaghasimi komutema na amaghena. Hano bhaare komutema, abhaimererri bhakaruusi chingebho chaabho, bhaghachitora ko omomura omwe. Omomura oyo, aare kubherekeru Sauri korri achichonge.
Hano bhaare ghutema Sitebhano na amaghena, ewe aare kubhasaasaama arabhughaa, “Eee Omutemi Yeesu, ugheghe omotema ghoone!”
Kumaruho akahighama, aghakuura ko riraka rikoro arabhughaa, “Omutemi, utakaabhakengera ebhiina ko ebhibhe bheebho bhino!” Hano aamarre kughamba ghayo aghaku.
Sauri wunsi naitabheriri no oghwitu ko Sitebhano. Mbe, abhanto bhano bhasookire Ghiteema bhakaryeka Sitebhano, bhakamukorra bhukongʼu. Orosiko roore Sitebhano aaitiru, abhaitabherri bha momoghi gho Yerusareemu, bhaghasimi kunyankibhu bhukongʼu, kuru bhakanyaraghana. Abhaaru mbangʼosire, ghasi abhatomu bha Yeesu abheene, nebhu bhaatamire Yerusareemu hayo. Bhano bhangʼosire. bhakangʼosera gho ekyaro ke Yuuteya na Samaariya

Enkaagha eyo, Sauri wunsi aaghasimi ghosiki abhaitabherri bha Yeesu. Aare ghusoha mochenyumba chaabho, arabharuta gho chenguru, abhasubhe na abhaghaikoro bhano aare kubhonamu, no okubhabhoha mokibhohe.
Abhaitabherri bhayo bhaakanyaraghaine, ahase hansi, bhakabha bhareeghi abhanto Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro ya Yeesu.
Firipo wunsi, akahiringita momoghi gho Samaariya, aghasimi kureghaneri abhanto bho omoghi ghuyo ighoro ya Kirisito.
Abhanto abhaaru bhaare komutegherra bhwaheene bhukongʼu, bharooghu no okurora ebhimanyerri bhino aare ghukora.
Aare ghutwambi emisambu koru ko abhanto abhaaru. Hano emisambu ghiyo ghware koru ko abhanto bhayo, ghakabha ghirakuura ko riraka rikoro. Nahoori abhanto abhaaru, kuru abhabheeru.
Ko ghayo, abhanto bha momoghi ghuyo bhaghachomeru bhukongʼu.
Mbe, momoghi ghuyo gho Samaariya, aaremu omoturutumbi omwe. Omoturutumbi oyo, aare kubherekeru Simeoni. Gho enkaagha entambe, naaroghoori abhanto bha momoghi ghuyo, ko obhoturutumbi bhooche. Aghiikumi ighoo, ewe namanyikaine.
Abhanto bhansi, abhasuuhu ko abhakoro, bhaare komutegherra bhwaheene bhukongʼu, bharabhughaa, “Omonto uno newe amanagha gha Ghiteema, ghano ghamanyikaine aghoo, ‘Amanagha Amakoro gha Ghiteema’!”
Abhanto bhayo, bhaakaghenderri komutegherra bhukongʼu, gho okubha naabharoghorri ko obhoturutumbi bhooche, gho enkaagha entambe.
Hano Firipo aabhareghaniiri Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro yo obhukangati bho Ghiteema, na ighoro ye eriina re Yeesu Kirisito, bhaghaitabherri. Kumaruho abhasubhe na abhaghaikoro bhakabhaatiisibhu.
Simeoni wunsi aghakumi Yeesu akabhaatiisibhu. Akabha aratambana Firipo kira ahase hano aare koghi. Hano aarooche ebhimanyerri na amakono amakoro ghano Firipo aare ghukora, akaroghoora bhukongʼu.
Hano abhatomu bha Yeesu, bhano bhaare bhasaghiire Yerusareemu, bhooghuure ighoo, abhanto bha Samaariya bhaitabheriiri Engʼana ya Ghiteema, bhaghatoma eyo Petiro na Yohana.
Hano bhaahikire, bhakabhasabhera abhaitabherri bhayo, korri bhabhone Enkoro Ehoreeru.
Gho okubha atareho kuru omwe waabho ono aare asekeriru ne Enkoro Ehoreeru. Ebhu bhaare kubhaatiisu ko eriina ryo Omutemi Yeesu eryene.
Petiro na Yohana bhaghatoora amabhoko ighoro ya abhanto bhayo, bhakahaabhu Enkoro Ehoreeru.
Hano omoturutumbi oyo Simeoni aarooche kubha abhanto bharahaabhu Enkoro Ehoreeru ko oghutooru amabhoko na abhatomu, akabhaha Petiro na Yohana chembiri, arabhughaa,
“Muuhe na eni amanagha ghano, korri kira omonto uno ndatoorre amabhoko ghaane, ahaabhu Enkoro Ehoreeru!”
Petiro akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Iye ne chembiri chaacho muhombere kure, gho okubha uraitegherra ighoo, etuho ya Ghiteema nkughorubhu yeeni gho chembiri!
Iye, toghusanga ko ghinsighinsi ko emeremo ghino ghe Ghiteema, gho okubha enkoro yaacho itare bhwaheene mbere yaache.
Bhoono, wishooreri Ghiteema, na omusaasaame ewe Omutemi, ubhone arakwabhera amaitegherro ghaacho amasineenu ghano ughoote momotema ghoocho.
N-obhuheene ngokurora neeni, wichwire orunyeera bhukongʼu ghote obhooro bhwe endore, na ghwiki ubhaire omubhohe we ebhibhe.”
Kumaruho Simeoni akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Inyu munsaasaamere ko Omutemi Ghiteema, korri ritakabhona kuru engʼana emwe ko ghayo ghano mwaaghambire.”
Petiro na Yohana hano bhaamarre kuragherri no okweghi amangʼana gha Omutemi Yeesu, bhakagharoka Yerusareemu. Enkaagha bhaare monchera, mbaahetiire mobhechichi ebheeru bhe Samaariya bharareghani Amangʼana Amachomu.
Mbe, maraika wo Omutemi Ghiteema akamubhoorra Firipo akabhughaa, “Tanora ughende orubhareka ro bhachuuta uhetere enchera eno ekohiringita koru momoghi gho Yerusareemu, iraghi momoghi gho Ghaza.” Enchera eyo eno maraika akughambera, iraheta mwiteregho.
Firipo aghatanora, akahetera ko enchera eyo. Hano aare kughenda, aghasikana no omukangati omwe wa gho ekyaro ke Ethiopia. Omukangati oyo, n-omochigharu aare. Ghwiki, aare omuwasiri we chembiri che Kandake, omukama we ekighaikoro gho ekyaro ke Ethiopia. Aare aghiire Yerusareemu oghusaasaama Ghiteema.
Na ko enkaagha eyo, aare aragharoka ka, aikaire morense yo omokokoteni ghooche gho okurotu ne chifaraasi, eno arasoma eghitabho kyo omurooti Isaaya.
Enkoro Ehoreeru akabhoorra Firipo akabhughaa, “Nooghi isokerra omokokoteni ghuyo, ughende naghu.”
Firipo akaryerera. Hano aahikire, akooghu arasoma eghitabho kyo omurooti Isaaya. Neho Firipo amubhoorri akabhughaa, “Amangʼana ghano oghusoma, nkoghongoraooni?”
Nawe akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Bhwe ngukora manye, na omonto atareho wo okonyerekeri?” Kumaruho omokoro oyo, akaghaghaani Firipo asohe morense yo omokokoteni ghooche bhaikare hamwe.
Amandeko Amahoreeru ghano omokoro oyo aare arasoma, n-gano, “Aaghakangatu ghote ringʼondi rino rekoghi ghochichu. Aare akirre ghote bhuno ringʼondi rirakirra hano bhakorighogha.
Bhaamusere no komukengera ekiina kyo omusari. Atareho omonto uno aghutora kughambera orwibhoro rooche, gho okubha aaitiru monse hano.”
Omonto oyo, akabhoori Firipo akabhughaa, “Ndasabha umborre, amangʼana gho omurooti oyo, n-ighoro ya uye? N-ighoro yaache omwene, ghasi ighoro yo omonto owonde?”
Neho Firipo asimiri na amandeko ghayo ghayo, komuragherri Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro ya Yeesu.
Enkaagha bhaare bharaghenderri na orughendo ko nchera eyo, bhakahika ahase hano haana amanche. Omonto oyo, akabhoorra Firipo akabhughaa, “Righeeri, ghano n-amanche! N-ke kino ghekundeki ntighe kubhaatiisu?” [
Firipo akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Hano uraitabherri Yeesu Kirisito gho enkoro yaacho yinsi, ngutorawooni kubhaatiisu.” Nawe akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Nitabheriri ighoo, Yeesu Kirisito newe Omoona wo Ghiteema.”]
Kumaruho akaimerri omokokoteni. Neho bhansi bhabhere bhasekire, bhaghasoha morense ya amanche, Firipo akamubhaatiisi.
Hano bhaaruure mumanche, Enkoro Ehoreeru yo Omutemi Ghiteema aghasara Firipo. Omochigharu oyo, tamorooche ghwiki, ghasi akaghenderri no orughendo rooche, achomiiru.
Mbe Firipo aghaitaki aani momoghi gho Azota. Koru omoghi ghuyo, akaghi orubhareka ro omoghi gho Kaisariya. Enkaagha aare araghi, aare kureghani Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro ya Yeesu komeghi ghinsi ghino aare kuheta.
Enkaagha eyo yinsi, Sauri akaghenderri kubhakora ehaho yo okobhaita, abhatambani bho Omutemi Yeesu. Orosiko romwe, akaghi ko omusengeri omokoro,
akamusabha amuhe enyarubha eno ekomumanyikani, aghi nayu gho chenyumba cho momoghi ghe Damasiko. Naakorre kehayo, korri hano arabhone abhasubhe hande abhaghaikoro bhano bhakughoota Enchera yo Omutemi Yeesu, anaghi kobhabhoha, abhareete momoghi gho Yerusareemu.
Neho, Sauri asimiri orughendo ro okoghi Damasiko. Hano aare haghuhe kohika omoghi ghuyo, hari remwe obhurabhu obhororo koru mwisaaro, bhukamumwereki ahase hansi.
Kumaruho akagho harense, akooghu riraka riramubhoori rirabhughaa, “Sauri! Sauri! Gho ke okunyanki?”
Sauri nawe akagharokeri akabhughaa, “Omutemi, iye ne-uye?” Akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Eni neeni Yeesu, ono iye okunyanki!
Bhoono, imerra! Nooghi usohe momoghi ghuyo, urabhoorru kino keghutunu ukore.”
Abhasubhe bhano aare kughendani nabhu hamwe, bhaghakira kiri gho okubha bhooghuure riraka gho ekiroghooro, ghasi bhataabhwine omonto wunsiwunsi.
Kumaruho Sauri akabhooka no okwimerra, ghasi hano aatunire korigheeri, tarooche eghento. Mbe, bhaghendi bhaache bhakamughoota okubhoko, bhakamohira Damasiko.
Aghaikara eyo, chensiko isato ahukure. Na gho enkaagha eyo, ataare kuraaghera kuru konyo eghento ghinsighinsi.
Mbe, Damasiko eyo, aareho omutamboni omwe wa Yeesu, ono aare kubherekeru Anania. Omutemi Yeesu, akamubherekera Anania mondooto akabhughaa, “Anania!” Nawe akaitabha akabhughaa, “Omutemi, neeni hano.”
Kumaruho Omutemi akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Bhooka ughende gho enchera ino ekubherekeru ‘Ya bhoronge’. Ubhoori morense ye enyumba ya Yuuta, omonto uno arweriire momoghi gho Tariso. Omonto oyo, arabherekeru Sauri. Righeeri bhoono arasaasaama Ghiteema.
Narootire ighoo iye Anania, urasoha morense ye enyumba no komutoora amabhoko, korri arore ghwiki.”
Ghasi Anania akagharokeri akabhughaa, “Omutemi, nooghuure koru ko abhanto abhaaru, ghote Sauri oyo, aare ghukorra amasineenu abhanto waacho Yerusareemu eyo!
Na bhoono aichire Damasiko hano, na amanagha koru ko abhakoro bha abhasengeri, korri abhohe bhansi bhano bhaghusaasaama ko eriina reecho.”
Ghasi Omutemi akamubhoorra Anania akabhughaa, “Iye nooghi! Omonto oyo, nemohwere abhe omubhaghasi waane, korri areghani eriina reene ko abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti na obhubhaahi bhoobho, na ko Abhaisiraeri abheene.
Eni omwene ndamwereki ghote aghotunu kunyankibhu bhukongʼu, ko okugheri ye eriina reene.”
Kumaruho Anania akaghi, aghasoha morense ye enyumba eyo. Aghatoora amabhoko ghaache ighoro ya Sauri, na akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Omonto waito Sauri, kubhe ino waare ghuucha, Omutemi Yeesu aakohyookire monchera. Bhoono ewe aantomire haare iye, korri unaghi kurora ghwiki, na wichoribhu Enkoro Ehoreeru.”
Hari remwe, ebhinto ghote amaghamba, ghakagho koru komaiso gha Sauri. Ewe akanaghi kurora ghwiki. Kumaruho akaimerra, akabhaatiisibhu.
Hano aamarre kuraaghera ebhyakori, akabhona chenguru ghwiki. Sauri aikaire na abhatambani bha Yeesu bhano bhaare Damasiko eyo, ko enkaagha ye chensiko nsuuhu echeene.
Hari remwe, aghasimi kweeghi mochenyumba cha Abhayahudi cho oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema ighoro ya Yeesu ighoo, Yeesu newe Omoona wo Ghiteema.
Abhanto bhansi bhano bhooghuure Sauri, bhaakaroghoora bhukongʼu. Bhakabhoorani bhakabhughaa “Omonto uno, tere woore aare oghwita abhatambani bha Yeesu, Yerusareemu yeere? Na aachire hano ko engʼana iyo iyo, korri abhabhohe no kobhahira ko abhakoro bha abhasengeri!”
Ghasi Sauri akabha akaghenderri kubhona chenguru, akaroghoori Abhayahuti bhano bhaare bhamenyire Damasiko ghokobhakumerri ighoo, Yeesu newe Kirisito. Akabheeghi kuhetera Amandeko Amahoreeru, kuhekera hano bhasindiru komunyeera chinkaani.
Hano chensiko echaaru chaahetire, Abhayahuti Bhakarwecha ekiina kyo komwita Sauri.
Abhayahuti bhakabha bharaghonyera Sauri, obhotiko no omwise ko emirango ghyo omoghi ghuyo, , korri bhamwite. Ghasi Sauri akabhoorru amangʼana ghayo.
Obhotiko bhomwe, abheegha bhaache bhakamusohi mo ensaho kino kyare kibhohirru chensiri. Kumaruho bhaghakiheti mwibhanga rikoro rye endighi ino yaare yinaare omoghi, bhaghasekeri ensaho kibhara yo omoghi ko chensiri cheere, akaghi.
Neho Sauri akaghi momoghi gho Yerusareemu. Hano aahikire eyo, aghasaki kughootana na abhatambani bha Yeesu. Ghasi nebhu bhansi bhaakamotiina, gho okubha bhatanaghiri komwitabherri ighoo, nawe obhuheene nomutambani wa Yeesu abhaire.
Ghasi Barinabha akaimoki Sauri, akamohira ko abhatomu. Akabhabhoorra ghote bhuno Sauri arooche Omutemi Yeesu monchera, enkaagha eno aare koghi Damasiko, na ghote bhuno Omutemi aghambaine nawe. Ghwiki akabhabhoorra ghote bhuno eeghiri abhanto bha eyo ko bhukare ighoro ya Yeesu.
Mbe, Sauri aghaikara na abhatomu bhayo momoghi gho Yerusareemu. Aare kughendani nabhu hamwe, areeghi abhanto kobhukare ighoro yo Omutemi Yeesu.
Gho enkaagha, aare araghamba no kubhoorani na Abhayahuti bhano bhaare kughamba Ekeyunaani, ghasi bhoobho bhaaghacharibhu komwita.
Abhaitabherri abhande hano bhaangʼurre engʼana eyo, bhakahira Sauri momoghi gho Kaisariya. Kumaruho koru eyo, bhakamutoma aghi momoghi gho Tariso.
Ko chensiko chiyo, ekanisa yaare ne emirembe ahase hansi ko mikowa ghye Yuudeya, Ghariraaya, na Samaariya. Abhaitabherri bhakaghenderri kunaghi, komutegherra Omutemi Yeesu na ko omotema na Enkoro Ehoreeru. Kehayo, bhakaghenderri kwiyengerri.
Petiro hano aare ghukora orughendo ahase hansi, orosiko romwe akahika ko abhanto bha Ghiteema bhano bhaare momoghi gho Rita.
Momoghi muyo, akabhona omonto omwe, eriina reeche Ayineya. Ewe aare omorwire wo kunyeeka, na ko enkaagha ye emeeka enaane, taruure kobhorre.
Petiro akamubhoorra Ayineya akabhughaa, “Yeesu Kirisito arakuhori! Imerra, waari obhorre bhoocho.” Hari remwe igho, Ayineya akaimerra.
Mbe, abhanto bhansi bhano bhaamenyire Rita na Saroni, hano bhaarooche Ayineya, bhakaishooreri Omutemi Yeesu.
Momoghi gho Yobha, aaremu omughaikoro omwe, omutamboni wa Yeesu. Omughaikoro oyo, aare kubherekeru Tabhita. Ko Ekeyunaani eriina reeche n-Dorikasi, ekyereki gheeche n-eghisara. Ewe aare arasakeri abhatobhu, ghwiki aare arakora amakora amachomu.
Enkaagha eyo, Dorikasi akabhabhara, aghaku. Abhanto bhakeeghi omobhere ghooche, bhakamuraari morense ye eghechumba ke moghorofa.
Enkaagha eyo, abhatambani bha Yeesu bhakooghu aghoo, Petiro aare Rita. Bhaghatoma abhasubhe bhabhere ko Petiro, gho okubha omoghi gho Rita ghware haghuhe na omoghi ghoobho gho Yobha. Abhasubhe bhayo hano bhaahikire, bhakabhoorra Petiro bhakabhughaa, “Ntoghusaasaamire uuche momoghi ghwitu, utakaghechere ghuucha!”
Mbe, Petiro aghatanora, akaghi hamwe nabhu. Hano bhaahikire Yobha, bhakamohira morense ye eghechumba ke moghorofa. Hano ahikire moghechumba kiyo akabhonamu abhasino abhaaru bhakamwinaara, bhakabha bharakuura. Bhakamwereki chingancho, na chingebho chende chino Dorikasi aare ghotuma enkaagha eno aare omuhoru.
Petiro akabhabhoorra bhansi bharichoke kibhara. Akahighima aghasaasaama Ghiteema. Kumaruho aghaishooreri omobhere gho omoku, akabhughaa, “Tabhita, bhooka!” Tabhita akaramoki amaiso. Hano aamorooche Petiro, aghaikara.
Petiro akamughoota okubhoko, akamutooreri kwimerra. Kumaruho akabherekera abhasino na abhaitabherri abhande, akabheereki Tabhita eno abhaire omuhoru ghwiki.
Engʼana eyo ikamanyikana bhukongʼu momoghi ghunsi gho Yobha. Abhanto abhaaru bhaghaitabherri Omutemi Yeesu.
Mbe, Petiro aghaikara Yobha hayo ko chensiko echaaru, aare aikaire morense ye enyumba yo omukori wa amaseero, uno aare kubherekeru Simeoni.
