Momoghi gho Kaisariya, aaremu omwimererri omwe wa abhasirikare. Omwimererri oyo, aare kubherekeru Korineriyo. Ewe aare araimererra eghekomo kya abhasirikare righana remwe ko ghekomo eghekoro kino kyare kubherekeru, Eghekomo ke Kiitariya.
Korineriyo aare omusaighi Ghiteema, hamwe na abhanto bhansi bhano bhaare waache ka. Aare ghutoori bhukongʼu Abhayahuti bhano bhaare abhatobhu, na ghusabha Ghiteema kira enkaagha.
Orosiko romwe, yaare ensa ya kenda yo omwise, Korineriyo akarora bhurabhu mokirooto ighoo, maraika wa Ghiteema amohyokiire. Maraika oyo, akamubherekera akabhughaa, “Korineriyo!”
Korineriyo akarigheeri maraika ko obhoobha, kumaruho akamubhoori akabhughaa, “Omutemi, nke keeho?” Maraika oyo, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Ghiteema oghuure amasabhi ghaacho na arooche muno oghutoori abhatobhu, na ko riyo arakohiita.
Ko riyo bhoono, toma abhanto nyabhurebhe bhaghende momoghi gho Yobha. Aaho omonto omwe eyo, arabherekeru Simeoni, eriina reeche erende newe Petiro. Omubhorre aache.
Araikara kyo omugheni ko omonto omwe omukori we ebhinto bhe eghiseero, eriina reeche arabherekeru Simooni. Enyumba yaache yeeni mbareka ye enyancha.”
Hano Maraika oyo, aamarre kubhoorra Korineriyo amangʼana ghayo, aghatanora. Kumaruho Korineriyo akabherekera abhabhaghasi bhabhere, hamwe na omosirikare omwe koru ko abhatooreri bhaache, uno aare kwighwera Ghiteema.
Korineriyo hano amarre kubhabhoorra ghansi ghano ghatokiire, akabhatoma bhaghende momoghi gho Yobha.
Etabhoori yaache, abhanto bhatato bhayo hano bhaahikire haghuhe na omoghi gho Yobha, Petiro akariina ighoro ye enyumba ghusaasaama Ghiteema. Yaare ghote ensa ya ghasansabha yo omwise.
Hano aare arasaasaama, akooghu arambokire, akaighombu kubhona ebhyakori. Enkaagha eno bhaare komukorra ebhyakori, akarora amaroro.
Ko amaroro ghayo, naarooche mwisaaro haraighoka, ne eghento ghote esuuka enkoro, irasekera harense ikabha ighootiru chimbareka chaache chinsi inye.
Morense ye esuuka muyo, chaaremu chetyenyi chino chiheteraine heteraine, chetyenyi cha amaghoro ane, chetyenyi chino chekwingʼoora enda, ne ebhinyonyi.
Hayo, Petiro akooghu riraka, rirabhughaa, “Petiro, bhooka, ochinche uraaghere!”
Ghasi, Petiro akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Hasehe, Omutemi! ntakaraaghiire ebhyakori bhinsibhinsi bhino amaragherri gha Musa ghakwanga gharabhugha n-ebhinabhi!”
Riraka riyo, rikamubhoorra ghwiki rikabhughaa, “Otighe kubherekera ebhinto bhino Ghiteema arabhiri aghoo n-ebhinabhi.”
Riraka riyo, ikaihonchokera hari ghatato. Neho esuuka yagharokiribhu mwisaaro.
Hano Petiro aare akeere aribhoori ighoro ye ekyereki kya amaroro ghayo, abhanto bhatato bhano bhaare bhaatomiru na Korineriyo bhakabha bherekiribhu enyumba ya Simooni. Bhaare bhaimeeriire mbere ye egheseku.
Bhakabherekera na bhakabhoori bhakabhughaa, “Omugheni uno akubherekeru Simooni eriina erende Petiro, hano aani?”
Na enkaagha Petiro aare akeere Araghenderri na amaitegherro ighoro ye ekyereki kye mokirooto keere, Enkoro Ehoreeru akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Tegherra! Bhaaho abhanto bhatato hano, bharaghotuna.
Sekera harense ughende nabhu, utakabha ne ehaho, gho okubha neeni omwene mbatomire haare iye.”
Petiro aghasekera harense, akabhabhoorra abhanto bhayo akabhughaa, “Eni newe ono moghotuna. N-gooke muchire?”
Bhakamubhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Ntutomiru no omwimererri omwe wa abhasirikare, eriina reeche Korineriyo. Korineriyo oyo ghusooku aani bhukongʼu na Abhayahuti bhansi, ko bhoore aghusoka ghiteema, ghwiki n-omonto omuchomu bhukongʼu. Bhoono maraika omuhoreeru wo Ghiteema amuragheriiri ighoo, aghukaribhisi ka waache, korri ategherre amangʼana ghano okomubhoorra.”
Mbe, Petiro akabhakaribhisi bhasohe nyumba, bhabhe abhagheni bhaache. Etabhoori yaache, Petiro na abhanto bhatato bhaare bhaghasimi orughendo na abhaitabherri abhande koru Yobha bhano bhaare ghutambana Petiro.
Orosiko ro kabhere, bhakahika momoghi gho Kaisariya. Hano bhaahikire, bhakabhona Korineriyo akeere arabhaghanya aani areghaini abhanto bha waabho na abhasaani bhaache bha haghuhe.
Hano Petiro ahikire, Korineriyo akamoturungʼana, akahighama akahiinya obhosho harense komusengera.
Ghasi Petiro akamwimerri akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Imerra! Eni ghwiki n-omonto ghote iye!”
Kumaruho Petiro aghasoha hamwe na Korineriyo morense ye enyumba bhaani bharaghamba, bhakabhona abhanto abhaaru mbaikomaine morense.
Petiro akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Inyu mumanyire bhwaheene aghoo, amaragherri ghiitu itu Abhayahudi nkwangaghaani ghwichoghana hande kubhataara abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti. Ghasi Ghiteema naaseghaini, ntakabherekera omonto wunsiwunsi ighoo, n-omunabhi ghasi ighoo, taghutakeru .
Kiyo nenku kigherri nichire hano mumberekiire, ntangire. Bhoono ndabhabhoori ighoo, gho ke mumberekiire?”
Korineriyo akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Chensiko isato chino chihetire, naare morense ye enyumba ndasaasaama Ghiteema, ko enkaagha ghote eno eno ko ensa kenda cho omwise. Hari remwe, nkarora omonto aimeriire mbere yaane, aswarre chingebho chino chekubharibhari.
Omonto oyo, Akamboorra akabhughaa ‘Korineriyo, Ghiteema oghuure amasabhi ghaacho, nkohiitaaani bhuno oghutoori abhatobhu.
Ko riyo, bhoono utome abhanto momoghi gho Yobha, bhareete Simooni eriina erende neru Petiro. araikara ghote omugheni o Simooni, omukori we ebhinto bhya amaseero, enyumba yaache yeeni mbareka ye enyancha.’
Nekyu kigherri ngatoma abhanto hari remwe haare iye. Na iye wunsi ukorre bhwaheene ghuucha. Mbe, bhoono itu bhansi, tooni hano mbere ya Ghiteema, korri tooghu amangʼana ghano Omutemi aghutomire ghotubhoorra.”
Hayo Petiro akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Bhoono manyire kemwe ighoo, obhuheene Ghiteema taghuchaghora abhanto
Ghasi, araitabherri abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti bhano bhakomusooka, no ghukora ghano akwenda mbere yaache.
Inyu mumanyire amangʼana ghano Ghiteema ahaire Abhaisiraeri. Abhareghaniiri Amangʼana Amachomu ighoo, bhabhone emirembe kuhetera Yeesu Kirisito. Yeesu oyo, newe Omutemi wa abhanto bhansi.
Ghwiki mumanyire amangʼana ghano ghatokiire ko omukowa ghunsi gho Yuudeya. Kuwansera Ghariraaya, kuru hano Yohana Omubhaatiisi kureghaneri abhanto ighoo, bhabhatiisibhu.
Mumanyire ighoo, Ghiteema naamohwire Yeesu wa Naasareeti, ko okomuha Enkoro Ehoreeru, na amanagha. Yeesu naaghiire eno na eno, arakora amangʼana amachomu no okuhori bhansi bhano bhaare kunyankibhu ne chenguru che Risambu. Naakorre kehayo, gho okubha Ghiteema aare hamwe nawe.
“Na itu nebhu abhaimererri bha amangʼana ghansi ghano Yeesu aakorre gho ekyaro kya Abhayahuti, na momoghi gho Yerusareemu. Kumaruho aghaitu gho okubhambu komusarabha.
Ghasi orosiko ro ghatato, Ghiteema akamoryokora, akamwereki ko abhanto.
Tere abhanto bhansi bhaamorooche, ghasi Ghiteema noohwere abhaimererri komurora. Abhaimererri bhayo, neghu itu. Kuru hano Yeesu aaryokire, twamorooche, tukaraaghera no okonyo hamwe nawe.
Nawe naaturagheriri kweeghi abhanto Amangʼana Amachomu no kureghani ighoo, ewe newe atomiru na Ghiteema, akengere ekiina abhahoru na abhaku.
Abharooti bhansi bhakabhugha ighoro yaache ighoo, omonto wunsiwunsi uno akomwitabherri, arabheru ebhibhe bheeche bhinsi, kuhetera ewe.”
Petiro hano aare akeere araghamba amangʼana ghayo, Enkoro Ehoreeru akabhasekerra bhansi bhano bhaare komutegherra.
Abhayahuti bhano bhaamwitabheriiri Yeesu, bhano bhaare bhaachire na Petiro koru Yobha, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu, kurora ighoo Ghiteema aitororiire Enkoro Ehoreeru kuru ko abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti.
Mbaamanyire kehayo, gho okubha bhooghuure abhanto bhayo, bharaghamba ekighambo kende, no oghutooni Ghiteema. Neho Petiro agharokiiri akabhughaa
“Abhanto bhayo bhabhwine Enkoro Ehoreeru ghote haare itu taabhwine. Bhoono, uye aghutora kubhaseghani bhatighe kubhaatiisu ko amanche?”
Ko riyo, Petiro akeerekerri ighoo, bhabhatiisibhu ko eriina re Yeesu Kirisito. Kumaruho bhaghasabha Petiro aikare nabhu ko chensiko chensuuhu.
Abhatomu bha Yeesu na abhaitabherri abhande ko omukowa gho Yuuteya yeere, bhakooghu ighoo, abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti bhansi bhaitabheriiri Engʼana ya Ghiteema.
Mbe, Petiro hano aagharokire Yerusareemu, Abhayahuti bhano bhaare bhaitabheriiri Yeesu, bhaghasimi komubheeha,
bharabhugha bharabhughaa, “Iye waasohire monyumba ya abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti na ukaraaghera ebhyakori hamwe nabhu!”
Neho Petiro asimiri kubhabhoorra bhwaheene arabhughaa,
“Orosiko romwe, naare momoghi gho Yafa, ndasaasaama Ghiteema. Kumaruho nkaghootu ne ekiroghooro, ngasimi kurora amaroro. Ku amaroro ghayo, nkarora eghento ghye esuuka enkoro eno yaare ighootiru chimbareka chaache inye chinsi. Eghento kiyo kyare ghusekeribhu koru mwisaaro haghuhe na eni.
ngakiroheera bhwaheene, chaaremu chetyenyi chino chighoote amaghoro ane, cha mwiteregho na cho ghotugha, chetyenyi chino chekwingʼoora enda, ne ebhinyonyi.
“Neho nooghuure riraka, riramboorra rirabhughaa ‘Petiro, imerra! Ughooghe, uraaghere!’
Ghasi nkaghamba, ‘Hasehe, Omutemi! Ntakarire ebhyakori bhinsibhinsi bhino amaragherri gha Musa ghakughamba kubha n-najisi!’
Kumaruho nkooghu riraka ghwiki koru mwisaaro irabhughaa, ‘Otighe kubherekera ebhinto bhino Ghiteema arabhiri kubha, n-najisi.’
Engʼana eyo yaaikorre hari ghatato, neho ebhinto bhiyo bhinsi bhikagharokibhu mwisaaro.
“Hari remwe abhanto bhatato bhakahika ko enyumba eno tware twikaire. Abhanto bhayo bhaare bhatomiru koru momoghi gho Kaisariya.
Enkoro Ehoreeru Akamboorra ighoo, ntambane nabhu ntaghaakubhi. Ko riyo, nkaghi hamwe nabhu. Bhaghendi bhaito bhasansabha bhayo hano bhaghantambana koghi Kaisariya. Hano twahikire eyo, tughasoha monyumba ya Korineriyo.
Ewe aghatubhoorra ghote maraika aimeriire waache ka, no komubhoorra akabhughaa ‘Utome abhanto bhaghende momoghi gho Yobha, bhabherekere Simooni, eriina reeche erende Petiro, aache.
Oyo, newe arakubhoorre amangʼana ghano ghakoghutoori iye hamwe na abhanto bhansi bha waacho ka.’
“Hano naasimiri kubhoorra abhanto bhayo amangʼana, Enkoro Ehoreeru akabhasekerra, ghote atusekeriire itu ekimbere.
Hayo neho naahiita engʼana eno Omutemi Yeesu aatubhoorire akabhughaa, ‘Yohana abhaatiisire abhanto ku amanche, ghasi inyu murabhaatiisibhu gho Enkoro Ehoreeru.’
Ko riyo, ghote Ghiteema abhahaire abhanto bhano etuho yeere yeere eno aatuhaire itu hano twaitabheriiri Omutemi Yeesu Kirisito, bhoono, eni ne-wuuye kuru nnaghi kureki Ghiteema?”
Mbe, Abhayahuti bhayo, hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaghakira. Bhaghaitumi Ghiteema bharaghamba bharabhughaa, “Ghiteema ahaire kuru abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti omweya gho ghotiita ebhibhe bheebho, korri bhabhone obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi!”
Kuru hano Sitefano aaitiru, abhaitabherri bhaghasimi kunyankibhu ghwiki no oghotyamba. Abhande bhoobho bhakangʼosera mokyaro ke Foyinike, Kipuro na abhande momoghi gho Antiyokiya. Na eyo hansi, bhakabha bhareeghi amangʼana ighoro gha Yeesu ko Abhayahuti abheene.
Ghasi mubhayo bhaareho abhaitabherri abhande bhano bhaachire Antiyokiya koru Kipuro na momoghi gho Kirene. Ebhu bhaghasimi kweeghi abhanto amangʼana amachomu ighoro yo Omutemi Yeesu, kuru kubhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti.
Amanagha gho Omutemi Ghiteema ghaare hamwe nabhu, na abhanto abhaaru bhukongʼu bhaghaitabherri no ghwishooreri Omutemi Yeesu.
Abhaitabherri bhe ekanisa ya Yerusareemu, hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaghatoma Bharinabha aghi eyo.
Hano aahikire eyo, akarora ghote muno Ghiteema ahaire abhanto bhayo enooko yaache. Aghachomeru bhukongʼu, akabhakumerri kubha bhaghenderri kwighwera Omutemi Yeesu ko emetema gheebho ghansi.
Bharinabha aare omonto omuchomu na aare aichwire Enkoro Ehoreeru no obhwitabherri. Na abhanto bhano bhaare ghwitabherri Omutemi Yeesu, bhakiyengeri bhukongʼu.
Kumaruho Bharinabha akaghi momoghi gho Tariso ghotuna Sauri.
Hano aamobhwine, akamureeta hayo Antiyokiya. ko riyo, Bharinabha na Sauri bhaghaikomana ne ekanisa gho enkaagha yo omoka omoghi, bhakabha bhareeghi abhanto abhaaru bhukongʼu. Na Antiyokiya hayo, neho abhatambani bha Yeesu bhaasimiri kubherekeru, Abhakirisito.
Gho chensiko chiyo, abharooti koru Yerusareemu bhaghaacha Antiyokiya.
Omwe waabho, aare arabherekeru Aghabho. Aghabho oyo akaimerra koghikomo kye ekanisa, akaruusi obhurooti ku amanagha ghe Enkoro Ehoreeru akabhughaa, omuramboko omororo ghuraacha gho ense engima. Omuramboko ghuyo, neghu ghoore ghwachire, enkaagha eno Kaisari Kiraudiyo aare kubhaaha.
Gho okugheri kwo obhurooti bhuyo, abhatambani bha Yeesu bhaghakenga ekiina ighoo, kira omwe waabho, kurengʼaana na amanagha ghaache, aruusi ghutooreri Abhakirisito bhaghendi bhaabho bhano bhaani ko omukowa gho Yuuteya.
Mbe, bhaghakora kee hayo, bhakaha Bharinabha na Sauri omotweno ghuyo, korri bhaghohire ku abhagharuka bhe ekanisa ya Yerusareemu.
Gho chensiko chiyo, omutemi Herote Aghiribha aghasimi kughoota abhande bha abhaitabherri bhe ekanisa no okubhanyanki.
Akaghamba ighoo, Yaakobho murra waabho Yohana aitu gho ekinyamaino.
Hano aarooche ighoo rikora riyo rirachomeru Abhayahuti, akaghamba ighoo, Petiro wunsi aghootu. Ghayo ghansi ghaghakorru enkaagha ye enyangi ya Abhayahuti eno ekubherekeru Ebhaasaka, eno bhataghutoora ehamiira mo emighaate.
Hano aamarre komughoota, akaghamba ighoo, Petiro atooru mokibhohe. Akamubhati ko ebhikomo bhine bhya abhasirikare bhane bhane, korri bhamurende bhwaheene. Naatunire komukengera ekiina mbere ya abhanto enkaagha eno enyangi eyo ye Ebhaasaka eghosira.
Ko riyo, Petiro aare mokibhohe, ghasi bhoono abhaitabherri bhe ekanisa bhaare ghwikongʼi komusaasaamera haare Ghiteema.
Obhotiko bho okubhookera orosiko runo omutemi Herote aare ghotuna komukengera ekiina, Petiro aare amisiri ghati ya abhasirikare bhabhere, abhohiru ne eminyorro ebhere. Abhasirikare abhande, bhaare bhararigheeri ko omurango gho kibhara gho mokibhohe.
Hari remwe, maraika wo Omutemi Ghiteema akahyoka moghechumba kino Petiro aaremu, emirengaari emeroro ghikamoreki moghechumba muyo. Maraika oyo, aghaturi Petiro ko orubharu komubhooki, aramubhoorra arabhughaa, “Bhooka bhongo!” Hari remwe eminyorro ghino ghyare ghemubhohire mumabhoko, ghikabhotoka, ghikagho harense.
Kumaruho maraika oyo, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Swara chingebho chaacho ne ebhiraato bheecho.” Petiro aghakora kee hayo. Maraika akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Swara eghooti yaacho, untambane!”
Petiro akaru mokibhohe muyo, aratambana na maraika oyo. Petiro taamanyire kubha, ghano ghakorekire n-gho obhuheene ghaare. Araitegherra ighoo, n-amaroro aare kurora.
Petiro na maraika oyo akaheta ku abharendi bha ghwansa, na bha kabhere, bhakahika ko omurango ghwe ekyoma gho ghusohera momoghi. Omurango ghuyo, ghukabhaighokera oghwene, bhakaru mokibhohe. Bhakahetera enchera emwe, hari remwe maraika oyo, aghatigha Petiro.
Petiro akangʼura ghano ghaahyokire n-gho obhuheene ghaare, akaghamba akabhughaa, “Bhoono manyire, n-obhuheene aghoo, Omutemi Ghiteema antomiire maraika waache korri antoorri koru mumabhoko gha Herote, na koru ghansi ghano Abhayahuti bhaare ghwitengʼera aghankoriire.”
Hano Petiro aamarre kumanya ghayo, akaghi o Mariyamu, nyakuwaabho Yohana. Yohana oyo eriina erende aare kubherekeru Maariko. Abhanto abhaaru bhaare bhasikaine hayo ghusaasaama Ghiteema (ko okugheri ya Petiro).
Hano Petiro aahikire, aghatema hooti ko omurango gho kibhara. Omonke omwe omukori emeremo, eriina reeche Roda, akaghi ghutegherra, ne-wuuye.
Ghasi bhoono hano ongwere riraka riyo n-nde Petiro, aghachomeru bhukongʼu, akaryera aghasoha nyumba, akeebha kuru komwighorra. Akabhabhoorra bhansi akabhughaa, “Petiro aani momurango!”
Ebhu bhakamubhoorra bhakabhughaa, “nochurre kana!” Ghasi omonke oyo, akaghenderri kubhakumerri ighoo, n-obhuheene. Ebhu bhakaghamba bharabhughaa, “Oyo m-maraika waache.”
Enkaagha eyo, Petiro aare kughenderri ghukongʼonta omurango. Hano bhamwighorire bhakamurora, bhakaroghoora bhukongʼu.
Petiro akabheereki no okubhoko bhakire. Akabhabhoorra muno Omutemi Ghiteema amoruusiri mokibhohe. Akaghenderri kubhabhoorra arabhughaa, “Amangʼana ghano, mubhoorre Yaakobho na abhaitabherri bhaitu abhande.” Kumaruho Petiro akaru hayo, akaghi ahase ahande.
Hano bhwaakiire, abhasirikare bhaare bha mokibhohe, bhakaghootu no obhoobha obhooru ighoro ya kino kebhwine Petiro.
Omutemi Herote akaghamba ighoo, Petiro atunu, ghasi bhoono bhataamobhwine. Ko riyo, akaghamba ighoo, abharendi bhaare, bhabhooribhu. Kumaruho akaghamba ighoo, bhaitu. Herote omwene akahiringita koru ekyaro ke Yuuteya koghi momoghi gho Kaisariya, aghaikara eyo chensiko nsuuhu.
Mbe, Herote aare akarariire bhukongʼu abhanto bhe emeghi ghe Tiiro na Sitooni. Bhoono, abhanto bhe emeghi ebhere ghiyo, bhakaghootana hamwe, bhaghatuna ghosikana nawe. Abhanto bhayo bhaare bhaitabheriribhu na Bhurasito. Bhurasito oyo, newe aare omonto wa haghuhe wa Herote, na aare omwimererri wa amangʼana ghaache. Mbaasabhire amaitabherrani ghe emirembe, gho okubha ebhyaro bheebho, bhiritengʼera ebhyakori koru gho ekyaro kyo omutemi Herote.
Orosiko runo omutemi Herote oohwere kurorana no ghosikana na abhanto bhayo, aghaswara chingebho chaache che eghikama, aghaikara koghetumbe gheeche kye eghikama, aghasimi kughamba mbere ya abhanto bhansi.
Abhanto bhano bhaare bhaikomaini hayo, bhaghasimi komoririryetera bharaghamba bharabhughaa, “Riyo ritare riraka ryo omonto! Ne-riraka rye ghiteema!”
Gho okubhaHerote taaitumiri Ghiteema, hayo hayo, maraika wo Omutemi Ghiteema, akamukengera ekiina. Ko riyo, akabhabhara emichango monda aghaku.
Ghasi bhoono Engʼana ya Ghiteema, ikabha iraghenderri ghusaancha kubhanto, abhaaru bhakayitabherri.
Hano Bharinabha na Sauri bhaamarre emeremo gheebho ghyo ghutooreri abhaitabherri momoghi gho Yerusareemu, bhakaghegha Yohana ono akubherekeru Maariko, bhakagharoka nawe Antiyokiya.
Mokanisa yo omoghi gho Antiyokiya bhaareho abharooti na abheeghi. Abhanto bhayo m-mbano, Bharinabha, Simeoni uno aare kubherekeru Nigheri, Rukio koru omoghi gho Kirene, Manaeni uno aare arerru hamwe na omutemi Herote Antipasi, na owonde aare Sauri.
Hano bhaare ghusaasaama Omutemi Ghiteema na kwiyima ebhyakori, Enkoro Ehoreeru akaghamba akabhughaa, “Monyoohorre Bharinabha na Sauri ko emeremo ghino mbabherekeriire.”
Neho bhaamarre kwiyima ebhyakori no oghusaasaama Ghiteema, bhaghatoora amabhoko ghaabho ighoro ya Bharinabha na Sauri. Kumaruho, bhakabhaitabherri bhaghende.
Hano Bharinabha na Sauri bhatomiru ne Enkoro Ehoreeru, bhakangʼarara kohikera momoghi gho Sereukiya. Koru hayo bhaghatanora no obhooto, bhakaghi momoghi gho Kipuro.
Hano bhaahikire momoghi gho Sarami, bhaghasimi kureghaneri abhanto Engʼana ya Ghiteema mochenyumba cha Abhayahudi cho oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema. Mbaakorre kee hayo hamwe na Yohana Maariko, omutooreri waabho.
Hano bhaamarre kuheta ahase hansi ha Kipuro, bhakahika momoghi gho Pafo. Hayo bhaghasikana no Omuyahuti omwe omoturutumbi. Aare omurooti wo obhurongo, eriina reeche Bhari-Yeesu.
Omonto oyo, aare aghutooreri Serighiyo Pauro, omubhaahi we righinga riyo, omubhaahi oyo aare omonto wo obhungʼaini bhukongʼu. Akabherekera Bharinabha na Sauri bhaghende waache, gho okubha naatunire kooghu Engʼana ya Ghiteema
Ghasi bhoono Bhari-Yeesu omoturutumbi (eriina reeche gho Ekeyunaani n-ighoo Erima) aghatonani nabhu, aare ghotuna kwangera omubhaahi oyo korri ataghaitabherri Yeesu.
Neho, Sauri, ono aare kubherekeru Pauro, aani aichwire Enkoro Ehoreeru, akamoghorra Erima omoturutumbi,
akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Iye omoona we Risambu! Iye no-omobhisa wa ghansi ghano ghaani gho obhoronge mbere ya Ghiteema. Wichwire obhungʼainigʼaini no obhurongo. Iye tookurosa ghucharibhu ghoshoori eseemi enchomu ya Omutemi!
Bhoono, tegherra! Omutemi arakughootera enchagho. Urabha omohukuru, tokurora obhurabhu bhwe ereebha gho enkaagha.” Hari remwe endumbe ne ekeruutu bhikamokundekeri, nawe akaghenda eno na yeere aghatuna omonto wo komughoota okubhoko, korri amwereki nchera.
Omubhaahi, hano aarooche engʼana eyo, aghaitabherri Omutemi Yeesu. Ghwiki aare kuroghooribhu bhukongʼu ighoro ya ameeghi ghano oghuure amangʼana gho Omutemi Yeesu.
Kumaruho, Pauro na bhaghendi bhaache bhakariina mo obhooto, bhakaghi orughendo koru Pafo, bhakahika momoghi gho Perighe ko omukowa gho Pamufiriya. Ghasi Yohana Maariko akabhatigha hayo, ewe akagharoka Yerusareemu.
Ghasi bhoono, Pauro na Bharinabha bhakaru Perighe bhakaghenderri kohikera omoghi gho Antiyokiya gho ekyaro ke Pisidia. Orosiko rwe Esabhaato bhaghasoha mo enyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, bhaghaikara.
Hano bhaamarre ghusoma mobhitabho bhya amaragherri gha Musa na mobhitabho bhya abharooti, abhabhaahi bha monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema eyo bhakabhatomera amangʼana bharabhughaa, “Bhaghendi bhaitu, ubhone mughoote engʼana yo okubhaha omotema abhanto bhano, turabhasabha moyighambe.”
Pauro akaimerra, akabhaimokeri okubhoko korri bhakire, akaghamba akabhughaa, “Inyu Abhaisiraeri bhaghendi bhaitu na bhansi bhano moghusoka Ghiteema, muntegheerre!
Ghiteema wa abhanto bha Abhaisiraeri, newe oohwere bhasookoro bhiitu. Gho enkaagha eno bhaare bhaamenyire kya abhagheni mokyaro ke Miisiri, akabhakora kubha ekabhira enkoro bhukongʼu. Ku amanagha ghaache amakoro, akabhakangata no okubharuusi mokyaro kiyo.
Hano bhaare mwibhara, akabha arabhaghomerri amakora ghaabho gho enkaagha ye emeeka mirongo ene.
Nawe enkaagha eno amarre ghosiki amakabhira mohungate ghano ghaare ghamenyire mokyaro ghe Kanaani, akaha Abhaisiraeri ekyaro kiyo kibhe eghabho yaabho. Amangʼana ghayo ghansi ngaagheghire enkaagha ye emeeka maghana ane na mirongo etaano(450) igho.
“Hano amangʼana ghayo ghaasirre, Ghiteema akabhaha abhaamori ghukangata abhanto, kohikera enkaagha yo omurooti Saamweri.
Neho, abhanto bhaasabhire bhahaabhu omutemi. Ghiteema akabhaha Sauri, omoona wa Kishi, koru mokabhira ya Bhenyamini. Newe abhaire omutemi ko emeeka mirongo ene(40).
Hano Ghiteema aruusi Sauri ko obhukama, aghatooraho Tauti kubha omutemi waabho. Ghiteema akaghamba ighoro ya Tauti akabhughaa ‘Ndooche Tauti omoona wa Yeese,omonto ono aghuchomera omotema ghoone. Ewe arahekerani amaigha ghaane ghansi.’
“Koru ko orwibhoro ro Tauti, Ghiteema areetiire Abhaisiraeri Omutoori Yeesu, kee bhoore arengire.
Enkaagha Yeesu ataamara asimi emeremo gheeche, Yohana aare kureghaneri abhanto bhansi bha Abhaisiraeri arabhughaa, bhatiite ebhibhe bheebho, na bhabhatiisibhu.
Hano Yohana aare kumareeri emeremo gheeche, akaghamba akabhughaa, ‘Inyu muraitegherra eni ne-wuuye? Eni tere woore Kirisito ono aghuucha! Muntegheerre! Ewe araacha nyuma yaane. Eni ntaisire kuru ghusanchora chensiri che bhiraato ku amaghoro ghaache!’
“Abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaane, abhanto bha orwibhoro ro Bhurahamu, na inyu bhano mutare Abhayahuti bhano musaighire Ghiteema, amangʼana gho obhutoori bhuyo n-gokugheri yiitu!
Abhamenyi bha Yerusareemu na abhabhaahi bhaabho bhataamanyire kubha Yeesu newe Omutoori. Ghwiki bhataamanyire amangʼana gha abharooti ghano ghaghambiru kira Esabhaato. mbaahekeraini amangʼana ghayo ko ghukengera ekiina Yeesu.
Nankabha bhataabhwine risari rinsirinsi ryo komukengera ekiina kyo oghoku, bhaghasabha Piraato aitabherri korri Yeesu aitu.
Hano bhaamarre ghukora amangʼana ghansi ghano ghaandekiru ighoro Yeesu, bhakamusekeri koru komusarabha no komoryeka mombeehera.
Ghasi, Ghiteema akamoryokora koru mubhaku.
Yeesu nawe, gho chensiko echaaru, akabha arahyokera abhanto bhano bhaare kughenda hamwe nawe koru Ghariraaya, kohikera Yerusareemu. Bhoono, bhayo bhabhaire abhaimererri bhaache ku abhanto bha Isiraeri.
“Itu turabhareetera amangʼana amachomu, ghano Ghiteema aarengire bhasookoro bhiitu,
bhoono aghahekeraini haare itu, itu abhaana bhaabho. Gho koryokora Yeesu, Ghiteema ahekeraine ghano ghaandekiru ko Sabhuri ya kabhere ighoo, ‘Iye ni-iye omoona waane, reero eni nimbaire Isawaanyu.’
“Ghwiki, Ghiteema naaryokwere Yeesu koru mubhaku korri atakaaghunda ghwiki. Ighoro ya riyo, Ghiteema akaghamba akabhughaa, ‘Ndabhaha inyu chaghati cho obhuheene, chino naarengire Tauti.’
“Ghote muno aghambire ko Sabhuri yende akabhughaa ‘Taaghotigha Omuhoreeru waacho aghunde ghwiki.’”
“Mbe, enkaagha eno Tauti ahekeraini amangʼana ghansi ghano Ghiteema aare amuragheriiri akore ko enkaagha yo orwibhoro rooche, aghaku, akaryeku haghuhe na bhasookoro bhaache, omobhere ghooche ghukaghunda.
Ghasi bhoono ono Ghiteema aamoryokwere koru mubhaku, ewe taaghundire.
“Ko riyo abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaane, ndatuna inyu mumanye ighoo, gho kuhetera Yeesu, amaabhera ghe ebhibhe gharareghanibhu haare inyu.
Gho kuhetera ewe, kira omonto ono araitabherri Yeesu, arabharru obhoronge. Engʼana eno itakunaghibhu gho kughoota amaragherri gha Musa.
Ko riyo mwiyangarre, ghatakaabhabhona amangʼana ghano ghaaghambiru na abharooti ighoo,
‘Mwiyangarre, inyu bhano moghusera! Muroghoore, mosike, gho okubha ndakora engʼana enkaagha yaanyu, engʼana eno mutaaghwitabherri, kuru ghote omonto akubhabhoorra!’”
Mbe, Pauro na Bharinabha, hano bhaare korichoka kibhara ye enyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, abhanto bhakabhasaasaama bhaghambane nabhu ghwiki amangʼana ghayo, Esabhaato eno eghuucha.
Kuru hano risengero re enyumba ryasiire, Abhayahuti abhaaru na abhanto abhande bhano bhaasohire mu Abhayahuti gho oghusaigha Ghiteema, bhaghatambana Pauro na Bharinabha. Nabhu bhakaghambana nabhu bharabhakumerri bhaghenderri ghwitengʼera enooko ya Ghiteema.
Orosiko rwe Esabhaato eno yatambane, haghuhe na abhanto bhansi momoghi ghuyo bhaghaacha ghutegherra Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro ya Omutemi Yeesu.
Ghasi bhoono Abhayahuti hano bhaarooche obhooru bhwa abhanto, bhakabha no orunyeera, bhaghasimi okunyeerana chinkaani no kughamba amangʼana ghoghusera ighoro ya amangʼana ghano Pauro aare akughamba.
Neho Pauro na Bharinabha bhbhagharokiiri ko bhukare, bharabhughaa , “Ghiteema aatunire inyu Abhayahuti kubha bha ghwansa kubhona engʼana yaache. Ghasi gho okubha moyaangire, mwikengiire ekiina abheene ighoo mutaisire kughegha obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi, bhoono turabhaishooreri abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti.
Gho okubhaOmutemi Ghiteema aghatubhoorra ighoo, ‘Nengukorre iye ubhe obhurabhu ku abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, korri abhanto bhabhone ghutooribhu monse yinsi.’”
Mbe, abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaghachomeru, no ghokumi Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro ya Omutemi Yeesu. Bhansi bhano bhoohwiru kubha no obhuhoru bhwa amakora ghansi, bhaghaitabherri Omutemi Yeesu.
Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro yo Omutemi Yeesu ghaare ghusancha mokyaro kiyo ghinsi.
Ghasi bhoono, Abhayahuti bhaghasegheeri abhaghaikoro bhe chinsoni bhano bhaasaighire Ghiteema, hamwe na abhakangati bho omoghi. Bhayo, bhaghasimi kunyanki Pauro na Bharinabha na bhakabhabheeha bharu mokyaro keebho.
Ko riyo, Pauro na Bharinabha bhaghakongʼonta orotu koru ku amaghoro ghaabho, korri kubhaseghani, nabhu bhakaghi momoghi gho Ikoniyo.
Ghasi bhoono abhatambani bha Yeesu bhano bhaatamire Antiyokiya ya Pisidia eyo, bhakabha bharachomeru bhukongʼu no ghwichoribhu Enkoro Ehoreeru.
Enkaagha Pauro na Bharinabha bhaare momoghi gho Ikoniyo, bhaghasoha mo enyumba ya Abhayahuti yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, ghote bhaare bhanarre. Bhakeeghi ighoro ya Yeesu, kuru Abhayahudi abhaaru hamwe na Abhayunaani, bhaghaitabherri.
Ghasi bhoono Abhayahuti abhande, bhataitabheriiri, bhaghasimi kubhasegherri abhande momoghi bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, korri bhareghe abhaitabherri bhayo.
Pauro na Bharinabha bhakaghenderri kubha Ikoniyo hayo chensiko echaaru. Bhaare kweeghi abhanto ko bhukare ighoro yo Omutemi Yeesu ne enooko yaache. Omutemi nawe, akabha arabhaimererra ighoo amangʼana ghaabho ghaare gho obhuheene, ko okubhaha amanagha gho ghukora ebhimanyerri na amakono.
Ghasi bhoono, abhanto bho omoghi ghuyo, bhaghatwenekana ebhikomo bhibhere. Abhande bhakabha orubhareka rwa Abhayahudi bhe chinkaani, na abhande bhakabha orubhareka rwa abhatomu.
Kumaruho, abhande bha Abhayahuti na abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, bhakaghootana na abhakangati bhaabho, bhaghakora omorwecho gho okubhakorra amasineenu Pauro na Bharinabha no okubhatema na amaghena.
Ghasi bhoono, hano abhatomu bhaamanyire omorwecho ghuyo, bhakangʼosera ahase ha Rikaoniya, bhakahika momeghi gho Risitira na Deribe, na momeghi ghende ghe mbareka ye ekyaro kiyo.
Eyo, bhakaghenderri kweeghi abhanto Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro gha Yeesu.
Momoghi gho Risitira muyo, aaremu omonto omwe. Omonto oyo, aare omubheeru ghokoru okwibhoru ghooche, na takunaghi kughenda.
Hano Pauro aare kweeghi, omonto oyo wunsi aare aikaire hayo, aramutegherra. Pauro akamorigheeri akamurora naghoote obhwitabherri bho kuhoribhu.
Kumaruho, akamubhoorra ko riraka rikoro akabhughaa, “Imerra na amaghoro ghaacho!” Hari remwe, omonto oyo, akaimerra bhongo, aghasimi kughenda omwene.
Hano eghekomo kya abhanto bhayo, bhaarooche ghote Pauro aahorri omonto oyo, bhaghatiiri riraka gho ekighambo keebho kye kirikaoniya bhakabhughaa, “Emisambu ghetusekeriire gho etuubho ya abhanto!”
Bhakabherekera Bharinabha Zewu, eriina re ghiteema waabho omokoro. Na Pauro bhakamubherekera Herime, eriina re ghiteema waabho owonde, gho okubha ewe newe aare omughambi.
Kibhara yo omoghi ghuyo, yaareho enyumba ya ghiteema Zewu. Mbe, omusengeri wa Zewu, akareeta amaghaini ghe chingʼombe chino chatooriru ebhibharyo, mogheseku kyo ghusohera momoghi. Ewe omwene hamwe ne eghekomo kya abhanto, mbaatunire koruuseri ekemwenso abhatomu.
Ghasi bhoono, hano abhatomu Bharinabha na Pauro bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaghatandora chingebho chaabho gho kwereeki ghote bhaakaraire. Kumaruho bhakariyerera abhanto bhaare, bhakabhabhoorra ko riraka rikoro bhakabhughaa,
“Bhamura bhaito! Motighe ghukora igho! Itu bhansi na-abhanto, ghote inyu! Tuuchire hano, kubhabhoorra Amangʼana Amachomu ighoo, motighe ghusaasaama chisanamu chino chitaana ewaara. Mwishooreri Ghiteema ono aani muhoru! Ewe newe aateemire risaaro, ense, enyancha na bhinsi bhino bheemu.
Ono kare hayo, aatighire abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti bhaikare ghote bhaatunire.
Ghasi bhoono, taatighire kwiyereki kubha nehwani. Aare kubhakorra amachomu, gho kureeta embura koru mwisaaro, korri mubhone ebhyakori ne ebhyakori. Aare arabhaha ebhyakori bhyo oghwisa no ghwichori emetema ghaanyu amachomeru.”
gho kughamba amangʼana ghayo, Pauro na Bharinabha bhakanaghi kureki abhanto bhayo gho etaabhu, bhatakaabhamwensera ekemwenso.
Mbe, bhaghaacha Abhayahuti abhande koru momeghi ghe Antiyokiya na Ikoniyo. Bhakangʼaina eghikomo kya abhanto, nabhu bhaghaitabherri. Ko riyo, bhansi bhaghatema Pauro na amaghena, kumaruho, bhakamoruta kohikera kibhara yo omoghi, gho okubha mbaitegheriire kubha, nakuure.
Ghasi bhoono, hano abhatambani bhande bha Yeesu bhaaikomane no okwinaara, Pauro, akabhooka akagharoka momoghi. Icho yaache, ewe na Bharinabha bhaghatanora koghi momoghi gho Deribe.
Pauro na Bharinabha mbaareghaini Amangʼana Amachomu, momoghi gho Deribe, no kubhona abhatambani bha Yeesu abhaaru. Kumaruho bhakagharoka momeghi ghe Risitira, Ikoniyo na Antiyokiya ya Pisidia.
Bhaare ghokumeeri abhatambani bha Yeesu momeghi ghiyo, no okubhaha omotema bhaghenderri ko obhwitabherri. Bhaare kubhabhoorra bharabhughaa, “Itu bhansi turatunu tuhetere ko enyanko eyaaru, korri tusohe mo Obhukama bha Ghiteema.”
Pauro na Bharinabha bhaghachaghorra chikanisa chinsi abhagharuka. Ko ghusabha no kwiyima ebhyakori, bhakabhakabhisi ku amabhoko gho Omutemi ono bhaghwitabherri.
Kumaruho bhakahetera mo omukowa gho Pisidiya, bhaghasoha mo omukowa gho Pamufiiriya,
bhakahika momoghi gho Perighe. Eyo, bhakareghani Engʼana ya Ghiteema. Hano bhaamarre, bhakahiringita momoghi gho Atariya.
Koru Atariya eyo, bhakahetera konyancha no obhooto, bhakagharoka momoghi gho Antiyokiya mo omukowa gho Siriya. Eyo, neho kare abhaitabherri bhaare bhabhasabhire enooko ya Ghiteema ko emeremo ghino bhaare bhaamarre.
Hano bhaahikire Antiyokiya eyo, bhaghakomani hamwe ekanisa. Bhakabhoorra abhaitabherri bhansi ghano Ghiteema akorre kuhetera ebhu, na ghote ahaire abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti omweya gho ghwitabherri Yeesu.
Pauro na Bharinabha bhaghaikara na abhatambani bha Yeesu Antiyokiya hayo, gho enkaagha entambe.
Abhanto nyabhurebhe bhakaru ko omukowa gho Yuudeya, bhakahiringita momoghi gho Antiyokiya. Abhanto bhayo bhaghasimi kweeghi abhaitabherri bharabhughaa, “Hano mutasaaru, kurengʼaana na amaragherri ghano twaahaabhiru na Musa, mutakunaghi ghutooribhu.”
Engʼana eyo ikagheri Pauro na Bharinabha bhatonani na abhanto bhayo, kohikera kughamba amangʼana amakongʼu bhukongʼu. Komohiko, abhaitabherri bhaghakenga ekiina ighoo, Pauro na Bharinabha hamwe na abhande ghati yaabho, bhariine koghi Yerusareemu, korri bhasabhe obhughambi koru ku abhatomu bha Yeesu na abhagharuka bhe ekanisa.
Ko riyo, abhaitabherri bha Antiyokiya bhayo bhakabharagha, nabhu bhakaheta momukowa gho Foinike, na Samaariya, bhakabha bharabhoorra abhaitabherri bha eyo, ghote abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti bhaamwishooriire Ghiteema. Engʼana eyo, ighachomera bhukongʼu abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaabho bhansi bha eyo.
Hano Pauro na bhaghendi bhaache bhayo bhaahikire Yerusareemu, bhakaghaghanibhu bhwaheene na abhatomu bha Yeesu, abhagharuka bhe ekanisa hamwe na abhanto abhande bhe ekanisa. Kumaruho bhaghasimi kubhabhoorra ghansi ghano Ghiteema aare ghukora kuhetera ebhu.
Neho, abhande bha abhaitabherri bha Yeesu, bha ko eghekomo kya Amabharisaayo, bhakaimerra bhakaghamba bhakabhughaa, “Abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, nabhu bharatunu bhabhe bharasaaru, na bhabhoorru ighoo, bhabhe bharaghoota amaragherri ghinsi gha Musa.”
Mbe, abhatomu bha Yeesu na abhagharuka bhe ekanisa bhayo, bhaghakora omoghutano, korri bharoherre bhwaheene engʼana eyo.
Kuru hano enkaagha entambe yo oghutonani, Petiro akaimerra, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Inyu abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaane, mumanyire ighoo, ekimbere hayo, Ghiteema naanchaghwere eni ghati yaanyu, korri ko omonu ghoone, abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti bhooghu Amangʼana ghaache Amachomu, kuhekera bhabhone ghwitabherri.
Ghiteema newe amanyire ghansi ghano ghaani mometema ghya abhanto. Erekiri ighoo, abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti bhansi, nabhaitabheriiri gho okubhaha Enkoro Ehoreeru, ghote aatuhaire itu.
Ghiteema toohwere ghati yiito na ebhu, gho okubha bhansi, naarabhiri emetema gheebho gho nchera yo ghwitabherri Yeesu.
Bhoono, ngooke moghusaghasa Ghiteema, gho okubhanderri abhatambani bha Yeesu bhayo, bhaghoote amaragherri gha Musa? Kuru bhasookoro bhiitu na itu abheene ntutamiru naghu!
Itu turaitabherri ighoo, turatooribhu ko enooko yo Omutemi Yeesu eyeene. Na ebhu bhansi, bharatooribhu ko enooko eyo.”
Mbe, abhanto bhansi bhano bhaare ko omoghutano hayo, bhaghakira kiri. Bharinabha na Pauro, bhakabha bharabhabhoorra ghote Ghiteema aare ghukora ebhimanyerri na amakono kubhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti kuhetera ebhu.
Hano bhaamarre kughamba, Yaakobho nawe, akaghamba akabhughaa, “Abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaane, Muntegheerre.
Simooni atubhooriire ghote Ghiteema aanyankire abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, korri ohore abhande bhaabho, bhabhe abhanto bhaache.
Amangʼana ghayo, ghararengerrani na amangʼana gha Ghiteema ghano ghaandekiru na abharooti ighoo,
‘Hano amangʼana ghayo gharasire, ndagharoka, ndaabheka bhohe enyumba ya Tauti eno yahanyokire. Ndaabheka enyumba eyo, no okoyimerri ghwiki.
Kee hayo, abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti na abhande, bhansi bhano mberekiire korri bhabhe abhanto waane, bharantuna, eni Omutemi.
Omutemi Ghiteema naabhooriire abhanto engʼana eno koru kare.’”
Yaakobho akaghenderri kughamba arabhughaa, “N-go kubha ino, eni ndarora ighoo, totighe kunyanki abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, bhano bhaishooriiri Ghiteema.
Ghasi bhoono, turatunu tubhandekere ebharuwa yo kubhabhoorra ighoo, bhatakaaraghera ebhyakori bhyo moghiro bhino bhisengiire omusambu. Ghwiki bhatakaabha bharakorra obhotwari, bhatighe kori enyama ye etyenyi eno ebhuusiru, na bhatighe kori amaanyinga.
Koru kare, amaragherri gha Musa ghareeghibhu kira omoghi, gho okubha gharasomu mochenyumba cha Abhayahuti kira orosiko rwe Esabhaato.”
Kumaruho, abhatomu bha Yeesu, abhagharuka bhe ekanisa hamwe na abhaitabherri abhande bhansi bho omoghi gho Yerusareemu hayo, bhaghakenga ekiina okoohora abhanto bhande ghati yaabho, korri bhaghende momoghi gho Antiyokiya hamwe na Pauro na Bharinabha. Mbe, bhakoohora abhakoro bhabhere mubhayo, Yuuta ono eriina erende aare akubherekeru Bharisabha, hamwe na Sira.
Hano bhaamarre, akabhaha enyarubha. Ebharuwa eyo, yaare yandekiru ighoo, “Itu abhatomu hamwe na abhagharuka bhe ekanisa, itu abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaanyu, turabhakeeri inyu bhano mutare Abhayahuti, inyu bha momoghi gho Antiyokiya, na ko mikowa ghe Siriya na Kirikiya.
Tooghuure ighoo, bhaghendi bhiitu abhande koru haare itu mbaahikire haare inyu, bhakabhanyanki na amangʼana ghaabho, mughasari omurembe mochinkoro chaanyu. Ghasi bhoono itu tutaabhatomire.
Ko riyo, twitabherraini hamwe, okoohora abhanto bhande no kubhareta haare inyu korri bhabhe, hamwe na abhasaigha bhaitu Bharinabha na Pauro.
Bhabhere bhayo, bhairuusiri obhuhoru bhoobho, ko okugheri ko ghukorra emeremo Omutemi waito Yeesu Kirisito.
Turabhatoma haare inyu Yuuda na Sira. Bhayo nebhu bharabhabhoorre amangʼana ghano tubhandekiire.
Mbe, Enkoro Ehoreeru na itu torooche mbwaheene ighoo tutakaabhaitweki omorigho ghonde omorito, ghukera amangʼana amakoro ghano ghaghuucha.
Mutaghaacha kori ebhyakori bhino bhisengiire omusambu, motighe kori amaanyinga, kuru enyama ye etyenyi eno ebhuusiru, na motighe ghukora obhotwari. Hano moghotigha ghayo, neho mokubha mukoriire bhwaheene. Obhukeerani.”
kee hayo bhakaragha, bhaghateremoka koghi momoghi gho Antiyokiya. Hano bhaahikire, bhaghakomani abhaitabherri bhansi, akabhaha enyarubha eyo.
Nabhu hano bhaamarre koyisoma, bhaghachomeru bhukongʼu, ku amangʼana ghayo gho okubhaha omotema.
Yuuta na Sira bhaare abharooti, bhakabhoorra abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhoobho amangʼana amaaru gho okubhaha omotema no okubharuuseri ehaho ko obhwitabherri bhoobho.
Hano bhaamarre ghwikara Antiyokiya eyo gho enkaagha nyabhurebhe, abhaitabherri bha eyo bhakabhaitabherri bhagharoke ne mirembe ku bhano bhaabhatomire. [
Ghasi bhoono Sira ewe akarora ighoo, mbwaheene atame eyo.]
Pauro na Bharinabha nabhu, mbaatamire Antiyokiya eyo. Ebhu, hamwe na abhanto abhande abhaaru, bhakabha bharareghani na bhareeghi abhanto Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro yo Omutemi Yeesu.
Hano chensiko nsuuhu chaahetire, Pauro akabhoorra Bharinabha akabhughaa, “Tugharoke tutaare abhaitabherri momeghi ghinsi ghino tweeghiri Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro yo Omutemi Yeesu, korri tubhe turaroherra ghote bhaghendi bhaitu bhakughenderri.”
Bharinabha naatunire ighoo, bhaghende hamwe na Yohana ono eriina erende aare akubherekeru Maariko.
Ghasi bhoono Pauro naarooche, tare bhwaheene bhaghende hamwe na Maariko oyo, gho okubha naare abhatighire ko omukowa gho Pamufiiriya, na aare angire kughenderri ghukora emeremo hamwe nabhu.
Mbe, ghukabha ne chinkaani chindoro ghati ya Pauro na Bharinabha ighoro ye engʼana eyo. Ko riyo, bhaghaitweni. Bharinabha akaghegha Maariko, bhakaghi hamwe mo obhooto kwighinga re Kipuro.
Pauro nawe, akaghegha Sira. Hano abhaitabherri bha eyo bhaamarre komusabhera enooko yo Omutemi Yeesu, akaru hayo.
Akahetera ko mikowa ghe Siriya na Kirikiya, arakongʼerri chikanisa.
Pauro akahika momeghi gho Deribe, na Risitira. Risitira eyo, aareho omutamboni omwe wa Yeesu. Omutamboni oyo, aare kubherekeru Timoteo. Nyakuwaabho aare Omuyahuti na aare aitabheriiri Yeesu. Ghasi bhoono, isawaabho aare Omoyunaani.
Timoteo aare arakumibhu bhukongʼu ghati ya abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaache bha Risitira na Ikoniyo eyo.
Pauro naatunire ighoo, bhabhe bharaghi hamwe ko orughendo na Timoteo oyo. Ghasi bhoono Abhayahuti bhansi bhano bhaare bhamenyire ahase hayo, mbaamanyire ighoo isawaabho Timoteo n-Omoyunaani. Ko riyo, Pauro akaghamba ighoo, Timoteo asaaru, korri bhachomeru.
Hano Pauro na bhaghendi bhaache bhayo bhaare kuheta momeghi gheere, bhakabha bharabhaha abhaitabherri amaragherri ghano ghamwiru na abhatomu na abhagharuka momoghi gho Yerusareemu, korri bhaghaghoote.
Ko riyo, abhaitabherri bha eyo bhakaghenderri ghukongʼa ko obhwitabherri, na bhakabha bharaaruha kira orosiko.
Pauro na bhaghendi bhaache bhayo, bhaare bhaseghainibhu ne Enkoro Ehoreeru kubha bhatighe kweeghi Engʼana ya Ghiteema mo omukowa gho Asiya. Ko riyo, bhakaheta mo mikowa ghe Furighiya na Gharatiya.
Hano bhaahikire ko oroghumba ro omukowa gho Misiya, bhaghacharibhu ghusoha omukowa gho Bhitiniya, ghasi bhoono Enkoro wa Yeesu atabhaitabheriiri.
Ko riyo, bhakahetera Misiya, bhakaghi momoghi gho Turowa.
Hano bhaahikire eyo, obhotiko Pauro aghaicheru na amaroro. Mu amaroro ghayo, naarooche omonto aimeriire ko omukowa gho Makedoniya, arasaasaama bhukongʼu arabhughaa, “Omboka enyancha, uuche Makedoniya eno, otusakeri!”
Mbe, hano Pauro aamarre kurora amaroro ghayo, hari remwe tughaiseemi koghi Makedoniya eyo, gho okubha ntwaarooche aghoo, obhuheene Ghiteema atubherekiire kureghani Amangʼana Amachomu ku abhanto bha eyo.
Mbe, tukaru Turowa hayo no obhooto, tukaghi kemwe kemwe kuhekera ko righinga rino rekubherekeru, Samotirake. Hano bhwaakiire, tukaghi ghwiki no obhooto, tukahika momoghi gho Neyapori.
Koru eyo, tukaghi kuhekera momoghi gho Firipi, omoghi omokoro mo omukowa gho Makedoniya, na neghu omoghi ghuno Abharumi bhaare bhamenyire. Mbe, tughaikara momoghi ghuyo gho chensiko nsuuhu.
Orosiko rwe Esabhaato, tukaghi kibhara yo omoghi ghuyo, mbareka yo orooche, gho okubha tware turaitegherra ighoo, turabhona ahase ho ghusaasaamera. Ntwaaikaire, tughasimi kughambana na abhaghaikoro bhano bhaare bhaikomaine hayo.
Mu bhano bhaare ghotutegherra, aareho omughaikoro omwe wo omoghi gho Tiyatira, eriina reeche aare kubherekeru Ridiya. Ridiya oyo, aare omughori we chingebho chinchomu che erangi ya sambarau, na aare Omoyunaani ono aghusoka Ghiteema. Hano Pauro abhabhooriire Amangʼana Amachomu gha Yeesu, Omutemi Ghiteema akaighora enkoro ya Ridiya, aghaitabherri ameeghi gha Pauro.
Neho akabhatisibhu, ewe hamwe na abhanto bha monyumba yaache. Kumaruho aghatusaasaama bhukongʼu arabhughaa, “Ghote murooche ighoo, obhuheene eni ndaitabherri Omutemi Yeesu, ndabhaghaghaani mwikare waane.” Akaghenderri ghotusaasaama bhukongʼu tughende waache.
Orosiko romwe, hano tware koghi ahase haare ho ghusaasaamera, tughasikana no omubhaghasi omwe we kighaikoro. Omonke oyo, aare no omusambu. Omusambu ghuyo, ghware komuha amanagha gho kuroota amangʼana ghano ghakubha mbere. Kuhetera obhurooti bhooche bhuyo, abhakoro bhaache bhaare kubhona chembiri echaaru.
Omonke oyo, akabha aratambana Pauro na itu, eno aratema ekereghe arabhughaa, “Abhanto bhano n-abhabhaghasi bha Ghiteema wa ighoro ya bhinsi. Bharabhareghaneri ghote mokunaghi ghutooribhu!”
Omonke oyo, akaghenderri ghukora kee hayo, gho chensiko echaaru. Kumaruho Pauro aghakarra bhukongʼu. Aghaishoori no kubhoorra omusambu ghoore ighoo, “Ndakubhoora ko eriina re Yeesu Kirisito oru ko omonke ono!” Hayo hayo, omusambu ghuyo ghukamoru.
Mbe, hano abhakoro bho omonke oyo, bhaarooche aghoo, bhataana enchera yende yo kubhona chembiri, bhakaghoota Pauro na Sira, bhakabharuta kuhekera mwitongo mbere ya abhabhaahi bho omoghi.
Hano bhaahikire ku abhaamori, bhakabhasemera ighoo, “Abhasubhe bhano n-Abhayahuti, bharareeta riihe momoghi ghwitu.
Ghwiki bharatweeghi amangʼana ghe eteemo eno haare itu Abharumi, tutaghotunu koyitabherri no okoighoota.”
Hari remwe, obhooru bho abhanto bhano bhaare bhaikomaine hayo, bhakaghi ko ghukarra bhaghaitani Pauro na Sira. Abhaamori bhaare bhakabharuusi chingebho chaabho gho chenguru, bhaghakenga ekiina ighoo, bhatemu bhorro.
Na hano bhaamarre okubhatema bhorro, bhakabhatoora mokibhohe, kumaruho bhakabhoorra omosirikare omokoro we kibhohe abharende bhwaheene.
Kurengʼaana na amaragherri ghayo, omokoro we kibhohe oyo akabhatoorra mo eghechumba ke morense, akabhabhoha amaghoro ghaabho ne eminyorro.
Mbe, obhotiko ke ghati, Pauro na Sira bhaare bharasaasaama Ghiteema no kubhenerra amareeti gho ghwitumi. Abhabhohe bhaghendi bhoobho bhaare kubhategherra.
Hari remwe, ekerighiti ekerito bhukongʼu ghikahyoka, kuru omosingi ghwe kibhohe ghughasingisibhu. Hayo hayo, emirango ghe kibhohe ghikaighoka ne eminyorro ghino ghyare ghibhohire kira omwe ghighatanchoka.
Omokoro we kibhohe woore, akabhooka. Hano aarooche emirango ghe kibhohe ghighokire, akaruta ekinyamaino gheeche, aghatuna kwiyita, gho okubha aare aghwitegherra ighoo, abhabhohe bhansi mbangʼosire.
Ghasi bhoono Pauro aghatema ekereghe ko riraka rikoro akabhughaa, “Utakaiyita! Bhansi muno tooni!”
Hayo, omokoro we kibhohe oyo, akaragherri ighoo etara ireetu. Hano yaareetiru, aghasoha bhongo muyo mokibhohe, akahighama mbere ya Pauro na Sira eno araghankana.
Kumaruho akabhahira kibhara, akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Abhakoro bhaane, ndatunu nkore ke korri ntoribhu?”
Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, “Witabherri Omutemi Yeesu, iye na abhanto bhano bhaani waacho ka, neho mughutooribhu.”
Mbe, Pauro na Sira bhakamweeghi Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro yo Omutemi Yeesu, ewe hamwe na abhanto bhansi bhano bhaare waache ka.
Enkaagha yeere yeere obhotiko, omokoro we kibhohe oyo, akabhaghegha akabheeghi ebhetonda bheebho. Kumaruho akabhatiisu ewe na abhanto bhaache bhansi.
Hano aamarre akabhahira waache ka, akabhaseemeri ebhyakori. Aghachomeru bhukongʼu hamwe na bha waabho bhayo bhansi, gho okubha aitabheriire Ghiteema.
Hano bhwaakiire, abhaamori bhaare bhaghatoma abhakoro bha abhasirikare ko omokoro we kibhohe, bhamubhoorre bhabhughee, “Bhatanchora abhanto bhaare ubhatighe bhaghende echaabho.”
Omokoro we kibhohe oyo, hano aabhooriiru kee hayo, akabhoorra Pauro akabhughaa, “Abhaamori bhatomire abhanto ighoo, mbatanchore. Bhoono moru kibhara, mughende ne mirembe.”
Ghasi bhoono Pauro akabhoorra abhakoro bha abhasirikare bhaare akabhughaa, “Ake abhaamori bhayo bhatutemire bhorro bhukongʼu mbere ya abhanto bhira ghotukengera ekiina, na itu m-mbarumi tooni! Bhaghatutoora mokibhohe. Na bhoono bharatuna obhuheene ghotoruusi muno ko kebhisire? Hasehe! Bhaache abheene bhatoruusi mokibhohe muyo.”
Abhakoro bha abhasirikare bhayo bhakagharoka, bhakabhoorra abhaamori bhaare amangʼana ghayo. Mbe, abhaamori bhayo hano bhooghuure kee hayo, Pauro na Sira m-Mbarumi, bhakoobhoha bhukongʼu.
Ko riyo, bhakaghi kubhasaasaama, bhakabharuusi mokibhohe, kumaruho bhakabhasaasaama bharu momoghi muyo.
Pauro na Sira, hano bhaaruure mokibhohe, bhakaghi ka mo Ridiya. Bhaghaikomana hayo na abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhoobho, bhakabhaha omotema, neho bhaghatanora.
Pauro na Sira mbaahetire momeghi ghe Amufipori na Aporoniya, kuhekera bhakahika momoghi gho Tesaronike. Tesaronike hayo, yaareho enyumba ya Abhayahuti yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema
Pauro akabha arasoha mo enyumba ye bhiina ya Abhayahuti, ghote muno aare anarre. Ko enkaagha ye Esabhaato ye che wiiki etato, akabha araghambana nabhu, aghoote Amandeko Amahoreeru.
Akabhabhoorra na kubheereki ighoo, Kirisito aare ghotunu anyankibhu, no oghwitu, na ghwiki ighoo, aare ghotunu aryoke koru mubhaku. Pauro akaghenderri kubhabhoorra ighoo, “Kirisito uno ndabhabhoorra ighoro yaache, newe Yeesu.”
Amangʼana ghayo Pauro aare arabhugha, Abhayahuti abhande bhaghaitabherri, hamwe na Abhayunaani abhaaru bhano bhaare ghusooka Ghiteema. Kuru abhaghaikoro abhaaru bhano bhaasookiru gho ekyaro kiyo, bhansi bhaghaitabherri. Bhayo bhansi bhakaghootana na Pauro na Sira.
Ghasi Abhayahuti bhano bhataitabheriiri, bhakabha na orunyeera. Ko riyo, bhakaghi momoteera bhaghakoodisi abhasineenu, kumaruho bhaghakora riihe momoghi ghunsi. Abhasineenu bhayo, bhakaghi bhaghasoha gho chenguru o Yasooni ka ghotuna Pauro na Sira, korri bhabhahire mbere ye eghekomo kya abhanto.
Na hano bhataabhabhwine, bhakaghoota Yasooni na abhaitabherri abhande bhakabhahira mbere ya abhabhaahi bho omoghi, eno bharatema ekereghe ighoo, “Abhanto bhano bhaare bharakorra riihe ko ebhyaro ebheeru, bhoono bhahikire kuru hano!
Yasooni ono abhakaribhisiri waache ka. Bhansi bharasari amaragherri gha Kaisari, gho kughamba ighoo, aareho omutemi owonde ono aare kubherekeru Yeesu.”
Abhabhaahi bha omoghi hamwe na obhooru bha abhanto bhayo, hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaghaitaki na ghukarra bhukongʼu.
Bhakaghoota enchagho Yasooni na bhaghendi bhaache enchagho, kumaruho bhakabhatigha.
Hano obhotiko bhwasohire, abhaitabherri bhaare bhakahira Pauro na Sira momoghi gho Bherooya. Nebhu, hano bhaahikire eyo, bhaghasoha mo enyumba ya Abhayahuti yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema.
Abhayahuti bha Bherooya hayo, bhaare abhaheene ghukera bhaare bha momoghi gho Tesaronike. Ko riyo, hano Pauro aabhareghaniiri amangʼana gha Ghiteema, bhakaghategherra ko ghwikongʼi bhukongʼu. Bhakabha bhararoherra ku Amandeko Amahoreeru gha Ghiteema kira orosiko, korri bharore ghote amangʼana ghano Pauro aabhughire n-ga obhuheene.
Mbe, Abhayahuti abhaaru bhaghaitabherri Yeesu, hamwe na Abhayunaani abhaaru, bhansi abhasubhe na abhaghaikoro bhano bhaare ghusooku.
Mbe, Abhayahuti bha Tesaronike bhaare, hano bhaamanyire ighoo, Pauro areeghi Engʼana ya Ghiteema momoghi gho Bherooya ghwiki, bhakaghi eyo. Hano bhaahikire, bhaghasegheeri eghekomo kya abhanto bhano bhaare hayo, kuhekera riihe rikahyoka.
Neho abhaitabherri bha Bherooya hayo bhakamohira Pauro kuhekera mongoghoni. Ghasi Sira na Timoteo abheene bhatame Bherooya hayo.
Abhaitabherri bhano bhaherekeriire Pauro, bhakamohira kohikera momoghi gho Atene. Kumaruho bhakagharoka Bherooya, bhaare bhatomiru na Pauro ighoo, bhabhoorre Sira na Timoteo ighoo, bhamutambane bhongo.
Hano Pauro aare kughanya Sira na Timoteo momoghi gho Atene eyo, akarora omoghi ghunsi ghwichwire emisambu. Hano aarooche kee hayo, akanyahaareka bhukongʼu momotema ghooche.
Ko riyo, akabha araghi mochenyumba kughambana na Abhayahudi na Abhayunaani bhano bhaare bharamusooka Ghiteema. Ghwiki kira orosiko aare araghambana na abhanto bhano aare ghosikana nabhu momoteera.
Mbe, Pauro aghasikana ghwiki na abhasomi bhasuuhu bhe eghekomo ke Ekiyepikuriyo, na ke Ekisitoyiko. Nabhu bhaghasimi okunyeerana chinkaani nawe. Abhande ghati yaabho bhakabhugha ighoo “Omutemi we egheturi ono aratuna kughamba ke?” Abhande bhakabhugha ighoo, “Ironekana ighoo arareghani ighoro ya bhaghiteemi abhagheni.” Bhakabhugha igho, gho okubha naareghaini ighoro ya Yeesu na okuryoka mubhaku.
Mbe, abhasomi bhayo bhakahira Pauro ghwitongo rinene rino ryare kubherekeru ighoo, Areopagho. Hano bhaahikire ghwitongo riyo, bhakamubhoori ighoo, “Ameeghi amahe ghano okweeghi m-meeghi ke? Turatuna tughamanye!
Iye uratureetera amangʼana amahe, ko riyo turatuna tumanye, amangʼana ghayo, ghote ghaanyi.”
Bhakabhugha igho, gho okubha abhanto bha Atene eyo, hamwe na abhagheni koru ko ebhyaro ebhende bhano bhaare bhamenyire muyo, bhaare ghotumia enkaagha yaabho ghutegherra no kughamba ighoro ya amangʼana amahe agheene.
Neho Pauro akaimerra ghatighati ye ritongo re Areopagho riyo, akaghamba akabhughaa, “Inyu abhanto bha Atene! Ndarora ighoo, inyu na-abhanto bhano murasaigha bhukongʼu amangʼana ghansi ghe etiini.
Hano naare kughenda ghenda momoghi muno, ndooche amangʼana ghaanyu gho ghusaasaama. Ndooche kuru amasengero ghano ghaandekiru amangʼana ghano, o ghiteema ono atamanyikaine. Mbe, Ghiteema ono moghusaasaama bhira komumanya, newe eni nkubhareghaneri.
“Ghiteema n-omokoro wa mwisaaro na monse, gho okubha newe aateemire ense ne ebhinto bhinsi bhino bheemu. Taghwikara mu ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema hano haabhekiru na abhanto.
Ewe ataghote chitaabhu, ko ighoo abhanto bhamukorre emeremo. Omwene newe arabhaha abhanto bhansi obhuhoru no omwika ne ebhinto bhinsi.
Ewe newe aateemire amakabhira ghansi, koru ko omonto omwe, korri bhaikare mokyaro ghinsi. Akabhatorra ne enkaagha yo kumenya bhano aare atunire koru kare, akabhatoorra no mpaka ghwa ahase hano bharamenye.
Ghiteema akorre kee hayo, korri abhanto bhamotune, nankabha gho kwabhaabha abhaabha, kuhekera bhamubhone. Ghasi bhoono, Ghiteema atare kure itu,
gho okubha newe aghukora itu turabhaho, turaghenda no kubha no obhuhoru bhwitu. N-ghote muno omwe waanyu, omwandeki we rireeti, aabhughire ighoo, ‘Itu bhansi n-abhaana bhaache.’
“Mbe, ko kubha itu n-abhaana bha Ghiteema, tutaghaitegherra kubha, arahekaana ne emisambu ghino gheghukoru na amadiini ghe chisahabhu, hande ku amadiini ghe chembiri, hande na amaghena. ghiyo ghinsi ghirakoru ko obhumanyi no obhungʼaini bhwa abhanto.
Hayo kare abhanto bhaare bharakorra ghayo ko obhukangi, na Ghiteema aikorre ghote atakugharora. Ghasi bhoono, arabhoorra abhanto bhansi bha kira ahase ighoo, bhamwishooreri.
Ko riyo, aatoorre orosiko runo arakengera abhanto bhansi bha ense ebhiina ko obhoronge. Arakora kee hayo, gho kuhetera omonto ono aamohwere. Ghiteema eerekiiri obhuheene bhwe engʼana eyo, gho koryokora omonto oyo koru mubhaku!”
Mbe, hano bhooghuure Pauro arabhugha ighoro ya amangʼana gho okuryoka mubhaku, abhande bhaghasimi komusera, ghasi abhande bhakamubhoorra ighoo, “Turaghutegherra ghwiki ighoro ye engʼana eyo.”
Ko riyo, Pauro akaru ghwitongo reere, akaghi chaache.
Ghasi bhoono abhanto abhande bhakaghootana na Pauro, bhaghaitabherri Yeesu. Mubhayo aaremu Diyonisiyo, omwe we ritongo reere re Areopagho, na omughaikoro omwe ono aare kubherekeru Damari, hamwe na abhanto abhande.
Amangʼana ghayo hano ghaasirre, Pauro akaru momoghi gho Atene hayo, akaghi momoghi gho Korinto.
Eyo aghasikana no Omuyahuti omwe. Omuyahuti oyo aare kubherekeru Akira, na aare omumenyi wa momukowa gho Ponto. Akira oyo, hamwe purisira mughaache, bhaare bharweriire momoghi gho Ruumi, mokyaro ke Itaariya gho chensiko chiyo chiyo. Mbaarweriire eyo, gho okubha Kaisari Kiraudiyo aare ghotuna, Abhayahuti bhansi bharu momoghi ghuyo. Mbe, Pauro aghakeri Akira na mughaache.
Pauro aare arakora emeremo ghyo ghotuma amahooru ghote ebhu, ko riyo aghaikara waabho, bhakabha bharakorra emeremo hamwe.
Kira orosiko rwe Esabhaato, Pauro aare ghusoha mo enyumba ye bhiina ko Abhayahuti, akabha araghamba nebhu ighoro ya Yeesu. Aare ghucharibhu koruta Abhayahuti na Abhayunaani, korri nabhu bhamwitabherri.
Sira na Timoteo hano bhaahikire hayo, koru Makedoniya, Pauro aghasimi koruusi enkaagha yaache yinsi kweeghi engʼana ye Ghiteema ko Abhayahuti, akabhakumerri ighoo, Yeesu newe Kirisito.
Ghasi, Abhayahuti bhayo, bhaghasimi komunyeera chinkaani no komutoka. Ewe akabhakongʼontera chingebho chaache kwereki ighoo, araiyohora nabhu, ino arabhabhoorra ighoo, “Amaanyinga yaanyu, ghabhe ighoro yaanyu abheene! Eni tingoote obhusari, niimarre ghukora aghaane ghano ngotunu nkore. Kuwansera bhoono igho, ndaghi ku abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti.”
Kumaruho Pauro akaru ko enyumba ye bhiina eyo, aghasoha mo enyumba yo omonto omwe. Omonto oyo, aare arabherekeru Tiito Yusito, na aare Omoyunaani ono asaighire Ghiteema. Enyumba yaache yaare haghuhe na enyumba ye bhiina eyo.
Omokoro we enyumba ye bhiina eyo, eriina reeche Kirisipo, aghaitabherri Omutemi Yeesu, hamwe na abhanto bhansi bha ka waache. Na kuru Abhakorinto abhande abhaaru bhano bhooghuure amangʼana gho Pauro, bhaghaitabherri Yeesu, bhakabhaatiisibhu.
Orosiko romwe obhotiko, Omutemi Yeesu akabhoorra Pauro ko amaroro ighoo, “Tigha koobhoha, ghenderri kweeghi, utaghakira.
Eni neni hamwe na iye, tareho kuru omonto omwe eyo ono araaghoturi, korri akunyahaare. Gho kubha, ningoote abhanto abhaaru momoghi muno bhano bharaanyishooreri.”
Ko riyo, Pauro aghaikara Korinto eyo, enkaagha yo omoka ghomwe ne ritingita, areeghi abhanto Engʼana ya Ghiteema
Enkaagha Ghariyo aare omukangati wo omukowa gho Akaya, Abhayahuti bhansi hamwe bhakaghoota Pauro. Bhakamohira mbere ya eghetumbe kyo ghukengera ebhiina kyo Ghariyo,
bhakasemera Pauro ighoo, “Omonto ono arangʼaina abhanto bhasengere Ghiteema gho nchera eno itaghwitabherribhu ku amaragherri ghiitu.”
Pauro hano aatunire kughamba, Ghariyo akabhoorra Abhayahuti bhayo ighoo, “Inyu Abhayahuti, hano mwaghachongire omonto ono ighoro ya obhosineenu hande obhusari, hayo naare kubhategherra.
Ghasi, gho okubha muranyeerana chinkaani ighoro ya amangʼana agheene, amariina, na amaragherri ghaanyu, mughamare inyu abheene. Eni ntare omwamori wa amangʼana ghano.”
Kumaruho Ghariyo akabhatyambi mbere ye eghetumbe gheeche kyo ghukengera ebhiina.
Neho bhansi bhakaghoota Sositene, omokoro we enyumba ye bhiina. Bhakamutema hayo hayo mbere ya eghetumbe ke ghukengera ebhiina. Ghasi ghano bhaakorre, Ghariyo taarooche kubha ne-engʼana.
Pauro akengeri chensiko chende echaaru momoghi gho Korinto. Hano aamarre enkaagha eyo, akaragha abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaache bha hayo, akaghi momoghi gho Kenkireya. Hayo akaghasa rituuki reeche gho okubha aare ariire emuuma. Kumaruho ewe hamwe na purisira na Akira bhakariina mobhooto, bhakaghi ko omukowa gho Siriya.
Hano bhaahikire momoghi gho Efeso, Pauro aghatigha Purisira na Akira eyo. Ewe aghasoha mo enyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, akaghambana na Abhayahuti.
Abhayahuti bhayo bhaghasabha Pauro engeri chensiko chende cho kubha nabhu hayo, ghasi ataitabhiriire.
Hano abharaghire, akabhabhoorra ighoo, “Ghiteema arasaighe, ndagharoka ghwiki.” Kumaruho aghatanora hayo Efeso ko bhooto.
Pauro hano aahikire momoghi gho Kaisariya, akariina momoghi gho Yerusareemu, ghukeeri ekanisa ya eyo. Kumaruho akahiringita momoghi gho Antiyokiya.
Hano aare amarre chensiko nsuuhu echeene, akaru hayo, akabha araheta mo mikowa ghe Gharatiya na Furighiya, aani arakongʼerri abhatambani bhansi.
Ko enkaagha eyo, Omuyahuti omwe aahikire momoghi gho Efeso, uno aare kubherekeru Aporo. Ewe aare omwibhoru wo omoghi gho Arekisandiriya, na aare na amanagha amakoro bha kughamba, na kumanya Amandeko Amahoreeru.
Omonto oyo, aare eghiribhu Enchera yo Omutemi Yeesu. Na gho okubha enkoro yaache yaare ghooka, aaghasimi kughamba no okweghi ko obhuheene amangʼana ighoro ya Yeesu. Ghasi bhoono ko orubhareka ro obhubhaatiiso, aare amanyire ighoro yo obhubhaatiiso bho Yohana obhwene .
Mbe, Aporo oyo aghasoha mo enyumba ya Abhayahuti yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, aghasimi kweeghi abhanto ko bhukare. Purisira na Akira, hano bhooghuure areeghi, bhakamughegha, bhakamuragherri enchera ya Omutemi ko bhuheene bhukongʼu.
Enkaagha yende, Aporo aghatuna koghi omukowa gho Akaya. Abhatambani bhaghendi bhaache bhakamwitabherri, bhakabhandekera abhatambani bhaghendi bhaabho bha eyo enyarubha ighoo, bhamughaghaani bhwaheene. Hano aahikire eyo, akabha aratoorri bhukongʼu bhano bhaare bharaitabherri Yeesu ko enooko ya Ghiteema.
Aporo akabhatooreri ko ghukera Abhayahuti harabhu. Akeereki Abhayahuti bhayo koru mu Amandeko Amahoreeru ighoo Yeesu newe Kirisito.
Hano Aporo aare momoghi gho Korinto, Pauro akabha araheta momeghi ghyo orukereghe, akaherengetera momoghi gho Efeso. Eyo, aghasikana na abhatambani bha Yeesu abhande,
akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Hano mwaitabheriiri Yeesu, mukabhoona ne Enkoro Ehoreeru?” Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, “Hasehe, kuru tutakooghwiire ighoo, aaho Enkoro Ehoreeru.”
Neho, Pauro akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Mbubhaatiisu ke mwabhaatiisiru?” Bhakamugharokeri bhakabhughaa, “Ko obhubhaatiiso bhuno Yohana eeghiri.”
Pauro akabhughaa, “Yohana aare arabhaatiisi abhanto bhano bhaare bhaishooriiri Ghiteema, akabha arabhabhoorra ighoo, bhaache bhamwitabherri uno aghuucha nyuma yaache, na oyo newe Yeesu.”
Hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhakabhaatiisibhu ko eriina ryo Omutemi Yeesu.
Enkaagha eno Pauro aare kubhatoora amabhoko ghaache, Enkoro Ehoreeru akabhasekerra, bhaghasimi kughamba ko ebhighambo ebhende no okoruusi obhurooti.
Abhanto bhayo bhansi, bhaare abhasubhe ghote ikomi na bhabhere.
Gho enkaagha ye emieri etato, Pauro aare araghi monyumba ya Abhayahudi yo oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, akabha araghamba kobhukare, amangʼana ghano ghaghuchomera abhanto ighoro yo obhukangati bho Ghiteema, korri bhamwitabherri.
Ghasi abhande bhaghakora emetema gheebho ghibhe emikongʼu. Bhakabha bharanga ghwitabherri amangʼana ghaache ighoro ya Yeesu, bhaghasimi koghasera mbere yo obhooru bha abhanto. Ko riyo, Pauro aghatighana nabhu, akoohora abhatambani, akaghi nabhu koridarasa re Tirano. Kira orosiko akabha araghambana nabhu muyo ighoro ya Yeesu.
Pauro akamara muyo emeeka ebhere, areeghi ighoro ya Yeesu, kuhekera abhamenyi bhansi bho omukowa gho Asiya, Abhayahuti na bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, bhakabha bhoghuure Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro ya Omutemi Yeesu.
Ghiteema akorre amakono gho kuroghoori ko kuhetera amabhoko gha Pauro.
Kuru ebhitambaara ne chingebho chino chaaruure ko omobhere gho Pauro, chikahiru ko abharwire. Nabhu bhakahora amarwire ghaabho, na emisambu ghikaru haare ebhu.
Bhaareho Abhayahuti abhande bhano bhaare bharaghenda ino na ino, bharatyambi emisambu koru ko abhanto. Bhakabha bharacharibhu kotyambi emisambu koghotumia eriina ryo Omutemi Yeesu, bharabhughaa, “Ko eriina rye Yeesu, uno Pauro arareghani, ndabhabhoorra ndabhughaa, moru ko omonto uno!”
Ghati ya bhano bhaare bharakorra kehayo, bhaare abhaana mohungate bha Sikewa. Ewe aare Omuyahuti na omokoro wa abhasengeri.
Ghasi omusambu ghukabhagharokeri ghukabhughaa, “Yeesu tomumanyire, na Pauro wunsi tomumanyire. Bhoono inyu ne-wuuye?”
Hari remwe, omonto uno aare na omusambu akabhabhurukera, akabhatema akabhakeri chenguru bhansi. Bhakaru monyumba muyo bhararyera, bhaani kingʼaabhi ino bhanyaharekire.
Amangʼana ghayo ghakamanyikana bhukongʼu ko bhansi bhano bhaare bhamenyire momoghi gho Efeso, Abhayahuti na bhano bhatare Abhayahuti. Bhayo bhansi bhakobhoobha, bhaghaitumi eriina ro Omutemi Yeesu bhukongʼu.
Mbe, abhanto abhaaru ghati ya bhano bhaitabheriiri Yeesu, bhaaichire bhakaghootana mbere ya abhanto amakora ghaabho amasineenu ghano bhaare bhakorre.
Ekirengero eghekoro kya bhaare bhano bhaakorre amangʼana gho obhureri, bhakareeta ebhitabho bheebho no okobhechuki no omorro mbere ya abhanto bhansi. Hano bharooche obhughori bhwe ebhinto bhiyo bhakabhona, chaare chembiri echaaru bhukongʼu, ghote ebhikwe mirongo etaano.
Igho nighoo Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro ya Omutemi Yeesu ghaare gharasancha, na kubha ne chenguru.
Amangʼana ghayo hano ghaasirre, Pauro akarora aghi momoghi gho Yerusareemu, ko kuhetera mo mikowa ghe Makedoniya na Akaya. Akabhughaa, “Hano nkohika eyo, ndatunu kohika momoghi gho Ruumi ghwiki.”
Ko riyo, ghati ya abhatooreri bhaache, aghatoma Timoteo na Erasito, bhaghende Makedoniya. Ewe omwene aghatama gho enkaagha mo omukowa gho Asiya.
Ko enkaagha eyo, riihe rikoro rikaibhoru momoghi gho Efeso, ighoro ya abhaitabherri bha Omutemi Yeesu.
Aareho omonto omwe momoghi ghuyo aare omukori we chembiri, eriina reeche aare kubherekeru Demetiriyo, aare aratuna chisanamu cha ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema waabho we ekighaikoro, rino ryare kubherekeru Aritemi. Emeremo ghiyo ghyare kubhareha abhabhaghasi bhaache chiwaara chinkoro.
Orosiko romwe, Demetiriyo aghakomani hamwe abhakori bhe emeremo bhaghendi bhaache na abhande bhano bhaare ghukora emeremo ke ghiyo. Kumaruho akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Abhasubhe bhano, mumanyire ighoo, obhwame bhwitu ko emeremo ghino bhokorwera.
Ghasi bhoono, inyu abheene nkurora mooni no okooghu bhuno Pauro oyo, amarre koruta no oghoshoori abhanto abhaaru bha Efeso hano, hamwe na abhanto bha ahase hansi ho omukowa gho Asiya. Araghamba ighoo, ghiteema bhano bhaghukoru na abhanto, bhatare Ghiteema bho obhuheene.
Ko riyo, nkoobhoha neeni, emeremo ghiitu ghino ghiraseru bhukongʼu. Ghwiki ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema waito we ekighaikoro, Aritemi omokoro, ghwiki haramanyikana kubha tare eghento. Na kuru ghiteema waito Aritemi omwene, uno aghusaasaamu Asiya yinsi na ense yinsi, araruusibhu obhokoro bhooche.”
Hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo gha Demetiriyo, bhaghakarra bhukongʼu. Bhaghasimi ghutema ekereghe bharabhughaa, “Aritemi wo Efeso newe omokoro!”
Kumaruho omoghi ghunsi gho Efeso ghughaichora riihe. Bhakaghoota Ghaayo na Arisitariko, abhanto bha Makedoniya bhano bhaare bharaghi orughendo hamwe na Pauro, bhakaghi nabhu ko ahase hano bhaare ghughora Ribhina.
Pauro naatunire ghusoha ghati yo obhooru bho abhanto, ghasi abhatambani bha Yeesu bhatamumasire.
Kuru abhabhaahi abhande bha Asiya eyo, bhano bhaare abhasaani bha Pauro, bhaghatoma abhanto, korri bhamusaasaame ighoo, ataghaasoha ko ahase hayo ho kubharanera.
Abhanto bhano bhaare bhaikomaine hayo bhakabha bharatema egheturi. Omonto wunsi akabha arakura orooche, abhande rino abhande rino. abhaaru ghati yaabho bhatamanyire kino kigherri bhaikomaine hayo he.
Abhayahuti bhakaimerri Arekisanda mbere ya abhanto bhayo, bhakamwerekereeri amangʼana gho kughamba. Arekisanda akabhakiri gho kubherekeri na amabhoko abhanto bhansi, gho okubha aare ghotuna ghwikorerra mbere yaabho.
Ghasi hano bhaamanyire kubha n-Omuyahuti, bhansi bhaghatema ekereghe ko riraka remwe, gho enkaagha ye chinsa ebhere, bharabhughaa, “Aritemi wo Efeso newe omokoro!”
Komohiko omwandeki omokoro wo omoghi ghuyo, aghakiri abhanto bhayo. Akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Inyu abhasubhe bha omoghi gho Efeso, uye atamanyire ighoo, omoghi ghuno neghu ghokurenda ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema weitu Aritemi, hamwe ne esanamu yaache ino yaasekiire koru mwisaaro?
Tareho omonto uno aghutora kwanga amangʼana ghayo! Ko riyo, mutende, mutaghaakora eghento ghinsighinsi ko bhongobhongo.
Mureetire abhanto bhano hano, nankabha bhataibhire ebhinto mo ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema waito. Kuru bhatatokire ghiteema waito.
Mbe, ghote Demetiriyo na bhaghendi bhaache bhaana engʼana ighoro yo omonto wunsiwunsi, ritongo nehoreeni, na abhaamori nehobhaani. Nkunaghi bhaani kohira ekiina keebho eyo.
Ghwiki urabhone mughoote engʼana yende yinsiyinsi ino moghotuna koyireeta, mooyehire ko omoghutano ghino gheghwitabheribhu na amaragherri ghiitu.
Ko bhuno tukore reero, ngotunu yaare tusemeru, gho okubha tukore riihe ereeru. Na turasemeru ighoro ya amangʼana ghano, tutaghoote ngʼana iyo yinsiyinsi ino ekugheri tuhaatoru.”
Hano riihe re Efeso hayo ryaasirre, Pauro akabherekera abhatambani bha Yeesu, akabhateremi bhatighe kobhooha. Kumaruho akabhabhoorra akaghi, aghatanora koghi mo omukowa gho Makedoniya.
Akabha araheta gho ekyaro kiyo, arabhabhoorra abhaitabherri amangʼana amaaru gho okubhateremi bhatighe koobhoha. Kumaruho akahika gho ekyaro ke Ughiriki,
akamara eyo emieri etato. Hano aare haghuhe kugharoka ko omukowa gho Siriya na aare ko obhooto , akabhona amangʼana ighoo, Abhayahuti bhabhoorraine komukorra amasineenu. Ko riyo, akarora agharoke ko kuhetera omukowa gho Makedoniya.
gho enkaagha eyo, Pauro aare aratambana na Sopatero omoona wa Piro, wo momoghi gho Bherooya, Arisitariko na Sekundo, abhanto bho momoghi gho Thesaronike, Ghaayo, omonto wo momoghi gho Deribhe, Timoteo, na abhanto bhabhere koru omukowa gho Asiya, Tikiko na Torofimo.
Abhanto bhayo, bhaghakangata koghi momoghi gho Tirowa bhaghatughanya eyo.
Hano enyangi ye emighaate ghino ghitatorru ehamiira yaasirre, tukaru momoghi gho Firipi ko obhooto. Tughakora orughendo ro chensiko isaano, neho twahikire Tirowa. Hano twaahikire eyo, tughasikana na bhaghendi bhiitu bhayo. Tughaikara hayo, chensiko mohungate.
Orosiko ro ghwansa rwe wiiki, tughaikomana hamwe, korri tusonore omughaate. Neho, Pauro aghasimi kweeghi abhanto, akaghenderri kuhekera obhotiko bho ghati, gho okubha etabhoori yaache ngutanora aare.
Chaaremu chitara echaaru chirooka mokenyumba kiyo ke ghatato ke eghorofa kino tware twikomanirre.
Ko ridirisha re eghechumba kiyo, aare aikaire omomura omwe uno aare kubherekeru Eutiko. Omomura oyo aghasimi kohuna mbaka chitoro chikamohira akamisi, gho okubha Pauro naghenderiri kweeghi gho enkaagha entambe. Hano aare amisiri, akahetera ko ridirisha riyo, koru moghorofa ya ghatato, akagho harense. Abhanto hano bhaaghire komughegha, bhakabhona amarre ghoku.
Pauro nawe akahiringita harense. Akabhumara ighoro yo omomura oyo, akamokumbatiya, akabhoorra abhanto bhayo akabhughaa, “Mutakoobhoha! No muhoru!”
Kumaruho Pauro akariina ghwiki mo eghechumba kiyo, aghasoonora omughaate akari. Akaghenderri kweeghi kuhekera etabhoori, neho atanwere.
Abhanto bhayo bhakaghegha omomura woore aghwiire, bhakamohira ka aani omuhoru, bhaghachomeru bhukongʼu.
Pauro akaghi momoghi gho Aso ko amaghoro, ghote muno aare atunire. Itu tukariina mobhooto tughakangata koghi eyo.
Tughasikana Aso eyo, tukamughegha mobhooto, tukaghi hamwe momoghi gho Mitirene.
Etabhoori yaache, tukaghenderri no obhooto bhuyo, tukaheta mbareka mo righinga rino reere kubherekeru, Kio. Hano bhwaakiire, tukaghenderri no orughendo, tukahika ko righinga rino reere kubherekeru Samo, tughaikara momoghi gho Tiroghiriyo. Orosiko runo , tukahika momoghi gho Mireto.
Pauro aare aseemiri kughenderri no orughendo bhira kuheta momoghi gho Efeso, korri ataghaacha kughechera ko omukowa gho Asiya eyo. Aare aratuna kubha momoghi gho Yerusareemu bhongo, itamaraehika enyangi ya Bhentekosite etaraahika, ghote ekanaghire.
Pauro hano aahikire Mireto, aghatoma amangʼana momoghi gho Efeso, kubherekera abhagharuka bha ekanisa bhaache arorane nabhu.
Hano bhaachire, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Inyu abheene mumanyire bhuno namenyire na inyu, koru orosiko runo naahikire mo omukowa gho Asiya hano.
Naare ndakora emeremo Omutemi Yeesu ko obhwitabherri bhukongʼu na ko chengisori. Naare ndaghomerri amacharibhu ghano ghaare kumbona, gho okugheri Abhayahuti bhano bhankoriire omorwecho.
Mumanyire ighoo, ntinaatighire kubhareghaneri engʼana yinsiyinsi ino okobhatoreri inyu. Nekyu kyaagheri naare kweeghi bhurabhu bhurabhu na enyumba ko enyumba.
Naare ndabhabhoorra Abhayahuti hamwe na bhano bhatare Abhayahuti ighoo, bhamwishooreri Ghiteema na oghwitabherri Omutemi waito Yeesu Kirisito.
“Bhoono, eni nenkumeriribhu ne Enkoro Ehoreeru ighoo, ngende momoghi gho Yerusareemu. Ko riyo nakaghi, nankabha timanyire kino ghekumbona eyo.
Ghasi, kino manyire n-ighoo, momeghi ghinsi ghino naare kuheta, Enkoro Ehoreeru aare konyereki ighoo, ebhibhohe ne enyanko nkunganya bheeni.
Kuru ndaku, tere eghento haare eni, gho okubha ndatuna ghimarre emeremo ghino Omutemi Yeesu ahaire nkore. Emeremo ghiyo, n-okureghanerri abhanto Amangʼana Amachomu ghe enooko ya Ghiteema.
“Ghasi bhoono nimanyire ighoo, inyu bhansi, bhano nareghanirri obhukangati bho Ghiteema, mutakundora ghwiki.
Ko riyo, ndabhabhoorra bhurabhu reero ino ighoo, ghote omwe waanyu asirre, amaanyinga ghaache ghataakubha ighoro yaane,
gho okubha kira rino Ghiteema aatunire mumanye, naare ndabhabhoorra bhira koobhoha.
Enkoro Ehoreeru abhatoore inyu, kubha abhaimererri bha abhaitabherri bha Ghiteema. Ko riyo, mwiyangarre, na mubhe murangara abhaitabherri bhaache, gho okubha Yeesu omwene nahomwere amaanyinga ghaache ghutoori abhaitabherri bhayo.
“Nimanyire ighoo, hano ndabha atanwere, abheeghi bho obhurongo bharaacha bhasohe mo ekanisa. Mbarasoha ghote esunche ko eghikomo kya amangʼondi na bhaatakwabhera abhaitabherri.
Kuru koru ghati yaanyu abheene, bharahyoka abhanto bhano bharatabhuta obhuheene, korri bharute abhatambani bhabhatambane.
Ko riyo, mwiyangarre! Mubhe murahiita ighoo, ko enkaagha ye emeeka etato, obhotiko no omwise ntinaatighire kubhasaasaama kira omwe waanyu, ko chengisori.
“Bhoono mbe, ndabhatoora mumabhoko gha Ghiteema na amaragherri ghe enooko yaache. Ewe aghoote amanagha gho kobhabheka na kubhasakeri kunaghi, mubhone omurembe ghuno aatorire abhanto bhaache, bhano bharabhiribhu.
“Eni ntinare kwighombu chembiri cho omonto wunsiwunsi, kuru chizahabhu chaache hande engebho yaache.
Inyu abheene mumanyire ighoo, naare ghukora emeremo ko amabhoko ghaane omwene, korri kubhona bhino naare ghotuna eni na bhino bhaghendi bhaane bhaare bhaare ghotuna.
Kira engʼana ino naare ghukora, naabherekeriri ighoo, ko enchera yo oghukora emeremo ko ghwikongʼi, turatunu ghutoori bhano bhataana amanagha. Mubhe murahiita amangʼana ghano Omutemi Yeesu omwene aabhughiree, ‘Koruusi ghuchomu, ghukera kuhaabhu.’ ”
Pauro hano aamarre kughamba amangʼana ghayo, akahighima hamwe na bhayo bhansi, aghasaasaama Ghiteema.
Kumaruho bhansi bhaghakuura bhukongʼu, bhaghakumbatia Pauro no okomobhusu.
Engʼana eno yaakorre bhabhabhayere bhukongʼu, n-ighoo aare abhabhoriire ighoo, bhatakomurora ghwiki. Mbe, bhakamuherekerra, bhakamohiki ko obhooto bhoore.
Hano twaamarre kuaghana na abhagharuka bhe ekanisa ye Efeso hayo, tukariina mo obhooto, tukaghi kemwe kemwe mbaka tukahika mo eghesiwa kino kyare kubherekeru Kosi. Hano bhwaakiire, tukaghi mo eghesiwa kino kyare kubherekeru Roto. Koru hayo, tukaghi ghwiki kuhekera tukahika momoghi gho Patara.
Hayo, tukabhona ho obhooto obhonde bhuno bhware komboka koghi mo omukowa gho Foinike. Tukariina muyo tukaghi nabhu.
Hano twahikire ahase hano tware kurora eghesiwa ke Kipuro, tukaheta orubhareka ro bhachuuta, tukaghenderri kuhekera tukahika mo omukowa gho Siriya. Hano twahikire momoghi gho Tiiro mo omukowa ghuyo, tughasekera koru mo obhooto bhuyo, gho okubha hayo neho bhaare ghusekerri emerigho.
Tughasikana na abhatambani bha Yeesu bha eyo, tughaikara nabhu chensiko mohungate. Abhatambani bhayo, bhakabha bharaghamba ko amanagha ghe Enkoro Ehoreeru, bhaghaseghani Pauro atakaaghi momoghi gho Yerusareemu.
Hano chensiko chiitu cho kubha hayo chaasirre, tughatanora kughenderri no orughendo rwiitu. Abhatambani bhansi, abhasubhe hamwe na bhakaabho na abhaana bhoobho, bhaghatuherekera mbaka kibhara yo omoghi ghuyo. Tukahighama mongoghoni hayo, tughasaasaama Ghiteema.
Kumaruho tukaaghana, tukariina mo obhooto bhuyo, ebhu bhakagharoka ka.
Tukaghenderri no orughendo rwiitu koru Tiiro hayo, tukahika momoghi gho Toremayi. Tughakeeri abhaitabherri bha hayo, tughaikara nabhu orosiko romwe.
Etabhoori yaache, tughatanora mbaka momoghi gho Kaisariya. Tughaikara mo enyumba ya Firipo, uno aare omweghi wa Amangʼana Amachomu ighoro ya Yeesu. Na wunsi aare omwe wa abhatooreri mohungate bha abhatomu bhano bhaare bhachaghwiiru Yerusareemu eyo.
Firipo oyo, aare na abhanke bhane, bhano bhaare bhakeere ghutetu na bhaare na amanagha gho koruusi obhurooti.
Hano tware twikaire orosiko nyabhurebhe Kaisariya hayo, aachire omurooti omwe, koru omukowa gho Yuudeya. Omurooti oyo, aare kubherekeru Aghabho.
Aghabho oyo, aghaacha haare itu, akaghegha omukanda gho Pauro, akaibhoha ko amaghoro na amabhoko ghaache omwene. Kumaruho akabhughaa, “Enkoro Ehoreeru aghambire abhughiree, ‘Igho niigho Abhayahuti bharamubhoha omwene omukanda ghuno Yerusareemu eyo, no komughooti ko abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti.’”
Mbe, hano tooghwiire kehayo, itu hamwe na abhaitabherri bha hayo, tughasaasaama Pauro bhukongʼu aghoo, atakaaghi Yerusareemu.
Ghasi Pauro akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Ndasabha motighe ghunkoorra no okonyita omotema. Eni nibhangire kubhohu kuru ghokweera Yerusareemu hayo, gho okugheri yo Omutemi Yeesu.”
Hano twaarooche Bhauro taaghotuteghera, tukamotigha, tukabhughaa, “Amaigha gho Omutemi ghakorru.”
Amangʼana ghayo hano ghaasirre, tughaiseemi, tughasimi orughendo ro koghi Yerusareemu.
Abhatambani abhande bha Yeesu bha Kaisariya hayo, bhaghatutambana, bhaghatohiki Yerusareemu o Munasoni, uno tware koghi ghwikara waache. Munasoni oyo aare omonto we eghesiwa ke Kipuro, na aare omwe wa abhatambani bha ghwansa.
Hano twaahikire Yerusareemu hayo, abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhiitu bhaghatughaghani ko amachomeru.
Etabhoori yaache, tukaghi na Pauro ghosikana na Yaakobho. Na abhagharuka bhe ekanisa bhansi neho bhaareho.
Hano Pauro amarre kobhakeeri akabhabhoorra amangʼana ghansi remwe kuru erende, ghano Ghiteema aare ghukora ko abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti gho kuhetera amabhoko ghaache.
Hano bhooghuure amangʼana ghayo, bhaghaitumi Ghiteema. Kumaruho bhakabhoorra Pauro bhakabhughaa, “Omwitabherri mughendi waitu, urarora ghote muno Abhayahuti ebhikwe ko ebhikwe bhaitabherri Yeesu. Bhayo bhansi, bhaana gwikong'i bhukongʼu kughoota amaragherri gha Musa.
Ghasi, bhabhooriiru ighoro yaacho aghoo, ureeghi Abhayahuti bhansi bhano bhamenyire ko ebhyaro bha abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, bhatighe kughoota amaragherri ghayo. Ghwiki aghoo, urabhaseghani ighoo, bhatighe ghusaara abhaana bhaabho, na bhatighe kughoota esemoka ya Abhayahuti.
Bhoono tukore bhwe? Obhuheene bharooghu ighoo, ooni hano.
Ko riyo, ukore engʼana ino toghokubhoorra. Ghati yiito hano, neho bhaani abhasubhe bhane, bhano bhaariire emuuma mbere ya Ghiteema.
Mbe, mughootane nabhu, mwiirabhi hamwe nabhu, obharehere bhaghasu chetuuki chaabho. Ko ghukora igho, kira omonto aramanya aghoo, amangʼana ghano bhaabhooriiru ighoro yaache, ghataare gho obhuheene na ghwiki aghoo, iye uraghoota amaragherri gha Musa.
Ghasi, ko orubhareka ro bhano bhatare Abhayahuti, bhano bhaghwitabherri Yeesu, twaabhandekiire amangʼana ghano twaaroche. Twaaroche aghoo, bhatakaabha bhararaaghera ebhyakori muno bhino okubhona bhisengirru emisambu, bhatakaabha bharari amaanyinga, kuru enyama ye etyenyi ino ebhuusiru, na bhataghaacha ghotwara.”
Neho icho yaache, Pauro akabhahira abhasubhe bhane bhayo, akairabhi hamwe nabhu. Aghasoha mo ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema, korri kureghani orosiko runo okurabhibhu koobho koghosira, na kira omwe waabho iratunu aruusi ekemwenso.
Hano chensiko mohungate cho okurabhibhu koobho kwahekeraine, Abhayahuti abhande koru omukowa gho Asiya, bhaarooche Pauro mo ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema. Bhaghasegheeri obhooru bha abhanto bhansi, bhakamughoota.
Ko riraka rikoro bhakabhughaa, “Inyu Abhaisiraeri bhaghendi bhiitu, motusakeri! Omonto uno newe areeghi abhanto bhansi bha kira ahase ighoo, bhabhe bharatuserra no ghusera amaragherri gha Musa, kuru ne enyumba yo ghusengera Omutemi ghiteema ino. Ghotigha ghayo ghansi, asohiri abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti mo ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema, ko riyo, akore ahase ahahoreeru hano habhaire ahanabhi.”
Mbaabhughire kehayo, gho okubha bhaare bhaarooche Pauro momoghi hamwe na Torofimo. Ko riyo, mbaitegheriire aghoo, Pauro aare amusohiri mo ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema. Torofimo oyo, aare omonto wa Efeso.
Ko riyo, omoghi Yerusareemu ghunsi ghughaichora riihe. Abhanto bhaghaacha bhararyera koru ahase hansi, bhakaghoota Pauro. Kumaruho bhakamoruta koru mo ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema muyo. Emirango ghe enyumba ya ghiteema ghikaigharu.
Hano bhaare bharatuna komwita, amangʼana ghakahekeera omokoro wa abhasirikare bha Abharumi aghoo, omoghi gho Yerusareemu ghunsi ghwichwire riihe.
Hari remwe, akaimoki eghikomo kya abhasirikare hamwe na abhaimererri bhaabho, bhaghasekera bhararyera koghi ko riihe eyo. Abhanto bhano bhaakorre riihe hano bhaarooche omokoro oyo na abhasirikare bharaacha, bhaghatigha ghutema Pauro.
Kumaruho omokoro oyo, aghaisuka akaghoota Pauro, akahamerra ighoo, abhohu ne eminyorro ebhere. Akamara akabhughaa, “Uno ne-uye? Na ke akorre?”
Hari remwe, abhanto abhande ghati ya obhooru bhoore, bhaghatema ekereghe bhukongʼu, abhande bharabhugha rino, abhande reere. Omokoro oyo, akarora aghoo, taghutora kumanya obhuheene bho kino ghikoru, akaghamba aghoo, Pauro ahiru ko ahase ha abhasirikare.
Hano Pauro aahikire ko engazi, abhasirikare bhakamusambeka, gho okubha riihe rya abhanto bhaare, ryare rikoro bhukongʼu.
Abhanto bhaare komutambana, bhakaghenderri ghutema ekereghe bharabhughaa, “Momwite oyo!”
Hano abhasirikare bhayo bhaare haghuhe ghusohi Pauro mo ahase haabho, Pauro akabhoori omokoro waabho oyo akabhughaa, “Kana, ndaitabheribhu nkubhorre engʼana emwe?” Kumaruho omokoro oyo, akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Kana, iye umanyire Ekeyunaani!
Iye utare Omomiisiri uno gho chensiko cha bhongo hano aasimiri riihe, no okwerekerri bhaitu ebhikwe bhine, koghi mwiteregho?”
Pauro akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Eni n-Omuyahuti, omwibhoru wo omoghi gho Tariso mo omukowa gho Kirikiya. Omoghi ghuyo n-omokoro bhukongʼu. Ndaghusabha onyitabherri ngambane na abhanto bhano.”
Mbe, omokoro oyo akamwitabherri, Pauro akaimerra ko engazi, akaimoki abhanto bhayo okubhoko, korri bhakire. Bhansi bhaghakira, Pauro akaghambana nabhu, ko ekighambo keebho ke Ekeebhurania. Akabhugha,
“Inyu abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaane na bha taata, mutegherre, nikoorre mbere yaanyu!”
Abhanto bhayo, hano bhooghuure Pauro araghamba gho ekighambo keebho ke Ekeebhurania, bhaghakira kiri. Pauro akaghenderri kughamba arabhughaa,
“Eni n-Omuyahuti, omwibhoru wo omoghi gho Tariso mo omukowa gho Kirikiya. Ghasi hano Yerusareemu nareriiru . Ghamarieri newe anyeghiiri kughoota no kwangarra amaragherri ghano twaahaabhiru na bhasookoro bhiitu. Naikongʼiri bhukongʼu ghukorra emeremo ghe Ghiteema, ghote bhuno inyu murakora reero ino.
“Naare kunyanki bhukongʼu abhanto bhano bhaaghootire Enchera yo Omutemi Yeesu, kuru abhande bhaghaitu. Naare ndaghoota abhasubhe na abhaghaikoro no akabhabhoha mokibhohe.
Ghayo nkubhabhoorra inyu, kuru Omusengeri omokoro hamwe na abhakoro Abhayahuti bhansi ghughaimerera bhaare.
