Abhakoro bhayo nebhu bhaare bhahaire chinyarubha cho kobhaheerra Abhayahuti bhaghendi bhaitu bho moghi ghuno ghokubherekeru Damasiko. ngatanora koghi eyo, korri mbabhohe abhatambani bha Yeesu bha eyo, mbarete Yerusareemu hano , korri bhateneru ekiina
“Hano naare haghuhe kohika Damasiko, yaare ghote ensa ya ghasansabha cho omwise, hari remwe emirengaari emeroro koru mwisaaro ghikamoreki ahase hansi.
Nkagho harense, nkooghu riraka riramboorra rirabhughaa, ‘Sauri, Sauri! N-gooke okunyanki?’
Nkagharokeri nkabhughaa, ‘Omutemi iye ne-uye?’ Nawe akagharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Eni neeni Yeesu wo Naasareeti, uno iye okunyanki.’
Bhaghendi bhaane bhano tware kughendani nabhu, mbaarooche emirengaari gheere, ghasi bhatoghwiire riraka ryo omonto uno aare kughambana na eni.
Nkamubhoori nkabhughaa, ‘Omutemi, nkore bhwe?’ Nawe akagharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Imerra! Usohe Damasiko. Muyo, urabhoorru amangʼana ghansi ghano oghutakeru ghukora.’
Enkaagha eyo ntaare kurora, gho okubha emirengaari gheere ghyare ghyehukuri. Neho, bhaghendi bhangoteriire amabhoko, bhakahira Damasiko.
“Mbe, Damasiko hayo, aareho omonto omwe. Omonto oyo, aare kubherekeru Anania. Ewe aare kwighwera Ghiteema na aare ghwikongʼi bhukongʼu kughoota amaragherri ghaitu, ghwiki aare arakumibhu bhukongʼu na Abhayahuti bhansi bha eyo, aghoo, aare omonto omuchomu.
Akanyichera akaimerra mbareka yaane, Akamboorra akabhughaa, ‘Omwitabherri mughendi waane Sauri, unaghi kurora ghwiki!’ Hayo hayo, amaiso ghaane ghakaramoki ghwiki, nkamurora.
“Kumaruho akaghenderri kumboorra akabhughaa, ‘Ghiteema wa bhasookoro bhaitu, akohwiire korri umanye amaigha ghaache. Aratuna umanye aghoo, newe omwene obhuheene, na omongu araghamba ko omonu ghooche omwene.
Akorre igho, gho okubha urabha omwimererri waache ko abhanto, urabhabhoorra amangʼana ghansi ghano waarooche no okooghu.
Bhoono n-ke ukeere uraghanya? Imerra! Ubhaatiisibhu, omusaasaame Ghiteema korri weghibhu ebhibhe bheecho.’
“Kumaruho nkagharoka Yerusareemu. Hano naare ndasaasaama Ghiteema mo ahase ho oghusengera Omutemi Ghiteema, hari remwe, nkaroghoora, nkarora amaroro.
Ko amaroro ghayo, naarooche Omutemi Yeesu aramboorraa, ‘Kooranguru, oru momoghi gho Yerusareemu muno, gho okubha abhanto bha momoghi ghuno bhataghwitabherri obhwimererri bhuno okubha uraruusi ighoro yaane.’
Kumaruho eni nkamugharokeri nkabhughaa, ‘Ghasi Omutemi, abheene mbamanyire bhuno naare koghi mochenyumba cha Abhayahuti cho oghusaasaameramu Ghiteema, korri mbabhohe mokibhohe no okubhatema abhanto bhano bhaare koghitabheeri.
Kuru enkaagha ino amaanyinga gho omwimererri waacho Sitebhano ghaitekiire, eni ghwiki naare nimeriire haghuhe. Ngaitabherri aghoo, aitu, ne chingebho cha bhano bhamwiitire, neeni naare ghochirenda.’
Yeesu wunsi akamugharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Nooghi, gho okubha ndaghutoma ughende kure, ko abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti.’ ”
Eghikomo kya abhanto bhaare, ghutegherra bhaare Pauro bhwaheene. Ghasi hano abhughire engʼana yo kumarerri eyo, bhaghasimi ghutema ekereghe bharabhughaa, “Omonto uno taghutakeru abhe omuhoru, Momwite!”
Hano abhanto bhayo, bhaare ghutema ekereghe no okoghucha ghuncha chingebho chaabho ighoro, ino bharamincha orotu.
Omokoro wa abhasirikare woore hano aarooche kehayo, akabhoorra abhasirikare bhaache ighoo, bhasohi Pauro ko ahase yaabho ho kubhohera abhanto, bhamuteme ne emicharichi, korri aghambe kino kigherri abhanto bhayo bhamukomore.
Ghasi, abhasirikare hano bhaamarre komubhoha gho chensiri, korri bhamuteme, Pauro akabhoori omwimererri waabho uno aare aimeriire hayo akabhughaa, “N-obhuheene amaragherri gha Abharumi ghwitabherri ghaani komutema Omorumi, kuru akeere ghukengeru ekiina kubha, nasarri?”
Omwimererri oyo, hano ooghwiire amangʼana ghayo, akaghi kubhoori omokoro wa abhasirikare arabhughaa, “Uratuna komukorra bhwe? Omonto uno no-Morumi.”
Mbe, omokoro wa abhasirikare oyo, akaghi haare Pauro, akamubhoori akabhughaa, “Mborra, iye no-Morumi?” Pauro akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Ee no-Morumi neeni.”
Omokoro oyo wa abhasirikare akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Eni naarusiri obhwame obhooru bhukongʼu kubha Omorumi.” Pauro akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Ghasi eni no-Morumi wo okwibhoru.”
Hari remwe, abhasirikare bhano bhaare ghotuna kumubhooreri amangʼana, bhakamotigha. Omokoro waabho, akoobhoha bhukongʼu kooghu aghoo, Pauro no-Morumi, gho okubha aare amubhohire ko eminyorro.
Omokoro wa abhasirikare oyo, aatunire kumanya obhuheene bho kino kigherri Pauro aghasemeru na Abhayahuti. Ko riyo, hano bhwaakiire, akamutanchora no kuragherri abhakoro bha abhasengeri ne ritongo rinene rinsi bhaikomane. Kumaruho akareeta Pauro, akamwimerri mbere yaabho.
Pauro akabhamoghorra abhanto bhe ritongo rikoro, akabhughaa, “Bhaghendi bhaane, nimbaire ndaikara ko omotema omuchomu mbere ya Ghiteema, kuhekera reero ino.”
Omusengeri omokoro Anania hano ooghuure kehayo, akabhoorra bhano bhaare bhaimeeriire haghuhe na Pauro aghoo, bhamuteme ekoofi komonu.
Kumaruho Pauro akabhoorra Anania akabhughaa, “Ghiteema wunsi araghutema, iye omwitaami! Ooni nke endighi ino ihakiru echokaa! Iye wikaire hano, korri unkengere ekiina ghote amaragherri ghaani. Ghasi, iye omwene toghughakora amaragherri ghayo, gho okubha urarora aghoo, ntemu ekoofi.”
Abhanto bhano bhaare bhaimeeriire haghuhe na Pauro, bhakamubhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Iye, uratoka omusengeri omokoro wo Omutemi Ghiteema?”
Pauro akabhagharokeri akabhughaa, “Bhaghendi bhaane, naare timanyire kehayo, newe omusengeri omokoro! Nimanyire yandekiru irabhughaa, ‘Utakaamughamba amasineenu omubhaahi waanyu.’ ”
Enkaagha eyo, Pauro aare amanyire aghoo, ghati ya abhanto bhayo, abhande na-Masadukaayo na abhande n-Amabharisaayo. Ko riyo, akabhugha ko riraka rikoro mbere ye ritongo riyo akabhughaa, “Bhaghendi bhaane, eni no-Mobharisaayo, omoona wa Amabharisaayo. Ninsemeeru hano, gho okubha ndaitengʼera kubha, abhaku bhararyoka.”
Hano aamarre kughamba igho, riihe righasimi ghati ya Amabharisaayo na Amasatukaayo. Ritongo riighatwenekana,
Amasatukaayo bhaare kwanga kubha, abhaku bhataakoryoka, koru abhamaraika ne chinkoro chitareho, kuru Amasatukaayo ngaamanyire ghayo ghansi ghatareho he .
Mbe, ghati ya abhanto bhayo, hakabhaho no oghutonani bhukongʼu. Abheeghi abhande bha amaragherri gha Musa bho orubhareka ro Amabharisaayo bhakaimerra, bhaghatonani bharabhughaa, “Tutakurora obhosineenu bhuyo bhunsi bhunsi ko omonto uno! Ubhone n-emisambu hande maraika, newe akabhugha nawe!”
Riihe rikabha rikoro, kuhekera omokoro wa abhasirikare akoobhoha aghoo, abhanto bhe ritongo riyo, bhaana komunyahaara Pauro. Kehayo, akahamera abhasirikare bhaghende bharuusi Pauro ghati yaabho gho chenguru, bhamusohi ko ahase ha abhasirikare haabho.
Obhotiko bhuyo bhuyo, Omutemi Yeesu akaimerra haghuhe na Pauro, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Teremi omotema ghoocho! Ghote bhuno wanyimererire momoghi gho Yerusareemu hano, kehayo hayo iratunu onyimerere na momoghi gho Ruumi.”
Hano bhwaakiire, Abhayahuti abhande bhaghakora omorwecho gho kwibhisa, bhakari emuuma aghoo, bhayime ebhyakori no okonyo kuhekera hano bhaghwita Pauro.
Abhanto bhano bhaariire emuuma eyo, bhaare kuheteera mirongo ene.
Kee hayo, bhakaghi ko abhakoro bha abhasengeri na abhakoro bha Abhayahuti, bhakabhabhoorra bhakabhughaa, “Ntorire emuuma aghoo, tuyinyima kuraaghera no okonyo eghento kiyo ghinsighinsi, kuhekera hano toghwita Pauro.
Mbe bhoono, inyu hamwe na abhakoro bhaghendi bhaanyu bhe ritongo, musabhe omokoro wa abhasirikare, areete Pauro haare inyu. Mwikori aghoo, muratuna komurohera bhwaheene ighoro ya amangʼana ghano tokomusemera. Itu twiseemiri komwita, enkaagha eno atamarahiika hano.”
Ghasi, omwiho wo Pauro nooghwiire ighoro yo oghuseemi koobho kuyo. Ko riyo, akaghi ko ahase ha abhasirikare bhayo, akabhoorra Pauro.
Neho, Pauro akabherekera omwimererri omwe wa abhasirikare, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Hira omomura uno ko omokoro waanyu, naghoote engʼana yo okomubhoorra.”
Kumaruho, omwimererri wa abhasirikare oyo, akamohira ko omokoro waabho, akamubhoorra akabhughaa, “Omubhohe Pauro, naamberekiire no oghusabha aghoo, ndeete omomura uno haare iye, naghoote engʼana yo oghokubhoorra.”
Omokoro wa abhasirikare oyo, akaghoota omomura oyo okubhoko, akaghi nawe ahase hano bhakubha abheene, kumaruho akamubhoori akabhughaa, “Nke oghotuna umborre?”
Omomura oyo, akamubhoorraa, “Abhayahuti bhaitabheraini aghoo, bhaghusabhe ohire Pauro etabhoori ghwitongo reebho. Bharaikori aghoo, bharatuna komurohera bhwaheene ighoro ya amangʼana ghano bhakomusemera.
Mbe, iye otighe ghwitabherri, gho okubha abhanto bhayo bharaheteera mirongo ene, na bharaghonyera Pauro monchera, korri hano akuheta, bhamwite. Abhanto bhayo, bhaariire emuuma yo kwiyima kuraaghera no okonyo eghento ghinsighinsi, kuhekera hano bhakomwita. Bhoono mbaiseemiri bharaghanya oghwitabherri ghoocho.”
Kumaruho omokoro oyo, akabhoorra omomura oyo akabhughaa, “Utaghaacha kubhoorra omonto wunsiwunsi aghoo, umbooriire omorwecho ghuyo!” Kumara akamwitabherri aghende.
Mbe, omokoro wa abhasirikare oyo, akabherekera abhaimererri bhabhere bha abhasirikare, akabhabhoorra akabhughaa, “Mubhange abhasirikare amaghana abhere bhaghende gho kughenda na amaghoro, abhasirikare mirongo mohungate ebhu bhabhe ne chifaraasi, na abhasirikare maghana abhere ebhu bhabhe na amatimo. Bhaghende momoghi gho Kaisariya enkaagha ye ensa ya ghatato obhotiko.
Mubhangere Pauro wunsi, efaraasi yo komughegha, korri ahike bhwaheene o Feriki, omubhaahi wa Abharumi.”
Omokoro wa abhasirikare oyo, akaandeka enyarubha irabhughaa,
“Iye omusooke Feriki, omubhaahi waitu, Ndaghukeeri eni Kiraudiyo Risiya.
Omonto uno akaghootu na Abhayahuti, bhaghatuna komwita.Hano naabhwine amangʼana aghoo, no-Morumi, nkaghi hamwe na abhasirikare, nkamutoori.
Naatunire kumanya eghento kino ghekugheri Abhayahuti bhayo bharamusemerra, ko riyo, nkamohira ghwitongo reebho.
Nkarora aghoo, bharamusemerra ighoro ya amangʼana gha amaragherri ghoobho. Ghasi ko ghano bhaare komusemera, itareho engʼana kuru emwe ino yakagheeri aitu hande abhohu.
Hano naabhooriiru aghoo, Abhayahuti mbakorre omorwecho ighoro yo omonto uno, ndooche ighoo, nemureete haare iye eyo nguru. Na mbaabhooriire abhanto bhano bhakomusemera ighoo, bhaache komusemera haare iye.”
Mbe, abhasirikare bhayo, bhakaghegha Pauro, ghote muno bhaare bhaabhooriiru, bhakamohira obhotiko bhuyo, kuhekera momoghi ghuno ghware kubherekeru Antibhatiri.
Hano bhwaakiire, abhasirikare bhano bhaare koghi bharaghenda na amaghoro bhakagharoka, bhaghatigha bhaghendi bhoobho bhe chifaraasi bhahire Pauro.
Mbe, hano bhaahikire momoghi gho Kaisariya, bhakamuha omubhaahi we Ekerumi enyarubha yeere hamwe na Pauro.
Nawe hano aamarre ghusoma enyarubha eyo, akabhabhoori akabhughaa, “Omonto uno, w-ahayi?” Hano abhaabhooriire aghoo, w-omukowa gho Kirikiya,
akabhoorra Pauro akabhughaa, “Ndaghutegherra, hano bhano bhaghoghusemera bhakohika.” Kumaruho akahamera aghoo, Pauro arendu morense ya ahase ahakoro ho omutemi Herote.
Chensiko esano hano chaahetire, omusengeri omokoro Anania, akahiringita momoghi gho Kaisariya, aani hamwe na abhakoro abhande bha Abhayahuti, no omuragherri omwe wa amaragherri ghe ense. Omuragherri oyo, aare kubherekeru Terituro. Bhayo bhansi, mbaakaghi o Feriki, omubhaahi we Ekerumi, komusemera Pauro.
Hano Pauro areetiru, Terituro aghasimi komusemera arabhughaa, “Eee omusooke Feriki, iye niye oghukora turabha ne emirembe chensiko chino chinsi. Obhubhaahi bhoocho bho obhungʼaini bhurakorra amangʼana amasineenu gharabha amachomu monse muno.
Turaitabherri obhubhaahi bhoocho ko amachomeru chensiko chinsi, na turaghokumi bhukongʼu kira ahase, na gho kira enchera.
Bhoono ntaghaacha ghokurosi bhukongʼu, ndaghusabha ko obhwitabherri bhoocho, otutegheerre hasuuhu.
“Torooche aghoo, omonto uno, n-omusegherri bhukongʼu. Ewe arasegherri Abhayahuti kobyaro bhinsi no oghotuna riihe resimi ghati yaabho. Hamwe na ghayo, newe omokoro we etiini yo obhurongo ya Abhanasareti.
Hano aaseemiri ghusari ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema, hari remwe tukamughoota. [Tughatuna komukengera ekiina kurengʼaana bhuno amaragherri ghaitu ghakwenda.
Ghasi, Risiya omokoro wa abhasirikare, aghaacha akamoruusi mo amabhoko ghaitu gho chenguru,
akabhugha aghoo, itu bhano tokomusemera, tuuche komusemera haare iye.] Ko riyo, iye omwene uranaghi uramurohera no okumanya obhuheene ighoro ya amangʼana ghansi ghano tokomusemera.”
Amangʼana gha Terituro ghayo, Abhayahuti bhaghaitabherri aghoo, n-go obhuheene.
Kumaruho, Feriki akorota Pauro ekeera, korri wunsi aghambe. Mbe, Pauro aghasimi kughamba arabhughaa, “Eni nimanyire aghoo, iye ubhaire omwamori we ekyaro kino ko enkaagha ye emeeka emeeru. Ko riyo, ndaikorerra bhira ehaho.
Iye omwene uranaghi kumanya aghoo, chitamara chiheta chensiko ikomi na ebhere, koru hano naaghire momoghi gho Yerusareemu, ghusaasaama Ghiteema.
Bhano bhano bhaghunsemera, bhataabhwine ndanyerana chinkaani hande ndasegherri omonto wunsiwunsi ko ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema, hande mochenyumba cha Abhayahuti cho ghusaasaameramu Ghiteema hande ahase ahande hansihansi momoghi ghuyo.
Kuru amangʼana ghano bhaghunsemera bhoono, bhatakunaghi kwereki aghoo, n-go obhuheene.
“Ghasi, ndaitabherri mbere yaacho ighoo, ndasaasaama Ghiteema wa bhasookoro bhaitu na ndaghoota Enchera yo Omutemi Yeesu ino ebhu bhakoibherekera aghoo, ne-tiini yo obhurongo. Hamwe na ghayo, ndaitabherri amangʼana ghansi ghano gharaghambu na amaragherri gha Musa, na ghano ghaandekiru ko ebhitabho bhya abharooti.
Eni ningoote obhwisegho o Ghiteema aghoo, araryokora abhaku bhansi, bho obhuheene na bhe ebhibhe. Abhanto bhayo bhansi bharaitabherri ke hayo hayo.
Ke hayo, chensiko chinsi ndaikongʼi, kubha no omotema omuchomu mbere ya Ghiteema na mbere ya abhanto.
“Mbe, hano emeeka emeeru ghaahetire nkahochoka Yerusareemu, nkaghi eyo ne ebhinto bho ghutoori abhanto bhe ekyaro keene abhatobhu, no okoruusi ekemwenso o Ghiteema.
Hano abhanto bhano bhaabhwine ko ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema ndakora amangʼana ghayo, enkaagha eyo naare marre kurabhibhu. No orosiko runo nasohire ne eghikomo kya abhanto kuru ntakorre riihe rinsirinsi muyo. Ghasi ko ghusengera Ghiteema, bhaareho Abhayahuti abhande koru ekyaro ke Asiya.
Bhayo nebhu bhaghotunu kwimerra mbere yaacho no ghunchongera haare iye, ghote bhakabhaire ne engʼana haare eni.
“Hande abhanto bhano bhaani hano, bhaghambe obhusari bhuno bhaarooche haare eni hano naimeriire mbere ye ritongo reebho rikoro.
Ubhone mbaarooche obhosineenu, hano naaghambire engʼana emwe ko riraka rikoro, ghatighati yaabho nkabhughaa, ‘Nchongiiru mbere yaanyu hano reero, gho okubha ndaitabherri aghoo, abhaku bhararyoka.’”
Mbe, Feriki naare amanyire obhuheene ighoro ye Enchera yo Omutemi Yeesu. Ko riyo, aaghakubhi ekiina keere gho kughamba arabhughaa, “Ndaakenga ekiina keenyu, hano omokoro woore wa abhasirikare Risiya, aghuucha.”
Kumaruho, Feriki akamubhoorra omwimererri wa abhasirikare oyo aare hayo aghoo, arende Pauro. Ghasi, abhe aramutegherra omweya gho ghukora amangʼana ghaache, ataghaseghani abhasaani bhaache, komutoori ko amanagha ghaache ghano aghotuna.
Hano chaahetire chensiko nsuuhu, Feriki oyo, aghaacha hamwe na mughaache uno aare kubherekeru Durusira, na Durusira oyo n-Omuyahuti aare. Mbe, aghatoma aghoo, Pauro abherekeru. Pauro hano aahikire, omubhaahi Feriki aghasimi komutegherra, arabhugha ighoro yo ghwitabherri Kirisito Yeesu.
Pauro aghasimi kubhabhoorra ghansi ghano ghaghotunu mbere ya Ghiteema, na ighoro yo kwireki ghukora amasineenu, na ghote bhuno Ghiteema arakengera abhanto ekiina. Feriki hano ooghuure ke hayo, akoobhoha. Akabhoorra Pauro akabhughaa, “Bhoono iye utaghi. Ndakubherekera ghwiki, hano nkubhona omweya.”
Hamwe na ghayo, Feriki aare ghwitegherra aghoo, Pauro aramuhonga, ko riyo, aare komubherekera bherekera hari kaaru, araghambana ghambana nawe.
Hano emeeka ebhere ghyaahetire, Porikiyo Fesito akabha omubhaahi, ko omweya gho Feriki. Na ko kubha Feriki aare aratuna ghwichomi ko Abhayahuti, akamotigha Pauro mokibhohe.
Enkaagha Fesito aare amarre chensiko etato echeene cho obhubhaahi ko omukowa gho Yuudeya, akaru momoghi gho Kaisariya, akariina koghi momoghi gho Yerusareemu.
Eyo, abhakoro bha abhasengeri na abhakoro abhande bha Abhayahuti, bhakamutambana bhakamubhoorra ghansi ghano bhaare komusemera Pauro. Bhakabha bharamusaasaama bhukongʼu
ighoo, abhakorre bhwaheene ko kubhagharokeri Pauro Yerusareemu hayo. Bhaare bharamusaasaama, gho okubha bhaare bhakorre omorwecho ghwiki gho ghwitera Pauro monchera.
Fesito akabhagharokeri ighoo, “Pauro ararendu Kaisariya eyo, na eni omwene ndagharoka eyo bhongo hano.
Ko riyo, tughende hamwe na abhande bha abhakoro bhaanyu, bhaghende bharamuchongera eyo, ghote asarri engʼana yinsiyinsi.”
Fesito hano aamarre ghwikara nabhu, ko enkaagha ye chensiko inyaanye hande ikomi, akagharoka Kaisariya. Etabhoori yaache, akabherekera eritongo, aghaikara ko eghetumbe gheeche ke ghukengera ebhiina, akaghamba ighoo, Pauro areetu.
Pauro hano aahikire hayo, Abhayahuti bhano bhaare bharweriire Yerusareemu, bhakaimerra ko okwinaara, bhaghasimi komusemera amangʼana amaaru amarito. Ghasi mbaatamiru kwereki obhuheene bho amangʼana ghayo.
Neho, Pauro aghasimi ghwikorerra, ighoo, “Eni ntasarri engʼana yinsiyinsi ighoro ya amaragherri gha Abhayahuti, hande ighoro ya ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema, hande ighoro ya Kaisari.”
Fesito aare aratuna ghwichomi ku Abhayahuti, ko riyo akabhorri Pauro ighoo, “Uraitabherri koghi Yerusareemu, korri ukengeru ekiina eyo, mbere yaane, ko amangʼana ghayo?”
Pauro akamugharokeri ighoo, “Nimeriire ghati ya abhaamori bhano bhoohwiru na Kaisari, na neho hano ngotunu nkengeru ekiina. Iye omwene umanyire bhwaheene ighoo, ntasariiri Abhayahuti eghento ghinsighinsi.
Mbe, ubhone nasarri engʼana eno eghunkora ndatuneru ghoku, ntakuseghani ghoku. Ghasi, ghote amangʼana ghano Abhayahuti bhano bhaghusemere ghatare gho obhuheene, atareho uno aghutora ghuntoora mumabhoko yaabho! Ndasabha ighoo, ekiina keene ghikengeru na Kaisari omwene!”
Mbe, Fesito hano aamarre kughambana na abhanto bhe ritongo, akagharokeri ighoo, “Urasabha ighoo, Kaisari newe aghukengere ekiina. Mbe bhoono, uraghi ko Kaisari!”
Chensiko nsuuhu echeene hano chaahetire, omutemi Herote Aghiribha hamwe na Bherinike monke waache, bhakahika Kaisariya, korri komukeri omubhaahi Fesito.
Mbaaikaire hayo, chensiko echaaru. Orosiko romwe, Fesito akabhoorra omutemi Aghiribha amangʼana ighoro ya Pauro, arabhugha ighoo, “Aani hano omonto omwe, aatighiru mokibhohe na omubhaahi Feriki.
Hano naare Yerusareemu, abhakoro bha abhasengeri, hamwe na abhakoro bha Abhayahuti, mbaambooriire amangʼana ghano bhaare bharamuserra. Bhaghasaasaama ighoo, mukengere ekiina.
Nkabhagharokeri nkabhughaa, itu Abharumi, tutaghukengera ekiina omonto enkaagha ataraikorerra mbere ya abhasemeri bhaache.
Ko riyo, nkaghaeroka hano, hamwe na abhasemeri bha Pauro bhayo. Etabhoori yaache, ntaghechiire, nkaikara ko eghetumbe keene ke ghukengera ebhiina, nkakenga ekiina ighoo, Pauro areetu.
Hano areetiru, abhasemeri bhaache bhakaimerra, bhaghasimi komusemera, ghasi amangʼana ghano bhaamusemiire, ghataare amasineenu ghote muno naitegheriire.
Bhaare okunyeerana chinkaani na Pauro ighoro ya etiini yaabho abheene, na ighoro ya omonto omwe uno arabherekeru Yeesu. Omonto oyo aakuure, ghasi Pauro, ewe araghamba ighoo, aani muhoru.
Na eni, timanyire ghote muno nkanaghiri kumanya obhuheene bho amangʼana ghayo. Mbe, nkabhoori Pauro ghote aghaitabheriir koghi Yerusareemu, korri akengeru ekiina eyo ighoro ya amangʼana ghano.
Ghasi, Pauro aghasaasaama ighoo, ekiina gheeche ghikengu na Kaisari, na ighoo, atame hano mokibhohe kuhekera enkaagha eyo. Ko riyo, ngakenga ekiina arendu, kuhekera hano nkomohira eyo.”
Neho, Aghiribha akamubhoorra Fesito ighoo, “Eni nawe, ndasaigha komutegherra omonto oyo.” Fesito akamugharokeri ighoo, “Uramutegherra etabhoori.”
Hano bhwaakiire, Aghiribha hamwe na Bherinike, bhaghaacha ko obhuchomu bhukongʼu. Bhaghasoha eghechumba kye ritongo, hamwe na abhakoro bha abhasirikare, na abhakoro bha momoghi. Kumaruho omubhaahi Fesito akaragherri ighoo, Pauro areetu.
Mbe, Fesito akabhugha ighoo, “Omutemi Aghiribha, na inyu bhansi bhano mooni hamwe na itu hano, murarora omonto uno! Ehamate yinsi ya Abhayahuti bha Yerusareemu na bha Kaisariya hano, bhansaasaamire mbatoorri komukengera ekiina, eno bharatema ekereghe ighoo, taghotunu aghenderri kubha muhoru.
“Eni omwene ndooche ighoo, takorre eghento ghinsighinsi kino ghekugheri aitu. Ghasi ansabhire ighoo, amangʼana ghano ghakengeru ekiina na Kaisari, ko riyo, ngakenga ekiina ighoo, ahiru momoghi gho Ruumi.
Eni timanyire obhuheene bhunsibhunsi ighoro ya omonto ono, bho kwandekera omukama waitu omokoro. Ko riyo, mureetire mbere yaanyu hano, ekinene haare iye omutemi Aghiribha, korri hano tokumara komubhoori eno, mbone eghento ghyo kwandeka ighoro yaache.
Eni ndarora ighoo, tare bhwaheene kohira omubhohe Ruumi eyo, bhira kwereki amangʼana ghano arasemeru.”
Neho Aghiribha akabhoorra Pauro ighoo, “Witabherribhu ghwikorerra.” Igho, Pauro akaimoki okubhoko, aghasimi ghwikorerra ighoo,
“Eee omutemi Aghiribha, ndairora ngoote ebhahati, gho okubha nimeriire mbere yaacho reero, ghwikorerra ku ghansi ghano Abhayahuti bhaghunsemera.
Ndaghamba kee hayo gho okubha iye umanyire bhwaheene esemoka yinsi cho Abhayahuti, na ghansi ghano bhakunyeerana chinkaani. Ko riyo, ndaghusabha ughomerri ghuntegherra.
“Abhayahuti bhansi bhamanyire bhwaheene eteemo ino naare neyu ko ekyaro ghiitu, koru obhoona bhoone, kuhekera kohika enkaagha eno naamenyire momoghi gho Yerusareemu.
Bhoobho mbamanyire ko enkaagha entambe, na ghote bharatuna, bharatora konduuseri obhwimererri ighoo, naare Omubharisaayo. Na Amabharisaayo, nebhu bhaghwikongʼi bhukongʼu kughoota amaragherri ghansi ghe Ekiyahuti, kuru ghukera abhande bhansi bhe etiini yiito.
Bhoono, nimeriire hano, nkengeru ekiina gho okubha ndasaigha okurengi kuno Ghiteema aabharengire bhasookoro bhiitu.
Kuno neku okurengi kuno amakabhira ikomi na abhere ghe ekyaro ghiitu, gharaitenga kurora irahekeerana. Kiyo nekyu keghukora bharasaasaama Ghiteema omwise na obhotiko. Na eni reero, ee omutemi, ndasemeru na Abhayahuti gho kugheri ko ghwitengʼera rirengi riyo!
Ngooke inyu mokwanga ghwitabherri ighoo, Ghiteema araryoki abhaku?
“Eni omwene naare ghwitegherra ighoo, ndatunu ghukora ghansi ghano nkunaghi, korri kureki eriina re Yeesu wo Naasareeti.
Ghayo neghu, naakorre Yerusareemu eyo. Ku amanagha gho obhubhaahi koru ku abhakoro bha abhasengeri, naabhohire abhaitabherri abhaaru mokibhohe. Na enkaagha eno bhaare ghukengeru ekiina kyo ghoku, eni ghwiki naare ghati ya bhayo bhaare kubhakengera ekiina.
Hari kaaru naare ndaghi mochenyumba chinsi, korri kubhaghoota enchagho no kubhahamerri bhatighe Yeesu. Ghukarra koone haare ebhu ikagheri ngende kuru momeghi ghende mobhyaro ebhende, korri mbanyanki.
“Orosiko romwe, naare monchera ndaghi momoghi gho Damasiko, ghukora emeremo ghiyo ko amanagha gha amaragherri koru ko abhakoro gha abhasengeri.
Eee omutemi, hano naare ko nchera iyo, enkaagha ye ensa isansabha omwise igho, nkarora obhurabhu obhorro bhukongʼu, koru mwisaaro. Obhurabhu bhuyo, bhware ghooka ghukera ereebha. Kumaruho, bhukamorekeri ahase hansi, hamwe na bhano naare nabhu.
Bhansi tukagho harense. Neho nooghure riraka riramboorra gho Ekeebhurania ighoo, ‘Sauri, Sauri! ghooke okunyanki? Ake urainyahaara bhuchu, ghote entekere eno aratema omuseghere ehimbo yo omutemi waache!’
“Kumaruho nkabhoori nkabhughaa, ‘Omutemi, iye ne-wuuye?’ Nawe Omutemi akagharokeri akabhughaa, ‘Eni neeni Yeesu, ono iye okunyanki.
Bhoono, bhooka wimerre! Nkohyokiire, korri ngukore ubhe omubhaghasi waane. Urabha urareghaneri abhanto abhande, amangʼana ghano orooche reero, na ghano nkubha ndakwereki.
Ndabha ndaghutoori koru ku Abhayahuti bhaghendi bhaacho, na ku abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti. Ndabha ndaghutoma koobho,
korri ubharamoki maiso, bhaishoori koru mokeruutu, bhasohe mo obhurabhu, bharu mo amanagha ghe Risambu, bhaishooreri Ghiteema. Ko ghukora igho, neho kwabheru ebhibhe bheebho, bharabha hamwe na abhande bhansi, bhano bharabhiribhu gho nchera yo okonyitabherri eni.’
“Ko riyo, ee omutemi Aghiribha, tinaatighire ghukora ghote muno naabhooriiru ku amaroro ghayo koru mwisaaro.
Ghasi, ngasimi kweeghi abhanto bha Damasiko, ighoo bhatiite ebhibhe bheebho, bhaishooreri Ghiteema na ghukora ghano ghakwereki ighoo bhaishoorire mo emetema gheebho. Ghwiki nkeeghi amangʼana ghayo ghayo, ko abhanto bha Yerusareemu, na ko abhanto bha mo omukowa ghunsi gho Yuudeya. Kuru ko abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti naare kubheeghi kee hayo hayo.
Ghayo neghu naakorre Abhayahuti bhakangoota, hano bhaabhwine ahase ho oghusengera Omuteemi Ghiteema, bhaghatuna konyita.
Ghasi, Ghiteema ansakiire kuhekera kohika orosiko ro reero. Kiyo nekyu ghekugheri ndaimerra mbere ya abhanto, abhakoro na abhasuuhu, koruusi obhwimererri bho amangʼana ghano naarooche. Ghatareho amangʼana aghande ghano nkughamba, ghasi n-gaare ghaare ghano ghaaghambiru na abharooti na Musa ighoo, gharahyoka.
Bhansi bhakabhugha ighoo, Kirisito aranyankibhu, na ighoo, ewe arabha wo ghwansa okuryoka koru mobhaku, korri areghani ighoo, amangʼana amachomu ighoro ya omutoori, bhoono aramorekeri abhanto bhansi, Abhayahuti na abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti.”
Hano Pauro aare akeere arikorerra, omubhaahi Fesito akamuteneeri ko riraka rikoro akabhughaa, “Iye Pauro, nochuurre! Ghasi obhumanyi bhoocho obhooru bhoghukorre ochuurre?”
Ghasi, Pauro akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Eee omusooke Fesito, eni ntare omochuuru. Amangʼana ghano nkughamba n-go obhuheene na n-go obhungʼaini.
Kuru omutemi amanyire bhwaheene ighoro ya amangʼana ghano. Nimanyire ighoo, itareho engʼana kuru emwe ghati ya ghano eno atamanyire, gho okubha ghataare ghahyokire kebhisire. Ko riyo, nkomubhoorra naare ghayo, bira ehaho.
Eee omutemi Aghiribha, ghansi ghano ghaaghambiru na abharooti, uraghaitabherri? Eni nimanyire bhwaheene aghoo, uraghaitabherri.”
Hayo, Aghiribha akabhoori Pauro akabhughaa, “Uraitegherra aghoo, uransegheri nibhe Omokirisito ku amangʼana amasuuhu kee ghano?”
Pauro akamugharokeri akabhughaa, “Ibhe n-ku amangʼana amasuuhu, hande ku amangʼana amaaru, ndasaasaama Ghiteema ighoro yaacho, na ighoro ya abhande bhansi bhano bhaghuntegherra reero ighoo, bhabhe ghote muno eni neni, ghasi bhira kubhohu ne eminyorro ghino.”
Hayo omutemi akaimerra, hamwe na omubhaahi Fesito na Bherinike, na abhande bhano bhaare bhaikaire hamwe.
Enkaagha eno bhaare ghutanora hayo, bhakaragherrani ighoo, “Omonto ono takorre engʼana yinsiyinsi eno ekugheri aitu, hande abhohu mokibhohe.”
Kumaruho, Aghiribha akabhoorra Fesito akabhughaa, “Yakabhaire aghoo, omonto ono ataasabhire ekiina gheeche ghikengu na Kaisari, aare kuhaatooru.”
Kumaruho ekiina ghikabhotorru ighoo, tughende ko obhooto mokyaro ke Itariya. Pauro na abhabhohe abhande bhaghatooru ko omwimererri omwe wa abhasirikare. Omwimererri oyo, aare kubherekeru Yuriyo, we ghekomo kya abhasirikare bhano bhaabherekiiru ighoo, “Eghekomo ke Kaisari Augosuto.”
Tukariina mo obhooto bhuno bhwaruure momoghi gho Adiramitiyo. Obhooto bhuyo, bhware ghotuna koghi ko chino cheeni mongoghoni yo omukowa gho Asiya. Tughasimi orughendo ro itu hamwe na Arisitariko, omonto koru momoghi gho Tesaronike mo omukowa gho Makedoniya.
Etabhoori yaache, tukahika ko mongoghoni yo omoghi gho Sitooni. Yuriyo aghakora Pauro amachomu, ko komwitabherri aghi kurorana na abhasaani chaache, korri bhamuhe ebhinto muno aare ghotuna.
Koru yeere, tukaheta mbareka ye righinga rino rekubherekeru Kipuro, gho okubha obhukama obhorro bhoruure eno tware turaghi.
Tukoomboka enyancha, orubhareka rwe mikowa ghe Kirikiya na Bhambiriya, tukahika momoghi gho Mira omukowa gho Rikiya.
Eyo, omwimererri wa abhasirikare oyo, akabhona obhooto bha momoghi gho Arekisandiriya bhuno bhwaghiire Itariya, aghatoriini muyo.
Tukaghi ihoraihora gho enkaagha ye chensiko echaaru na gho etaabhu bhukongʼu, kuhekera tukahika haghuhe na omoghi gho Nido. Hano twatunire kuheta, obhukama obhororo hughatureki, bhukagheri twinaare orubhareka ro bhachuuta bho righinga re Kirete, haghuhe na rasi eno yaare kubherekeru Sarimone.
Tukaheta mbareka ko chitaabhu bhukongʼu, kuhekera tukahika ahase hano haabherekiiru ighoo, “ Enchomu,” haghuhe na omoghi gho Raseya.
Tware tumarre enkaagha entambe konyancha, no orughendo rwitu rughasimi kubha rwe enyanko, gho okubha enkaagha yo obhukama obhororo konyancha bhware bhosimiri. Ko riyo, Pauro akabharagherri bhaghendi bhaache bhayo ighoo,
“Bhamure, ndarora ighoo, orughendo ro itu runo, rurareeta enyanko enkoro, tare ko obhooto ne emerigho ebhyene, ghasi kuru itu abheene.”
Ghasi, omwimererri wa abhasirikare oyo, ataitabhiriire obhughambi bho Pauro, akarora ighoo, bhutaana ewaara, aghaitabherri amangʼana gho omukangati wo obhooto n-omwene obhooto.
Mbe, bandari yeere bhaareho itaare no omweya enchomu gho ghwikara, enkaagha ye embeho endoro. Ko riyo, abhanto abhaaru ghati yaabho bhaghaitabherri ghutanora koore, ahande bhaare kunaghi kohika Bhoyinike no ghwikara eyo enkaagha ye embeho. Bhoyinike n-bandari eno yaare ko righinga re Kirete, yaare orubhareka ro ghoosi ya roghoro na bhachuuta ya roghoro, hano na obhukama.
Mbe, obhukama obhuchomu bhughasimi kuherra, koru orubhareka ro bhachuuta. Bhukagheri bho obhooto bhaitegherre ighoo, bharanaghi kohika hano bhaghutuna. Kumaruho bhakaiha enanga bhakaghenderri no orughendo roobho, bhakaheta mbareka mongoghoni ye righinga re Kirete.
Ghasi, hano yaahetire enkaagha ensuuhu eyeene, obhukama obhororo bhuno bhokubherekeru “Eurakiro,” bhughasimi kuherra koru koru kwighinga re Kirete.
Obhukama bhuyo, bhukabha bhuratema tema orubhareka ro obhooto. Tughasaki ghosindana nabhu, ghasi tughatamu. Tughatigha bhotohire ghatighati ye enyancha.
Tukaheta nyuma ya righinga hasuuhu rino rekubherekeru Kauda, righatureki hasuuhu ekiruumbe kiyo. Hayo tukanaghi ko nyanko ghutoori obhooto obhosuuhu bho ghutooreri abhanto, bhuno bhware kohiru na amanche.
Hano abhakori bhe emeremo bho obhooto bhaamarre koriini obhooto obhosuuhu morense yo obhoobho bhoore, bhakainaari chensiri obhooto bhoobho bhunsi, bhakabhoha . Bhaare bharoobhoha ighoo, bhaare kunaghi kuhaghaeru mwisense re enyancha ye ekyaro ke Ribhiya. Ghotiina kuyo, ghukagheri bhaghasekeri matanga, bhaghatigha obhooto bhohiru no obhukama.
Amayengo ghenderri ghutema obhooto bhuyo ko chenguru. Etabhoori yaache, abhakori bhe emeremo bhayo, bhaghasimi ghutabhuta emerigho monyancha.
Orosiko ro ghatato, bhaghasimi ghutabhuta ebhinto bhyo obhooto monyancha na amabhoko ghaabho abheene.
Chikaheta chensiko echaaru ereebha na chinchota bhitakoonekana, na enyancha ikabha iraghenderri ghusareka. Ikagheri toku emetema kubha tutakuhona.
Hano echaaru chaahetire bhira kuraaghera eghento, Pauro akaimerra ghati yaabho, akabhugha ighoo, “Inyu abhasubhe, mware ghotunu kooghu na ghotigha ghutanora koru yeere Kirete. Hano mwaghantegherire, ghano ghansi ghataare ghotubhona.
Bhoono ndabhasabha ighoo, mutaaghaku omotema, gho okubha atareho kuru omwe waanyu ono aghoku, ghasi obhooto bhuno nebhu bhoghusareka.
Ndaghamba kee hayo, gho okubha eni u-wa Ghiteema na newe ono ndasengera. Obhotiko bho reero maraika waache ahyokiire,
akamboorra akabhughaa, ‘Pauro, tigha koobhoha! Uratunu kwimerra mbere ya Kaisari. Na umanye ighoo, Ghiteema arabhatoori ko enooko yaache, bhansi bhano wooni hamwe nabhu ko orughendo.’
Mbe bhoono, eni ghwiki ndabhabhoorra ighoo, mutaaghaku omotema! Eni ndaitabherri ighoo ghano Ghiteema ambooriire, gharakoru.
Ghasi, turahingiru ko righinga nyabhurebhe.”
Tukamaraho chensiko ikomi na inye, turahingiru no obhukama obhorro, koghi eno na eyo, ko enyancha ya Adiriya. Orosiko ro ikomi na kane ruyo, obhotiko bho ghati, abhakori bhe emeremo ghyo obhooto, bhakarora ghote bhaani haghuhe ne ekyaro .
Ko riyo bhakarengi obhutambe bhwa amanche, bhakabhona ebhekubha mirongo ebhere. Kumaruho bhaghaisuka mbere hasuuhu, bhakarenga ghwiki, bhakabhona ebhikubha ikomi na bhitaano.
Bhakoobhoha ighoo, obhooto bhuraitema ku amaghena, ko riyo bhakaimerra bhakarekera chensika inye mu amanche, nyuma yo obhooto. Kumaruho bhaghasabha ighoo, bhoki bhongo.
Abhakori bhe emeremo bho obhooto bhayo, bhaghatuna kungʼosa bhatighe obhooto. Ko riyo, bhaghasekeri mumanche obhooto bho ghutooreri abhanto, bhaghaikori ighoo bharasekeri chensika chende orubhareka ro mbere ro obhooto.
Hari remwe, Pauro akabhoorra omwimererri wa abhasirikare oyo, hamwe na abhasirikare bhaache akabhughaa, “Uraabhone abhakori bhe emeremo bho obhooto bhano bhatatamire mo obhooto muno, tutakuhona!”
Ko riyo, abhasirikare bhayo bhaghakenga chensiri chino chaare chibhohire obhooto bho ghutooreri abhanto bhuyo, bhakabhotigha bhugheghu na amanche.
Hano bhwaatunire ghoki, Pauro aghasimi kusaasaama bhaghendi bhaache bhayo bhari ebhyakori, arabhabhoorra arabhughaa, “Reero n-orosiko ro ikomi na kane koru mughootu no ghotiina na mutaakarire eghento ghinsighinsi.
Bhoono, ndabhasaasaama muraaghere, korri mutaaghaku na omuramboko. Muraaghere, gho okubha kuru orotuuki ro ko omotwe gho omwe waanyu rutaghosira.”
Hano aamarre kughamba igho, akaimoki omughaate, aghakumi Ghiteema mbere yaabho bhansi, aghasoonora, aghasimi kuraaghera.
Hari remwe bhansi bhakabha no omotema, bhaghasimi kuraaghera.
Bhansi bhano tware mo obhooto muyo, tware ghote maghana ebhere na mirongo mohungate na bhasansabha.
Hano bhaighotire, bhakarekera engano monyancha, korri bhasuuhi obhorito bho obhooto.
Etabhoori , abhakori bhe emeremo mo obhooto bhuyo, bhataamanyire ekyaro keere, ghasi bhaarooche na omweya gho kohika ko mongoghoni. Bhaghakenga ekiina koghi kohika eyo obhooto bhoobho ghote ekanaghire.
Igho, bhaghakenga chensiri che chensika bhaghachetigha monyancha. Ghwiki bhakanyoonyooghi chensiri chino chaare chibhohire obhosikani bho obhooto. Bhakahaneka ritanga risuuhu mbere yo obhooto korri riichori obhukama, bhakaghi ko .
Ghasi, hano obhooto bhwaisukire mbere hasuuhu, bhakahika ahase hano emingeri ghya amanche gheghosikana. Ororeme ro obhooto rughatocha momusense gho chenguru, rukangeramu. Ahase ha nyuma haghatemu temu na amayengo, kuhekera bhughasimi kubhaaroka ebhetene tene.
Kumaruho, abhasirikare bhaghatuna ghwita abhabhohe bhansi, korri bhataghaacha kurabhacha bhangʼose.
Ghasi, omwimererri wa abhasirikare oyo, aatunire ghutoori Pauro, ko riyo, akabhareki bhataghakora igho. Akaghamba akabhughaa, bhano bhakunaghi kurabhacha, bharabhache kuhekera mongoghoni,
na abhande bhano bhatamanyire kurabhacha, bhaghoote chimbao ne ebhinto bhende bhyo obhooto. Ko ghukora kee hayo, abhanto bhansi mbaahikire gho ekyaro bhwaheene.
Hano twaruure konyancha kuyo bhwaheene, neho twamanyire kubha, tooni ko righinga rino rekubherekeru Merita.
Abhamenyi bha hayo, bhaghatughaghaani bhwaheene bhukongʼu. Bhaghatuhembera omorro, gho okubha yaare enkaagha ye embeho, na embura yaare iteekire, bhaghatughaghaani bhansi ghoota omorro ghuyo.
Pauro aghateenya omorigho obhosuuhu igho ghweo chinkwe. Hano aare ghochitoora momorro, enchoka ikaru mo chinkwe chiyo, gho kugheri kwe ebhyowa bhyo omorro, ikainaanjera gho okubhoko pouro ikamuroma.
Abhamenyi bhe righinga riyo, hano bhaarooche enchoka eyo, eritunda gho okubhoko gho Pauro, bhaghasemerrani bharabhughaa, “Omonto uno n-omwiti. Nankabha ahonire kwibheera monyancha muno, omokoro waitu ono akubherekeru ‘Omuheene’, takomotigha aghenderri kubha omuhoru.”
Ghasi, Pauro aghasamunsera enchoka eyo momorro, tanyaharekire kuru hasuuhu.
Abhanto bhayo bhaghaitegherra ighoo, arabhimba hande aragho harense, hari remwe aku. Ghasi hano bhaghanyire gho enkaagha entambe no kurora ghitareho kino kemobhweni, bhaghashoori obhughambi bhoobho, no kughamba ighoo, ewe n-omwe wa bhaghiteemi bhaabho.
Mbe, hano toombokire, haare haghuhe ne emeghondo ghyo omokoro we righinga riyo. Omokoro oyo, aare kubherekeru Pubhuriyo. Pubhuriyo oyo, aghatughaghaani bhwaheene waache ka, tukamara eyo chensiko isato.
Ko enkaagha eyo, isawaabho Pubhuriyo aare amisiri kobhorre, abhabhaire, aghoote ehooma na aare ghusaaha amaanyinga. Pauro aghasoha monyumba komurora. Hano aamarre komusaasaamera haare Ghiteema, akamutoorra amabhoko ighoro yaache, akahora.
Hano engʼana eyo yaaikorre, abharwire abhande bhansi ko righinga riyo, bhakabha bharaichera Pauro, nawe akabha arabhahori.
Abhanto bha hayo, bhakabha bharatusooka bhukongʼu. Na hano twatunire ghutanora, bhaghatoriineri mobhooto ebhinto bhinsi bhino twaatunire.
Hano twamarre emieri etato ko righinga riyo, tughasimi orughendo ro obhooto bhuno bhware bhusekiiri chensika, bhuraghanya enkaagha ye embeho eyo esire. Obhooto bhuyo, bhware bho momoghi gho Arekisandiriya, na bhware bhungʼorru esanamu ya Bhaghiteemi Ebhisare.
Tukahika momoghi gho Sirakusa, tughaikara hayo chensiko isato.
Hano twaruure hayo, tukainaara mbareka mo enyancha, tukahika momoghi gho Reghiyo. Etabhoori yaache, obhukama bhukahuuta koru orubhareka ro bhachuuta, bhukagheri orosiko ro kabhere tukahika momoghi gho Puteori.
Eyo, tughasikana na abhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaitu haare Kirisito, bhaghatusaasaama bharabhughaa, tubhe nabhu chensiko mohungate. Hano chaasirre, tukaghoota nchera koghi momoghi gho Ruumi.
Abhakirisito bhaghendi bhaitu bha Ruumi eyo, hano bhooghuure ighoo, tooni monchera turaghi haare ebhu, bhaghaacha mo Momoteera gho Apiyo, na ahase hano hakubhekeru “Chenyumba cha bhagheni Etato” ghotuturungʼana. Hano Pauro aabharooche, aghakumi Ghiteema na aghasambaroka bhukongʼu.
Hano twahikire momoghi gho Ruumi, Pauro aghaitabheribhu kubha monyumba yaache omwene, hamwe na omosirikare wo komurenda.
Hano chensiko etato chaasirre, akabherekera hamwe abhakoro bha Abhayahuti bha hayo. Hano bhaikomaine, akabhabhoorra ighoo, “Bhaitabherri bhaghendi bhaane, nankabha ntakorre engʼana ensineenu ko abhanto bhiitu, ghasi ko esemoka ya bhasookoro bhiitu, ghasi naaghootiru momoghi gho Yerusareemu, nkahiru ku Abharumi.
Hano Abharumi bhayo bhaamarre kumboorerri, bhaghatuna kuhaatora, gho okubha bhataabhwine ne risari rino rekugheri niitu.
Ghasi Abhayahuti bhakanga, ntakaahatoru. Ko riyo, ngasaasaama ighoo, ekiina keene ghikengu na Kaisari Ruumi eyo. Tare aghoo, naare ngotuna kubhasemera abhanto bhe ekyaro keene.
Mbe, ghayo neghu ghagheri mbabherekiire, korri mbarore tughambane hamwe. Eni hano mbohiru gho okubha ndaitabhirrirya Kirisito oyo newe ubhweseghe bho Abhaisiraeri bhansi.”
Hayo, abhakoro bha Abhayahuti bhayo, bhakamugharokeri ighoo, “Itu tutamarabhona enyarubha yinsiyinsi koru ko omukowa gho Yuudeya, ino iraghamba ighoro yaacho. Na omonto wunsiwunsi tamarahika hano kughamba amangʼana amasineenu ighoro yaacho.
Ghasi itu, toratuna kooghu muno iye uraitegherra, gho okubha tumanyire ighoo etiini ino uraghoota, iraghambu amasineenu kira ahase.”
Ko riyo, bhaghaikererrani na Pauro orosiko rono bhariikomana. Hano orosiko ruyo rohikire, bhaghaacha abhanto abhaaru morense ya enyumba ino aare ekaire. Pauro akabhabhoorra na kubhahonyorra ighoro yo obhukangati bho Ghiteema, koru etabhoori kuhekera omughoroobha, aatunire ighoo, bhoobho bhaitabherri Yeesu. Ikagheri abheeghi amangʼana ighoro ya Yeesu ko oghutumira amaragherri gha Musa, na ebhitabho bhe abharooti.
Abhande bhaghaitabherri amangʼana ghano aabhughire, ghasi abhande bhataitabhiriire.
Ko riyo, abheene ko abheene bhataitabherraine. Mbe, hano bhaare bharaghi, Pauro akabhabhoorra engʼana emwe ighoo, “Enkoro Ehoreeru akabhugha amangʼana gho obhuheene, arabhabhoorra bhasookoro bhiitu kuhetera ko omurooti Isaaya ighoo,
‘Oghi ko abhanto bhano, abhabhoorre ighoo, Kooghu murooghu, ghasi mutakongora. Ukorigheri murarigheri, ghasi mutakurora.
Erabha igho, gho okubha emetema ghe abhanto bhano n-emikongʼu, amatwe ghoobho ghatakooghu, maiso gheebho bhaghahunderri. Bhataghotuna maiso ghoobho gharore, hande amatwe ghoobho ghaighu, hande emetema gheebho ghyongore, bhataghaache bhakanyishooreri na eni mbatoori.’”
Pauro akaghenderri kughamba ighoo, “Mbe, bhoono mumanye ighoo, amangʼana gho Ghiteema ighoro yo omutoori uno, ghahirru ko abhanto bhano bhatare Abhayahuti. Bhoobho bharaghaghoota!” [
Hano aamarre kughamba amangʼana ghayo, bhakaghi bharanyeerani chinkaani abheene ko abheene.]
Pauro akamara emeeka ebhere emighima morense ya enyumba eyo ino aare araikara omwene. Aakaribhisiri muyo bhansi bhano bhaare bharaacha ko iye.
Aareghaneri obhukangati bho Ghiteema nu kweeghi abhanto ighoro ya Omutemi Yeesu Kirisito ko bhokare, bira atakurekiru.
